(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_LOADING_EXPERIENCE_V1__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_LOADING_EXPERIENCE_V1__ = true;
  var hideTimer = null;
  var failTimer = null;
  function ready(fn){ if (document.readyState === 'loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', fn, false); } else { fn(); } }
  function text(v){ return String(v || ''); }
  function ensure(){
    var existing = document.getElementById('mle-loading-experience');
    if (existing) { return existing; }
    if (!document.body) { return null; }
    var wrap = document.createElement('div');
    wrap.id = 'mle-loading-experience';
    wrap.className = 'mle-loading-experience';
    wrap.setAttribute('role', 'status');
    wrap.setAttribute('aria-live', 'polite');
    wrap.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Loading MyLottoExpert workspace');
    wrap.innerHTML = '<div class="mle-loading-experience__panel"><div class="mle-loading-experience__eyebrow">MyLottoExpert is preparing your workspace</div><div class="mle-loading-experience__title" id="mle-loading-experience-title">Loading your lottery intelligence</div><p class="mle-loading-experience__copy" id="mle-loading-experience-copy">We are organizing your lotteries, saved predictions, scored results, and learning signals. Larger accounts can take a few extra seconds.</p><div class="mle-loading-experience__steps"><div class="mle-loading-experience__step">Loading lottery cards</div><div class="mle-loading-experience__step">Checking pending runs</div><div class="mle-loading-experience__step">Reviewing scored results</div><div class="mle-loading-experience__step">Preparing learning signals</div></div><div class="mle-loading-experience__bar"><span></span></div><div class="mle-loading-experience__recovery" id="mle-loading-experience-recovery"><button type="button" data-mle-loading-dismiss="1">Stay on this page</button><button type="button" data-mle-loading-reload="1">Reload workspace</button></div></div>';
    document.body.appendChild(wrap);
    return wrap;
  }
  function showRecovery(){
    var wrap = ensure();
    if (!wrap) { return; }
    wrap.className = 'mle-loading-experience is-active';
  }
  function armFailSafe(ms){
    if (failTimer) { window.clearTimeout(failTimer); failTimer = null; }
    return;
  }
  function show(title, copy){
    var wrap = ensure();
    if (!wrap) { return; }
    var t = document.getElementById('mle-loading-experience-title');
    var c = document.getElementById('mle-loading-experience-copy');
    if (t && title) { t.textContent = text(title); }
    if (c && copy) { c.textContent = text(copy); }
    if (hideTimer) { window.clearTimeout(hideTimer); hideTimer = null; }
    wrap.className = 'mle-loading-experience is-active';
    armFailSafe(15000);
  }
  function hide(delay){
    var wrap = document.getElementById('mle-loading-experience');
    if (!wrap) { return; }
    if (failTimer) { window.clearTimeout(failTimer); failTimer = null; }
    if (hideTimer) { window.clearTimeout(hideTimer); }
    hideTimer = window.setTimeout(function(){
      wrap.className = 'mle-loading-experience is-active is-hiding';
      window.setTimeout(function(){ wrap.className = 'mle-loading-experience'; }, 220);
    }, typeof delay === 'number' ? delay : 0);
  }
  function isSamePageHash(href){ return href && href.charAt(0) === '#'; }
  function isJavascriptHref(href){ return /^javascript:/i.test(href || ''); }
  function linkWillLoadPage(el){
    var href = el.getAttribute('href') || '';
    if (!href || isSamePageHash(href) || isJavascriptHref(href)) { return false; }
    if ((el.getAttribute('target') || '').toLowerCase() === '_blank') { return false; }
    if (/^(mailto:|tel:)/i.test(href)) { return false; }
    return true;
  }
  function isLightweightToggle(el){
    if (!el || !el.closest) { return false; }
    return !!el.closest('.mle-precision-lock-toggle,.mle-precision-lock-detail-btn,[data-mle-precision-toggle],[data-mle-method-toggle],[data-mle-disclosure-toggle],[data-mle-no-loading],.mle-remove-watched-lottery-btn');
  }
  window.mleShowLoadingExperience = show;
  window.mleHideLoadingExperience = hide;
  ready(function(){
    ensure();
    show('Loading your MyLottoExpert workspace','We are organizing your lotteries, saved predictions, scored results, and learning signals. Larger accounts can take a few extra seconds.');
    window.setTimeout(function(){ hide(0); }, 850);
  });
  window.addEventListener('load', function(){ hide(250); }, false);
  window.addEventListener('pageshow', function(){ hide(120); }, false);
  document.addEventListener('submit', function(ev){
    var form = ev.target;
    if (!form || form.getAttribute('data-mle-no-loading') === '1') { return; }
    show('Updating your MyLottoExpert workspace','We are saving your request and refreshing the related lottery data.');
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var target = ev.target;
    if (!target || !target.closest) { return; }
    var el = target.closest('a,button,input[type="submit"]');
    if (!el || isLightweightToggle(el)) { return; }
    if (el.getAttribute && el.getAttribute('data-mle-loading-dismiss') === '1') { hide(0); return; }
    if (el.getAttribute && el.getAttribute('data-mle-loading-reload') === '1') { window.location.reload(); return; }
    if (el.tagName && el.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'a') {
      if (!linkWillLoadPage(el)) { return; }
      show('Loading your selected lottery view','We are refreshing the lottery card, saved predictions, scored results, and learning context.');
      return;
    }
    if (el.type && String(el.type).toLowerCase() === 'submit') {
      show('Updating your MyLottoExpert workspace','We are applying your request and preparing the latest lottery context.');
      return;
    }
    if (el.className && /mle-v38-primary-action|mle-status-action-jump|mle-scan-pill--clickable|mle-adv-meta-item--action-needed/.test(String(el.className))) {
      show('Preparing your next LottoExpert action','We are checking the lottery context, saved runs, and available SKAI batch path.');
    }
  }, true);
}());

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_SKAI_CARD_HANDOFF_HARD_FIX_V2__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_SKAI_CARD_HANDOFF_HARD_FIX_V2__ = true;

  function closest(el, sel){ return el && el.closest ? el.closest(sel) : null; }
  function qs(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector(sel); }
  function text(el){ return String((el && (el.textContent || el.innerText)) || ''); }
  function hasClass(el, c){ return !!(el && el.classList && el.classList.contains(c)); }
  function isSkaiUrl(url){ return !!(url && String(url).indexOf('skai-lottery-prediction') !== -1); }
  function addParam(url, key, value){
    var hash = '';
    var parts;
    if (!url) { return url; }
    url = String(url);
    parts = url.split('#');
    url = parts[0];
    hash = parts.length > 1 ? '#' + parts.slice(1).join('#') : '';
    if (url.indexOf(key + '=') !== -1) { return url + hash; }
    url += (url.indexOf('?') === -1 ? '?' : '&') + encodeURIComponent(key) + '=' + encodeURIComponent(value);
    return url + hash;
  }
  function ensureBatchUrl(url, precision){
    if (!isSkaiUrl(url)) { return url || ''; }
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_skai_batch', '1');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_skai_bridge', '1');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_global_batch', '1');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_batch_scope', 'exact_lottery');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_command_source', 'mylottoexpert');
    url = addParam(url, 'source', 'mylottoexpert');
    if (precision) {
      url = addParam(url, 'mle_precision_batch', '1');
      url = addParam(url, 'mle_guided_mode', 'required');
      url = addParam(url, 'mle_required_action', 'precision_batch');
      url = addParam(url, 'open', 'precision_batch');
    } else {
      url = addParam(url, 'mle_guided_mode', 'global_learning');
      url = addParam(url, 'mle_required_action', 'regular_9_batch');
      url = addParam(url, 'mle_batch_type', 'regular_global_learning');
      url = addParam(url, 'open', 'regular_9_batch');
      url = addParam(url, 'mle_single_mode', 'best_global_settings');
      url = addParam(url, 'mle_single_source', 'global_learning');
    }
    return url;
  }
  function markStarted(el, label){
    if (!el || !el.setAttribute) { return; }
    if (!el.getAttribute('data-mle-original-label')) { el.setAttribute('data-mle-original-label', text(el)); }
    if (label && el.tagName && el.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'button') { el.textContent = label; }
    try { el.setAttribute('aria-busy', 'true'); } catch(e) {}
  }
  function clearSkaiHandoffLoading(){
    var wrap;
    try { if (typeof window.mleHideLoadingExperience === 'function') { window.mleHideLoadingExperience(0); } } catch(e1) {}
    try {
      wrap = document.getElementById('mle-loading-experience');
      if (wrap) { wrap.className = 'mle-loading-experience'; }
    } catch(e2) {}
  }
  function restoreHandoffButton(el){
    var original;
    if (!el || !el.getAttribute) { return; }
    try { el.removeAttribute('aria-busy'); } catch(e1) {}
    original = el.getAttribute('data-mle-original-label') || '';
    if (original && el.tagName && el.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'button') { el.textContent = original; }
    try { if (el.disabled !== undefined) { el.disabled = false; } } catch(e2) {}
    try { el.removeAttribute('aria-disabled'); } catch(e3) {}
  }
  function finishExternalSkaiHandoff(el){
    clearSkaiHandoffLoading();
    window.setTimeout(function(){ clearSkaiHandoffLoading(); restoreHandoffButton(el); }, 700);
    window.setTimeout(function(){ clearSkaiHandoffLoading(); restoreHandoffButton(el); }, 2200);
  }
  function storePrecisionPayload(el){
    var raw;
    var payload;
    if (!el || !el.getAttribute) { return; }
    raw = el.getAttribute('data-batch-payload') || '';
    if (!raw) { return; }
    try {
      payload = JSON.parse(raw);
      if (payload && payload.runs && payload.runs.length === 9) {
        localStorage.setItem('mle_precision_lock_batch_payload_v1', JSON.stringify(payload));
        sessionStorage.setItem('mle_precision_lock_batch_payload_v1', JSON.stringify(payload));
      }
    } catch(e) {}
  }
  function openUrl(url){
    var win;
    if (!url) { return false; }
    try {
      win = window.open(url, '_blank');
      if (win) { try { win.opener = null; } catch(ignore) {} clearSkaiHandoffLoading(); return true; }
    } catch(e) {}
    clearSkaiHandoffLoading();
    if (window.alert) { window.alert('SKAI could not open in a new tab/window. Please allow pop-ups for LottoExpert and try again.'); }
    return false;
  }
  function submitCreateBatchForm(form, button){
    if (!form) { return false; }
    if (!qs('input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', form)) { return false; }
    try { form.setAttribute('data-mle-no-loading', '1'); } catch(e2) {}
    markStarted(button || form, 'Creating 9BATCH run...');
    if (typeof form.requestSubmit === 'function') {
      if (button && button.tagName && /^(button|input)$/i.test(button.tagName) && /^(submit|image)$/i.test(String(button.getAttribute('type') || 'submit').toLowerCase())) { form.requestSubmit(button); }
      else { form.requestSubmit(); }
    } else { form.submit(); }
    finishExternalSkaiHandoff(button || form);
    return true;
  }
  function findInlineBatchForm(btn){
    var journey;
    var plan;
    var card;
    var form;
    var regularScope;
    var lotteryId;
    var fallbackCard;
    if (!btn) { return null; }
    journey = closest(btn, '.mle-v38-user-journey');
    if (journey) {
      form = qs('form.mle-v38-batch-action-form', journey);
      if (form) { return form; }
    }
    card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card');
    plan = String(btn.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '').toLowerCase();
    if (card && (plan === 'history_window_check' || plan === 'horizon_batch' || plan === 'horizon_ready_batch')) {
      form = qs('form.mle-history-window-action-form, form.mle-v38-batch-action-form[data-mle-v38-batch-action-form="horizon"]', card);
      if (form) { return form; }
    }
    if (card && (plan === 'prediction_9_batch' || plan === 'settings_batch' || plan === 'settings_ready_batch' || plan === 'next_settings' || plan === 'precision_batch')) {
      form = qs('form.mle-next-settings-run__form, form.mle-skai-batch-test__form, form.mle-v38-batch-action-form[data-mle-v38-batch-action-form="settings"]', card);
      if (form) { return form; }
    }
    if (card && (plan === 'regular_skai_batch' || plan === 'regular_skai' || isRegularSkaiButton(btn))) {
      form = qs('form.mle-regular-batch-action-form, form[data-mle-v38-batch-action-form="regular"]', card);
      if (form) { return form; }
      regularScope = qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', card);
      if (regularScope && regularScope.form) {
        form = regularScope.form;
        if (qs('input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular_9_batch"], input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular"], input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular_skai_batch"]', form)) { return form; }
      }
      lotteryId = String(card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || btn.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
      if (!lotteryId) {
        fallbackCard = closest(btn, '.mle-lottery-outer');
        lotteryId = String((fallbackCard && fallbackCard.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id')) || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
      }
      if (lotteryId) {
        fallbackCard = qs('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id="' + lotteryId + '"], [data-mle-lottery-card][data-lottery-id="' + lotteryId + '"]', document);
        if (fallbackCard) {
          form = qs('form.mle-regular-batch-action-form, form[data-mle-v38-batch-action-form="regular"]', fallbackCard);
          if (form) { return form; }
          regularScope = qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', fallbackCard);
          if (regularScope && regularScope.form) {
            form = regularScope.form;
            if (qs('input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular_9_batch"], input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular"], input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular_skai_batch"]', form)) { return form; }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return null;
  }
  function isRegularSkaiButton(el){
    var hay;
    if (!el || !el.getAttribute) { return false; }
    hay = text(el) + ' ' + String(el.className || '') + ' ' + String(el.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '');
    return /regular_skai_batch|regular_skai|global-learning|open skai global|9\s*-?batch/i.test(hay) && !!(el.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || el.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || el.getAttribute('href'));
  }
  function handleClick(ev){
    var el = closest(ev.target, '.mle-open-skai-precision-batch, .mle-regular-skai-batch-action-btn, button[data-skai-url], button[data-skai-regular-url], a[data-skai-url], a[data-skai-regular-url], a[href*="skai-lottery-prediction"], .mle-v38-primary-action, .mle-v73-btn[data-mle-v73-action="run-batch"], .mle-v73-btn[data-mle-v73-action="open-skai"]');
    var card;
    var form;
    var url;
    var action;
    var precision;
    if (!el) { return; }
    action = String(el.getAttribute('data-action-target') || el.getAttribute('data-mle-v73-action') || '').toLowerCase();

    if (action === 'history_window_check' || action === 'prediction_9_batch' || action === 'horizon_batch' || action === 'settings_batch' || action === 'next_settings' || action === 'precision_batch') {
      form = findInlineBatchForm(el);
      if (form) {
        ev.preventDefault();
        if (ev.stopPropagation) { ev.stopPropagation(); }
        if (ev.stopImmediatePropagation) { ev.stopImmediatePropagation(); }
        submitCreateBatchForm(form, qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"],button[type="submit"],input[type="submit"]', form) || el);
        return;
      }
    }

    if (hasClass(el, 'mle-open-skai-precision-batch')) {
      url = el.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || el.getAttribute('href') || '';
      precision = true;
      storePrecisionPayload(el);
    } else if (isRegularSkaiButton(el) || action === 'regular_skai_batch' || action === 'regular_skai') {
      form = findInlineBatchForm(el);
      if (form) {
        ev.preventDefault();
        if (ev.stopPropagation) { ev.stopPropagation(); }
        if (ev.stopImmediatePropagation) { ev.stopImmediatePropagation(); }
        submitCreateBatchForm(form, qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"],button[type="submit"],input[type="submit"]', form) || el);
        return;
      }
      ev.preventDefault();
      if (ev.stopPropagation) { ev.stopPropagation(); }
      if (ev.stopImmediatePropagation) { ev.stopImmediatePropagation(); }
      restoreHandoffButton(el);
      clearSkaiHandoffLoading();
      if (window.alert) { window.alert('The tracked 9-run batch form is missing. Please refresh and try again.'); }
      return;
    } else if (action === 'open-skai') {
      url = el.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || el.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || el.getAttribute('href') || '';
      precision = false;
      if (!url) {
        card = closest(el, '.mle-advisory-card');
        if (card) { url = card.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || card.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || ''; }
      }
    } else {
      return;
    }

    url = ensureBatchUrl(url, precision);
    if (!isSkaiUrl(url)) { return; }
    ev.preventDefault();
    if (ev.stopPropagation) { ev.stopPropagation(); }
    if (ev.stopImmediatePropagation) { ev.stopImmediatePropagation(); }
    markStarted(el, precision ? 'Opening SKAI batch...' : 'Opening SKAI 9BATCH...');
    openUrl(url);
    finishExternalSkaiHandoff(el);
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', handleClick, true);
})();


(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_SKAI_EXTERNAL_HANDOFF_LOADING_RESET_V1__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_SKAI_EXTERNAL_HANDOFF_LOADING_RESET_V1__ = true;
  function hideLoading(){
    var wrap;
    try { if (typeof window.mleHideLoadingExperience === 'function') { window.mleHideLoadingExperience(0); } } catch(e1) {}
    try { wrap = document.getElementById('mle-loading-experience'); if (wrap) { wrap.className = 'mle-loading-experience'; } } catch(e2) {}
  }
  function isSkaiHandoff(el){
    var hay;
    if (!el || !el.getAttribute) { return false; }
    hay = String(el.getAttribute('href') || '') + ' ' + String(el.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || '') + ' ' + String(el.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || '') + ' ' + String(el.className || '') + ' ' + String(el.textContent || '') + ' ' + String(el.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '');
    return /skai-lottery-prediction|open skai|9\s*-?batch|global-learning|mle-open-skai-precision-batch|mle-regular-skai-batch-action-btn/i.test(hay);
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var el = ev.target && ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('a,button,input[type="submit"]') : null;
    if (!isSkaiHandoff(el)) { return; }
    window.setTimeout(hideLoading, 120);
    window.setTimeout(hideLoading, 900);
    window.setTimeout(hideLoading, 2400);
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('submit', function(ev){
    var form = ev.target;
    var action;
    if (!form || !form.querySelector) { return; }
    action = form.querySelector('input[name="mle_action"]');
    if (!action || String(action.value || '').toLowerCase() !== 'create_skai_batch') { return; }
    try { form.setAttribute('data-mle-no-loading', '1'); } catch(e) {}
    window.setTimeout(hideLoading, 120);
    window.setTimeout(hideLoading, 900);
    window.setTimeout(hideLoading, 2400);
  }, true);
}());


(function(){
  function qsa(sel, root){return Array.prototype.slice.call((root||document).querySelectorAll(sel));}
  function clearCollapsedStorage(){
    try {
      var remove=[];
      for (var i=0;i<localStorage.length;i++) {
        var k=localStorage.key(i) || '';
        if (k.indexOf('mle_outer_collapsed_')===0 || k.indexOf('lottery_collapsed_')===0) { remove.push(k); }
      }
      for (var j=0;j<remove.length;j++) { localStorage.removeItem(remove[j]); }
    } catch(e) {}
  }
  function openLotteryCards(){
    var i, btn;
    qsa('.mle-lottery-outer').forEach(function(outer){
      outer.classList.remove('body-collapsed','collapsed');
      outer.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');
      qsa('.mle-lottery-outer-body', outer).forEach(function(body){body.removeAttribute('hidden');body.style.display='';body.style.maxHeight='none';body.style.opacity='1';body.style.pointerEvents='';});
      qsa('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn]', outer).forEach(function(b){b.textContent='Open';b.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');b.setAttribute('aria-label','Lottery card is open');});
    });
    qsa('.lottery-group').forEach(function(group){
      group.classList.remove('collapsed');
      group.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');
      qsa('.lottery-collapsible-content', group).forEach(function(body){body.removeAttribute('hidden');body.style.display='';body.style.maxHeight='none';body.style.opacity='1';body.style.pointerEvents='';});
      qsa('.lottery-collapse-toggle,[data-lottery-toggle-btn]', group).forEach(function(b){b.textContent='Open';b.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');b.setAttribute('aria-label','Lottery card is open');});
    });
  }
  window.mleForceLotteryCardsOpen=function(){ return false; };
  clearCollapsedStorage();
  if (document.readyState==='loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){clearCollapsedStorage();openLotteryCards();}); }
  else { clearCollapsedStorage();openLotteryCards(); }
  window.setTimeout(openLotteryCards, 250);
  window.setTimeout(openLotteryCards, 900);
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var t=ev.target && ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn],.lottery-collapse-toggle,[data-lottery-toggle-btn],[data-lottery-collapse-all-btn],[data-lottery-expand-all-btn]') : null;
    if (!t) { return; }
    ev.preventDefault();
    ev.stopPropagation();
    clearCollapsedStorage();
    openLotteryCards();
    return false;
  }, true);
}());

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_HARD_NO_LOAD_JUMP_V1__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_HARD_NO_LOAD_JUMP_V1__ = true;
  var userIntent = false;
  function markUserIntent(){ userIntent = true; }
  function clearStoredScroll(){
    try { sessionStorage.removeItem('mle_keep_position_after_update_v2'); } catch(e1) {}
    try { sessionStorage.removeItem('mle_restore_anchor_v2'); } catch(e2) {}
    try { sessionStorage.removeItem('mle_restore_anchor'); } catch(e3) {}
    try { sessionStorage.removeItem('mle_scroll_restore'); } catch(e4) {}
  }
  function clearHashJump(){
    try {
      if (window.location && window.location.hash) {
        history.replaceState(null, document.title, window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
      }
    } catch(e) {}
  }
  function keepTop(){
    if (userIntent) { return; }
    try { window.scrollTo(0, 0); } catch(e) {}
  }
  try { if ('scrollRestoration' in history) { history.scrollRestoration = 'manual'; } } catch(e5) {}
  clearStoredScroll();
  clearHashJump();
  try {
    ['pointerdown','mousedown','touchstart','keydown','wheel','scroll'].forEach(function(evt){
      document.addEventListener(evt, markUserIntent, {capture:true, passive:true, once:true});
    });
  } catch(e6) {}
  keepTop();
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ clearStoredScroll(); clearHashJump(); keepTop(); }, false);
  } else {
    clearStoredScroll(); clearHashJump(); keepTop();
  }
  window.addEventListener('load', function(){ clearStoredScroll(); clearHashJump(); keepTop(); window.setTimeout(keepTop, 120); }, false);
}());


(function(){
  'use strict';
})();


function leEscapeHtml(value) {
  return String(value == null ? '' : value)
    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
    .replace(/'/g, '&#039;');
}
function leSetText(el, value) {
  if (!el) { return; }
  el.textContent = String(value == null ? '' : value);
}
function mleRenderNoteDisplay(display, noteVal) {
  if (!display) { return; }
  while (display.firstChild) { display.removeChild(display.firstChild); }
  noteVal = String(noteVal || '');
  if (!noteVal) {
    display.style.display = 'none';
    return;
  }
  var strong = document.createElement('strong');
  strong.style.color = '#334155';
  strong.appendChild(document.createTextNode('Note:'));
  display.appendChild(strong);
  display.appendChild(document.createTextNode(' '));
  var lines = noteVal.split(/\r?\n/);
  for (var i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    if (i > 0) { display.appendChild(document.createElement('br')); }
    display.appendChild(document.createTextNode(lines[i]));
  }
  display.style.display = 'block';
}
function mleSanitizePrintHtml(html) {
  var tpl = document.createElement('template');
  tpl.innerHTML = String(html || '');
  var banned = tpl.content.querySelectorAll('script, iframe, object, embed, link[rel="import"]');
  var i;
  for (i = banned.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (banned[i] && banned[i].parentNode) { banned[i].parentNode.removeChild(banned[i]); }
  }
  var nodes = tpl.content.querySelectorAll('*');
  for (i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
    var attrs = Array.prototype.slice.call(nodes[i].attributes || []);
    for (var a = 0; a < attrs.length; a++) {
      var attrName = attrs[a].name;
      var name = String(attrName || '').toLowerCase();
      var val = String(attrs[a].value || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (name.indexOf('on') === 0 || val.indexOf('javascript:') === 0) {
        nodes[i].removeAttribute(attrName);
      }
    }
  }
  var wrapper = document.createElement('div');
  wrapper.appendChild(tpl.content.cloneNode(true));
  return wrapper.innerHTML;
}

function mleActionJump(el) {
  try {
    if (!el || !el.getAttribute) { return true; }
    var href = el.getAttribute('data-href') || el.getAttribute('href') || '';
    var cardId = el.getAttribute('data-target-card') || '';
    var sectionId = el.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
    var panelId = el.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || '';
    if ((el.getAttribute('data-open-lottery-card-only') || '') === '1') { sectionId = ''; panelId = ''; }
    var target = null;
    var card = null;
    if (!cardId && href && href.charAt(0) === '#') { cardId = href.substring(1); }
    if (cardId) { card = document.getElementById(cardId); }
    if (card) {
      var outer = card.closest ? card.closest('.mle-lottery-outer') : null;
      if (outer && outer.classList && outer.classList.contains('body-collapsed') && typeof skaiLotterySetOneOuter === 'function') { skaiLotterySetOneOuter(outer, false); }
      var group = card.closest ? card.closest('.lottery-group') : null;
      if (group && group.classList && group.classList.contains('collapsed') && typeof skaiLotterySetOneGroup === 'function') { skaiLotterySetOneGroup(group, false); }
      var body = card.querySelector ? card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body') : null;
      var toggle = card.querySelector ? card.querySelector('.mle-lottery-toggle') : null;
      if (body) { body.style.display = ''; body.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false'); }
      if (toggle) {
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
        var sp = toggle.querySelector ? toggle.querySelector('span') : null;
        if (sp) { sp.textContent = 'Collapse'; }
      }
      if (card.classList) { card.classList.add('is-expanded'); }
    }
    if ((el.getAttribute('data-open-lottery-card-only') || '') === '1') { target = card; }
    if (!target && sectionId) { target = document.getElementById(sectionId); }
    if (!target && panelId) { target = document.getElementById(panelId); }
    if (!target && href && href.charAt(0) === '#') { target = document.getElementById(href.substring(1)); }
    if (!target) { target = card; }
    if (panelId) {
      var panel = document.getElementById(panelId);
      if (panel) {
        panel.style.display = '';
        panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
        target = panel;
      }
    }
    if (target) {
      setTimeout(function(){
        try { target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); } catch(e) { try { target.scrollIntoView(true); } catch(ignore) {} }
        if (target.classList) { target.classList.add('mle-action-jump-target'); }
        if (!target.hasAttribute || !target.hasAttribute('tabindex')) { try { target.setAttribute('tabindex','-1'); } catch(ignore2) {} }
        try { target.focus({preventScroll:true}); } catch(fe) { try { target.focus(); } catch(ignore3) {} }
        setTimeout(function(){ try { if (target.classList) { target.classList.remove('mle-action-jump-target'); } } catch(e2){} }, 2200);
      }, 90);
      return false;
    }
  } catch (err) {}
  return true;
}
window.mleActionJump = mleActionJump;

(function(){
  var el = document.getElementById('mle-skai-request-context');
  var raw = el ? (el.getAttribute('data-skai-request') || '{}') : '{}';
  try { window.__MLE_SKAI_REQUEST_CONTEXT__ = JSON.parse(raw); }
  catch (e) { window.__MLE_SKAI_REQUEST_CONTEXT__ = {}; }
})();

(function () {
  'use strict';
  function byId(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }
  function qsa(sel, root) {
    var ctx = root || document;
    if (!ctx.querySelectorAll) { return []; }
    return ctx.querySelectorAll(sel);
  }
  function safeLS(action, key, val) {
    try {
      if (action === 'get') { return localStorage.getItem(key); }
      if (action === 'set') { localStorage.setItem(key, val); }
    } catch (e) {}
    return null;
  }
  function initToggle(btn) {
    if (!btn || btn.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-init')) { return; }
    btn.setAttribute('data-mle-rs-init', '1');
    var targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-toggle');
    var lsKey    = btn.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-ls-key');
    var panel    = targetId ? byId(targetId) : null;
    if (!panel) { return; }
    var iconEl   = btn.querySelector('.mle-rs-group__toggle-icon');
    
    var savedCollapsed = lsKey ? safeLS('get', lsKey) : null;
    if (savedCollapsed === '1') {
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
      panel.setAttribute('hidden', '');
      if (iconEl) { iconEl.innerHTML = '&#9660;'; }
    } else if (savedCollapsed === '0') {
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
      panel.removeAttribute('hidden');
      if (iconEl) { iconEl.innerHTML = '&#9650;'; }
    }
    btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
      var isExpanded = btn.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
      if (isExpanded) {
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        panel.setAttribute('hidden', '');
        if (iconEl) { iconEl.innerHTML = '&#9660;'; }
        if (lsKey) { safeLS('set', lsKey, '1'); }
      } else {
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
        panel.removeAttribute('hidden');
        if (iconEl) { iconEl.innerHTML = '&#9650;'; }
        if (lsKey) { safeLS('set', lsKey, '0'); }
      }
    });
  }

  function getFormCheckboxes(form) {
    return qsa('.mle-rs-select-checkbox[name="selected_saved_ids[]"]:not([disabled])', form);
  }

  function countChecked(checkboxes) {
    var i;
    var c = 0;
    for (i = 0; i < checkboxes.length; i++) {
      if (checkboxes[i].checked) { c++; }
    }
    return c;
  }

  function updateGroupCounts(form) {
    var groupBodies = qsa('[data-mle-rs-group-body]', form);
    var i;
    var j;
    for (i = 0; i < groupBodies.length; i++) {
      var groupId = groupBodies[i].getAttribute('data-mle-rs-group-body');
      var out = qsa('[data-mle-rs-group-count="' + groupId + '"]', form);
      var checks = qsa('.mle-rs-select-checkbox[name="selected_saved_ids[]"]:not([disabled])', groupBodies[i]);
      var selected = 0;
      for (j = 0; j < checks.length; j++) {
        if (checks[j].checked) { selected++; }
      }
      if (out.length > 0) { out[0].innerHTML = String(selected); }
    }
  }

  function updateSelectedCounts(form) {
    var all = getFormCheckboxes(form);
    var total = countChecked(all);
    var out = qsa('[data-mle-rs-selected-total]', form);
    if (out.length > 0) { out[0].innerHTML = String(total); }
    updateGroupCounts(form);
  }

  function setCheckedByFilter(form, filterFn, checkedVal) {
    var all = getFormCheckboxes(form);
    var i;
    for (i = 0; i < all.length; i++) {
      if (filterFn(all[i])) { all[i].checked = checkedVal; }
    }
    updateSelectedCounts(form);
  }

  function isVisible(el) {
    if (!el) { return false; }
    if (el.offsetParent !== null) { return true; }
    if (el.getClientRects && el.getClientRects().length > 0) { return true; }
    return false;
  }

  function wireBulkForm(form) {
    if (!form || form.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-bulk-init') === '1') { return; }
    form.setAttribute('data-mle-rs-bulk-init', '1');

    form.addEventListener('change', function (evt) {
      var t = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
      if (!t) { return; }
      if (t.className && t.className.indexOf('mle-rs-select-checkbox') !== -1) {
        updateSelectedCounts(form);
      }
      if (t.getAttribute && t.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-bulk-action')) {
        var confirmInput = qsa('input[data-mle-rs-delete-confirm="1"]', form);
        if (confirmInput.length > 0 && t.value !== 'delete_permanently') {
          confirmInput[0].value = '';
        }
      }
    });

    form.addEventListener('click', function (evt) {
      var t = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
      if (!t || !t.getAttribute) { return; }

      var selectVisibleKey = t.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-select-visible');
      if (selectVisibleKey !== null) {
        setCheckedByFilter(form, function (cb) { return isVisible(cb); }, true);
        return;
      }

      var clearAllKey = t.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-clear-all');
      if (clearAllKey !== null) {
        setCheckedByFilter(form, function () { return true; }, false);
        return;
      }

      var groupAll = t.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-group-select-all');
      if (groupAll) {
        setCheckedByFilter(form, function (cb) {
          return cb.getAttribute('data-group-body-id') === groupAll;
        }, true);
        return;
      }

      var groupClear = t.getAttribute('data-mle-rs-group-clear');
      if (groupClear) {
        setCheckedByFilter(form, function (cb) {
          return cb.getAttribute('data-group-body-id') === groupClear;
        }, false);
      }
    });

    form.addEventListener('submit', function (evt) {
      var actionSel = qsa('[data-mle-rs-bulk-action]', form);
      var actionVal = (actionSel.length > 0) ? String(actionSel[0].value || '') : '';
      var selected = countChecked(getFormCheckboxes(form));
      var confirmTyped = qsa('[data-mle-rs-delete-typed]', form);
      var confirmInput = qsa('input[data-mle-rs-delete-confirm="1"]', form);
      var typedVal = (confirmTyped.length > 0) ? String(confirmTyped[0].value || '') : '';
      var promptVal = '';

      if (selected <= 0) {
        if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }
        window.alert('Please select at least one run.');
        return;
      }
      if (actionVal === '') {
        if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }
        window.alert('Please choose a bulk action.');
        return;
      }

      if (actionVal === 'delete_permanently') {
        if (typedVal !== 'DELETE') {
          if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }
          window.alert('Delete blocked. Type DELETE in the confirmation box.');
          return;
        }
        promptVal = window.prompt('This will permanently delete the selected runs. Type DELETE in the confirmation box to continue.', '');
        if (promptVal !== 'DELETE') {
          if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }
          window.alert('Delete cancelled.');
          return;
        }
        if (confirmInput.length > 0) { confirmInput[0].value = 'DELETE'; }
      } else {
        if (confirmInput.length > 0) { confirmInput[0].value = ''; }
      }
    });

    updateSelectedCounts(form);
  }

  function wireCheckboxGroupLinksToBody() {
    var bodies = qsa('[data-mle-rs-group-body]');
    var i;
    var j;
    for (i = 0; i < bodies.length; i++) {
      var bodyId = bodies[i].getAttribute('data-mle-rs-group-body');
      var checks = qsa('.mle-rs-select-checkbox[name="selected_saved_ids[]"]', bodies[i]);
      for (j = 0; j < checks.length; j++) {
        checks[j].setAttribute('data-group-body-id', bodyId);
      }
    }
  }

  function wireAll() {
    var i;
    var btns = qsa('[data-mle-rs-toggle]');
    var forms = qsa('form.mle-rs-bulk-form');
    for (i = 0; i < btns.length; i++) { initToggle(btns[i]); }
    wireCheckboxGroupLinksToBody();
    for (i = 0; i < forms.length; i++) { wireBulkForm(forms[i]); }
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', wireAll);
  } else {
    wireAll();
  }
}());

(function(){
  "use strict";
  if (window.__MLE_SKAI_PRECISION_BRIDGE_INIT__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_SKAI_PRECISION_BRIDGE_INIT__ = true;
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var btn = ev.target && ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.mle-open-skai-precision-batch') : null;
    var href = '';
    if (!btn) { return; }
    var payloadRaw = btn.getAttribute('data-batch-payload') || '';
    var url = btn.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || '';
    href = btn.getAttribute('href') || '';
    if (!url) { url = href; }
    ev.preventDefault();
    function openPrecisionBatchUrl(openUrl) {
      var win;
      if (!openUrl) { return false; }
      try {
        win = window.open(openUrl, '_blank');
        if (win) {
          try { win.opener = null; } catch (ignore) {}
          return true;
        }
      } catch (e) {}
      if (window.alert) { window.alert('SKAI could not open in a new tab/window. Please allow pop-ups for LottoExpert and try again.'); }
      return false;
    }
    try {
      var payload = JSON.parse(payloadRaw);
      if (!payload || !payload.runs || payload.runs.length !== 9) {
        if (url) { openPrecisionBatchUrl(url); return; }
        alert('This Precision Focus batch does not contain exactly 9 runnable SKAI settings.');
        return;
      }
      localStorage.setItem('mle_precision_lock_batch_payload_v1', JSON.stringify(payload));
      sessionStorage.setItem('mle_precision_lock_batch_payload_v1', JSON.stringify(payload));
    } catch (e) {
      if (url) { openPrecisionBatchUrl(url); return; }
      alert('This Precision Focus batch could not be prepared for SKAI. Please refresh and try again.');
      return;
    }
    if (url) { openPrecisionBatchUrl(url); return; }
    alert('This Precision Focus batch is missing its SKAI destination URL. Please refresh and try again.');
  }, false);
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_9BATCH_SUBMIT_GUARD__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_9BATCH_SUBMIT_GUARD__ = true;
  var LOCK_TIMEOUT_MS = 15000;
  function isCreateSkaiBatchForm(form){
    var actionInput;
    if (!form || !form.querySelector) { return false; }
    actionInput = form.querySelector('input[name="mle_action"]');
    return !!(actionInput && String(actionInput.value || '').toLowerCase() === 'create_skai_batch');
  }
  function isNineBatchForm(form){
    if (!form || !form.classList) { return false; }
    if (form.classList.contains('mle-next-settings-run__form')) { return true; }
    if (form.classList.contains('mle-v38-batch-action-form')) { return true; }
    if (form.classList.contains('mle-skai-batch-test__form')) { return true; }
    if (form.classList.contains('mle-history-window-action-form')) { return true; }
    return isCreateSkaiBatchForm(form);
  }
  function unlockForm(form){
    var btn;
    if (!form || !form.getAttribute) { return; }
    form.removeAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked');
    form.removeAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked-at');
    btn = form.querySelector('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"], button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if (!btn) { return; }
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.removeAttribute('aria-disabled');
    if (btn.tagName && btn.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'button') {
      if (btn.getAttribute('data-mle-original-label')) { btn.textContent = btn.getAttribute('data-mle-original-label'); }
    } else if (btn.value && btn.getAttribute('data-mle-original-label')) {
      btn.value = btn.getAttribute('data-mle-original-label');
    }
  }
  function isLockStale(form){
    var at = parseInt(String(form.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked-at') || '0'), 10);
    if (!at || isNaN(at)) { return true; }
    return (Date.now() - at) > LOCK_TIMEOUT_MS;
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var trigger = ev.target && ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"]') : null;
    var form;
    if (!trigger) { return; }
    form = trigger.form || (trigger.closest ? trigger.closest('form') : null);
    if (!isNineBatchForm(form)) { return; }
    if (form.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked') === '1') {
      if (isLockStale(form)) { unlockForm(form); }
      else {
        ev.preventDefault();
        return;
      }
    }
    if (form.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked') === '1') {
      ev.preventDefault();
      return;
    }
    ev.preventDefault();
    if (typeof form.requestSubmit === 'function') {
      if (trigger && trigger.tagName && /^(button|input)$/i.test(trigger.tagName) && /^(submit|image)$/i.test((trigger.getAttribute('type') || '').toLowerCase())) {
        form.requestSubmit(trigger);
      } else {
        form.requestSubmit();
      }
    } else { form.submit(); }
  }, false);
  document.addEventListener('submit', function(ev){
    var form = ev.target;
    var btn;
    var lotteryField;
    var lotteryId;
    if (!isNineBatchForm(form)) { return; }
    if (ev.defaultPrevented) { return; }
    if (form.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked') === '1') {
      if (isLockStale(form)) { unlockForm(form); }
      else {
        ev.preventDefault();
        return;
      }
    }
    if (form.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked') === '1') {
      ev.preventDefault();
      return;
    }
    lotteryField = form.querySelector('input[name="lottery_id"]') || form.querySelector('input[name="mle_lottery_id"]');
    lotteryId = lotteryField ? parseInt(String(lotteryField.value || ''), 10) : 0;
    if (!lotteryId || lotteryId <= 0) {
      ev.preventDefault();
      form.removeAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked');
      if (window.alert) { window.alert('9BATCH could not start because the lottery selection is missing. Please refresh and try again.'); }
      return;
    }
    form.setAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked', '1');
    form.setAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked-at', String(Date.now()));
    btn = form.querySelector('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"], button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    if (btn) {
      btn.disabled = true;
      btn.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
      if (btn.tagName && btn.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'button') {
        btn.setAttribute('data-mle-original-label', btn.textContent || '');
        btn.textContent = 'Creating 9BATCH run...';
      } else if (btn.value) {
        btn.setAttribute('data-mle-original-label', btn.value);
        btn.value = 'Creating 9BATCH run...';
      }
    }
  }, false);
})();

(function(){
  function hasClass(el,name){return el&&el.className&&(' '+el.className+' ').indexOf(' '+name+' ')>-1;}
  function findButton(el){while(el&&el!==document){if(el.tagName&&el.tagName.toUpperCase()==='BUTTON'){return el;}el=el.parentNode;}return null;}
  function setButtonText(btn,open){var span=btn.querySelector('span');var node=span||btn;var txt=node.textContent||'';if(txt==='Expand'||txt==='Collapse'){node.textContent=open?'Collapse':'Expand';return;}if(txt.indexOf('Show ')===0){node.textContent=(open?'Hide ':'Show ')+txt.substring(5);return;}if(txt.indexOf('Hide ')===0){node.textContent=(open?'Hide ':'Show ')+txt.substring(5);return;}if(txt.indexOf('View ')===0){node.textContent=(open?'Hide ':'View ')+txt.substring(5);return;}}
  function openPanel(id){var panel=document.getElementById(id);if(!panel){return false;}panel.style.display='block';panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');var toggles=document.querySelectorAll('[aria-controls="'+id+'"]');var i;for(i=0;i<toggles.length;i++){toggles[i].setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');setButtonText(toggles[i],true);}if(panel.scrollIntoView){panel.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'nearest'});}return true;}
  function localMessage(btn,msg){var wrap=btn.parentNode;var box=document.createElement('div');box.className='mle-local-message';box.appendChild(document.createTextNode(msg));wrap.appendChild(box);}
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){var btn=findButton(e.target);if(!btn){return;}if(hasClass(btn,'mle-lottery-toggle')||hasClass(btn,'mle-section-toggle')){e.preventDefault();var id=btn.getAttribute('aria-controls');var body=id?document.getElementById(id):null;if(!body){localMessage(btn,'This section could not be opened because its target was not found.');return;}var open=(body.style.display==='none'||body.style.display==='');body.style.display=open?'block':'none';body.setAttribute('aria-hidden',open?'false':'true');btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded',open?'true':'false');setButtonText(btn,open);return;}if(hasClass(btn,'mle-review-runs-btn')){e.preventDefault();if(window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource&&((btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel')||'').indexOf('pending')!==-1||(btn.getAttribute('data-target-section')||'').indexOf('pending')!==-1||(btn.getAttribute('data-open-details')||'').indexOf('pending')!==-1)){return window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource(btn);}if(!openPanel(btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel'))){localMessage(btn,'This section could not be opened because its target was not found.');}return;}if(hasClass(btn,'mle-leave-as-is-btn')){e.preventDefault();localMessage(btn,'No changes applied. Your saved history was left as is.');return;}}
  ,false);
}());

(function(){
  'use strict';
  function qsa(sel, root){ var ctx = root || document; return ctx.querySelectorAll ? ctx.querySelectorAll(sel) : []; }
  function findCard(node){
    while(node && node !== document){
      if(node.className && String(node.className).indexOf('mle-advisory-card') !== -1){ return node; }
      node = node.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function setMode(card, mode){
    var i;
    var buttons = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-btn]', card);
    var sections = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-section]', card);
    for(i = 0; i < buttons.length; i++){
      var active = buttons[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-btn') === mode;
      buttons[i].setAttribute('aria-selected', active ? 'true' : 'false');
      buttons[i].setAttribute('tabindex', active ? '0' : '-1');
      if (active) {
        if (buttons[i].className.indexOf('is-active') === -1) { buttons[i].className += ' is-active'; }
      } else {
        buttons[i].className = String(buttons[i].className).replace(/\s?is-active/g, '');
      }
    }
    for(i = 0; i < sections.length; i++){
      var sectionMode = sections[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '';
      if (sectionMode === mode) {
        sections[i].style.display = '';
        sections[i].removeAttribute('hidden');
        sections[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
      } else {
        sections[i].style.display = 'none';
        sections[i].setAttribute('hidden', 'hidden');
        sections[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      }
    }
  }
  function initCardModes(card){
    var buttons = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-btn]', card);
    var i;
    if (!buttons.length) { return; }
    setMode(card, 'overview');
    for(i = 0; i < buttons.length; i++){
      buttons[i].setAttribute('role', 'tab');
      buttons[i].addEventListener('click', function(e){
        var btn = e.currentTarget || this;
        setMode(card, btn.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-btn') || 'overview');
      });
      buttons[i].addEventListener('keydown', function(e){
        var key = e.keyCode || e.which;
        var curr = e.currentTarget || this;
        var idx = -1;
        var j;
        for (j = 0; j < buttons.length; j++) { if (buttons[j] === curr) { idx = j; break; } }
        if (idx < 0) { return; }
        if (key === 37 || key === 38) {
          e.preventDefault();
          buttons[(idx - 1 + buttons.length) % buttons.length].focus();
        } else if (key === 39 || key === 40) {
          e.preventDefault();
          buttons[(idx + 1) % buttons.length].focus();
        } else if (key === 36) {
          e.preventDefault();
          buttons[0].focus();
        } else if (key === 35) {
          e.preventDefault();
          buttons[buttons.length - 1].focus();
        } else if (key === 13 || key === 32) {
          e.preventDefault();
          setMode(card, curr.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-btn') || 'overview');
        }
      });
    }
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    var node = e.target;
    if (!node || !node.getAttribute) { return; }
    if (node.getAttribute('data-target-section') && (node.getAttribute('data-target-section').indexOf('mle-card-mode-') === 0 || node.getAttribute('data-target-section').indexOf('mle-section-') === 0)) {
      var targetId = node.getAttribute('data-target-section');
      var target = targetId ? document.getElementById(targetId) : null;
      var card = findCard(node);
      if (!target || !card) { return; }
      var modeSection = target.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '';
      if (modeSection !== '') { setMode(card, modeSection); }
    }
  }, false);
  function init(){
    var cards = qsa('.mle-advisory-card');
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < cards.length; i++){ initCardModes(cards[i]); }
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
  } else {
    init();
  }
}());

(function(){
  function hasClass(el, c){return !!(el && el.classList && el.classList.contains(c));}
  function setOuter(el, collapse){
    if(!el){return;}
    var head=el.querySelector('[data-outer-lottery-toggle]');
    var btn=el.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn]');
    var lid=el.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id') || '';
    if(collapse){
      el.classList.add('body-collapsed'); el.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
      if(head){head.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');}
      if(btn){btn.textContent='Expand'; btn.setAttribute('aria-label','Expand lottery section');}
      if(lid){try{localStorage.setItem('mle_outer_collapsed_'+lid,'true');}catch(e){}}
    }else{
      el.classList.remove('body-collapsed'); el.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');
      if(head){head.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');}
      if(btn){btn.textContent='Collapse'; btn.setAttribute('aria-label','Collapse lottery section');}
      if(lid){try{localStorage.setItem('mle_outer_collapsed_'+lid,'false');}catch(e){}}
    }
  }
  function setGroup(el, collapse){
    if(!el){return;}
    var btn=el.querySelector('.lottery-collapse-toggle,[data-lottery-toggle-btn]');
    var lotteryId=el.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
    var base=lotteryId ? lotteryId.split('-')[0] : '';
    if(collapse){
      el.classList.add('collapsed');
      if(btn){btn.textContent='Expand'; btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false'); btn.setAttribute('aria-label','Expand lottery section');}
      if(base){try{localStorage.setItem('lottery_collapsed_'+base,'true');}catch(e){}}
    }else{
      el.classList.remove('collapsed');
      if(btn){btn.textContent='Collapse'; btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true'); btn.setAttribute('aria-label','Collapse lottery section');}
      if(base){try{localStorage.setItem('lottery_collapsed_'+base,'false');}catch(e){}}
    }
  }
  function setDetails(collapse){
    var ds=document.querySelectorAll('details');
    for(var i=0;i<ds.length;i++){
      if(ds[i].closest && ds[i].closest('.mle-user-manual')){continue;}
      if(collapse){ds[i].removeAttribute('open');}else{ds[i].setAttribute('open','open');}
    }
  }
  window.mleVisibleCollapseAll=function(collapse){
    collapse=!!collapse;
    var outers=document.querySelectorAll('.mle-lottery-outer');
    var groups=document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group');
    for(var i=0;i<outers.length;i++){setOuter(outers[i],collapse);}
    for(var j=0;j<groups.length;j++){setGroup(groups[j],collapse);}
    setDetails(collapse);
    if(typeof window.skaiLotteryCollapseAll==='function'){try{window.skaiLotteryCollapseAll(collapse);}catch(e){}}
    return false;
  };
  window.mleVisibleJumpTo=function(id){
    var target=(id==='top')?(document.getElementById('top')||document.body):document.getElementById(id);
    if(!target){return false;}
    var outer=hasClass(target,'mle-lottery-outer')?target:(target.closest?target.closest('.mle-lottery-outer'):null);
    var group=hasClass(target,'lottery-group')?target:(target.closest?target.closest('.lottery-group'):null);
    if(outer){setOuter(outer,false);}
    if(group){setGroup(group,false);}
    setTimeout(function(){try{target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'});}catch(e){try{target.scrollIntoView(true);}catch(x){}} if(target!==document.body){if(!target.hasAttribute('tabindex')){target.setAttribute('tabindex','-1');} try{target.focus({preventScroll:true});}catch(fe){try{target.focus();}catch(x2){}}}},40);
    return false;
  };
})();

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  function S(str) {
    return String(str).replace(/\[\[/g, '\u003c').replace(/\]\]/g, '\u003e');
  }

  var card = document.getElementById('info-card');
  var btn  = document.getElementById('info-toggle');
  if (!card || !btn) return; 

  var key = 'myLottoExpertInfoOpen';

  
  var stored = null;
  try { stored = localStorage.getItem(key); } catch (e) { stored = null; }

  
  var isOpen = (stored === null) ? card.classList.contains('open') : (stored !== 'false');

  if (!isOpen) {
    card.classList.remove('open');
    btn.textContent = 'Expand';
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Expand info');
  } else {
    btn.textContent = 'Collapse';
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Collapse info');
  }

  btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
    var open = card.classList.toggle('open');
    try { localStorage.setItem(key, open ? 'true' : 'false'); } catch (e) {}
    btn.textContent = open ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand';
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-label', open ? 'Collapse info' : 'Expand info');
  });
});

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  var S = (window.S && typeof window.S === 'function')
  ? window.S
  : function(str) { return String(str).replace(/\[\[/g, '\u003c').replace(/\]\]/g, '\u003e'); };

var __SKAI_LIVE_V__ = 1;
var __SKAI_LIVE_NS__ = 'skai_live_v' + __SKAI_LIVE_V__ + '_';

function SimpleSet() { this._d = {}; this.size = 0; }
SimpleSet.prototype.has = function(v) { return Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(this._d, ''+v); };
SimpleSet.prototype.add = function(v) { if (!this.has(v)) { this._d[''+v] = +v; this.size++; } return this; };
SimpleSet.prototype['delete'] = function(v) { if (this.has(v)) { delete this._d[''+v]; this.size--; return true; } return false; };
SimpleSet.prototype.clear = function() { this._d = {}; this.size = 0; };
SimpleSet.prototype.values = function() { var out = []; for (var k in this._d) { if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(this._d, k)) out.push(this._d[k]); } return out; };

function arrayToSimpleSet(arr) { var s = new SimpleSet(); for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) { s.add(arr[i]); } return s; }

function skaiSafeJsonParse(str, fallback){
  try { return JSON.parse(str); } catch(e){ return fallback; }
}
function skaiSafeJsonStringify(obj, fallback){
  try { return JSON.stringify(obj); } catch(e){ return fallback || '[]'; }
}
function skaiLiveKey(lotteryId){
  return __SKAI_LIVE_NS__ + 'lottery_' + String(lotteryId || 'unknown');
}
function skaiLiveAppend(lotteryId, entry, maxKeep){
  maxKeep = (typeof maxKeep === 'number' && maxKeep > 3) ? maxKeep : 12;

  var key = skaiLiveKey(lotteryId);
  var arr = [];
  try {
    arr = skaiSafeJsonParse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]', []);
    if (!Array.isArray(arr)) arr = [];
  } catch(e){
    arr = [];
  }

  arr.push(entry);
  if (arr.length > maxKeep) arr = arr.slice(arr.length - maxKeep);

  try { localStorage.setItem(key, skaiSafeJsonStringify(arr, '[]')); } catch(e){}
  return arr;
}
function skaiTrendSentence(arr, field, label){
  label = label || 'Signal';
  if (!arr || arr.length < 3) return '';

  var last3 = arr.slice(-3);
  var a = Number(last3[0] && last3[0][field]);
  var b = Number(last3[1] && last3[1][field]);
  var c = Number(last3[2] && last3[2][field]);
  if (!isFinite(a) || !isFinite(b) || !isFinite(c)) return '';

  var delta = c - a;
  if (delta >= 2) return label + ' is rising over the last 3 runs.';
  if (-2 >= delta) return label + ' is weakening over the last 3 runs.';

  var vol = Math.abs(b - a) + Math.abs(c - b);
  if (vol >= 4) return label + ' has been volatile recently.';
  return label + ' has been relatively steady.';
}
function skaiConfidenceTrend(arr){
  if (!arr || arr.length < 3) return '';
  var map = { 'Single-method':0, 'Exploratory':1, 'Balanced':2, 'High':3 };
  var last3 = arr.slice(-3).map(function(x){
    var k = (x && x.levelLabel) ? x.levelLabel : 'Exploratory';
    return map[k] || 0;
  });
  var a = last3[0], b = last3[1], c = last3[2];
  var delta = c - a;

  if (delta >= 2) return 'Confidence posture is improving across recent runs.';
  if (-2 >= delta) return 'Confidence posture has softened across recent runs.';
  if (Math.abs((b - a)) + Math.abs((c - b)) >= 3) return 'Confidence posture has been inconsistent recently.';
  return 'Confidence posture has been stable recently.';
}
function skaiPosture(levelLabel, methodsUsed, overlapScore, evidenceScore){
  methodsUsed = Number(methodsUsed) || 0;
  overlapScore = Number(overlapScore) || 0;
  evidenceScore = Number(evidenceScore) || 0;

  if (1 >= methodsUsed || levelLabel === 'Single-method') {
    return 'Signal quality is limited because only one method is active - useful for exploration, but not for agreement.';
  }
  if (levelLabel === 'High') {
    return 'Signal quality looks consistent - multiple methods are pointing in similar directions.';
  }
  if (levelLabel === 'Balanced') {
    return 'Signal quality is workable - some agreement exists, with normal uncertainty.';
  }
  if (overlapScore === 0 && evidenceScore === 0) {
    return 'Signal quality is early-stage - treat this run as learning-focused and keep building history.';
  }
  return 'Signal quality is exploratory - good for learning patterns, not for precision.';
}
function skaiNextSteps(levelLabel, checkedLen, methodsUsed, overlapScore, evidenceScore){
  var steps = [];

  checkedLen    = Number(checkedLen) || 0;
  methodsUsed   = Number(methodsUsed) || 0;
  overlapScore  = Number(overlapScore) || 0;
  evidenceScore = Number(evidenceScore) || 0;

  if (checkedLen === 1) {
    steps.push('Add one more method so you can measure agreement (not just one viewpoint).');
    steps.push('Try "Compare All" once - it helps you see where methods overlap.');
    return steps;
  }

  
  if (methodsUsed >= 2 && overlapScore === 0) {
    steps.push("Your selected methods disagree right now. That's useful - it means you're seeing different viewpoints.");
    steps.push('Try adjusting one setting at a time (draw window, epochs/walks, or smoothing), then save a new run.');
    steps.push('Aim for at least 1-2 overlaps before treating anything as a "core" set.');
    return steps;
  }

  
  if (methodsUsed >= 2 && overlapScore > 0 && evidenceScore === 0) {
    steps.push('You have some agreement. Next: build evidence by saving a few more runs so trends can appear.');
    steps.push("Mix in a few mid-rank numbers (#4-#10) from each method so you're not all-in on #1 picks.");
    return steps;
  }

  
  if (levelLabel === 'High' || levelLabel === 'Balanced') {
    steps.push('This is a reasonable baseline. Keep your core stable and iterate slowly (one setting change per run).');
    steps.push('After the next draw, use "post" mode to see which ranks actually hit and tune toward those ranges.');
    return steps;
  }

  return steps;
}


document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
  var el = ev.target;
  if (!el) return;

  
  var link = el.closest ? el.closest('[data-skai-reset-learning]') : null;
  if (!link) return;

  ev.preventDefault();

  var lotteryId = link.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
  if (!lotteryId) return;

  var ok = confirm('Reset learning history for this lottery? This clears trend memory used by the living analysis.');
  if (!ok) return;

  try {
    
    var prefixes = ['skai_live_', 'skai_learning_', 'skai_learn_', 'skai_mem_'];
    for (var i = localStorage.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      var k = localStorage.key(i);
      if (!k) continue;

      
      var hasPrefix = false;
      for (var p = 0; p < prefixes.length; p++) {
        if (k.indexOf(prefixes[p]) === 0) { hasPrefix = true; break; }
      }
      if (!hasPrefix) continue;

      if (k.indexOf(lotteryId) !== -1) {
        localStorage.removeItem(k);
      }
    }
  } catch(e){}

  
  try {
    var group = document.querySelector('.lottery-group[data-lottery-id="' + lotteryId + '"]');
    if (group) {
      var first = group.querySelector('.card-compare-checkbox');
      if (first) {
        ['input','change'].forEach(function(type){
          first.dispatchEvent(new Event(type, { bubbles:true, cancelable:true }));
        });
      }
    }
  } catch(e){}
});

function renderSelectionHeatmap(group, selStats, methods, labelShort, maxMain, checked) {
  var host   = group.querySelector('[data-sel-heatmap]');
  var status = group.querySelector('[data-sel-hm-status]');
  if (!host) return;

  
  if (!checked || checked.length === 0) {
    host.innerHTML = '\u003cp class="sel-hm-placeholder"\u003eTick a \u003cstrong\u003eCompare\u003c/strong\u003e checkbox on any prediction card above to see the live heatmap here.\u003c/p\u003e';
    if (status) { leSetText(status, 'No runs selected.'); }
    return;
  }

  
  if (status) {
    var chips = '';
    for (var ci = 0; ci < checked.length; ci++) {
      var card = checked[ci].closest ? checked[ci].closest('.prediction-card') : null;
      if (!card) continue;
      var mLabel = String(card.getAttribute('data-source')||'').replace(/_/g,' ');
      var badgeEl = card.querySelector('.source-badge');
      if (badgeEl) mLabel = badgeEl.textContent.trim();
        chips += '\u003cspan class="sel-hm-chip"\u003e' + leEscapeHtml(mLabel) + '\u003c/span\u003e';
    }
    status.innerHTML = 'Currently showing: ' + chips + ' (' + checked.length + ' run' + (checked.length !== 1 ? 's' : '') + ')';
  }

  
  var html = '\u003ctable\u003e';
  html += '\u003cthead\u003e\u003ctr\u003e';
  html += '\u003cth style="text-align:left;"\u003eMethod\u003c/th\u003e';
  for (var c = 1; maxMain >= c; c++) html += '\u003cth\u003e' + c + '\u003c/th\u003e';
  html += '\u003cth\u003eTotal\u003c/th\u003e';
  html += '\u003c/tr\u003e\u003c/thead\u003e';
  html += '\u003ctbody\u003e';

  var hasAnyData = false;
  methods.forEach(function(m) {
    if (!selStats[m] || !selStats[m].runs) return;
    hasAnyData = true;
    var rowTotal = 0;
    
    var rowMax = 0;
    for (var r2 = 1; maxMain >= r2; r2++) {
      var v2 = selStats[m].main[r2]|0;
      if (v2 > rowMax) rowMax = v2;
    }
    html += '\u003ctr\u003e';
    html += '\u003ctd style="text-align:left; font-weight:700;"\u003e' + leEscapeHtml(labelShort[m] || m) + '\u003c/td\u003e';
    for (var r = 1; maxMain >= r; r++) {
      var v = selStats[m].main[r]|0;
      rowTotal += v;
      var cls = 'zero', style = '';
      if (v !== 0) {
        cls = 'nonzero';
        
        var MAX_HUE = 240, BASE_LIGHT = 52, INTENSITY_ADJ = 8;
        var hue = Math.round(MAX_HUE * (r - 1) / Math.max(1, maxMain - 1));
        var intensity = rowMax > 0 ? (v / rowMax) : 0;
        var light = Math.round(BASE_LIGHT - intensity * INTENSITY_ADJ);
        style = 'background:hsl(' + hue + ',90%,' + light + '%);color:#fff;font-weight:700;';
      }
      html += '\u003ctd class="' + cls + '" title="Rank #' + r + ': ' + v + ' hit(s)" style="' + style + '"\u003e' + v + '\u003c/td\u003e';
    }
    html += '\u003ctd style="font-weight:700;"\u003e' + rowTotal + '\u003c/td\u003e';
    html += '\u003c/tr\u003e';
  });

  html += '\u003c/tbody\u003e\u003c/table\u003e';

  if (!hasAnyData) {
    host.innerHTML = '\u003cp class="sel-hm-placeholder"\u003eNo hit data available for the selected run(s) yet - results will appear after the draw date has passed.\u003c/p\u003e';
    return;
  }

  host.innerHTML = html;
}

Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group'), function(group) {

    var compareBoxes = group.querySelectorAll('.card-compare-checkbox');
    var commonCard   = group.querySelector('.prediction-card.common-card[data-common-bar]');
    var numbersDiv   = commonCard ? commonCard.querySelector('.common-numbers') : null;
    var cards        = group.querySelectorAll('.prediction-card');

Array.prototype.forEach.call(compareBoxes, function(cb) {
  cb.addEventListener('change', function() {
    if (cb.checked) {
      
      var myCard   = cb.closest ? cb.closest('.prediction-card') : null;
      var myMethod = myCard ? String(myCard.getAttribute('data-source') || '').trim() : '';
      if (myMethod) {
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(compareBoxes, function(other) {
          if (other === cb) return;
          var otherCard   = other.closest ? other.closest('.prediction-card') : null;
          var otherMethod = otherCard ? String(otherCard.getAttribute('data-source') || '').trim() : '';
          if (otherMethod === myMethod) { other.checked = false; }
        });
      }
    }
    try { update(); } catch(e) { console.warn('[MyLotto] update() error:', e); }
  });
});

(function autoSelectOnePerMethod(){
  var chosen = Object.create(null); 
  var boxes = group.querySelectorAll('.prediction-card .card-compare-checkbox');

  Array.prototype.forEach.call(boxes, function(cb) {
    var card   = cb.closest ? cb.closest('.prediction-card') : null;
    var method = card ? String(card.getAttribute('data-source')||'').trim() : '';
    if (!chosen[method]) {
      cb.checked = true;      
      chosen[method] = true;
    } else {
      cb.checked = false;     
    }
  });

  
  var first = boxes[0];
  if (first) {
    try { first.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles:true, cancelable:true })); }
    catch(e) { try { update(); } catch(e2){} }
  } else {
    
    try { update(); } catch(e) {}
  }
})();
