    skaiCiSetCollapsed(sections[j].id, shouldCollapse);
  }
  skaiCiRefreshToggleAll();
}
(function () {
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-ci-section');
  for (var i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
    var sec = sections[i];
    var collapsed = false;
    try { collapsed = localStorage.getItem('mle_ci_collapsed_' + sec.id) === 'true'; } catch (e) {}
    skaiCiSetCollapsed(sec.id, collapsed);
  }
  skaiCiRefreshToggleAll();
})();

if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
  window.skaiCiToggle = skaiCiToggle;
  window.skaiCiToggleAll = skaiCiToggleAll;
  window.mleCiHeaderKeydown = mleCiHeaderKeydown;
  window.skaiPrcToggle = skaiPrcToggle;
  window.mleHistoricalHeaderKeydown = mleHistoricalHeaderKeydown;
  window.mlePrintHistoricalAll = mlePrintHistoricalAll;
  window.mlePrintHistoricalLottery = mlePrintHistoricalLottery;
  window.skaiLotteryToggle = skaiLotteryToggle;
  window.skaiLotteryToggleAll = skaiLotteryToggleAll;
  window.mleOuterLotteryToggle = mleOuterLotteryToggle;
  window.mlePrintCard = mlePrintCard;
  window.mlePrintGroup = mlePrintGroup;
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(evt) {
  var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  var node = target;

  while (node && node.nodeType === 1) {
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle')) {
      skaiCiToggle(node.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle-btn') === '1') {
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); } else { evt.cancelBubble = true; }
      skaiCiToggle(node.getAttribute('data-ci-id'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.id === 'mle-ci-toggle-all') {
      skaiCiToggleAll();
      return;
    }
    if (node.id === 'mle-print-historical-all') {
      mlePrintHistoricalAll();
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle')) {
      skaiPrcToggle(node.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle-btn') === '1') {
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); } else { evt.cancelBubble = true; }
      skaiPrcToggle(node.getAttribute('data-prc-id'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-print-lottery') === '1') {
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); } else { evt.cancelBubble = true; }
      mlePrintHistoricalLottery(node);
      return;
    }
    if (node.id === 'mle-go-to-favorites-btn') {
      if (typeof scrollToFavorites === 'function') { scrollToFavorites(); }
      return;
    }
    node = node.parentNode;
  }
});

document.addEventListener('keydown', function(evt) {
  evt = evt || window.event;
  var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  if (!target || !target.getAttribute) { return; }

  if (target.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle')) {
    mleCiHeaderKeydown(evt, target.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle'));
    return;
  }
  if (target.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle')) {
    mleHistoricalHeaderKeydown(evt, target.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle'));
    return;
  }
});

document.addEventListener('click', function(evt) {
  var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  var node = target;

  while (node && node.nodeType === 1) {
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-clear-btn') === '1') {
      skaiPrcClearCheckboxes(node.getAttribute('data-prc-section-id'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-select-upcoming-btn') === '1') {
      skaiPrcSelectUpcoming(node.getAttribute('data-prc-section-id'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-lottery-collapse-all-btn') === '1') {
      skaiLotteryCollapseAll(true);
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-lottery-expand-all-btn') === '1') {
      skaiLotteryCollapseAll(false);
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-lottery-toggle-all-btn') === '1') {
      skaiLotteryToggleAll(node);
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-lottery-toggle-btn') === '1') {
      skaiLotteryToggle(node);
      return;
    }
    
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn') !== null) {
      var outerEl = node.closest ? node.closest('.mle-lottery-outer') : (function() {
        var el = node;
        while (el && !(el.classList && el.classList.contains('mle-lottery-outer'))) { el = el.parentElement; }
        return el;
      }());
      if (outerEl) { mleOuterLotteryToggle(outerEl); }
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); } else { evt.cancelBubble = true; }
      return;
    }
    
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-toggle') !== null) {
      var outerEl2 = node.closest ? node.closest('.mle-lottery-outer') : (function() {
        var el = node;
        while (el && !(el.classList && el.classList.contains('mle-lottery-outer'))) { el = el.parentElement; }
        return el;
      }());
      if (outerEl2) { mleOuterLotteryToggle(outerEl2); }
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-print-group-btn') === '1') {
      mlePrintGroup(node);
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-print-card-btn') === '1') {
      mlePrintCard(node);
      return;
    }
    node = node.parentNode;
  }
});


document.addEventListener('click', function(evt) {
  var link = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('.mle-quick-nav a[href^="#"], .mle-section-jump a[href^="#"], .mle-lottery-control-strip a[href^="#"], .mle-strategic-nav a[href^="#"]') : null;
  if (!link) { return; }
  var href = link.getAttribute('href') || '';
  if (href.length < 2) { return; }
  var targetId = decodeURIComponent(href.substring(1));
  var target = targetId === 'top' ? document.getElementById('top') || document.body : document.getElementById(targetId);
  if (!target) { return; }
  if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }

  
  var outer = target.classList && target.classList.contains('mle-lottery-outer') ? target : (target.closest ? target.closest('.mle-lottery-outer') : null);
  if (outer && outer.classList.contains('body-collapsed')) { mleOuterLotteryToggle(outer); }
  var group = target.classList && target.classList.contains('lottery-group') ? target : (target.closest ? target.closest('.lottery-group') : null);
  if (group && group.classList.contains('collapsed')) {
    var tbtn = group.querySelector('.lottery-collapse-toggle');
    if (tbtn) { skaiLotteryToggle(tbtn); }
    else { group.classList.remove('collapsed'); }
  }

  try { target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' }); }
  catch (e) { try { target.scrollIntoView(true); } catch (ignore) {} }
  if (target !== document.body) {
    if (!target.hasAttribute('tabindex')) { target.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); }
    try { target.focus({ preventScroll: true }); } catch (focusErr) { try { target.focus(); } catch (ignore2) {} }
  }
});

document.addEventListener('change', function(evt) {
  var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  if (!target || !target.getAttribute) { return; }
  if (target.getAttribute('data-auto-submit-select') === '1' && target.form && typeof target.form.submit === 'function') {
    target.form.submit();
  }
});

document.addEventListener('submit', function(evt) {
  evt = evt || window.event;
  var form = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  if (!form || !form.getAttribute) { return; }

  if (form.getAttribute('data-prc-delete-form') === '1') {
    if (!skaiPrcConfirmDelete(form, form.getAttribute('data-prc-section-id'))) {
      if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }
    }
    return;
  }

  var msg = form.getAttribute('data-confirm-submit');
  if (msg) {
    if (!window.confirm(msg)) {
      if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }
    }
  }
});


function mleToggleNoteEditor(settingId, show) {
  var editor  = document.getElementById('mle-note-editor-'  + settingId);
  var display = document.getElementById('mle-note-display-' + settingId);
  if (!editor) { return; }
  editor.style.display  = show ? 'block' : 'none';
  if (display) { display.style.display = show ? 'none' : (display.textContent.trim() ? 'block' : 'none'); }
  if (show) {
    var ta = editor.querySelector('textarea');
    if (ta) { ta.focus(); }
  }
}


function mleSaveNote(evt, settingId) {
  evt.preventDefault();
  var form = evt.target;
  if (typeof fetch === 'undefined') { form.submit(); return false; }
  var data = new FormData(form);
  fetch(window.location.href, { method: 'POST', body: data, credentials: 'same-origin' })
    .then(function(r) { return r.ok ? r.text() : Promise.reject(r.status); })
    .then(function() {
      var ta      = form.querySelector('textarea[name="user_notes"]');
      var noteVal = ta ? ta.value.trim() : '';
      var display = document.getElementById('mle-note-display-' + settingId);
      if (display) {
        mleRenderNoteDisplay(display, noteVal);
      }
      
      var btns = document.querySelectorAll('[data-note-toggle="' + settingId + '"]');
      for (var i = 0; i < btns.length; i++) {
        btns[i].textContent = (noteVal ? 'Edit Note' : 'Add Note');
      }
      mleToggleNoteEditor(settingId, false);
    })
    .catch(function(err) {
      
      var statusMsg = err ? ' (status ' + err + ')' : '';
      if (window.console) { console.warn('[MLE] Note save via fetch failed' + statusMsg + '; retrying via form submit.'); }
      form.submit();
    });
  return false;
}


function mleApplyRecallSettings(btn, settingId, lotteryId) {
  var raw = btn ? btn.getAttribute('data-mle-params') : null;
  var params;
  try { params = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null; } catch (e) { params = null; }
  if (!params) { return; }

  var destUrl  = (btn ? btn.getAttribute('data-mle-lottery-url') : null) || '';
  var gameId   = (btn ? btn.getAttribute('data-mle-game-id')     : null) || '';
  var source   = (btn ? btn.getAttribute('data-mle-source')       : null) || '';

  
  var payload = {
    settingId : settingId,
    lotteryId : lotteryId,
    gameId    : gameId,
    source    : source,
    params    : params
  };

  
  
  if (destUrl && destUrl !== '' && destUrl !== '#') {
    try {
      sessionStorage.setItem('mle_recall_settings', JSON.stringify(payload));
    } catch (ssErr) {
      if (window.console) { console.warn('[MLE] sessionStorage unavailable:', ssErr); }
    }
    
    var sep = (destUrl.indexOf('?') === -1) ? '?' : '&';
    window.location.href = destUrl + sep + 'mle_recall=1';
    return;
  }

  
  if (typeof mylottoRecallSettings === 'function') {
    mylottoRecallSettings(settingId, lotteryId, params);
  }
}


function mylottoRecallSettings(settingId, lotteryId, params) {
  if (typeof params !== 'object' || params === null) { return; }
  var detail = { settingId: settingId, lotteryId: lotteryId, params: params };
  var evt = null;
  try {
    evt = new CustomEvent('mylotto:recall-settings', { bubbles: true, cancelable: true, detail: detail });
  } catch (e) {
    
    evt = document.createEvent('CustomEvent');
    evt.initCustomEvent('mylotto:recall-settings', true, true, detail);
  }
  var handled = document.dispatchEvent(evt);
  
  
  
  if (handled) {
    var filled = 0;
    for (var k in params) {
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(params, k)) { continue; }
      var els = document.querySelectorAll('[name="' + k + '"], [data-setting-key="' + k + '"]');
      for (var i = 0; i < els.length; i++) {
        var el = els[i];
        if (el.tagName === 'SELECT') {
          for (var j = 0; j < el.options.length; j++) {
            if (String(el.options[j].value) === String(params[k])) { el.selectedIndex = j; filled++; break; }
          }
        } else if (el.type === 'checkbox') {
          el.checked = (String(params[k]) === '1' || String(params[k]).toLowerCase() === 'true');
          filled++;
        } else if (el.type !== 'hidden' && el.type !== 'submit' && el.type !== 'button') {
          el.value = params[k];
          filled++;
        }
      }
    }
    if (filled > 0) {
      
      var allInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input,select,textarea');
      for (var i2 = 0; i2 < allInputs.length; i2++) {
        try { allInputs[i2].dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true })); } catch(e2) {}
      }
    }
  }
}

(function() {
  'use strict';

  function mleAdvisoryShowProof(settingLabel, strongValue, weakValue) {
    var msg = 'Settings Advisor Proof\n\n'
      + 'Setting: ' + settingLabel + '\n\n'
      + 'Strong runs used: ' + strongValue + '\n'
      + 'Weak runs used: '   + weakValue   + '\n\n'
      + 'This pattern appeared consistently across multiple completed draws.\n'
      + 'Changing only one setting helps LottoExpert learn what actually helped.';
    alert(msg);
  }

  window.mleAdvisoryShowProof = mleAdvisoryShowProof;

  function mleAdvisoryUpdateStatus(runId, status) {
    if (!runId) { return; }
    var formEl = document.createElement('form');
    formEl.method = 'POST';
    formEl.action = window.location.href;
    var fields = { mle_action: 'update_advice_status', run_id: String(runId), status: String(status) };
    for (var k in fields) {
      if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(fields, k)) {
        var inp = document.createElement('input');
        inp.type  = 'hidden';
        inp.name  = k;
        inp.value = fields[k];
        formEl.appendChild(inp);
      }
    }
    var csrfInput = document.querySelector('input[name^="csrf.token"]') || document.querySelector('input[name$="_token"]');
    if (csrfInput) {
      var csrfCopy = document.createElement('input');
      csrfCopy.type  = 'hidden';
      csrfCopy.name  = csrfInput.name;
      csrfCopy.value = csrfInput.value;
      formEl.appendChild(csrfCopy);
    }
    document.body.appendChild(formEl);
    formEl.submit();
  }

  window.mleAdvisoryUpdateStatus = mleAdvisoryUpdateStatus;

}());

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV73ViewModeAwareButtonNavigation) { return; }
  window.__mleV73ViewModeAwareButtonNavigation = true;

  function byId(id){ id = String(id || '').replace(/^#/, ''); return id ? document.getElementById(id) : null; }
  function hasClass(el, cls){ return !!(el && el.className && (' ' + String(el.className) + ' ').indexOf(' ' + cls + ' ') >= 0); }
  function closest(el, sel){
    while (el && el !== document) {
      if (el.matches && el.matches(sel)) { return el; }
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function qsa(sel, root){ var ctx = root || document; return ctx.querySelectorAll ? ctx.querySelectorAll(sel) : []; }
  function qs(sel, root){ var ctx = root || document; return ctx.querySelector ? ctx.querySelector(sel) : null; }
  function show(el){
    if (!el || !el.style) { return; }
    el.style.display = '';
    try { el.removeAttribute('hidden'); } catch(e) {}
    try { el.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false'); } catch(e2) {}
    if (el.classList) {
      el.classList.remove('is-hidden');
      el.classList.remove('mle-hidden');
    }
  }
  function openAncestors(el){
    var cur = el;
    while (cur && cur !== document) {
      if (cur.tagName && String(cur.tagName).toLowerCase() === 'details') {
        try { cur.open = true; } catch(e) {}
        show(cur);
      }
      if (cur.style && (cur.getAttribute('hidden') !== null || cur.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'true')) { show(cur); }
      cur = cur.parentNode;
    }
  }
  function setToggleText(toggle, open){
    var span = toggle && toggle.querySelector ? toggle.querySelector('span') : null;
    var node = span || toggle;
    var txt = node ? (node.textContent || node.innerText || '') : '';
    if (!node) { return; }
    if (txt === 'Expand' || txt === 'Collapse') { node.textContent = open ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand'; return; }
    if (txt.indexOf('View ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'View ') + txt.substring(5); return; }
    if (txt.indexOf('Show ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ') + txt.substring(5); return; }
    if (txt.indexOf('Hide ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ') + txt.substring(5); return; }
  }
  function openControlledPanel(id, root){
    var panel = byId(id);
    var toggles, i;
    if (!panel) { return null; }
    show(panel);
    openAncestors(panel);
    toggles = qsa('[aria-controls="' + String(id).replace(/"/g, '\\"') + '"]', root || document);
    for (i = 0; i < toggles.length; i++) {
      toggles[i].setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
      setToggleText(toggles[i], true);
    }
    return panel;
  }
  function findCard(el){ return closest(el, '.mle-advisory-card') || closest(el, '.mle-lottery-outer') || closest(el, '.lottery-group'); }
  function openCard(card){
    var body, bodies, toggles, outer, group, i;
    if (!card) { return; }
    show(card);
    outer = closest(card, '.mle-lottery-outer');
    group = closest(card, '.lottery-group');
    try {
      if (outer && outer.classList && outer.classList.contains('body-collapsed') && typeof window.skaiLotterySetOneOuter === 'function') { window.skaiLotterySetOneOuter(outer, false); }
      if (group && group.classList && group.classList.contains('collapsed') && typeof window.skaiLotterySetOneGroup === 'function') { window.skaiLotterySetOneGroup(group, false); }
    } catch(e) {}
    bodies = qsa('.mle-advisory-card__body, .mle-lottery-outer-body, .mle-lottery-body', card);
    for (i = 0; i < bodies.length; i++) { show(bodies[i]); }
    body = qs('.mle-advisory-card__body, .mle-lottery-outer-body, .mle-lottery-body', card);
    if (body) { show(body); }
    toggles = qsa('.mle-lottery-toggle, .mle-lottery-outer-toggle', card);
    for (i = 0; i < toggles.length; i++) { toggles[i].setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); setToggleText(toggles[i], true); }
    if (card.classList) { card.classList.add('is-expanded'); }
  }
  function getModeForTarget(card, target){
    var cur = target;
    while (cur && cur !== document && cur !== card) {
      if (cur.getAttribute) {
        var mode = cur.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '';
        if (mode) { return mode; }
      }
      cur = cur.parentNode;
    }
    if (target && target.id) {
      if (target.id.indexOf('evidence-panel') >= 0 || hasClass(target, 'mle-batch-cleanup')) { return 'review-runs'; }
      if (target.id.indexOf('pending') >= 0 || hasClass(target, 'mle-pending-recommendations')) { return 'numbers'; }
      if (target.id.indexOf('next') >= 0 || target.id.indexOf('precision') >= 0 || target.id.indexOf('what-next') >= 0) { return 'next-step'; }
    }
    return '';
  }
  function setCardMode(card, mode){
    var buttons, sections, i, active, smode;
    if (!card || !mode) { return; }
    buttons = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-btn]', card);
    sections = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-section]', card);
    for (i = 0; i < buttons.length; i++) {
      active = (buttons[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-btn') === mode);
      buttons[i].setAttribute('aria-selected', active ? 'true' : 'false');
      if (buttons[i].classList) { if (active) { buttons[i].classList.add('is-active'); } else { buttons[i].classList.remove('is-active'); } }
    }
    for (i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
      smode = sections[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '';
      if (smode === mode) { show(sections[i]); }
      else {
        sections[i].style.display = 'none';
        sections[i].setAttribute('hidden', 'hidden');
        sections[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      }
    }
  }
  function setGlobalEvidenceView(mode){
    var html, details, i, btns;
    mode = (mode === 'quick' || mode === 'strategy') ? mode : 'full';
    html = document.documentElement;
    if (!html || !html.classList) { return; }
    html.classList.remove('mle-v34-mode-quick');
    html.classList.remove('mle-v34-mode-strategy');
    html.classList.remove('mle-v34-mode-full');
    html.classList.add('mle-v34-mode-' + mode);
    btns = qsa('button[data-mle-v34-mode]');
    for (i = 0; i < btns.length; i++) {
      btns[i].setAttribute('aria-pressed', btns[i].getAttribute('data-mle-v34-mode') === mode ? 'true' : 'false');
    }
    if (mode === 'full') {
      details = qsa('details.mle-compact-group');
      for (i = 0; i < details.length; i++) {
        try { details[i].open = true; } catch(e) {}
        show(details[i]);
      }
    }
    try { localStorage.setItem('mle.viewMode.v34', mode); } catch(e2) {}
  }
  function ensureGlobalViewForTarget(target, mode){
    var html, sectionMode;
    if (!target) { return; }
    html = document.documentElement;
    sectionMode = mode || '';
    if (!sectionMode && target.getAttribute) { sectionMode = target.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || ''; }
    if (sectionMode === 'review-runs' || sectionMode === 'details') {
      setGlobalEvidenceView('full');
      return;
    }
    if (html && html.classList && (html.classList.contains('mle-v34-mode-quick') || html.classList.contains('mle-v34-mode-strategy'))) {
      if (closest(target, '.mle-batch-cleanup') || closest(target, '.mle-adv-pred-summary') || closest(target, '.mle-strong-evidence') || closest(target, '.mle-visual-comparison') || closest(target, '.mle-v109-saved-runs') || closest(target, '.mle-lottery-roof-section')) {
        setGlobalEvidenceView('full');
      }
    }
  }
  function findBestReviewTarget(card, btn){
    var id, target;
    id = btn && btn.getAttribute ? (btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || '') : '';
    target = id ? byId(id) : null;
    if (target && (hasClass(target, 'mle-batch-cleanup') || target.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') === 'review-runs')) { return target; }
    target = qs('.mle-batch-cleanup[data-mle-card-mode-section="review-runs"], .mle-batch-cleanup', card);
    if (target) { return target; }
    target = qs('.mle-adv-pred-summary[data-mle-card-mode-section="review-runs"]', card);
    if (target) { return target; }
    if (id) { target = byId(id); if (target) { return target; } }
    target = qs('.mle-saved-runs-panel, [id*="saved-runs"], [id*="runs-body"]', card);
    return target || null;
  }
  function findGenericTarget(card, btn){
    var sid = btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
    var pid = btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-open-details') || '';
    var target = null;
    if (pid) { openControlledPanel(pid, card); }
    if (sid) { target = byId(sid); }
    if (!target && pid) { target = byId(pid); }
    if (!target && btn.getAttribute('data-mle-v71-open-saved-runs')) { target = byId(btn.getAttribute('data-mle-v71-open-saved-runs')); }
    return target;
  }
  function flashAndScroll(target){
    if (!target) { return; }
    show(target);
    openAncestors(target);
    if (!target.hasAttribute || !target.hasAttribute('tabindex')) { try { target.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); } catch(e) {} }
    if (target.classList) { target.classList.add('mle-action-jump-target'); target.classList.add('mle-v72-button-jump-target'); }
    window.setTimeout(function(){
      try { target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); } catch(e1) { try { target.scrollIntoView(true); } catch(e2) {} }
      try { target.focus({preventScroll:true}); } catch(e3) { try { target.focus(); } catch(e4) {} }
      window.setTimeout(function(){ if (target.classList) { target.classList.remove('mle-action-jump-target'); target.classList.remove('mle-v72-button-jump-target'); } }, 2400);
    }, 75);
  }
  function isSkaiExternalAction(btn){
    var action = String(btn.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '').toLowerCase();
    if (!action) { return false; }
    return /^(regular_skai_batch|regular_skai|horizon_ready_batch|settings_ready_batch|horizon_batch|settings_batch|next_settings|precision_batch)$/.test(action);
  }
  function isManagedButton(btn){
    if (!btn || !btn.getAttribute) { return false; }
    if (isSkaiExternalAction(btn)) { return false; }
    if (btn.getAttribute('data-mle-manage-outer-runs') === '1') { return true; }
    if (btn.getAttribute('data-mle-v71-open-saved-runs') !== null) { return true; }
    if (hasClass(btn, 'mle-lottery-outer-manage-runs-btn') || hasClass(btn, 'mle-advisory-manage-runs-btn') || hasClass(btn, 'mle-manage-runs-shortcut-btn') || hasClass(btn, 'mle-scan-pill--manage-runs')) { return true; }
    if (hasClass(btn, 'mle-method-status-jump')) { return true; }
    if (hasClass(btn, 'mle-section-shortcut-btn') && (btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-open-details'))) { return true; }
    if (hasClass(btn, 'mle-status-action-jump') && (btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel'))) { return true; }
    return false;
  }
  function handleButton(btn, evt){
    var card, target, mode, mk;
    if (!btn || !isManagedButton(btn)) { return false; }
    card = findCard(btn);
    if (!card) { return false; }

    if (evt) {
      if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); }
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); }
      if (evt.stopImmediatePropagation) { evt.stopImmediatePropagation(); }
    }

    openCard(card);

    mk = String(btn.getAttribute('data-method-key') || '').toLowerCase();
    if (mk === 'unknown') {
      target = findGenericTarget(card, btn) || qs('.mle-v68-unknown-trace-top, .mle-method-run-card--unknown, [id$="-unknown"]', card);
      if (target) { mode = getModeForTarget(card, target) || 'details'; ensureGlobalViewForTarget(target, mode); setCardMode(card, mode); show(target); flashAndScroll(target); return true; }
    }

    if (btn.getAttribute('data-mle-v71-open-saved-runs') !== null) {
      target = byId(btn.getAttribute('data-mle-v71-open-saved-runs'));
      if (target) { mode = getModeForTarget(card, target) || 'details'; ensureGlobalViewForTarget(target, mode); setCardMode(card, mode); openControlledPanel(target.id, card); flashAndScroll(target); return true; }
    }

    if (btn.getAttribute('data-mle-manage-outer-runs') === '1' || hasClass(btn, 'mle-lottery-outer-manage-runs-btn') || hasClass(btn, 'mle-advisory-manage-runs-btn') || hasClass(btn, 'mle-manage-runs-shortcut-btn') || hasClass(btn, 'mle-scan-pill--manage-runs')) {
      target = findBestReviewTarget(card, btn);
      if (target) { mode = getModeForTarget(card, target) || 'review-runs'; ensureGlobalViewForTarget(target, mode); setCardMode(card, mode); show(target); flashAndScroll(target); return true; }
    }

    target = findGenericTarget(card, btn);
    if (target) {
      mode = getModeForTarget(card, target);
      ensureGlobalViewForTarget(target, mode);
      if (mode) { setCardMode(card, mode); }
      if (target.id) { openControlledPanel(target.id, card); }
      show(target);
      flashAndScroll(target);
      return true;
    }

    return true;
  }

  window.mleV73OpenGeneratedLotteryTarget = function(btn){ return handleButton(btn, null); };
  window.mleManageOuterSavedRuns = function(btn){ handleButton(btn, null); return false; };

  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var btn = closest(evt.target, 'button, a');
    if (!btn) { return; }
    handleButton(btn, evt);
  }, true);

  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(evt){
    var key = evt.key || evt.keyCode;
    var btn;
    if (!(key === 'Enter' || key === ' ' || key === 13 || key === 32)) { return; }
    btn = closest(evt.target, 'button, a');
    if (!btn) { return; }
    handleButton(btn, evt);
  }, true);
})();

(function(){
  function hasClass(el, name){
    return !!(el && typeof el.className === 'string' && (' ' + el.className + ' ').indexOf(' ' + name + ' ') > -1);
  }
  function closestButton(el){
    while(el && el !== document){
      if(el.tagName && String(el.tagName).toUpperCase() === 'BUTTON'){
        return el;
      }
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function closestCard(el){
    while(el && el !== document){
      if(hasClass(el, 'mle-advisory-card')){
        return el;
      }
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function setShortcutActive(card, targetId){
    if(!card || !card.querySelectorAll){ return; }
    var shortcuts = card.querySelectorAll('.mle-section-shortcut-btn');
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < shortcuts.length; i++){
      shortcuts[i].className = String(shortcuts[i].className || '').replace(/\bis-active\b/g, '').replace(/\s{2,}/g, ' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
      shortcuts[i].removeAttribute('aria-current');
      var panelId = shortcuts[i].getAttribute('data-target-panel');
      var sectionId = shortcuts[i].getAttribute('data-target-section');
      if(targetId && (targetId === panelId || targetId === sectionId)){
        shortcuts[i].className += ' is-active';
        shortcuts[i].setAttribute('aria-current', 'true');
      }
    }
  }
  function collapseOtherPrimarySections(card, keepId){
    if(!card || !card.querySelectorAll){ return; }
    var sections = card.querySelectorAll('[data-mle-primary-section-body="1"]');
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < sections.length; i++){
      var section = sections[i];
      var sid = section.getAttribute('id') || '';
      if(!sid || sid === keepId){ continue; }
      section.style.display = 'none';
      section.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      var toggles = card.querySelectorAll('[aria-controls="' + sid + '"]');
      var t;
      for(t = 0; t < toggles.length; t++){
        toggles[t].setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        setText(toggles[t], false);
      }
    }
  }
  function setText(btn, open){
    var node = null;
    var spans = btn.getElementsByTagName ? btn.getElementsByTagName('span') : [];
    node = spans && spans.length ? spans[0] : btn;
    var txt = node.innerHTML || node.textContent || '';
    txt = String(txt).replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
    if(txt === 'Expand' || txt === 'Collapse'){
      node.innerHTML = open ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand';
      return;
    }
    if(txt.indexOf('Show ') === 0){
      node.innerHTML = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ') + txt.substring(5);
      return;
    }
    if(txt.indexOf('Hide ') === 0){
      node.innerHTML = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ') + txt.substring(5);
      return;
    }
    if(txt.indexOf('View ') === 0){
      node.innerHTML = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'View ') + txt.substring(5);
      return;
    }
  }
  function messageNear(btn, text){
    var host = btn.parentNode || btn;
    var msg = document.createElement('div');
    msg.className = 'mle-command-local-message';
    msg.appendChild(document.createTextNode(text));
    host.appendChild(msg);
  }
  function openTarget(id, sourceBtn){
    var el = id ? document.getElementById(id) : null;
    if(!el){ return false; }
    var card = closestCard(sourceBtn || el);
    if(card && el.getAttribute && el.getAttribute('data-mle-primary-section-body') === '1'){
      collapseOtherPrimarySections(card, id);
    }
    el.style.display = 'block';
    el.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
    var buttons = document.querySelectorAll ? document.querySelectorAll('[aria-controls="' + id + '"]') : [];
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < buttons.length; i++){
      buttons[i].setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
      setText(buttons[i], true);
    }
    if(card){
      setShortcutActive(card, id);
    }
    try {
      if(el.scrollIntoView){ el.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); }
    } catch(e) {}
    return true;
  }
  function toggleTarget(btn){
    var id = btn.getAttribute('aria-controls');
    var el = id ? document.getElementById(id) : null;
    if(!el){
      messageNear(btn, 'This section could not be opened because its target was not found.');
      return;
    }
    var currentHidden = el.getAttribute('aria-hidden');
    var currentlyClosed = (currentHidden === 'true' || el.style.display === 'none' || el.offsetParent === null);
    var open = currentlyClosed;
    el.style.display = open ? 'block' : 'none';
    el.setAttribute('aria-hidden', open ? 'false' : 'true');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');
    setText(btn, open);
    var card = closestCard(btn);
    if(card && open && el.getAttribute && el.getAttribute('data-mle-primary-section-body') === '1'){
      collapseOtherPrimarySections(card, id);
      setShortcutActive(card, id);
    } else if(card && open){
      setShortcutActive(card, id);
    } else if(card && !open){
      setShortcutActive(card, '');
    }
  }
  function openCardBodyForManagedRuns(card){
    if(!card || !card.querySelector){ return; }
    var body = card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body');
    if(body){
      body.style.display = 'block';
      body.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
    }
    var toggles = card.querySelectorAll ? card.querySelectorAll('.mle-lottery-toggle') : [];
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < toggles.length; i++){
      toggles[i].setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
      setText(toggles[i], true);
    }
  }
  function manageSavedRunsClick(btn){
    var card = closestCard(btn);
    var panelId = btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
    var panel;
    if(card){ openCardBodyForManagedRuns(card); }
    if(panelId && openTarget(panelId, btn)){
      return true;
    }
    panel = card && card.querySelector ? card.querySelector('.mle-saved-runs-panel') : null;
    if(panel && panel.getAttribute){
      return openTarget(panel.getAttribute('id'), btn);
    }
    messageNear(btn, 'Saved runs could not be opened because the panel was not found.');
    return false;
  }
  function commandClick(ev){
    var btn = closestButton(ev.target || ev.srcElement);
    if(!btn){ return; }
    if(hasClass(btn, 'mle-lottery-toggle') || hasClass(btn, 'mle-section-toggle')){
      if(ev.preventDefault){ ev.preventDefault(); }
      if(ev.stopPropagation){ ev.stopPropagation(); }
      toggleTarget(btn);
      return false;
    }
    if(hasClass(btn, 'mle-manage-runs-shortcut-btn')){
      if(ev.preventDefault){ ev.preventDefault(); }
      if(ev.stopPropagation){ ev.stopPropagation(); }
      manageSavedRunsClick(btn);
      return false;
    }
    if(hasClass(btn, 'mle-section-shortcut-btn')){
      var actionTargetMode = (btn.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '').toLowerCase();
      var pendingTargetId = String(btn.getAttribute('data-open-details') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '');
      if ((btn.getAttribute('data-mle-pending-source-button') === '1' || pendingTargetId.indexOf('mle-pending-predictions-') === 0 || /pending/i.test(pendingTargetId)) && window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource) {
        if(ev.preventDefault){ ev.preventDefault(); }
        if(ev.stopPropagation){ ev.stopPropagation(); }
        return window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource(btn);
      }
      if (/^(regular_skai_batch|regular_skai|horizon_ready_batch|settings_ready_batch|horizon_batch|settings_batch|next_settings)$/.test(actionTargetMode)) {
        
        
        
        return;
      }
      if(ev.preventDefault){ ev.preventDefault(); }
      if(ev.stopPropagation){ ev.stopPropagation(); }
      var panelId = btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel');
      var sectionId = btn.getAttribute('data-target-section');
      if(panelId){
        if(!openTarget(panelId, btn)){
          messageNear(btn, 'This section shortcut could not open because its target was not found.');
        } else {
          var sec = sectionId ? document.getElementById(sectionId) : null;
          try {
            if(sec && sec.scrollIntoView){ sec.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); }
          } catch(e) {}
        }
        return false;
      }
      var target = sectionId ? document.getElementById(sectionId) : null;
      if(!target){
        messageNear(btn, 'This section shortcut could not open because its target was not found.');
        return false;
      }
      setShortcutActive(closestCard(btn), sectionId);
      try {
        if(target.scrollIntoView){ target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); }
      } catch(e) {}
      return false;
    }
    if(hasClass(btn, 'mle-review-runs-btn')){
      if(ev.preventDefault){ ev.preventDefault(); }
      if(ev.stopPropagation){ ev.stopPropagation(); }
      if(!openTarget(btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel'), btn)){
        messageNear(btn, 'This section could not be opened because its target was not found.');
      }
      return false;
    }
    if(hasClass(btn, 'mle-leave-as-is-btn')){
      if(ev.preventDefault){ ev.preventDefault(); }
      if(ev.stopPropagation){ ev.stopPropagation(); }
      messageNear(btn, 'No changes applied. Your saved history was left as is.');
      return false;
    }
    if(btn.getAttribute('data-adv-print-card')){
      if(ev.preventDefault){ ev.preventDefault(); }
      if(ev.stopPropagation){ ev.stopPropagation(); }
      mleAdvisoryCardPrint(btn);
      return false;
    }
  }
  if(document.addEventListener){
    document.addEventListener('click', commandClick, true);
  } else if(document.attachEvent){
    document.attachEvent('onclick', commandClick);
  }
}());


function mleAdvisoryCardPrint(btn) {
  var LT = '\u003c', GT = '\u003e';
  function esc(s) {
    return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'\u0026amp;').replace(/\u003c/g,'\u0026lt;').replace(/\u003e/g,'\u0026gt;').replace(/"/g,'\u0026quot;');
  }
  
  var node = btn;
  while(node && node !== document){
    if(node.className && String(node.className).indexOf('mle-advisory-card') !== -1){ break; }
    node = node.parentNode;
  }
  if(!node || node === document){ return; }

  
  var clone = node.cloneNode(true);

  
  var body = clone.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body');
  if(body){ body.style.display='block'; body.removeAttribute('aria-hidden'); }

  
  var sbs = clone.querySelectorAll('.mle-section-body,[aria-hidden]');
  for(var s=0;s<sbs.length;s++){
    sbs[s].style.display='block';
    sbs[s].style.visibility='visible';
    sbs[s].style.height='auto';
    sbs[s].style.maxHeight='none';
    sbs[s].removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
  }

  
  var rm = clone.querySelectorAll(
    '.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-section-toggle,.mle-section-shortcuts,.mle-section-shortcut-btn,button,input[type="checkbox"],.mle-adv-print-btn,.mle-adv-results-link'
  );
  for(var r=rm.length-1;r>=0;r--){
    if(rm[r].parentNode){ rm[r].parentNode.removeChild(rm[r]); }
  }

  var lotteryTitle = '';
  var h3 = clone.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name');
  if(h3){ lotteryTitle = (h3.textContent || h3.innerText || '').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,''); }

  var bodyHtml = clone.innerHTML;

  
  var p = [];
  p.push(LT+'!DOCTYPE html'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'html lang="en"'+GT+LT+'head'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'meta charset="UTF-8"'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'meta name="color-scheme" content="light only"'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'title'+GT+esc(lotteryTitle||'Lottery Advisory Card')+LT+'/title'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'style'+GT);
  p.push('html,body{background:#fff !important;color:#111 !important;margin:0;padding:0;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;line-height:1.45;}');
  p.push('.mle-print-toolbar{position:sticky;top:0;z-index:9999;padding:10px 16px;background:#0A1A33;color:#fff;border-bottom:1px solid #d1d5db;}');
  p.push('.mle-print-toolbar-title{display:inline-block;font-size:15px;font-weight:700;vertical-align:middle;}');
  p.push('.mle-print-toolbar-actions{float:right;}');
  p.push('.mle-print-toolbar-btn{display:inline-block;margin-left:8px;padding:7px 12px;border:0;border-radius:6px;background:#1C66FF;color:#fff;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;}');
  p.push('.mle-print-toolbar-btn-secondary{background:#4b5563;}');
  p.push('.mle-print-doc{padding:20px;}');
  p.push('h3,h4,h5{margin:0 0 8px;color:#0A1A33;}');
  p.push('.mle-advisory-card__logo-fallback{display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;width:36px;height:36px;border-radius:10px;background:#0A1A33;color:#fff;font-size:.8rem;font-weight:900;}');
  p.push('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-ident{display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;margin-bottom:8px;}');
  p.push('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name{font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:900;color:#0A1A33;margin:0;}');
  p.push('.mle-adv-run-stats{display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:6px;margin:8px 0;}');
  p.push('.mle-adv-stat-chip{display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:999px;padding:4px 10px;font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:#334155;background:#f8fafc;}');
  p.push('.mle-adv-stat-chip--scored{background:#f0fdf9;border-color:#6ee7b7;}.mle-adv-stat-chip--pending{background:#fffbf0;border-color:#fcd34d;}.mle-adv-stat-chip--fresh-runs{background:#fff7ed;border-color:#fb923c;}.mle-adv-stat-chip--best-hits{background:#eff6ff;border-color:#93c5fd;}');
  p.push('.mle-adv-stat-value{font-weight:900;color:#0A1A33;font-size:.95rem;}.mle-adv-stat-label{font-size:.66rem;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.07em;color:#64748b;}');
  p.push('.mle-proof-badge{display:inline-block;padding:3px 9px;border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:999px;font-size:.72rem;font-weight:900;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.07em;}');
  p.push('.mle-proof-badge--strong-pattern{background:#ffedd5;color:#9a3412;border-color:#fb923c;}');
  p.push('.mle-proof-badge--trusted-recipe{background:#dcfce7;color:#166534;border-color:#86efac;}');
  p.push('.mle-proof-badge--good-test,.mle-proof-badge--close-race{background:#fef3c7;color:#92400e;border-color:#fcd34d;}');
  p.push('.mle-proof-badge--early-clue{background:#dbeafe;color:#1d4ed8;border-color:#93c5fd;}');
  p.push('.mle-proof-badge--too-early,.mle-proof-badge--no-clear-winner{background:#f1f5f9;color:#334155;border-color:#cbd5e1;}');
  p.push('.mle-advisory-card__collapsed{padding:14px;background:#f8fafc;border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:12px 12px 0 0;}');
  p.push('.mle-advisory-card__body{padding:14px;background:#fff;}');
  p.push('.mle-section-shortcuts{display:none !important;}');
  p.push('.mle-lottery-command-hero{background:#0A1A33;color:#fff;border-radius:12px;padding:14px;margin:0 0 12px;}');
  p.push('.mle-lottery-command-hero *{color:#fff !important;}');
  p.push('.mle-optimization-focus,.mle-visual-comparison,.mle-next-settings-run,.mle-adv-pred-summary,.mle-lottery-roof-section,.mle-batch-cleanup,.mle-precision-lock{border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:10px;padding:12px;margin:0 0 12px;background:#fff;}');
  p.push('.mle-optimization-focus__grid,.mle-next-settings-run__details,.mle-adv-pred-summary__grid{display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(2,1fr);gap:8px;}');
  p.push('.mle-optimization-focus__grid div,.mle-next-settings-run__details div,.mle-adv-pred-summary__grid div{border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:8px;padding:8px;background:#f8fafc;}');
  p.push('.mle-visual-row{border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:8px;padding:8px;margin:4px 0;background:#f8fafc;}');
  p.push('.mle-ball{display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;width:26px;height:26px;border-radius:999px;background:#edf2ff;border:1px solid #dbe4ff;color:#0A1A33;font-weight:800;font-size:11px;}');
  p.push('.mle-ball--match{background:#20C997;color:#fff;border-color:#20C997;}');
  p.push('.mle-card-roof-map{display:none;}');
  p.push('.mle-mini-card{border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:8px;padding:10px;background:#f8fafc;}');
  p.push('@media print{html,body{background:#fff !important;}body{margin:0 !important;}.mle-print-toolbar{display:none !important;}}');
  p.push(LT+'/style'+GT+LT+'/head'+GT+LT+'body'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'div class="mle-print-toolbar"'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'span class="mle-print-toolbar-title"'+GT+esc(lotteryTitle||'Lottery Advisory Card')+LT+'/span'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'span class="mle-print-toolbar-actions"'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'button type="button" class="mle-print-toolbar-btn" onclick="window.focus();window.print();"'+GT+'Print'+LT+'/button'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'button type="button" class="mle-print-toolbar-btn mle-print-toolbar-btn-secondary" onclick="window.close();"'+GT+'Close'+LT+'/button'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'/span'+GT+LT+'div style="clear:both"'+GT+LT+'/div'+GT+LT+'/div'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'div class="mle-print-doc"'+GT+bodyHtml+LT+'/div'+GT);
  p.push(LT+'script'+GT);
  p.push('(function(){var pr=false;function go(){if(pr){return;}pr=true;window.focus();window.setTimeout(function(){try{window.print();}catch(e){}},250);}');
  p.push('if(document.readyState==="complete"){window.setTimeout(go,250);}else if(window.addEventListener){window.addEventListener("load",function(){window.setTimeout(go,250);});}');
  p.push('if(window.addEventListener){window.addEventListener("afterprint",function(){window.close();});}');
  p.push('window.setTimeout(function(){try{window.close();}catch(e){}},120000);');
  p.push('})();');
  p.push(LT+'/script'+GT+LT+'/body'+GT+LT+'/html'+GT);

  var html = p.join('');
  var win = null;
  try { win = window.open('','_blank','width=1100,height=800,menubar=no,toolbar=yes,location=no,status=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes'); } catch(e){}
  if(!win){ return; }
  try { win.document.open(); win.document.write(html); win.document.close(); win.focus(); } catch(e){ try{win.close();}catch(e2){} }
}

(function(){
  'use strict';
  var STORE_KEY = 'mle_keep_position_after_update_v2';

  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function closest(el, sel){
    if (!el) { return null; }
    if (el.closest) { return el.closest(sel); }
    while (el && el.nodeType === 1) {
      if (matches(el, sel)) { return el; }
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function matches(el, sel){
    var fn = el.matches || el.msMatchesSelector || el.webkitMatchesSelector;
    return !!(fn && fn.call(el, sel));
  }
  function byId(id){ return id ? document.getElementById(id) : null; }
  function setExpandedButton(btn, open){
    if (!btn) { return; }
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');
    var node = btn.querySelector ? (btn.querySelector('span') || btn) : btn;
    var txt = (node.textContent || '').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
    if (txt === 'Expand' || txt === 'Collapse') { node.textContent = open ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand'; return; }
    if (txt.indexOf('Show ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ') + txt.substring(5); return; }
    if (txt.indexOf('Hide ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ') + txt.substring(5); return; }
    if (txt.indexOf('View ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'View ') + txt.substring(5); return; }
  }
  function openSectionById(id){
    var el = byId(id);
    if (!el) { return false; }
    el.style.display = 'block';
    el.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
    qsa('[aria-controls="' + cssEscape(id) + '"]').forEach(function(btn){ setExpandedButton(btn, true); });
    return true;
  }
  function cssEscape(v){
    if (window.CSS && CSS.escape) { return CSS.escape(String(v)); }
    return String(v).replace(/([ #;?%&,.+*~\':"!^$[\]()=>|\/])/g, '\\$1');
  }
  function openOuter(outer){
    if (!outer) { return; }
    outer.classList.remove('body-collapsed');
    outer.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
    var lid = outer.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id') || '';
    var head = outer.querySelector('[data-outer-lottery-toggle]');
    var btn = outer.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn]');
    if (head) { head.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); }
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = 'Collapse'; btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Collapse lottery section'); }
    if (lid) { try { localStorage.setItem('mle_outer_collapsed_' + lid, 'false'); } catch(e) {} }
  }
  function closeOuter(outer){
    if (!outer) { return; }
    outer.classList.add('body-collapsed');
    outer.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
    var lid = outer.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id') || '';
    var head = outer.querySelector('[data-outer-lottery-toggle]');
    var btn = outer.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn]');
    if (head) { head.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false'); }
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = 'Expand'; btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Expand lottery section'); }
    if (lid) { try { localStorage.setItem('mle_outer_collapsed_' + lid, 'true'); } catch(e) {} }
  }
  function openLotteryGroup(group){
    if (!group) { return; }
    group.classList.remove('collapsed');
    var lotteryId = group.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
    var base = lotteryId ? lotteryId.split('-')[0] : '';
    var btn = group.querySelector('.lottery-collapse-toggle,[data-lottery-toggle-btn]');
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = 'Collapse'; btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Collapse lottery section'); }
    if (base) { try { localStorage.setItem('lottery_collapsed_' + base, 'false'); } catch(e) {} }
  }
  function closeLotteryGroup(group){
    if (!group) { return; }
    group.classList.add('collapsed');
    var lotteryId = group.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
    var base = lotteryId ? lotteryId.split('-')[0] : '';
    var btn = group.querySelector('.lottery-collapse-toggle,[data-lottery-toggle-btn]');
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = 'Expand'; btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false'); btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Expand lottery section'); }
    if (base) { try { localStorage.setItem('lottery_collapsed_' + base, 'true'); } catch(e) {} }
  }
  function openAdvisoryCard(card){
    if (!card) { return; }
    var body = card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body');
    if (body && body.id) { openSectionById(body.id); }
    else if (body) { body.style.display = 'block'; body.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false'); }
    var btn = card.querySelector('.mle-lottery-toggle');
    if (btn) { setExpandedButton(btn, true); }
  }
  function openAncestors(el){
    if (!el) { return; }
    openOuter(closest(el, '.mle-lottery-outer'));
    openLotteryGroup(closest(el, '.lottery-group'));
    openAdvisoryCard(closest(el, '.mle-advisory-card'));
    var parentHidden = closest(el.parentNode, '.mle-section-body[aria-hidden="true"], .mle-advisory-card__body[aria-hidden="true"]');
    if (parentHidden && parentHidden.id) { openSectionById(parentHidden.id); }
  }
  function flash(el){
    if (!el || !el.classList) { return; }
    el.classList.remove('mle-shortcut-flash');
    setTimeout(function(){ el.classList.add('mle-shortcut-flash'); }, 10);
    setTimeout(function(){ el.classList.remove('mle-shortcut-flash'); }, 1400);
  }
  function scrollToTarget(el){
    if (!el) { return; }
    openAncestors(el);
    setTimeout(function(){
      try { el.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); }
      catch(e) { try { el.scrollIntoView(true); } catch(ignore) {} }
      if (!el.hasAttribute('tabindex')) { el.setAttribute('tabindex','-1'); }
      try { el.focus({preventScroll:true}); } catch(fe) { try { el.focus(); } catch(ignore2) {} }
      flash(el);
    }, 80);
  }
  function setCardShortcutActive(btn, targetId){
    var card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card');
    if (!card) { return; }
    qsa('.mle-section-shortcut-btn', card).forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.remove('is-active');
      b.removeAttribute('aria-current');
    });
    btn.classList.add('is-active');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-current','true');
  }
  function handleShortcut(btn, evt){
    
    if (btn && btn.getAttribute && btn.getAttribute('data-action-target') && (closest(btn, '.mle-status-action-jump') || closest(btn, '.mle-scan-pill--clickable'))) { return false; }
    var panelId = btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || '';
    var sectionId = btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
    var target = byId(panelId) || byId(sectionId);
    if (!target && sectionId) { target = byId(sectionId); }
    if (!target) { return false; }
    if (panelId) { openSectionById(panelId); }
    if (sectionId) {
      var sectionEl = byId(sectionId);
      if (sectionEl) { target = sectionEl; }
    }
    setCardShortcutActive(btn, target.id || panelId || sectionId);
    scrollToTarget(target);
    if (evt) {
      if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); }
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); }
      if (evt.stopImmediatePropagation) { evt.stopImmediatePropagation(); }
    }
    return true;
  }

  
  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var btn = closest(evt.target, '.mle-section-shortcut-btn');
    if (!btn) { return; }
    if (handleShortcut(btn, evt)) { return false; }
  }, true);

  
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(evt){
    var key = evt.key || evt.keyCode;
    var isActivate = (key === 'Enter' || key === ' ' || key === 13 || key === 32);
    if (!isActivate) { return; }
    var shortcut = closest(evt.target, '.mle-section-shortcut-btn');
    if (shortcut && handleShortcut(shortcut, evt)) { return false; }
    var outerHead = closest(evt.target, '[data-outer-lottery-toggle]');
    if (outerHead) {
      var outer = closest(outerHead, '.mle-lottery-outer');
      if (outer) {
        if (outer.classList.contains('body-collapsed')) { openOuter(outer); } else { closeOuter(outer); }
        evt.preventDefault();
      }
    }
  }, true);

  
  window.skaiLotteryCollapseAll = function(shouldCollapse){
    shouldCollapse = !!shouldCollapse;
    qsa('.mle-lottery-outer').forEach(function(outer){ shouldCollapse ? closeOuter(outer) : openOuter(outer); });
    qsa('.lottery-group').forEach(function(group){ shouldCollapse ? closeLotteryGroup(group) : openLotteryGroup(group); });
    qsa('[data-lottery-toggle-all-btn="1"]').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.textContent = shouldCollapse ? 'Expand All' : 'Collapse All';
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', shouldCollapse ? 'false' : 'true');
    });
    return false;
  };
  window.mleVisibleCollapseAll = window.skaiLotteryCollapseAll;

  
  function injectCollapseTools(){
    if (document.getElementById('mle-interaction-repair-tools')) { return; }
    var anchor = document.getElementById('my-lotteries');
    if (!anchor || !anchor.parentNode) { return; }
    var wrap = document.createElement('div');
    wrap.id = 'mle-interaction-repair-tools';
    wrap.className = 'mle-interaction-repair-tools';
    wrap.innerHTML = '<strong>Lottery tabs:</strong><button type="button" data-mle-repair-collapse-all="1">Collapse All</button><button type="button" data-mle-repair-expand-all="1">Expand All</button>';
    anchor.parentNode.insertBefore(wrap, anchor.nextSibling);
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var collapse = closest(evt.target, '[data-mle-repair-collapse-all="1"]');
    var expand = closest(evt.target, '[data-mle-repair-expand-all="1"]');
    if (!collapse && !expand) { return; }
    evt.preventDefault();
    window.skaiLotteryCollapseAll(!!collapse);
  }, true);

  function clearLegacyRestore(){
    try { sessionStorage.removeItem(STORE_KEY); } catch(e) {}
    try { sessionStorage.removeItem('mle_restore_anchor_v2'); } catch(e2) {}
  }
  function restorePosition(){
    clearLegacyRestore();
    try { if ('scrollRestoration' in history) { history.scrollRestoration = 'manual'; } } catch(e) {}
    return;
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ injectCollapseTools(); restorePosition(); });
  } else {
    injectCollapseTools();
    restorePosition();
  }
}());


(function(){
  'use strict';
  function qsa(sel, root){return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel));}
  function closest(el, sel){while(el && el.nodeType === 1){if(el.matches && el.matches(sel)){return el;} el = el.parentElement;} return null;}
  function idSafe(id){try{return document.getElementById(id);}catch(e){return null;}}
  function setBtn(btn, open){if(!btn){return;} btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false'); var s=btn.querySelector('span'); if(s){s.textContent=open?'Collapse':'Expand';} else {btn.textContent=open?'Collapse':'Expand';}}
  function openCard(card){
    if(!card){return;}
    var body = card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body');
    if(body){body.style.display='block';body.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');}
    setBtn(card.querySelector('.mle-lottery-toggle'), true);
    var outer = closest(card, '.mle-lottery-outer');
    if(outer){outer.classList.remove('body-collapsed');outer.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');setBtn(outer.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn]'), true);}
    var group = closest(card, '.lottery-group');
    if(group){group.classList.remove('collapsed');group.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');setBtn(group.querySelector('.lottery-collapse-toggle,[data-lottery-toggle-btn]'), true);}
  }
  function openPanelById(id){
    var panel = idSafe(id);
    if(!panel){return null;}
    panel.style.display='block';
    panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
    qsa('[aria-controls="' + id.replace(/(["\\])/g,'\\$1') + '"]').forEach(function(btn){setBtn(btn, true);});
    return panel;
  }
  function flash(el){if(!el||!el.classList){return;} el.classList.remove('mle-jump-target-flash'); setTimeout(function(){el.classList.add('mle-jump-target-flash');},10); setTimeout(function(){el.classList.remove('mle-jump-target-flash');},1600);}
  function scrollTo(el){
    if(!el){return;}
    setTimeout(function(){
      try{el.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'});}catch(e){try{el.scrollIntoView(true);}catch(ignore){}}
      if(!el.hasAttribute('tabindex')){el.setAttribute('tabindex','-1');}
      try{el.focus({preventScroll:true});}catch(e2){}
      flash(el);
    },80);
  }
  function targetFor(btn){
    var sid = btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
    var pid = btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || '';
    var card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card');
    if(card){openCard(card);}
    if(pid){openPanelById(pid);}
    var target = sid ? idSafe(sid) : null;
    if(!target && pid){target = idSafe(pid);}
    return target;
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    var btn = closest(e.target, '.mle-card-roof-map .mle-section-shortcut-btn, .mle-section-shortcuts .mle-section-shortcut-btn');
    if(!btn){return;}
    if(btn.tagName === 'A' && btn.getAttribute('href') && btn.getAttribute('href').charAt(0) !== '#'){return;}
    var target = targetFor(btn);
    if(!target){return;}
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    if(e.stopImmediatePropagation){e.stopImmediatePropagation();}
    var card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card');
    if(card){qsa('.mle-section-shortcut-btn', card).forEach(function(x){x.classList.remove('is-active');x.removeAttribute('aria-current');});}
    btn.classList.add('is-active');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-current','true');
    scrollTo(target);
    return false;
  }, true);
})();


(function(){
  'use strict';
  function byId(id){return document.getElementById(id);}
  function qs(sel, root){return (root || document).querySelector(sel);}
  function buildLegend(){
    var div = document.createElement('div');
    div.id = 'mle-status-legend-v8';
    div.className = 'mle-status-legend-v8';
    div.setAttribute('aria-label','Status color legend');
    div.innerHTML = ''+
      '<span class="mle-status-legend-v8__title">Status colors</span>'+
      '<span class="mle-status-legend-v8__item mle-status-legend-v8__item--blue"><span class="mle-status-legend-v8__dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Blue: guidance / next step</span>'+
      '<span class="mle-status-legend-v8__item mle-status-legend-v8__item--green"><span class="mle-status-legend-v8__dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Green: healthy / validated</span>'+
      '<span class="mle-status-legend-v8__item mle-status-legend-v8__item--amber"><span class="mle-status-legend-v8__dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Amber: review / attention</span>'+
      '<span class="mle-status-legend-v8__item mle-status-legend-v8__item--red"><span class="mle-status-legend-v8__dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Red: action needed</span>'+
      '<span class="mle-status-legend-v8__item mle-status-legend-v8__item--slate"><span class="mle-status-legend-v8__dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Slate: learning / neutral</span>';
    return div;
  }
  function injectLegend(){
    if(byId('mle-status-legend-v8')){return;}
    var lotteries = byId('my-lotteries') || qs('.mle-lottery-outer') || qs('.lottery-group') || qs('.mle-advisory-card');
    if(!lotteries || !lotteries.parentNode){return;}
    lotteries.parentNode.insertBefore(buildLegend(), lotteries);
  }
  if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', injectLegend);
  }else{
    injectLegend();
  }
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  var HELP_TEXT = {
    'Optimization Focus':'Jump to the main recommendation and decision section for this lottery.',
    'Precision Focus':'Jump to the History Window Range, Settings Precision Range, and Precision Progress explanation.',
    'Precision Focus Batches':'Jump to batches created by MyLottoExpert for controlled SKAI testing.',
    'Strong Evidence Runs':'Jump to saved runs that are currently supporting the recommendation.',
    'Settings That Repeat':'Jump to repeated settings and clusters LottoExpert is watching.',
    'Current Locked Settings':'Jump to settings currently being treated as stable control settings.',
    'Recommended Next Settings Run':'Jump to the recommended Settings Precision test.',
    'Visual Run Comparison':'Jump to charts and comparisons showing how runs performed.',
    'Saved Predictions':'Jump to saved prediction runs, including pending and scored runs.',
    'Saved Numbers to Play':'Jump to saved number sets for playing or review.',
    'Saved Settings':'Jump to saved SKAI settings and reusable templates.',
    'Advanced Details':'Jump to deeper diagnostics and supporting evidence.',
    'Review Runs':'Jump to the area where runs can be included or excluded from advice.',
    'Decision':'Jump to the main recommendation for this lottery.',
    'Narrowing method':'Jump to the section that shows the History Window Range and Settings Precision Range.',
    'Next settings run':'Jump to the recommended batch for this lottery: regular SKAI, History Window, or Settings Precision.',
    'Visual proof':'Jump to visual evidence and run comparisons.',
    'Saved runs':'Jump to saved prediction runs.',
    'Saved numbers':'Jump to saved numbers to play or review.',
    'Wheels':'Jump to favorite wheeling systems.'
  };
  function closest(el, sel){while(el && el.nodeType===1){if(el.matches && el.matches(sel)){return el;}el=el.parentNode;}return null;}
  function textOf(el){return (el.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();}
  function ensureShortcutTitles(){
    var btns = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-section-shortcut-btn');
    for(var i=0;i<btns.length;i++){
      var label = textOf(btns[i]);
      if(HELP_TEXT[label] && !btns[i].getAttribute('title')){btns[i].setAttribute('title', HELP_TEXT[label]);}
      if(HELP_TEXT[label] && !btns[i].getAttribute('aria-label')){btns[i].setAttribute('aria-label', label + '. ' + HELP_TEXT[label]);}
    }
  }
  var pop = null;
  function removePop(){if(pop && pop.parentNode){pop.parentNode.removeChild(pop);}pop=null;}
  function showPop(el){
    var msg = el.getAttribute('data-help') || el.getAttribute('title') || '';
    if(!msg){return;}
    removePop();
    pop = document.createElement('div');
    pop.className='mle-help-popover-v17';
    pop.setAttribute('role','tooltip');
    pop.textContent=msg;
    document.body.appendChild(pop);
    var r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
    var top = Math.max(8, r.top - pop.offsetHeight - 10);
    var left = Math.min(window.innerWidth - pop.offsetWidth - 8, Math.max(8, r.left + (r.width/2) - (pop.offsetWidth/2)));
    if(top < 8){top = Math.min(window.innerHeight - pop.offsetHeight - 8, r.bottom + 10);}
    pop.style.top = top + 'px';
    pop.style.left = left + 'px';
  }
  function confirmMessage(kind){
    if(kind === 'horizon-create'){
      return 'Create History Window Batch - Not a Prediction?\n\nImportant: this is a window-narrowing batch. Do not use the numbers from this run as predictions.\n\nThe purpose is to run controlled draw-history tests so LottoExpert can identify the best supported window before creating future Settings Precision prediction runs.\n\nRun 1 is the control. Runs 2 through 9 test history windows: 25, 50, 100, 150, 200, 300, 500, and 1000 draws back.\n\nBy continuing, you acknowledge this is a controlled History Window learning batch only, not a playable prediction batch. Continue?';
    }
    if(kind === 'precision-create'){
      return 'Create 9-Run SKAI Batch and Continue to SKAI?\n\nThis will create a controlled 9-run SKAI batch for this lottery and then take you to SKAI.\n\nRun 1 is the control. Runs 2 through 9 test the recommended setting range.\n\nContinue only if you are ready to create the batch and move to SKAI. This is a structured test, not a guarantee.';
    }
    if(kind === 'precision-open'){
      return 'Open 9-Run SKAI Batch in a New Window?\n\nSKAI will open in a new browser tab/window and load the MyLottoExpert-selected 9-run batch for this lottery.\n\nDo not create another batch for this lottery until these runs are generated and later scored.\n\nContinue?';
    }
    if(kind === 'skai-batch-open-new-window'){
      return 'Open SKAI 9-Run Batch in a New Window?\n\nThis will open SKAI in a new browser tab/window for this lottery so you can run the recommended 9-batch path.\n\nContinue?';
    }
    return '';
  }
  document.addEventListener('mouseover', function(e){var h=closest(e.target,'.mle-help-tip'); if(h){showPop(h);}});
  document.addEventListener('mouseout', function(e){var h=closest(e.target,'.mle-help-tip'); if(h){removePop();}});
  document.addEventListener('focusin', function(e){var h=closest(e.target,'.mle-help-tip'); if(h){showPop(h);}});
  document.addEventListener('focusout', function(e){var h=closest(e.target,'.mle-help-tip'); if(h){removePop();}});
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    var h=closest(e.target,'.mle-help-tip');
    if(h){e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); if(pop){removePop();}else{showPop(h);} return;}
    if(pop){removePop();}
    var target = closest(e.target, '[data-mle-confirm]');
    if(target && target.tagName !== 'FORM'){
      var msg = confirmMessage(target.getAttribute('data-mle-confirm'));
      if(msg && !window.confirm(msg)){e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();}
    }
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('submit', function(e){
    var f = e.target;
    if(!f || !f.getAttribute){return;}
    var kind = f.getAttribute('data-mle-confirm');
    var msg = confirmMessage(kind);
    if(msg && !window.confirm(msg)){e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();}
  }, true);
  if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', ensureShortcutTitles);
  }else{
    ensureShortcutTitles();
  }
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  var currentTip = null;
  var currentAnchor = null;
  var hideTimer = null;

  function closest(el, sel){
    while(el && el.nodeType === 1){
      if(el.matches && el.matches(sel)){return el;}
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function removeOldPopovers(){
    var old = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-help-popover-v17,#mle-help-popover-v22');
    for(var i=0;i<old.length;i++){
      if(old[i].parentNode){old[i].parentNode.removeChild(old[i]);}
    }
    var active = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-help-tip[aria-expanded="true"]');
    for(var j=0;j<active.length;j++){active[j].setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');}
    currentTip = null;
    currentAnchor = null;
  }
  function getHelpText(el){
    return (el.getAttribute('data-help') || el.getAttribute('aria-label') || el.getAttribute('title') || '').replace(/^.* help$/i,'').trim();
  }
  function positionTip(anchor, tip){
    var r = anchor.getBoundingClientRect();
    var vw = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth;
    var vh = window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight;
    var top = r.top - tip.offsetHeight - 12;
    var placement = 'top';
    if(top < 10){
      top = r.bottom + 12;
      placement = 'bottom';
    }
    var left = r.left + (r.width / 2) - (tip.offsetWidth / 2);
    left = Math.max(10, Math.min(vw - tip.offsetWidth - 10, left));
    if(top + tip.offsetHeight > vh - 10){top = Math.max(10, vh - tip.offsetHeight - 10);}
    tip.style.left = left + 'px';
    tip.style.top = top + 'px';
    tip.setAttribute('data-placement', placement);
    var arrowLeft = Math.max(16, Math.min(tip.offsetWidth - 24, (r.left + r.width/2) - left));
    tip.style.setProperty('--mle-tip-arrow-left', arrowLeft + 'px');
  }
  function showTip(anchor){
    if(!anchor){return;}
    var msg = getHelpText(anchor);
    if(!msg){return;}
    if(currentAnchor === anchor && currentTip){return;}
    removeOldPopovers();
    var tip = document.createElement('div');
    tip.id = 'mle-help-popover-v22';
    tip.setAttribute('role','tooltip');
    tip.textContent = msg;
    document.body.appendChild(tip);
    anchor.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');
    currentTip = tip;
    currentAnchor = anchor;
    positionTip(anchor, tip);
  }
  function scheduleHide(){
    clearTimeout(hideTimer);
    hideTimer = setTimeout(function(){removeOldPopovers();}, 120);
  }
  function cancelHide(){clearTimeout(hideTimer);}
  function prepareHelpIcons(){
    var tips = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-help-tip');
    for(var i=0;i<tips.length;i++){
      tips[i].setAttribute('role','button');
      tips[i].setAttribute('tabindex','0');
      tips[i].setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
      var msg = tips[i].getAttribute('data-help');
      if(msg){tips[i].setAttribute('title', msg);}
    }
  }

  document.addEventListener('mouseover', function(e){
    var h = closest(e.target, '.mle-help-tip');
    if(h){cancelHide(); showTip(h);}
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('mouseout', function(e){
    var h = closest(e.target, '.mle-help-tip');
    if(h){scheduleHide();}
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('focusin', function(e){
    var h = closest(e.target, '.mle-help-tip');
    if(h){showTip(h);}
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('focusout', function(e){
    var h = closest(e.target, '.mle-help-tip');
    if(h){scheduleHide();}
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    var h = closest(e.target, '.mle-help-tip');
    if(h){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      if(currentAnchor === h && currentTip){removeOldPopovers();}
      else{showTip(h);}
      return false;
    }
    if(!closest(e.target, '#mle-help-popover-v22')){removeOldPopovers();}
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e){
    var h = closest(e.target, '.mle-help-tip');
    if(h && (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ')){
      e.preventDefault();
      if(currentAnchor === h && currentTip){removeOldPopovers();}else{showTip(h);}
    }
    if(e.key === 'Escape'){removeOldPopovers();}
  }, true);
  window.addEventListener('scroll', function(){if(currentAnchor && currentTip){positionTip(currentAnchor, currentTip);}}, true);
  window.addEventListener('resize', function(){if(currentAnchor && currentTip){positionTip(currentAnchor, currentTip);}});
  if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', prepareHelpIcons);
  }else{
    prepareHelpIcons();
  }
})();


(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_SOURCE_PENDING_RUNS_CANONICAL_CONTROLLER__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_SOURCE_PENDING_RUNS_CANONICAL_CONTROLLER__ = true;

  function qs(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector ? (root || document).querySelector(sel) : null; }
  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll ? (root || document).querySelectorAll(sel) : []); }
  function closest(el, sel){ while(el && el !== document){ if(el.matches && el.matches(sel)){ return el; } el = el.parentNode; } return null; }
  function setText(el, text){ if(el){ el.textContent = text; } }
  function show(el){ if(!el){ return; } try{ el.hidden = false; el.removeAttribute('hidden'); el.style.display = ''; el.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false'); }catch(e){} }
  function openDetailsParents(el){
    var d = el && el.closest ? el.closest('details') : null;
    while(d){ try{ d.open = true; show(d); }catch(e){} d = d.parentElement && d.parentElement.closest ? d.parentElement.closest('details') : null; }
  }
  function openOuter(card){
    var outer = closest(card, '.mle-lottery-outer');
    var head, btn;
    if(outer){
      try{ outer.classList.remove('body-collapsed'); outer.classList.add('is-expanded'); outer.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true'); }catch(e){}
      head = qs('[data-outer-lottery-toggle]', outer);
      btn = qs('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn]', outer);
      if(head){ head.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true'); }
      if(btn){ setText(btn,'Collapse'); btn.setAttribute('aria-label','Collapse lottery section'); }
    }
  }
  function openCard(card){
    var body, toggle, span;
    if(!card){ return; }
    openOuter(card);
    try{ card.classList.remove('is-collapsed','mle-is-collapsed','body-collapsed'); card.classList.add('is-expanded','mle-is-expanded'); card.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true'); }catch(e){}
    body = qs('.mle-advisory-card__body', card);
    show(body);
    toggle = qs('.mle-lottery-toggle', card);
    if(toggle){ toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true'); span = qs('span', toggle); setText(span || toggle, 'Collapse'); }
  }
  function targetFromButton(btn, card){
    var id, el, lid;
    if(btn && btn.getAttribute){
      id = btn.getAttribute('data-open-details') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
      if(id){ el = document.getElementById(id); if(el){ return el; } }
    }
    lid = card && card.getAttribute ? (card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || card.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id') || '') : '';
    if(lid){
      el = document.getElementById('mle-pending-predictions-' + lid);
      if(el){ return el; }
    }
    return qs('[data-mle-pending-source="1"]', card) ||
           qs('.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown, .mle-pending-predictions-dropdown-v36, .mle-pending-recommendations, [id^="mle-pending-predictions-"]', card) ||
           qs('.mle-method-pending-details', card) ||
           qs('.mle-visual-comparison', card) ||
           card;
  }
  function revealCardMode(card, target){
    var owner, mode, sections, i, btns, active;
    if(!card || !target){ return; }
    owner = target.closest ? target.closest('[data-mle-card-mode-section]') : null;
    if(!owner){ owner = qs('[data-mle-card-mode-section] .mle-pending-predictions-dropdown, [data-mle-card-mode-section] .mle-pending-recommendations', card); if(owner && owner.closest){ owner = owner.closest('[data-mle-card-mode-section]'); } }
    if(!owner || !owner.getAttribute){ return; }
    mode = owner.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '';
    if(!mode){ return; }
    sections = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-section]', card);
    for(i=0;i<sections.length;i++){
      if((sections[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '') === mode || sections[i].contains(target)){
        show(sections[i]);
      } else {
        try{ sections[i].style.display = 'none'; sections[i].setAttribute('hidden','hidden'); sections[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden','true'); }catch(e){}
      }
    }
    btns = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-btn], [data-mle-v83-mode], [data-mle-v84-mode], [data-mle-v86-mode]', card);
    for(i=0;i<btns.length;i++){
      active = (btns[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-btn') || btns[i].getAttribute('data-mle-v83-mode') || btns[i].getAttribute('data-mle-v84-mode') || btns[i].getAttribute('data-mle-v86-mode') || '') === mode;
      btns[i].setAttribute('aria-selected', active ? 'true' : 'false');
      btns[i].setAttribute('tabindex', active ? '0' : '-1');
      if(active && btns[i].className.indexOf('is-active') === -1){ btns[i].className += ' is-active'; }
      if(!active){ btns[i].className = String(btns[i].className).replace(/\s?is-active/g,''); }
    }
  }
  function focusTarget(target){
    if(!target){ return; }
    try{ target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); }catch(e){ try{ target.scrollIntoView(true); }catch(ignore){} }
    try{ if(!target.getAttribute('tabindex')){ target.setAttribute('tabindex','-1'); } target.focus({preventScroll:true}); }catch(e2){ try{ target.focus(); }catch(ignore2){} }
    try{ target.classList.add('mle-action-jump-target'); setTimeout(function(){ target.classList.remove('mle-action-jump-target'); }, 2200); }catch(e3){}
  }
  window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource = function(source){
    var card = null, btn = null, target;
    if(source && source.getAttribute && (source.tagName || source.nodeType === 1)){
      if((source.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '') || (source.className && String(source.className).indexOf('mle-advisory-card') !== -1)){ card = source; }
      else { btn = source; card = closest(source, '.mle-advisory-card') || closest(source, '.mle-lottery-outer'); }
    }
    if(!card && source && source.nodeType === 1){ card = closest(source, '.mle-advisory-card') || closest(source, '.mle-lottery-outer'); }
    if(!card){ return false; }
    openCard(card);
    target = targetFromButton(btn, card);
    if(!target){ return false; }
    revealCardMode(card, target);
    show(target);
    openDetailsParents(target);
    if(target.tagName && target.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'details'){ target.open = true; }
    qsa('details', target).forEach(function(d){ d.open = true; show(d); });
    focusTarget(target);
    return false;
  };
})();

(function(){
  if (window.__mleActionJumpV30Bound) { return; }
  window.__mleActionJumpV30Bound = true;
  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var el = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('.mle-action-jump') : null;
