    if (!el) { return; }
    if (typeof window.mleActionJump === 'function') {
      var ok = window.mleActionJump(el);
      if (ok === false) { evt.preventDefault(); }
    }
  }, true);
})();


(function(){
  'use strict';
  function closest(el, sel){while(el && el.nodeType===1){if(el.matches && el.matches(sel)){return el;}el=el.parentElement;}return null;}
  function byId(id){id=String(id||'').replace(/^#/,'');return id?document.getElementById(id):null;}
  function openLotteryCardFrom(el){
    var card = closest(el, '.mle-advisory-card');
    if(!card){return null;}
    var body = card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body, .mle-lottery-card-body, .mle-card-body');
    var toggle = card.querySelector('.mle-lottery-toggle, [aria-controls]');
    if(body){
      body.style.display='block';
      body.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
      if(toggle){toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');}
    }
    return card;
  }
  function revealTarget(btn){
    var targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-open-details') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
    var target = byId(targetId);
    var card;
    var modeSection;
    var modeName;
    var sections;
    var i;
    if(!target){return false;}
    card = openLotteryCardFrom(btn);
    if(card && target.closest){
      modeSection = target.closest('[data-mle-card-mode-section]');
      if(modeSection && modeSection.getAttribute){
        modeName = modeSection.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '';
        if(modeName !== ''){
          sections = card.querySelectorAll ? card.querySelectorAll('[data-mle-card-mode-section]') : [];
          for(i=0;i<sections.length;i++){
            if((sections[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '') === modeName){
              sections[i].style.display = '';
              sections[i].removeAttribute('hidden');
              sections[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
            }else if(!sections[i].contains(target)){
              sections[i].style.display = 'none';
              sections[i].setAttribute('hidden','hidden');
              sections[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    if(target.tagName && target.tagName.toLowerCase()==='details'){
      target.open = true;
    }
    var parentDetails = target.closest ? target.closest('details') : null;
    while(parentDetails){parentDetails.open=true;parentDetails.removeAttribute('hidden');parentDetails.style.display='';parentDetails.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');parentDetails=parentDetails.parentElement ? parentDetails.parentElement.closest('details') : null;}
    if(target.style){
      target.style.display='';
      target.removeAttribute('hidden');
      target.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
    }
    setTimeout(function(){
      try{target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'});}catch(_){target.scrollIntoView(true);}
      target.classList.add('mle-action-target-flash');
      setTimeout(function(){target.classList.remove('mle-action-target-flash');}, 1500);
    }, 60);
    return true;
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var btn = closest(evt.target, '.mle-section-shortcut-btn[data-open-details], .mle-section-shortcut-btn[data-target-panel], .mle-print-pending-btn');
    if(!btn){return;}
    if(btn.classList.contains('mle-print-pending-btn') || btn.getAttribute('data-mle-print-pending')==='1'){
      evt.preventDefault();
      if(evt.stopPropagation){evt.stopPropagation();}
      if(evt.stopImmediatePropagation){evt.stopImmediatePropagation();}
      var cardForPrint = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card');
      if(window.mlePrintPendingBatchOnly && cardForPrint){
        window.mlePrintPendingBatchOnly(cardForPrint);
        return;
      }
      var source = closest(btn, '.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown');
      if(source){source.open = true;}
      return;
    }
    if(btn.getAttribute('data-open-details') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-section')){
      var targetId = String(btn.getAttribute('data-open-details') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '');
      if ((btn.getAttribute('data-mle-pending-source-button') === '1' || targetId.indexOf('mle-pending-predictions-') === 0 || /pending/i.test(targetId)) && window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource) {
        evt.preventDefault();
        if(evt.stopPropagation){evt.stopPropagation();}
        if(evt.stopImmediatePropagation){evt.stopImmediatePropagation();}
        window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource(btn);
        return;
      }
      evt.preventDefault();
      revealTarget(btn);
    }
  }, true);
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV63SingleRunDecisionPanel) { return; }
  window.__mleV63SingleRunDecisionPanel = true;

  function qs(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector(sel); }
  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function closest(el, sel){ return el && el.closest ? el.closest(sel) : null; }
  function text(el){ return (el && el.textContent ? el.textContent : '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim(); }
  function intFrom(s){ var m = String(s || '').match(/(\d+)/); return m ? parseInt(m[1], 10) : 0; }

  function decodeB64(v){
    try { return v ? atob(v) : ''; } catch (_) { return ''; }
  }

  function cardSkaiUrl(card){
    if (!card || !card.getAttribute) { return ''; }
    var b64 = card.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url-b64') || '';
    var decoded = decodeB64(b64);
    if (decoded && decoded.indexOf('skai-lottery-prediction') !== -1) { return decoded; }
    var direct = card.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || card.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || '';
    if (direct && direct !== '#' && direct.indexOf('skai-lottery-prediction') !== -1) { return direct; }
    var a = qs('a[href*="skai-lottery-prediction"]', card);
    if (a && a.getAttribute('href') && a.getAttribute('href') !== '#') { return a.getAttribute('href'); }
    return '';
  }

  function pendingCount(card){
    var p = text(qs('.mle-adv-stat-chip--pending .mle-adv-stat-value', card)) || text(qs('.mle-scan-pill--pending strong', card)) || text(card);
    var m = p.match(/(\d+)\s*pending/i);
    return m ? parseInt(m[1], 10) : 0;
  }

  function batchForm(card){
    var forms = qsa('form', card);
    for (var i = 0; i < forms.length; i++) {
      var v = (qs('input[name="mle_action"]', forms[i]) || {}).value || '';
      if (/create_skai_batch|create.*batch|skai_batch|precision.*batch|horizon.*batch/i.test(v)) { return forms[i]; }
      if (forms[i].className && /skai-batch|batch-test|next-settings/i.test(String(forms[i].className))) { return forms[i]; }
    }
    return null;
  }

  function hasFocusBatch(card){
    
    return !!(
      batchForm(card) ||
      qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', card) ||
      qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"]', card) ||
      qs('.mle-open-skai-precision-batch', card)
    );
  }

  function openCard(card){
    if (!card) { return; }
    card.classList.remove('is-collapsed', 'mle-is-collapsed');
    card.classList.add('is-expanded', 'mle-is-expanded');
    var body = qs('.mle-advisory-card__body', card);
    if (body) { body.style.display = ''; body.removeAttribute('hidden'); }
    var details = qs('details.mle-compact-group--action, details.mle-compact-group--progress', card);
    if (details) { details.open = true; }
  }

  function scrollTo(el){
    if (!el) { return; }
    try { el.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); } catch (_) { el.scrollIntoView(true); }
    el.classList.add('mle-flash-target');
    setTimeout(function(){ el.classList.remove('mle-flash-target'); }, 1600);
  }

  function reviewPending(card){
    if (window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource) { return window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource(card); }
    return false;
  }

  function submitFocusBatch(card){
    var openBtn = qs('.mle-open-skai-precision-batch', card);
    var f = qs('form.mle-next-settings-run__form', card);
    var createActionInput;
    var btn;
    var lockedAt;
    if (!f) {
      createActionInput = qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', card);
      f = createActionInput ? closest(createActionInput, 'form') : null;
    }
    if (!f) {
      var explicitSubmit = qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"]', card);
      f = explicitSubmit ? closest(explicitSubmit, 'form') : null;
    }
    if (openBtn) { openBtn.click(); return true; }
    if (!f) { f = batchForm(card); }
    if (!f) { return false; }
    if (f.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked') === '1') {
      lockedAt = parseInt(String(f.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked-at') || '0'), 10);
      if (!lockedAt || isNaN(lockedAt) || (Date.now() - lockedAt) > 15000) {
        f.removeAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked');
        f.removeAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked-at');
      } else {
        return true;
      }
    }
    btn = qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"], button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]', f);
    if (typeof f.requestSubmit === 'function') {
      if (btn && btn.tagName && /^(button|input)$/i.test(btn.tagName) && /^(submit|image)$/i.test((btn.getAttribute('type') || '').toLowerCase())) { f.requestSubmit(btn); } else { f.requestSubmit(); }
    } else if (btn) { btn.click(); }
    else { f.submit(); }
    return true;
  }

  function makeLink(label, url, cls){
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    a.className = cls || 'mle-v37-btn';
    a.textContent = label;
    a.href = url || '#';
    a.setAttribute('data-mle-v63-skai-link', '1');
    if (url) { a.target = '_blank'; a.rel = 'noopener noreferrer'; }
    if (/9-?Batch|9-Run/i.test(label || '')) { a.setAttribute('data-mle-confirm', 'skai-batch-open-new-window'); }
    return a;
  }

  function applySkaiMeta(el, card){
    if (!el || !card || !card.getAttribute) { return el; }
    ['game-id','st','stn','gm'].forEach(function(name){
      var value = card.getAttribute('data-' + name) || '';
      if (value) { el.setAttribute('data-' + name, value); }
    });
    return el;
  }

  function makeButton(label, cls){
    var b = document.createElement('button');
    b.type = 'button';
    b.className = cls || 'mle-v37-btn';
    b.textContent = label;
    return b;
  }

  function buildRunPanel(card){
    if (!card) { return; }
    
    qsa('.mle-v37-run-panel', card).forEach(function(panel){ panel.parentNode && panel.parentNode.removeChild(panel); });

    var p = pendingCount(card);
    var url = cardSkaiUrl(card);
    var ready = hasFocusBatch(card) && p <= 0;

    var panel = document.createElement('section');
    panel.className = 'mle-v37-run-panel mle-v63-run-panel';
    panel.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Choose your next run');

    var recTitle = 'Build Regular SKAI Evidence';
    var recBody = 'Use this only while the lottery is still building evidence. It is not the History Window or Settings Precision narrowing phase yet.';
    var recNote = 'After this evidence-building batch is scored, LottoExpert will decide whether the next step is History Window narrowing or Settings Precision.';
    var recButton = 'Open SKAI Global-Learning 9-Batch';
    var mode = 'regular';

    if (p > 0) {
      recTitle = 'Batch already in progress';
      recBody = p + ' pending run' + (p === 1 ? ' is' : 's are') + ' already waiting for the next official draw result. Do not start another batch until these are scored.';
      recNote = 'Current action is already complete. Wait for the draw, then score the pending runs.';
      recButton = 'Review Pending Runs';
      mode = 'pending';
    } else if (ready) {
      recTitle = 'MyLottoExpert Controlled Narrowing Batch';
      recBody = 'Use this only when LottoExpert has prepared a History Window or Settings Precision batch. Run 1 is the control; runs 2-9 test the recommended range.';
      recNote = 'This is the predetermined MyLottoExpert narrowing batch. It is different from the regular SKAI evidence-building 9-batch.';
      recButton = 'Create 9-Run Batch and Open New Window';
      mode = 'focus';
    }

    panel.innerHTML = '<div class="mle-v37-run-panel__head"><div><span class="mle-v37-run-panel__eyebrow">Choose your next run</span><h4>Recommended batch path and best-known single prediction</h4><p>The 9-run batch is the strongest learning path. The single prediction uses the best global settings currently known for this exact lottery, but it gives less comparison evidence than a batch.</p></div></div><div class="mle-v37-run-options"><article class="mle-v37-run-option mle-v37-run-option--recommended"><span class="mle-v37-run-badge">Recommended</span><strong></strong><p></p><div class="mle-v37-run-actions"></div><div class="mle-v37-run-note"></div></article><article class="mle-v37-run-option"><span class="mle-v37-run-badge">Optional</span><strong>Best Global Settings Single SKAI Prediction</strong><p>Use this when you want one quick prediction. SKAI will apply the best known global settings for this lottery before the single run.</p><div class="mle-v37-run-actions"></div><div class="mle-v37-run-note">If LottoExpert recommends a 9-run batch, the batch remains better for learning because it compares bracketed settings against the same draw.</div></article></div>';

    if (mode === 'pending') {
      qs('.mle-v37-run-option--recommended', panel).classList.add('mle-v37-run-option--pending');
    }
    qs('.mle-v37-run-option--recommended strong', panel).textContent = recTitle;
    qs('.mle-v37-run-option--recommended p', panel).textContent = recBody;
    qs('.mle-v37-run-option--recommended .mle-v37-run-note', panel).textContent = recNote;

    var recActions = qs('.mle-v37-run-option--recommended .mle-v37-run-actions', panel);
    if (mode === 'pending') {
      var rb = makeButton('Review Pending Runs', 'mle-v37-btn mle-v37-btn--primary');
      rb.addEventListener('click', function(){ reviewPending(card); });
      recActions.appendChild(rb);
    } else if (mode === 'focus') {
      var fb = makeButton(recButton, 'mle-v37-btn mle-v37-btn--primary mle-v90-approval-cta');
      fb.addEventListener('click', function(){ if (!submitFocusBatch(card)) { reviewPending(card); } });
      recActions.appendChild(fb);
      if (url) { recActions.appendChild(applySkaiMeta(makeLink('Open SKAI Global-Learning 9-Batch Instead', url, 'mle-v37-btn mle-v37-btn--secondary'), card)); }
    } else {
      recActions.appendChild(applySkaiMeta(makeLink(recButton, url, 'mle-v37-btn mle-v37-btn--primary mle-v90-approval-cta'), card));
    }

    var singleActions = qs('.mle-v37-run-option:not(.mle-v37-run-option--recommended) .mle-v37-run-actions', panel);
    singleActions.appendChild(applySkaiMeta(makeLink('Open Best Settings Single SKAI Prediction', url, 'mle-v37-btn mle-v37-btn--secondary mle-v63-single-link'), card));

    var anchor = qs('.mle-v33-command', card) || qs('.mle-v34-priority-stack', card) || qs('.mle-card-next-guide', card) || qs('.mle-advisory-card__body', card);
    if (!anchor) { return; }
    if (anchor.classList && anchor.classList.contains('mle-v33-command')) { anchor.parentNode.insertBefore(panel, anchor.nextSibling); }
    else { anchor.parentNode.insertBefore(panel, anchor); }
  }

  function apply(){
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(function(card){
      buildRunPanel(card);
      var url = cardSkaiUrl(card);
      if (url) {
        qsa('a[data-mle-v37-single], a[data-mle-v63-skai-link], a[href="#"]', card).forEach(function(a){
          if (/Open SKAI|Regular 9-Batch|Global-Learning 9-Batch|Single SKAI|Best Settings Single|Run new predictions|Run new runs/i.test(text(a))) {
            a.href = url;
            a.target = '_blank';
            a.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
            a.setAttribute('data-skai-regular-url', url);
            applySkaiMeta(a, card);
          }
        });
      }
    });
  }

  
  

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ setTimeout(apply, 120); setTimeout(apply, 800); });
  } else {
    setTimeout(apply, 120); setTimeout(apply, 800);
  }
  window.mleV63FixRunChoices = apply;
})();

(function(){
  if(window.__mleV38NumberBallRenderFix){return;}
  window.__mleV38NumberBallRenderFix=true;
  function qs(sel,root){return (root||document).querySelector(sel);}
  function qsa(sel,root){return Array.prototype.slice.call((root||document).querySelectorAll(sel));}
  function closest(el,sel){return el&&el.closest?el.closest(sel):null;}
  function clean(s){return String(s||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();}
  function esc(s){return String(s||'').replace(/[&<>"']/g,function(c){return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];});}
  function cloneBallHtml(root){
    if(!root){return '';}
    var set=qs('.mle-ball-set',root);
    if(set){return set.outerHTML;}
    var list=qs('.mle-ball-list',root);
    if(list){return list.outerHTML;}
    return '';
  }
  function ballsFromTokens(tokens){
    if(!tokens||tokens.length<3){return '';}
    var html='<span class="mle-v38-ball-inline mle-ball-list" aria-label="Lottery numbers">';
    for(var i=0;i<tokens.length;i++){
      html+='<span class="mle-ball">'+esc(tokens[i])+'</span>';
    }
    html+='</span>';
    return html;
  }
  function extractDelimitedNumbers(s){
    s=String(s||'');
    if(/%|score|lift|cycle|cycles|runs|draws|date|target|window|range|from|to|thru|through|between/i.test(s)){return [];}
    var tokens=s.match(/\b\d{1,2}\b/g)||[];
    if(tokens.length<3||tokens.length>30){return [];}
    return tokens;
  }
  function replaceSimpleNumberList(el){
    if(!el||el.getAttribute('data-mle-v38-ballified')==='1'){return;}
    if(qs('.mle-ball,.mle-ball-list,.mle-v38-ball-inline',el)){return;}
    var html=el.innerHTML;
    var txt=clean(el.textContent);
    var m=txt.match(/^(.*?)(numbers?|saved numbers?|recommended numbers?|predictions?)\s*[:\-]?\s*((?:\b\d{1,2}\b[\s,;|\-]*){3,30})(.*)$/i);
    if(!m){return;}
    var nums=(m[3].match(/\b\d{1,2}\b/g)||[]);
    if(nums.length<3){return;}
    el.innerHTML='<span class="mle-v38-summary-text">'+esc(clean((m[1]||'')+(m[2]||'Numbers')+':'))+'</span>'+ballsFromTokens(nums)+(m[4]?'<span class="mle-v38-summary-text"> '+esc(clean(m[4]))+'</span>':'');
    el.setAttribute('data-mle-v38-ballified','1');
  }
  function improveAtAGlance(card){
    var command=qs('.mle-v33-command',card);
    if(!command){return;}
    var resultCard=qs('.mle-v33-card--result',command);
    if(!resultCard){return;}
    var p=qs('p',resultCard);
    if(!p||resultCard.getAttribute('data-mle-v38-result-enhanced')==='1'){return;}

    var rec=qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card',card);
    if(rec){
      var title=clean(qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__title',rec)?qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__title',rec).textContent:'Top recommendation')||'Top recommendation';
      var strong=clean(qs('strong',rec)?qs('strong',rec).textContent:'');
      var score=clean(qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__score strong',rec)?qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__score strong',rec).textContent:'');
      var ballHtml=cloneBallHtml(qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__numbers',rec)||rec);
      var note=clean(qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card p',rec)?qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card p',rec).textContent:'');
      var out='<span class="mle-v38-summary-text"><strong>'+esc(title)+'</strong>'+(strong?' \u2014 '+esc(strong):'')+(score?' \u2022 Evidence '+esc(score):'')+'</span>';
      if(ballHtml){out+='<div class="mle-v38-ball-preview"><span class="mle-v38-ball-preview__label">Saved numbers</span>'+ballHtml+'</div>';}
      if(note){out+='<span class="mle-v38-summary-text">'+esc(note.substring(0,180))+'</span>';}
      p.innerHTML=out;
      resultCard.setAttribute('data-mle-v38-result-enhanced','1');
      return;
    }

    var rows=qsa('.mle-visual-row,.mle-run-result-row,.mle-saved-run-row',card);
    for(var i=0;i<rows.length;i++){
      var rt=clean(rows[i].textContent);
      if(rt && /actual draw|matched|hits|scored/i.test(rt) && !/upcoming|pending/i.test(rt)){
        var lists=qsa('.mle-ball-set,.mle-ball-list',rows[i]).slice(0,2);
        if(lists.length){
          var html='<span class="mle-v38-summary-text">Previous scored result is available. Review the saved numbers and actual result below.</span>';
          for(var j=0;j<lists.length;j++){
            html+='<div class="mle-v38-ball-preview"><span class="mle-v38-ball-preview__label">'+(j===0?'Saved numbers':'Actual / comparison')+'</span>'+lists[j].outerHTML+'</div>';
          }
          p.innerHTML=html;
          resultCard.setAttribute('data-mle-v38-result-enhanced','1');
          return;
        }
      }
    }
    replaceSimpleNumberList(p);
  }
  function improvePreviousResultPanels(card){
    qsa('.mle-v34-previous-result p,.mle-recommendation-result-v32 p,.mle-loop-v32-panel p',card).forEach(replaceSimpleNumberList);
  }
  function improveSettingsNumberLists(card){
    qsa('.mle-settings-repeat p,.mle-current-lock p,.mle-strong-evidence__item p,.mle-mini-card p',card).forEach(function(el){
      if(qs('.mle-ball,.mle-ball-list,.mle-v38-ball-inline',el)){return;}
      var txt=clean(el.textContent);
      var tokens=extractDelimitedNumbers(txt);
      if(tokens.length<3){return;}
      var strong=qs('strong',el);
      if(strong){
        var label=strong.outerHTML;
        el.innerHTML=label+' '+ballsFromTokens(tokens);
        el.setAttribute('data-mle-v38-ballified','1');
      }else{
        el.innerHTML=ballsFromTokens(tokens);
        el.setAttribute('data-mle-v38-ballified','1');
      }
    });
  }
  function apply(){
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(function(card){
      improveAtAGlance(card);
      improvePreviousResultPanels(card);
      improveSettingsNumberLists(card);
    });
    qsa('.mle-pending-prediction-row__numbers,.mle-pending-recommendation-card__numbers,.mle-visual-row').forEach(function(el){
      if(qs('.mle-ball,.mle-ball-list',el)){return;}
      replaceSimpleNumberList(el);
    });
  }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){setTimeout(apply,250);setTimeout(apply,1000);});
  }else{
    setTimeout(apply,250);setTimeout(apply,1000);
  }
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    if(closest(e.target,'.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-section-toggle,summary,.mle-section-shortcut-btn,.mle-v33-modebar__btn')){setTimeout(apply,250);}
  },true);
  window.mleV38ApplyNumberBallRender=apply;
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  var key='mleBetaModalDismissedV62';
  var modal=document.getElementById('mle-beta-modal');
  if(!modal){return;}
  var panel=modal.querySelector('.mle-beta-modal__panel');
  var checkbox=document.getElementById('mle-beta-modal-dontshow');
  var previousFocus=null;
  function isDismissed(){
    try{return window.localStorage.getItem(key)==='1';}catch(e){return false;}
  }
  function dismiss(){
    if(checkbox&&checkbox.checked){try{window.localStorage.setItem(key,'1');}catch(e){}}
    modal.setAttribute('hidden','hidden');
    document.body.classList.remove('mle-beta-modal-open');
    if(previousFocus&&typeof previousFocus.focus==='function'){try{previousFocus.focus();}catch(e){}}
  }
  function openModal(){
    previousFocus=document.activeElement;
    modal.removeAttribute('hidden');
    document.body.classList.add('mle-beta-modal-open');
    window.setTimeout(function(){if(panel){panel.focus();}},30);
  }
  modal.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    if(e.target&&e.target.getAttribute('data-mle-beta-close')==='1'){dismiss();}
    var feedbackTarget=e.target&&e.target.closest?e.target.closest('[data-mle-beta-feedback="1"]'):null;
    if(feedbackTarget){
      if(checkbox){checkbox.checked=false;}
      dismiss();
      return;
    }
  });
  document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){
    if(modal.hasAttribute('hidden')){return;}
    if(e.key==='Escape'){dismiss();}
  });
  if(!isDismissed()){
    if(document.readyState==='loading'){
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){window.setTimeout(openModal,450);});
    }else{
      window.setTimeout(openModal,450);
    }
  }
})();


(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV68ActionNextHardwiredRouter) { return; }
  window.__mleV68ActionNextHardwiredRouter = true;

  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function qs(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector(sel); }
  function byId(id){
    id = String(id || '').replace(/^#/, '');
    return id ? document.getElementById(id) : null;
  }
  function closest(el, sel){ return el && el.closest ? el.closest(sel) : null; }
  function cleanText(el){ return (el && el.textContent ? el.textContent : '').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim(); }
  function low(el){ return cleanText(el).toLowerCase(); }
  function decodeB64(value){ try { return value ? atob(value) : ''; } catch(e){ return ''; } }

  function cardOf(el){ return closest(el, '.mle-advisory-card, .mle-lottery-outer, .lottery-group'); }

  function openCard(card){
    var outer;
    var group;
    var outerLid;
    var groupLid;
    if (!card) { return; }

    outer = closest(card, '.mle-lottery-outer');
    if (outer) {
      outer.classList.remove('body-collapsed', 'collapsed');
      outer.classList.add('is-expanded', 'mle-is-expanded');
      outer.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
      qsa('.mle-lottery-outer-body', outer).forEach(function(body){
        body.style.display = '';
        body.style.maxHeight = '';
        body.style.opacity = '';
        body.style.overflow = '';
        body.style.pointerEvents = '';
        body.removeAttribute('hidden');
        body.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
      });
      qsa('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle, [data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn]', outer).forEach(function(t){
        t.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
        t.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Collapse lottery section');
        if (/expand/i.test(cleanText(t))) { t.textContent = 'Collapse'; }
      });
      outerLid = outer.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id') || outer.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
      if (outerLid) { try { localStorage.setItem('mle_outer_collapsed_' + outerLid, 'false'); } catch(ignoreOuterStore) {} }
    }

    group = closest(card, '.lottery-group');
    if (group) {
      group.classList.remove('collapsed', 'body-collapsed');
      group.classList.add('is-expanded');
      group.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
      qsa('.lottery-collapse-toggle, [data-lottery-toggle-btn]', group).forEach(function(t){
        t.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
        t.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Collapse lottery section');
        if (/expand/i.test(cleanText(t))) { t.textContent = 'Collapse'; }
      });
      groupLid = group.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
      if (groupLid) { try { localStorage.setItem('lottery_collapsed_' + groupLid, 'false'); } catch(ignoreGroupStore) {} }
    }

    card.classList.remove('is-collapsed','mle-is-collapsed','body-collapsed','collapsed');
    card.classList.add('is-expanded','mle-expanded','open');
    card.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card__body, .mle-lottery-card-body, .mle-card-body, .mle-advisory-card-body', card).forEach(function(body){
      body.style.display = 'block';
      body.removeAttribute('hidden');
      body.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
    });
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card__toggle, .mle-lottery-toggle, .mle-collapse-toggle, [aria-controls]', card).forEach(function(t){
      t.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');
      if (/expand/i.test(cleanText(t))) { t.textContent = 'Collapse'; }
    });
  }

  function openAncestors(target){
    if (!target) { return; }
    var n = target;
    while (n && n !== document.body) {
      if (n.tagName && n.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'details') { n.open = true; }
      if (n.classList && (n.classList.contains('mle-compact-group') || n.classList.contains('mle-section-collapsible'))) {
        n.classList.add('is-open','open');
      }
      if (n.style && (n.style.display === 'none' || n.getAttribute('hidden') !== null || n.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'true')) {
        n.style.display = 'block';
        n.removeAttribute('hidden');
        n.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
      }
      n = n.parentElement;
    }
  }

  function flash(target){
    if (!target) { return; }
    openAncestors(target);
    setTimeout(function(){
      try { target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); } catch(e) { target.scrollIntoView(true); }
      target.classList.add('mle-action-target-flash');
      setTimeout(function(){ target.classList.remove('mle-action-target-flash'); }, 1800);
    }, 40);
  }

  function skaiUrl(card, btn){
    var url = '';
    if (btn && btn.getAttribute) {
      url = btn.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || btn.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || '';
    }
    if (!url && card && card.getAttribute) {
      url = card.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || card.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || '';
      if (!url) { url = decodeB64(card.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url-b64') || ''); }
    }
    return url || '';
  }

  function pendingTarget(card){
    return qs('.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown, [id^="mle-pending-predictions-"], .mle-pending-recommendations, .mle-visual-comparison, [id*="upcoming"], [id*="pending"]', card) || card;
  }

  function batchTarget(card){
    return qs('.mle-v37-run-panel, .mle-v63-run-panel, .mle-v32-run-panel, .mle-skai-batch-test, .mle-next-settings-run, .mle-recommended-next-settings, [id$="-next-settings-run"], [id*="next-settings-run"], [class*="next-settings"], [class*="run-panel"]', card) || null;
  }

  function explicitTarget(btn, card){
    var id = '';
    if (btn && btn.getAttribute) {
      id = btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-open-details') || '';
    }
    var target = byId(id);
    if (!target && id) {
      target = qs('#' + id.replace(/([ !"#$%&'()*+,./:;<=>?@[\\]^`{|}~])/g, '\\$1'), card || document);
    }
    return target || null;
  }

  function stateFor(btn, card){
    var targetMode = (btn.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '').toLowerCase();
    if (targetMode === 'pending') { return 'pending'; }
    if (targetMode === 'precision_batch' || targetMode === 'next_settings' || targetMode === 'settings_batch' || targetMode === 'horizon_batch' || targetMode === 'regular_skai_batch' || targetMode === 'regular_skai' || targetMode === 'history_window_check' || targetMode === 'prediction_9_batch') { return 'action'; }
    if (targetMode === 'focus' || targetMode === 'learning') { return 'next'; }
    var classText = ' ' + ((btn && btn.className) ? String(btn.className) : '') + ' ';
    if (/mle-action-button-state--in-progress|mle-adv-meta-item--in-progress|mle-scan-pill--in-progress|mle-scan-pill--pending/.test(classText)) { return 'pending'; }
    if (/mle-action-button-state--urgent-batch|mle-action-button-state--action|mle-action-button-state--action-needed|mle-adv-meta-item--action-needed/.test(classText)) { return 'action'; }
    var txt = (low(btn) + ' ' + (btn.getAttribute('aria-label') || '').toLowerCase() + ' ' + low(qs('.mle-adv-stat-chip--pending', card)) + ' ' + low(qs('.mle-pending-recommendations', card)));
    if (/\b[1-9][0-9]*\s+pending\b/.test(txt) || /in progress|waiting for draw/.test(txt)) { return 'pending'; }
    if (/run new predictions|run new runs|regular 9-batch|9-run|9 batch|create recommended|create focus|recommended next|action|open skai/.test(txt)) { return 'action'; }
    return 'next';
  }

  function applyState(btn){
    var card = cardOf(btn);
    if (!card) { return; }
    var state = stateFor(btn, card);
    btn.setAttribute('data-mle-action-state', state);
    btn.setAttribute('role', btn.tagName && btn.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'button' ? 'button' : 'button');
    btn.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
    if (btn.tagName && btn.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'button') { btn.setAttribute('type','button'); }
    btn.classList.remove('mle-v68-action-pending','mle-v68-action-action','mle-v68-action-next');
    btn.classList.add(state === 'pending' ? 'mle-v68-action-pending' : (state === 'action' ? 'mle-v68-action-action' : 'mle-v68-action-next'));
  }

  function candidates(){
    return qsa('.mle-advisory-card .mle-v38-primary-action, .mle-advisory-card .mle-status-action-jump, .mle-advisory-card .mle-scan-pill--clickable, .mle-advisory-card .mle-adv-meta-item--action-needed, .mle-advisory-card .mle-adv-meta-item--in-progress');
  }

  function refresh(){ candidates().forEach(applyState); }

  function findActionControl(from){
    return closest(from, '.mle-advisory-card .mle-v38-primary-action, .mle-advisory-card .mle-status-action-jump, .mle-advisory-card .mle-scan-pill--clickable, .mle-advisory-card .mle-adv-meta-item--action-needed, .mle-advisory-card .mle-adv-meta-item--in-progress');
  }

  function ensureHiddenInput(form, name, value){
    var input;
    if (!form || !name) { return null; }
    input = qs('input[name="' + name + '"]', form);
    if (!input) {
      input = document.createElement('input');
      input.type = 'hidden';
      input.name = name;
      form.appendChild(input);
    }
    input.value = value;
    return input;
  }

  function submitActionBatchForm(card, btn, mode){
    var target = explicitTarget(btn, card);
    var f = null;
    var actionInput = null;
    var submitBtn = null;

    if (target) { openAncestors(target); }

    if (mode === 'horizon_batch') {
      f = qs('form.mle-v38-batch-action-form[data-mle-v38-batch-action-form="horizon"]', card);
    }

    if (mode === 'settings_batch') {
      f = qs('form.mle-v38-batch-action-form[data-mle-v38-batch-action-form="settings"]', card);
    }

    if (mode === 'next_settings') {
      f = qs('.mle-next-settings-run__form', card);
    }

    if (mode === 'regular_skai_batch' || mode === 'regular_skai') {
      f = qs('form.mle-regular-batch-action-form, form[data-mle-v38-batch-action-form="regular"]', card);
      if (!f) {
        actionInput = qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', card);
        if (actionInput && actionInput.form && qs('input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular_9_batch"], input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular"], input[name="mle_batch_plan"][value="regular_skai_batch"]', actionInput.form)) {
          f = actionInput.form;
        }
      }
    }

    if (!f && target) {
      actionInput = qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', target);
      f = actionInput ? closest(actionInput, 'form') : null;
    }

    if (!f) {
      actionInput = qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', card);
      f = actionInput ? closest(actionInput, 'form') : null;
    }

    if (!f) {
      if (target) { flash(target); return true; }
      return false;
    }

    if (mode === 'next_settings' || mode === 'settings_batch') {
      ensureHiddenInput(f, 'mle_batch_plan', 'settings');
    }
    if (mode === 'next_settings') {
      ensureHiddenInput(f, 'mle_force_next_batch', '1');
    }
    if (mode === 'horizon_batch') {
      ensureHiddenInput(f, 'mle_batch_plan', 'horizon');
    }
    if (mode === 'regular_skai_batch' || mode === 'regular_skai') {
      ensureHiddenInput(f, 'mle_batch_plan', 'regular_9_batch');
      ensureHiddenInput(f, 'mle_batch_phase', 'regular');
    }

    f.setAttribute('data-mle-v121-action-submit', '1');
    submitBtn = qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"], button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]', f);
    if (typeof f.requestSubmit === 'function') {
      if (submitBtn && submitBtn.tagName && /^(button|input)$/i.test(submitBtn.tagName) && /^(submit|image)$/i.test((submitBtn.getAttribute('type') || '').toLowerCase())) {
        f.requestSubmit(submitBtn);
      } else {
        f.requestSubmit();
      }
    } else if (submitBtn) {
      submitBtn.click();
    } else {
      f.submit();
    }
    return true;
  }

  function openReadyPhaseBatch(card, mode){
    var phase = mode === 'horizon_ready_batch' ? 'horizon' : 'settings';
    var link = null;
    var target = null;
    if (!card) { return false; }
    link = qs('.mle-open-skai-precision-batch[data-batch-phase="' + phase + '"]', card);
    if (!link) {
      target = qs('.mle-mini-card[data-batch-phase="' + phase + '"]', card);
      if (target) { flash(target); return true; }
      target = batchTarget(card);
      if (target) { flash(target); return true; }
      return false;
    }
    try { link.focus(); } catch(e) {}
    if (link.click) { link.click(); return true; }
    if (link.href) { return openSkaiInNewWindow(link.href); }
    return false;
  }

  function confirmRegularSkaiBatchOpen(){
    return window.confirm('Open SKAI 9-Run Batch in a New Window?\n\nThis will open SKAI in a new browser tab/window for this lottery so you can run the recommended 9-batch path.\n\nContinue only if you are ready to leave this dashboard card and run the SKAI batch.');
  }

  function openSkaiInNewWindow(url){
    if (!url) { return false; }
    var opened = null;
    try {
      opened = window.open(url, '_blank');
      if (opened) { try { opened.opener = null; } catch(ignore) {} }
    } catch(e) { opened = null; }
    if (!opened) {
      if (window.alert) { window.alert('SKAI could not open in a new tab/window. Please allow pop-ups for LottoExpert and try again.'); }
      return false;
    }
    return true;
  }

  function route(btn, evt){
    var card = cardOf(btn);
    if (!card) { return false; }
    if (evt) {
      evt.preventDefault();
      evt.stopPropagation();
      if (evt.stopImmediatePropagation) { evt.stopImmediatePropagation(); }
    }
    applyState(btn);
    openCard(card);
    var state = btn.getAttribute('data-mle-action-state') || stateFor(btn, card);
    var mode = (btn.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '').toLowerCase();
    var target = explicitTarget(btn, card);
    if (state === 'action' && mode === 'history_window_check') {
      var readyHorizonUrl = btn.getAttribute('data-ready-horizon-skai-url') || '';
      if (readyHorizonUrl) { return openSkaiInNewWindow(readyHorizonUrl); }
    }
    if (state === 'action' && mode === 'prediction_9_batch') {
      var readySettingsUrl = btn.getAttribute('data-ready-settings-skai-url') || '';
      if (readySettingsUrl) { return openSkaiInNewWindow(readySettingsUrl); }
    }
    if (state === 'action' && /^(horizon_ready_batch|settings_ready_batch)$/.test(mode)) {
      if (openReadyPhaseBatch(card, mode)) { return true; }
    }
    if (state === 'action' && mode === 'history_window_check') {
      if (qs('.mle-open-skai-precision-batch[data-batch-phase="horizon"]', card)) {
        if (openReadyPhaseBatch(card, 'horizon_ready_batch')) { return true; }
      }
      if (submitActionBatchForm(card, btn, 'horizon_batch')) { return true; }
    }
    if (state === 'action' && mode === 'prediction_9_batch') {
      if (qs('.mle-open-skai-precision-batch[data-batch-phase="settings"]', card)) {
        if (openReadyPhaseBatch(card, 'settings_ready_batch')) { return true; }
      }
      if (submitActionBatchForm(card, btn, 'settings_batch')) { return true; }
    }
    if (state === 'action' && /^(next_settings|settings_batch|horizon_batch)$/.test(mode)) {
      if (submitActionBatchForm(card, btn, mode)) { return true; }
    }
    if (state === 'action' && (mode === 'regular_skai_batch' || mode === 'regular_skai')) {
      if (submitActionBatchForm(card, btn, mode)) { return true; }
      if (window.alert) { window.alert('The tracked 9-run batch form is missing. Please refresh and try again.'); }
      return true;
    }
    if (state === 'pending') {
      flash(target || pendingTarget(card));
      return true;
    }
    if (target) {
      flash(target);
      return true;
    }
    target = batchTarget(card);
    if (target) {
      flash(target);
      return true;
    }
    var url = skaiUrl(card, btn);
    if (url) {
      return openSkaiInNewWindow(url);
    }
    flash(card);
    return true;
  }

  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var btn = findActionControl(evt.target);
    if (!btn) { return; }
    route(btn, evt);
  }, true);

  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(evt){
    if (evt.key !== 'Enter' && evt.key !== ' ') { return; }
    var btn = findActionControl(evt.target);
    if (!btn) { return; }
    route(btn, evt);
  }, true);

  window.mleV68RefreshActionNext = refresh;
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', refresh);
  if (document.readyState !== 'loading') { refresh(); }

  setTimeout(refresh, 1200);

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if(window.__mlePrintManifestLockV1){return;}
  window.__mlePrintManifestLockV1=true;
  function qsa(s,r){return Array.prototype.slice.call((r||document).querySelectorAll(s));}
  function qs(s,r){return (r||document).querySelector(s);}
  function clean(s){return String(s||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');}
  function txt(el){return clean(el && (el.textContent || el.innerText) ? (el.textContent || el.innerText) : '');}
  function csv(s){return clean(s).split(',').map(function(x){return clean(x);}).filter(Boolean);}
  function attr(row,name){return clean(row && row.getAttribute ? row.getAttribute(name) : '');}
  function tokenName(){
    var inputs=qsa('input[type="hidden"][name]');
    for(var i=0;i<inputs.length;i++){
      var n=inputs[i].getAttribute('name')||'';
      var v=inputs[i].getAttribute('value')||'';
      if(n && n!=='mle_action' && n!=='lottery_id' && v==='1'){return n;}
    }
    return '';
  }
  function endpoint(){return String(window.location.href||'').split('#')[0];}
  function encode(obj){var p=[];for(var k in obj){if(obj.hasOwnProperty(k)){p.push(encodeURIComponent(k)+'='+encodeURIComponent(obj[k]===undefined||obj[k]===null?'':String(obj[k])));}}return p.join('&');}
  function post(action,data,sync){
    data=data||{};data.mle_action=action;var t=tokenName();if(t){data[t]='1';}
    try{
      var x=new XMLHttpRequest();
      x.open('POST',endpoint(),sync===true?false:true);
      x.setRequestHeader('Content-Type','application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8');
      x.send(encode(data));
      if(sync===true){return JSON.parse(x.responseText||'{}');}
      return null;
    }catch(e){return null;}
  }
  function numbersFrom(node){
    var nums=[]; if(!node){return nums;}
    qsa('.mle-ball,.mle-v102-ball,.mle-v104-ball,.prc-num',node).forEach(function(ball){
      var m=clean(ball.getAttribute('data-number')||txt(ball)).match(/\d+/); if(m){nums.push(m[0]);}
    });
    if(nums.length){return nums;}
    var raw=txt(node).match(/\b\d{1,3}\b/g); return raw?raw.slice(0,30):[];
  }
  function rowNumbers(row){
    var main=csv(attr(row,'data-mle-visual-predicted-main'));
    var extra=csv(attr(row,'data-mle-visual-predicted-extra'));
    if(!main.length){
      var nbox=qs('.mle-pending-prediction-row__numbers',row)||qs('.mle-visual-row__balls',row)||row;
      var all=numbersFrom(nbox);
      main=all;
    }
    return {main:main,extra:extra};
  }
  function fingerprint(row){var n=rowNumbers(row);return n.main.join('-')+'|'+n.extra.join('-');}
  function rowPayload(row,idx){
    var nums=rowNumbers(row);
    return {
      index:idx,
      source_record_id:attr(row,'data-mle-source-record-id')||attr(row,'data-mle-saved-id'),
      saved_id:attr(row,'data-mle-saved-id'),
      run_uuid:attr(row,'data-mle-run-uuid'),
      snapshot_run_uuid:attr(row,'data-mle-snapshot-run-uuid'),
      run_identity_key:attr(row,'data-mle-run-identity-key'),
      batch_uuid:attr(row,'data-mle-batch-uuid'),
      batch_index:attr(row,'data-mle-batch-index'),
      batch_total:attr(row,'data-mle-batch-total'),
      prediction_target_id:attr(row,'data-mle-prediction-target-id'),
      prediction_target_key:attr(row,'data-mle-prediction-target-key'),
      analysis_method_key:attr(row,'data-mle-analysis-method-key'),
      origin_source:attr(row,'data-mle-origin-source'),
      source:attr(row,'data-mle-source'),
      predicted_main:nums.main,
      predicted_extra:nums.extra,
      fingerprint:nums.main.join('-')+'|'+nums.extra.join('-'),
      label:txt(qs('.mle-pending-prediction-row__head strong,.mle-visual-row__meta small',row)),
      method_label:txt(qs('.mle-pending-prediction-row__head small,.mle-visual-row__meta span',row))
    };
  }
  function bestValue(rows,key){for(var i=0;i<rows.length;i++){var v=clean(rows[i][key]||'');if(v){return v;}}return '';}
  function simpleHash(s){var h=2166136261;for(var i=0;i<s.length;i++){h^=s.charCodeAt(i);h+=(h<<1)+(h<<4)+(h<<7)+(h<<8)+(h<<24);}return 'mle_'+('00000000'+(h>>>0).toString(16)).slice(-8)+'_'+String(s.length);}
  function buildManifest(card,rows,mode,title){
    var r=[]; for(var i=0;i<rows.length;i++){r.push(rowPayload(rows[i],i));}
    var lotteryId=attr(card,'data-lottery-id');
    var gameId=attr(card,'data-game-id');
    var draw=txt(qs('.mle-title-next-draw strong',card)) || txt(qs('.mle-pending-recommendations__meta span:last-child',card));
    var payload={
      version:'MLE_PRINT_MANIFEST_LOCK_V1',
      mode:mode||'pending',
      title:title||'',
      lottery_id:lotteryId,
      game_id:gameId,
      target_draw_label:draw,
      printed_at:(new Date()).toISOString ? (new Date()).toISOString() : String(new Date()),
      batch_uuid:bestValue(r,'batch_uuid'),
      prediction_target_id:bestValue(r,'prediction_target_id'),
      prediction_target_key:bestValue(r,'prediction_target_key'),
      analysis_method_key:bestValue(r,'analysis_method_key'),
      rows:r
    };
    var json=JSON.stringify(payload);
    payload.manifest_hash=simpleHash(json);
    return payload;
  }
  function storageKey(card){return 'mle_print_manifest_v1_'+(attr(card,'data-lottery-id')||'0')+'_'+(attr(card,'data-game-id')||'game');}
  function saveManifest(card,rows,mode,title){
    if(mode && mode!=='pending'){return null;}
    var manifest=buildManifest(card,rows,'pending',title||'Prediction Sheet Before Draw');
    try{window.localStorage.setItem(storageKey(card),JSON.stringify(manifest));}catch(e){}
    var resp=post('save_print_manifest',{lottery_id:manifest.lottery_id,game_id:manifest.game_id,manifest_hash:manifest.manifest_hash,manifest_json:JSON.stringify(manifest)},true);
    if(resp && resp.ok){manifest.server_manifest_id=resp.manifest_id;manifest.server_manifest_hash=resp.manifest_hash||manifest.manifest_hash;try{window.localStorage.setItem(storageKey(card),JSON.stringify(manifest));}catch(e2){}}
    return manifest;
  }
  function loadLocal(card){try{var raw=window.localStorage.getItem(storageKey(card));return raw?JSON.parse(raw):null;}catch(e){return null;}}
  function getRecentManifests(card){
    var cacheKey='__mlePrintManifestRecent_'+(attr(card,'data-lottery-id')||'0')+'_'+(attr(card,'data-game-id')||'game');
    if(window[cacheKey]){return window[cacheKey];}
    var resp=post('get_print_manifest',{lottery_id:attr(card,'data-lottery-id'),game_id:attr(card,'data-game-id')},true);
    var list=(resp&&resp.ok&&resp.manifests)?resp.manifests:[];
    var local=loadLocal(card); if(local){list.unshift({id:local.server_manifest_id||0,manifest_hash:local.manifest_hash||'',manifest:local,printed_at:local.printed_at||''});}
    window[cacheKey]=list; return list;
  }
  function manifestRows(manifestWrap){var m=manifestWrap&&manifestWrap.manifest?manifestWrap.manifest:manifestWrap;return m&&m.rows?m.rows:[];}
  var MLE_MANIFEST_UNINDEXED_FALLBACK_RANK_OFFSET = 100000;
  function rowManifestEntry(row,manifestWrap){
    var rows=manifestRows(manifestWrap); if(!rows.length){return null;}
    var sid=attr(row,'data-mle-source-record-id')||attr(row,'data-mle-saved-id');
    var saved=attr(row,'data-mle-saved-id');
    var run=attr(row,'data-mle-run-uuid');
    var snap=attr(row,'data-mle-snapshot-run-uuid');
    var ident=attr(row,'data-mle-run-identity-key');
    var fp=fingerprint(row);
    for(var i=0;i<rows.length;i++){
      var r=rows[i]||{};
      if(sid && (String(r.source_record_id||'')===sid || String(r.saved_id||'')===sid)){return r;}
      if(saved && String(r.saved_id||'')===saved){return r;}
      if(run && String(r.run_uuid||'')===run){return r;}
      if(snap && String(r.snapshot_run_uuid||'')===snap){return r;}
      if(ident && String(r.run_identity_key||'')===ident){return r;}
      if(fp && String(r.fingerprint||'')===fp){return r;}
    }
    return null;
  }
  function rowMatches(row,manifestWrap){
    return !!rowManifestEntry(row, manifestWrap);
  }
  function pickManifest(card,rows){
    var list=getRecentManifests(card), best=null, bestScore=0;
    for(var i=0;i<list.length;i++){
      var score=0;
      for(var j=0;j<rows.length;j++){if(rowMatches(rows[j],list[i])){score++;}}
      if(score>bestScore){best=list[i];bestScore=score;}
    }
    if(best){best.match_count=bestScore;return best;}
    return list.length?list[0]:null;
  }
  function filterRows(card,rows){
    rows=rows||[]; var manifest=pickManifest(card,rows);
    if(!manifest || !manifestRows(manifest).length){return rows;}
    var out=[], matchedRows=[], i, entry, printedRank;
    for(i=0;i<rows.length;i++){
      entry=rowManifestEntry(rows[i],manifest);
      if(entry){
        rows[i].setAttribute('data-mle-print-verified','1');
        printedRank=parseInt(entry.index,10);
        if(isNaN(printedRank)){printedRank=MLE_MANIFEST_UNINDEXED_FALLBACK_RANK_OFFSET+i;}
        rows[i].setAttribute('data-mle-original-printed-group-number', String(printedRank + 1));
        rows[i].setAttribute('data-mle-saved-recommendation-rank', String(printedRank + 1));
        matchedRows.push({row:rows[i], manifestIndex:printedRank, fallbackIndex:i});
      } else {
        rows[i].setAttribute('data-mle-print-verified','0');
      }
    }
    matchedRows.sort(function(a,b){
      if(a.manifestIndex!==b.manifestIndex){return a.manifestIndex-b.manifestIndex;}
      return a.fallbackIndex-b.fallbackIndex;
    });
    for(i=0;i<matchedRows.length;i++){
      out.push(matchedRows[i].row);
    }
    card.setAttribute('data-mle-print-manifest-active','1');
    card.setAttribute('data-mle-print-manifest-matches',String(out.length));
    card.setAttribute('data-mle-print-manifest-hash',(manifest.manifest_hash||manifest.manifestHash||''));
    return out;
  }
  function status(card,rows){var manifest=pickManifest(card,rows||[]);return {has_manifest:!!manifest,hash:manifest?(manifest.manifest_hash||''):'',printed_at:manifest?(manifest.printed_at||''):'',row_count:manifestRows(manifest).length,match_count:manifest?(manifest.match_count||0):0};}
  window.mlePrintManifestSave=saveManifest;
  window.mlePrintManifestFilterRows=filterRows;
  window.mlePrintManifestStatus=status;
  window.mlePrintManifestBuild=buildManifest;
  window.mlePrintManifestAudit=function(){var cards=qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]');var out=[];for(var i=0;i<cards.length;i++){var rs=qsa('.mle-visual-row',cards[i]);out.push({index:i,title:txt(qs('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name',cards[i])),lottery_id:attr(cards[i],'data-lottery-id'),visual_rows:rs.length,status:status(cards[i],rs)});}if(window.console&&console.table){console.table(out);}else if(window.console){console.log(out);}return out;};
})();

  function cardName(card){return txt(qs('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name,.mle-lottery-name,.mle-card-title,h3,h4',card)) || 'This lottery';}
  function pendingCount(card){

    if(!isNaN(attr)&&attr>0){

  }
  function decodeB64(v){try{return v?atob(v):'';}catch(_){return '';}}
  function sanitizeSkaiUrl(u){
    u = clean(u || '');
    if(!u || u === '#'){ return ''; }
    if(/^\s*(javascript|data|vbscript)\s*:/i.test(u)){ return ''; }
    return u;
  }
  function skaiUrl(card){
    if(!card){return '';}
    var b64 = card.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url-b64') || '';
    var decoded = sanitizeSkaiUrl(decodeB64(b64));
    if(decoded){ return decoded; }
    var direct = sanitizeSkaiUrl(card.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || card.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || '');
    if(direct){ return direct; }
    var a = qs('a[data-skai-regular-url],a[href*="skai-lottery-prediction"],a[href]', card);
    var href = sanitizeSkaiUrl(a && a.getAttribute ? (a.getAttribute('href') || '') : '');
    if(href){ return href; }
    return sanitizeSkaiUrl(a && a.getAttribute ? (a.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || '') : '');
  }

  function batchForm(card){

      if(forms[i].className&&/skai-batch|batch-test|next-settings/i.test(String(forms[i].className))){return forms[i];}
    }
    return null;
  }

  }

  }
