  function buildCliffNotes(card,actionState){
    var progress=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-progress-label','Learning Stage');
    var settingsRange=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-settings-range','Still broad');
    var historyRange=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-history-range','25 to 1,000 draws back');
    var nextNeed=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-next-need','Keep scoring future completed draws to strengthen this lottery.');
    var reviewText=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-review-text','Runs used for advice are up to date');
    var topTarget=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-target-top','');
    var backupTarget=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-target-backup','');
    var narrowingTarget=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-target-narrowing','');
    var reviewTarget=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-target-review','');
    var drawCount=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-current-draws','0');
    var runCount=cliffAttr(card,'data-mle-cliff-current-runs','0');
    var statusLine=(actionState && actionState.pendingCount>0) ? 'Waiting for the official draw result to score the pending runs.' : 'Use these links to inspect the current recommendation and narrowing progress.';
    return '<div class="mle-v73-cliff" aria-label="Where you are now">'+
      '<div class="mle-v73-cliff__head"><span>Where You Are Now</span><strong>'+esc(progress)+'</strong></div>'+
      '<div class="mle-v73-cliff__grid">'+
        '<div><span>Precision progress</span><strong>'+esc(progress)+'</strong><small>'+esc(nextNeed)+'</small></div>'+
        '<div><span>Draw evidence</span><strong>'+esc(drawCount)+' draw cycle'+(String(drawCount)==='1'?'':'s')+'</strong><small>'+esc(runCount)+' scored run'+(String(runCount)==='1'?'':'s')+' analyzed so far.</small></div>'+
        '<div><span>Settings range</span><strong>'+esc(settingsRange)+'</strong><small>This shows the current best-supported setting range.</small></div>'+
        '<div><span>History window range</span><strong>'+esc(historyRange)+'</strong><small>'+esc(statusLine)+'</small></div>'+
      '</div>'+
      '<div class="mle-v73-cliff__links" aria-label="Recommendation path quick links">'+
        targetButton('View Top Recommendation',topTarget,'mle-v73-cliff-btn--primary')+
        targetButton('View Backup Recommendation',backupTarget,'')+
        targetButton('View Narrowing Progress',narrowingTarget,'')+
        targetButton(reviewText.indexOf('up to date')===-1 ? 'Manage Runs Used for Advice' : 'View Runs Used for Advice',reviewTarget,'')+
      '</div>'+
    '</div>';
  }
  function jumpToSection(card,targetId){
    if(!card||!targetId){return false;}
    var target=document.getElementById(targetId) || qs('#'+targetId,card);
    var mode='';
    if(target && target.getAttribute){mode=target.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section')||'';}
    if(!mode && /^mle-card-mode-/.test(targetId)){
      if(targetId.indexOf('-numbers')!==-1){mode='numbers';}
      else if(targetId.indexOf('-next-step')!==-1){mode='next-step';}
      else if(targetId.indexOf('-review-runs')!==-1){mode='review-runs';}
      else if(targetId.indexOf('-details')!==-1){mode='details';}
      else {mode='overview';}
    }
    if(mode){
      var btn=qs('[data-mle-card-mode-btn="'+mode+'"]',card);
      if(btn){try{btn.click();}catch(e){}}
    }
    if(!target){target=document.getElementById(targetId) || qs('#'+targetId,card);}
    if(target){
      var d=target.closest?target.closest('details'):null;
      while(d){d.open=true;d=d.parentElement&&d.parentElement.closest?d.parentElement.closest('details'):null;}
      try{target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'});}catch(e){try{target.scrollIntoView(true);}catch(_){} }
      if(target.classList){target.classList.add('mle-v34-flash');setTimeout(function(){target.classList.remove('mle-v34-flash');},2200);}
      return true;
    }
    return false;
  }
  function printBefore(card){
    if(window.mleV70PrintPredictionSheet){window.mleV70PrintPredictionSheet(card,'pending');return;}
    if(window.mlePrintPendingBatchOnly){window.mlePrintPendingBatchOnly(card);return;}
    reviewPending(card);setTimeout(function(){try{window.print();}catch(e){}},250);
  }
  function printAfter(card){
    if(window.mleV70PrintPredictionSheet){window.mleV70PrintPredictionSheet(card,'result');return;}
    try{window.print();}catch(e){}
  }
  function resolveActionState(card){
    var pending = pendingCount(card);
    var hasPendingGuide = !!qs('.mle-v70-guide--pending', card);
    
    if(hasPendingGuide && pending === 0){ pending = 1; }
    var scored = scoredCount(card);
    var scoreNeeded = /score needed|ready to score|draw result is available/i.test(txt(card));
    var createActionInput = qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', card);
    var createForm = qs('form.mle-next-settings-run__form', card) || (createActionInput ? closest(createActionInput,'form') : null) || batchForm(card);
    var submitBtn = createForm ? qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"],button[type="submit"],input[type="submit"]', createForm) : qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"]', card);
    var openPrecisionBtn = qs('.mle-open-skai-precision-batch', card);
    var url = skaiUrl(card);
    var demoMode = String(card.getAttribute('data-mle-demo-mode') || '0') === '1';
    var hasCreateBatchForm = !!createForm && !!createActionInput;
    var hasNineBatchSubmit = !!submitBtn;
    var hasOpenPrecisionBatchButton = !!openPrecisionBtn;
    var hasSkaiRegularUrl = !!url;
    var hasResultsReady = scored > 0;
    var canCreateFocusBatch = !demoMode && hasCreateBatchForm && hasNineBatchSubmit;
    var canOpenRegularSkai = hasSkaiRegularUrl;
    var nextActionType = 'unavailable';
    var nextActionLabel = 'Action Not Ready';
    var nextActionDescription = 'LottoExpert cannot create this batch because the batch form or lottery context is missing.';
    var fallbackReason = 'missing_batch_form_or_skai_url';
    if (pending > 0) {
      nextActionType = 'review_pending';
      nextActionLabel = 'Review Pending Runs';
      nextActionDescription = 'A prediction group is already waiting for the next draw.';
      fallbackReason = '';
    } else if (hasResultsReady) {
      nextActionType = 'review_results';
      nextActionLabel = 'Review Results';
      nextActionDescription = 'Scored evidence is ready to review.';
      fallbackReason = '';
    } else if (scoreNeeded) {
      nextActionType = 'score_runs';
      nextActionLabel = 'Score These Runs';
      nextActionDescription = 'The draw result is ready; score pending predictions now.';
      fallbackReason = '';
    } else if (canCreateFocusBatch) {
      nextActionType = 'create_focus_batch';
      nextActionLabel = 'Create Focus 9-Batch';
      nextActionDescription = 'Create the controlled 9-run batch and open SKAI.';
      fallbackReason = '';
    } else if (demoMode && canOpenRegularSkai) {
      nextActionType = 'demo_read_only';
      nextActionLabel = 'Demo Mode - View Only';
      nextActionDescription = 'Batch creation is disabled in demo mode. Open SKAI preview only.';
      fallbackReason = 'demo_mode';
    } else if (canOpenRegularSkai) {
      nextActionType = 'open_regular_skai';
      nextActionLabel = 'Open SKAI Global-Learning 9-Batch';
      nextActionDescription = 'Focus batch is not ready yet; open SKAI regular 9-batch.';
      fallbackReason = 'focus_batch_not_ready';
    } else if (demoMode) {
      nextActionType = 'demo_read_only';
      nextActionLabel = 'Demo Mode - View Only';
      nextActionDescription = 'Batch creation is disabled in demo mode.';
      fallbackReason = 'demo_mode';
    }
    return {
      pendingCount: pending,
      scoredCount: scored,
      hasPendingGuide: hasPendingGuide,
      hasCreateBatchForm: hasCreateBatchForm,
      hasNineBatchSubmit: hasNineBatchSubmit,
      hasOpenPrecisionBatchButton: hasOpenPrecisionBatchButton,
      hasSkaiRegularUrl: hasSkaiRegularUrl,
      hasResultsReady: hasResultsReady,
      hasScoreNeeded: scoreNeeded,
      canCreateFocusBatch: canCreateFocusBatch,
      canOpenRegularSkai: canOpenRegularSkai,
      nextActionType: nextActionType,
      nextActionLabel: nextActionLabel,
      nextActionDescription: nextActionDescription,
      fallbackReason: fallbackReason,
      createForm: createForm,
      submitButton: submitBtn,
      openPrecisionButton: openPrecisionBtn,
      skaiRegularUrl: url,
      isDemoMode: demoMode
    };
  }
  function debugSnapshot(card,state,extra){
    var payload = {
      cardFound: !!card,
      cardLotteryName: cardName(card),
      pendingCount: state.pendingCount,
      scoredCount: state.scoredCount,
      modeResolvedByV73: state.nextActionType,
      hasBatchAction: hasBatchAction(card),
      hasCreateBatchForm: state.hasCreateBatchForm,
      hasCreateSkaiActionInput: !!qs('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]', card),
      hasNineBatchSubmit: state.hasNineBatchSubmit,
      hasOpenPrecisionBatchButton: state.hasOpenPrecisionBatchButton,
      hasSkaiRegularUrl: state.hasSkaiRegularUrl,
      selectedFormAction: state.createForm && state.createForm.getAttribute ? (state.createForm.getAttribute('action') || '(same-page POST)') : '',
      selectedSubmitButton: state.submitButton ? (state.submitButton.tagName + (state.submitButton.className ? '.' + String(state.submitButton.className).split(/\s+/).join('.') : '')) : '',
      requestSubmitCalled: !!(extra && extra.requestSubmitCalled),
      fallbackReviewPendingCalled: !!(extra && extra.fallbackReviewPendingCalled),
      fallbackReason: (extra && extra.fallbackReason) || state.fallbackReason || ''
    };
    dbg('snapshot', payload);
    debugPanel(card, state, payload);
  }
  function openSkaiUrl(url){
    if(!url){return false;}
    try{
      var w = window.open(url,'_blank');
      if(w){ try { w.opener = null; } catch(ignore) {} return true; }
      if(window.alert){ window.alert('SKAI could not open in a new tab/window. Please allow pop-ups for LottoExpert and try again.'); }
      return false;
    }catch(_){
      if(window.alert){ window.alert('SKAI could not open in a new tab/window. Please allow pop-ups for LottoExpert and try again.'); }
    }
    return false;
  }
  function runBatch(card,actionState){
    var state = actionState || resolveActionState(card);
    var requestSubmitCalled = false;
    var fallbackReviewPendingCalled = false;
    var fallbackReason = '';
    debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:''});
    if (state.nextActionType === 'review_pending') { reviewPending(card); return; }
    if (state.nextActionType === 'review_results' || state.nextActionType === 'score_runs') { reviewPending(card); return; }
    if (state.nextActionType === 'open_regular_skai' || state.nextActionType === 'demo_read_only' || state.nextActionType === 'demo_view_only') {
      if (!openSkaiUrl(state.skaiRegularUrl)) {
        fallbackReason = 'missing_skai_url';
        showActionWarning(card,'LottoExpert cannot open SKAI because the lottery URL context is missing.');
      }
      debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:fallbackReason});
      return;
    }
    if (state.nextActionType !== 'create_focus_batch') {
      fallbackReason = state.fallbackReason || 'action_not_ready';
      showActionWarning(card,'LottoExpert cannot create this batch because the batch form or lottery context is missing.');
      debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:fallbackReason});
      return;
    }
    var f = state.createForm || batchForm(card);
    var b = state.submitButton || (f ? qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"],button[type="submit"],input[type="submit"]', f) : qs('[data-nine-batch-submit="1"]',card));
    var lockedAt;
    if (!f && state.openPrecisionButton) { state.openPrecisionButton.click(); debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:'open_precision_button'}); return; }
    if (!f) {
      fallbackReason = 'missing_create_batch_form';
      showActionWarning(card,'LottoExpert cannot create this batch because the batch form is missing in this lottery card.');
      debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:fallbackReason});
      return;
    }
    if (f.getAttribute && f.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked') === '1') {
      lockedAt = parseInt(String(f.getAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked-at') || '0'), 10);
      if (!lockedAt || isNaN(lockedAt) || (Date.now() - lockedAt) > LOCK_TIMEOUT_MS) {
        f.removeAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked');
        f.removeAttribute('data-mle-submit-locked-at');
      } else {
        fallbackReason = 'submit_lock_active';
        showActionWarning(card,'A previous 9-batch submit is still in progress. Please wait a moment and try again.');
        debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:fallbackReason});
        return;
      }
    }
    if(!b){ b = qs('button[type="submit"],input[type="submit"]',f||card); }
    if(f && typeof f.requestSubmit==='function'){
      if(b && b.tagName && /^(button|input)$/i.test(b.tagName) && /^(submit|image)$/i.test((b.getAttribute('type')||'').toLowerCase())){ f.requestSubmit(b); }
      else { f.requestSubmit(); }
      requestSubmitCalled = true;
      debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:requestSubmitCalled,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:''});
      return;
    }
    if(b){ b.click(); debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:''}); return; }
    if(openSkaiUrl(state.skaiRegularUrl)){ debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:'open_regular_skai_fallback'}); return; }
    fallbackReviewPendingCalled = true;
    fallbackReason = 'no_submit_button_no_skai_url';
    showActionWarning(card,'LottoExpert cannot create this batch because the submit control is missing.');
    reviewPending(card);
    debugSnapshot(card,state,{requestSubmitCalled:requestSubmitCalled,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:fallbackReviewPendingCalled,fallbackReason:fallbackReason});
  }
  function isPrimaryAdvisoryCard(card){
    if(!card || !card.querySelector){return false;}
    
    if(card.classList && (card.classList.contains('mle-optimizer-panel-card') || card.classList.contains('mle-optimizer-panel'))){return false;}
    if(!card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id')){return false;}
    if(!qs('.mle-advisory-card__collapsed',card)){return false;}
    if(!qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card)){return false;}
    if(!qs('.mle-lottery-toggle',card)){return false;}
    return true;
  }
  function purgeNonPrimaryPath(card){
    if(!card){return;}
    qsa('.mle-v73-path',card).forEach(function(old){if(old.parentNode){old.parentNode.removeChild(old);}});
    if(card.classList){card.classList.remove('mle-v73-active');}
  }
  function normalizePrimaryCollapseState(card){
    if(!isPrimaryAdvisoryCard(card)){return;}
    var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card);
    var btn=qs('.mle-lottery-toggle',card);
    if(!body||!btn){return;}
    var btnText=txt(btn).toLowerCase();
    var saysClosed=(btn.getAttribute('aria-expanded')==='false'||btnText.indexOf('expand')!==-1);
    var bodyClosed=(body.getAttribute('aria-hidden')==='true'||body.style.display==='none');
    if(saysClosed){
      body.style.display='none';
      body.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
      var sp=btn.querySelector('span');
      if(sp){sp.textContent='Expand';}else{btn.textContent='Expand';}
    } else if(bodyClosed){
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
      var sp2=btn.querySelector('span');
      if(sp2){sp2.textContent='Expand';}else{btn.textContent='Expand';}
    }
  }
  function build(card){
    if(!isPrimaryAdvisoryCard(card)){
      purgeNonPrimaryPath(card);
      return;
    }
    normalizePrimaryCollapseState(card);
    var body=findBody(card);if(!body){return;}
    
    var existingPaths = qsa('.mle-v73-path', card);
    existingPaths.forEach(function(path, idx){
      if(idx > 0 && path.parentNode){ path.parentNode.removeChild(path); }
    });
    existingPath = qs(':scope > .mle-v73-path', body) || qs('.mle-v73-path', body);
    if(debugEnabled()){
      var staleCount=qsa('.mle-v73-path',card).length;
      if(staleCount>1){dbg('build:stalePathsRemaining',{lottery:cardName(card),count:staleCount});}
    }
    body.classList.add('mle-v73-active');
    var existingPath = qs(':scope > .mle-v73-path', body) || qs('.mle-v73-path', body);
    var actionState = resolveActionState(card);
    var p=actionState.pendingCount, s=actionState.scoredCount, name=cardName(card), draw=drawLabel(card), mode='action';
    if(actionState.nextActionType==='review_pending'||actionState.hasPendingGuide){mode='pending';}
    else if(actionState.nextActionType==='review_results'){mode='result';}
    else if(actionState.nextActionType==='score_runs'){mode='score';}
    dbg('build:render',{lottery:name,mode:mode,nextActionType:actionState.nextActionType,pendingCount:p,hasPendingGuide:actionState.hasPendingGuide,scoredCount:s,fallbackReason:actionState.fallbackReason});
    var status='Needs Action', topTitle='Your Next Step', mainTitle='Create the prediction group', mainBody=actionState.nextActionDescription, primary=actionState.nextActionLabel;
    if(mode==='pending'){
      status='In Progress';
      topTitle='Waiting for the next draw result';
      mainTitle='No action needed right now';
      mainBody='You already created the recommended batch for this lottery. '+p+' prediction run'+(p===1?' is':'s are')+' waiting for the next official draw. After the result posts, score these runs so LottoExpert can update the evidence.';
      primary=actionState.nextActionLabel;
    } else if(mode==='result'){
      status='Results Ready';topTitle='Review the completed draw';mainTitle='Results are ready to review';mainBody='This draw has scored evidence available. Review the result sheet, compare the prediction runs, and continue the next evidence-building cycle.';primary=actionState.nextActionLabel;
    } else if(mode==='score'){
      status='Action Needed';topTitle='Score the pending predictions';mainTitle='The draw result is ready to compare';mainBody='The next step is to score the saved predictions against the official draw result so LottoExpert can update the evidence.';primary=actionState.nextActionLabel;
    } else if(actionState.nextActionType==='open_regular_skai'){
      status='Action Needed';topTitle='Your Next Step';mainTitle='Focus batch not ready yet';mainBody='Open regular SKAI 9-batch to keep building evidence until Focus batch controls are ready.';primary=actionState.nextActionLabel;
    } else if(actionState.nextActionType==='demo_read_only' || actionState.nextActionType==='demo_view_only'){
      status='Demo Mode';topTitle='Preview only';mainTitle='Batch creation is disabled';mainBody='This workspace is in demo/read-only mode. You can preview SKAI routing, but new batch creation is disabled.';primary=actionState.nextActionLabel;
    } else if(actionState.nextActionType==='unavailable'){
      status='Action Not Ready';topTitle='Action Not Ready';mainTitle='Batch controls are missing';mainBody='LottoExpert cannot create this batch because the batch form or lottery context is missing.';primary=actionState.nextActionLabel;
    }
    var stateClass=(mode==='pending'||mode==='result')?'pending':(mode==='score'?'score':'action');
    var pathRenderSeq = nextPathRenderSequence();
    var pathRenderTime = Date.now();
    var pathRenderState = (mode==='pending'?'pending':(mode==='result'?'result':(mode==='score'?'score':((actionState.nextActionType==='unavailable')?'unavailable':((actionState.nextActionType==='demo_read_only'||actionState.nextActionType==='demo_view_only')?'demo':'action')))));
    var ctaAction = mode==='pending' ? 'review' : (mode==='result' ? 'print-after' : (mode==='score' ? 'review' : (actionState.nextActionType==='create_focus_batch' ? 'run-batch' : (actionState.nextActionType==='open_regular_skai' ? 'open-skai' : ((actionState.nextActionType==='demo_read_only' || actionState.nextActionType==='demo_view_only') ? 'demo-view' : 'unavailable')))));
    var ctaClass = mode==='pending' ? 'mle-v73-btn--green' : (mode==='result' ? 'mle-v73-btn--green' : (mode==='score' ? 'mle-v73-btn--amber' : (actionState.nextActionType==='open_regular_skai' ? 'mle-v73-btn--blue' : (actionState.nextActionType==='unavailable' ? 'mle-v73-btn--soft' : ((actionState.nextActionType==='demo_read_only' || actionState.nextActionType==='demo_view_only') ? 'mle-v73-btn--soft' : 'mle-v73-btn--amber')))));
    var ctaDisabled = (actionState.nextActionType==='unavailable') ? ' aria-disabled="true"' : '';
    var warningText = actionState.nextActionType==='unavailable' ? 'LottoExpert cannot create this batch because the batch form or lottery context is missing.' : '';
    var html='<section class="mle-v73-path mle-v73-path--'+esc(stateClass)+'" aria-label="Recommendation path for '+esc(name)+'" data-mle-path-owner="V73_build" data-mle-path-render-time="'+esc(String(pathRenderTime))+'" data-mle-path-card-title="'+esc(name)+'" data-mle-path-state="'+esc(pathRenderState)+'" data-mle-path-pending-count="'+esc(String(p))+'" data-mle-path-render-sequence="'+esc(String(pathRenderSeq))+'">'+
      '<div class="mle-v73-path__top"><div><span class="mle-v73-path__eyebrow">Recommendation Path</span><h4>'+esc(topTitle)+'</h4><p>This summary replaces the repeated chooser/advice text. It tells you what has been done, where the lottery stands, and what to do next.</p></div><span class="mle-v73-pill">'+esc(primary)+'</span></div>'+
      '<div class="mle-v73-path__body"><div class="mle-v73-main"><div><span class="mle-v73-kicker">Current Status</span><h5>'+esc(mainTitle)+'</h5><p>'+esc(mainBody)+'</p>'+buildCliffNotes(card, actionState)+'</div><div class="mle-v73-main__actions">';
    if(mode==='pending'){
      html+='<button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--green" data-mle-v73-action="review">Review Pending Runs</button><button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--blue" data-mle-v73-action="print-before">Print / Reprint Sheet (Optional)</button>';
    } else if(mode==='result'){
      html+='<button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--green" data-mle-v73-action="print-after">Print Result Sheet</button><button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--soft" data-mle-v73-action="review">View Evidence</button>';
    } else if(mode==='score'){
      html+='<button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--amber" data-mle-v73-action="review">Score / Review Runs</button><button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--blue" data-mle-v73-action="print-before">Reprint Prediction Sheet</button>';
    } else {
      html+='<button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn '+esc(ctaClass)+'" data-mle-v73-action="'+esc(ctaAction)+'"'+ctaDisabled+'>'+esc(primary)+'</button><button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--soft" data-mle-v73-action="advanced">Other Run Options</button>';
    }
    html+='</div></div>'+(warningText?'<div class="mle-v73-inline-warning" data-mle-v73-warning="1">'+esc(warningText)+'</div>':'<div class="mle-v73-inline-warning" data-mle-v73-warning="1" hidden></div>')+'</div></section>';
    var renderKey = [pathRenderState, String(p), String(s), primary, topTitle, mainTitle].join('|');
    if(existingPath && existingPath.parentNode){
      if(existingPath.getAttribute('data-mle-v73-render-key') !== renderKey){
        existingPath.outerHTML = html;
        existingPath = qs(':scope > .mle-v73-path', body) || qs('.mle-v73-path', body);
        if(existingPath){ existingPath.setAttribute('data-mle-v73-render-key', renderKey); }
      }
    } else {
      body.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin',html);
      existingPath = qs(':scope > .mle-v73-path', body) || qs('.mle-v73-path', body);
      if(existingPath){ existingPath.setAttribute('data-mle-v73-render-key', renderKey); }
    }
    dbg('render',{lottery:cardName(card),actionState:actionState,pathOwner:'V73_build',pathRenderSequence:pathRenderSeq,pathRenderState:pathRenderState,pathRenderTime:pathRenderTime});
  }
  function apply(){
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(function(card){
      if(isPrimaryAdvisoryCard(card)){ build(card); }
      else { purgeNonPrimaryPath(card); }
    });
  }
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    var b=e.target&&e.target.closest?e.target.closest('[data-mle-v73-action],[data-mle-v73-jump-section]'):null;if(!b){return;}
    var card=closest(b,'.mle-advisory-card');if(!card){return;}
    e.preventDefault();e.stopPropagation();if(e.stopImmediatePropagation){e.stopImmediatePropagation();}
    var jumpTarget=b.getAttribute('data-mle-v73-jump-section');
    if(jumpTarget){jumpToSection(card,jumpTarget);return;}
    var a=b.getAttribute('data-mle-v73-action');
    var actionState = resolveActionState(card);
    debugSnapshot(card,actionState,{requestSubmitCalled:false,fallbackReviewPendingCalled:false,fallbackReason:'click:'+a});
    if(a==='review'||a==='advanced'){reviewPending(card);return;}
    if(a==='print-before'){printBefore(card);return;}
    if(a==='print-after'){printAfter(card);return;}
    if(a==='open-skai'||a==='demo-view'){
      if(!openSkaiUrl(actionState.skaiRegularUrl)){ showActionWarning(card,'LottoExpert cannot open SKAI because the lottery URL context is missing.'); }
      return;
    }
    if(a==='unavailable'){
      showActionWarning(card,'LottoExpert cannot create this batch because the batch form or lottery context is missing.');
      return;
    }
    if(a==='run-batch'){runBatch(card,actionState);return;}
  },true);
  function scheduleApply(delay){
    clearTimeout(window.__mleV73ApplyTimer);
    window.__mleV73ApplyTimer = setTimeout(apply, delay || 120);
  }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){scheduleApply(650);});
  } else {scheduleApply(650);}
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){if(e.target&&e.target.closest&&e.target.closest('.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-v34-modebar button,[data-mle-v73-action],[data-mle-v73-jump-section]')){scheduleApply(160);}},true);
  window.mleV73TopRecommendationPathRefresh=apply;
})();

(function(){
  if(window.__mleV74RemoveEmptyActionRecommendations){return;}
  window.__mleV74RemoveEmptyActionRecommendations=true;
  function qsa(s,r){return Array.prototype.slice.call((r||document).querySelectorAll(s));}
  function isVisibleNode(node){
    if(!node || node.nodeType!==1){return false;}
    if(node.classList && node.classList.contains('mle-v73-path')){return true;}
    var cs;
    try{cs=window.getComputedStyle(node);}catch(e){cs=null;}
    if(cs && (cs.display==='none' || cs.visibility==='hidden')){return false;}
    var txt=(node.textContent||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();
    if(txt.length>0){return true;}
    return !!(node.querySelector && node.querySelector('button,a,input,select,textarea,table,img,svg,canvas'));
  }
  function bodyHasMeaningfulContent(body){
    if(!body){return false;}
    var children=qsa(':scope > *', body);
    if(!children.length){return false;}
    for(var i=0;i<children.length;i++){
      if(isVisibleNode(children[i])){return true;}
    }
    return false;
  }
  function cleanupCard(card){
    qsa('details.mle-compact-group--action', card).forEach(function(group){
      var body=group.querySelector('.mle-compact-group__body');
      if(!bodyHasMeaningfulContent(body)){
        group.classList.add('mle-v74-remove-empty-action-card');
        if(group.parentNode){group.parentNode.removeChild(group);}
      }
    });
  }
  function cleanup(){qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(cleanupCard);}
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){setTimeout(cleanup,500);setTimeout(cleanup,1500);setTimeout(cleanup,3200);setTimeout(cleanup,5000);});
  } else {
    setTimeout(cleanup,500);setTimeout(cleanup,1500);setTimeout(cleanup,3200);setTimeout(cleanup,5000);
  }
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    if(e.target && e.target.closest && e.target.closest('.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-v34-modebar button,.mle-v73-btn,[data-mle-v73-action]')){
      setTimeout(cleanup,350);setTimeout(cleanup,1400);
    }
  },true);
  window.mleV74RemoveEmptyActionRecommendationsRefresh=cleanup;
})();


(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV75OnePagePredictionPrintSheet) { return; }
  window.__mleV75OnePagePredictionPrintSheet = true;

  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function qs(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector(sel); }
  function txt(el){ return (el && (el.textContent || el.innerText) ? String(el.textContent || el.innerText).replace(/\s+/g,' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'') : ''); }
  function esc(s){ return String(s == null ? '' : s).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;'); }
  function hasClass(el, cls){ return !!(el && el.className && (' ' + String(el.className) + ' ').indexOf(' ' + cls + ' ') !== -1); }
  function closest(el, sel){ while(el && el.nodeType === 1){ if(el.matches && el.matches(sel)){ return el; } el = el.parentElement; } return null; }
  function insideClass(el, cls, stop){ var n = el; while(n && n !== stop && n.nodeType === 1){ if(hasClass(n, cls)){ return true; } n = n.parentElement; } return false; }

  function cardName(card){
    return txt(qs('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name', card)) || txt(qs('h3', card)) || txt(qs('h2', card)) || 'Lottery Prediction Sheet';
  }
  function nextDraw(card){
    var selectors = ['.mle-v73-fact strong', '.mle-v70-path__summary-list span:nth-child(2)', '.mle-adv-draw-date', '.mle-draw-date'];
    for(var i=0;i<selectors.length;i++){
      var t = txt(qs(selectors[i], card));
      if(t && !/^status$/i.test(t)){ return t.replace(/^Target draw:\s*/i,'').replace(/^Target:\s*/i,''); }
    }
    var body = txt(card);
    var m = body.match(/Target draw:\s*([^\u2022\n\r]{3,40})/i);
    return m ? m[1].replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'') : 'Upcoming draw';
  }
  function pendingRows(card){
    var rows = qsa('.mle-pending-prediction-row', card);
    if(rows.length){ return rows; }
    return qsa('.mle-visual-row', card).filter(function(row){ return !!qs('.mle-visual-upcoming', row) || /upcoming|pending/i.test(txt(row)); });
  }
  function resultRows(card){
    return qsa('.mle-visual-row', card).filter(function(row){ return !qs('.mle-visual-upcoming', row); });
  }
  function ballTextList(nodes){
    var vals = [];
    for(var i=0;i<nodes.length;i++){
      var v = txt(nodes[i]).replace(/[^0-9]/g,'');
      if(v !== ''){ vals.push(v); }
    }
    return vals;
  }
  function extractBalls(row){
    var main = [];
    var extra = [];
    var mainBox = qs('.mle-ball-set__main', row);
    var extraBox = qs('.mle-ball-set__extra', row);
    if(mainBox){ main = ballTextList(qsa('.mle-ball', mainBox)); }
    if(extraBox){ extra = ballTextList(qsa('.mle-ball', extraBox)); }
    if(!main.length){
      qsa('.mle-ball', row).forEach(function(ball){
        if(insideClass(ball, 'mle-ball-set__extra', row) || insideClass(ball, 'mle-ball-list--extra', row) || hasClass(ball, 'mle-ball--extra')){ return; }
        var v = txt(ball).replace(/[^0-9]/g,'');
        if(v !== ''){ main.push(v); }
      });
    }
    if(!extra.length){
      qsa('.mle-ball-list--extra .mle-ball,.mle-ball--extra', row).forEach(function(ball){
        var v = txt(ball).replace(/[^0-9]/g,'');
        if(v !== '' && extra.indexOf(v) === -1){ extra.push(v); }
      });
    }
    if(!main.length){
      var raw = txt(qs('.mle-pending-prediction-row__numbers', row)) || txt(qs('.mle-visual-row__balls', row)) || txt(row);
      var nums = raw.match(/\d+/g) || [];
      main = nums.slice(0, 8);
    }
    return {main: main, extra: extra};
  }
  function extractRow(row, idx, mode){
    var rank = txt(qs('.mle-pending-prediction-row__rank', row)) || String(idx + 1);
    var title = txt(qs('.mle-pending-prediction-row__head strong', row)) || txt(qs('.mle-visual-row__meta strong', row)) || ('Run ' + rank);
    var settings = txt(qs('.mle-pending-prediction-row__head small', row)) || txt(qs('.mle-visual-row__meta small', row)) || txt(qs('.mle-visual-label', row)) || 'Saved prediction run';
    var score = txt(qs('.mle-pending-prediction-row__score', row));
    var result = mode === 'result' ? (txt(qs('.mle-visual-row__result', row)) || txt(qs('.mle-result-summary', row)) || '') : '';
    var balls = extractBalls(row);
    return {rank: rank, title: title, settings: settings, score: score, result: result, main: balls.main, extra: balls.extra};
  }
  function ballHtml(values, extra){
    if(!values || !values.length){ return '<span class="mle-v75-empty">Not saved</span>'; }
    var out = [];
    for(var i=0;i<values.length;i++){
      out.push('<span class="mle-v75-ball' + (extra ? ' mle-v75-ball--extra' : '') + '">' + esc(values[i]) + '</span>');
    }
    return out.join('');
  }
  function rowHtml(r){
    var extra = r.extra && r.extra.length ? '<span class="mle-v75-extra-label">Extra</span>' + ballHtml(r.extra, true) : '';
    var result = r.result ? '<div class="mle-v75-result">' + esc(r.result) + '</div>' : '';
    var score = r.score ? '<span class="mle-v75-score">' + esc(r.score) + '</span>' : '';
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="mle-v75-col-run"><strong>#' + esc(r.rank) + '</strong></td>' +
      '<td class="mle-v75-col-settings"><strong>' + esc(r.title) + '</strong><span>' + esc(r.settings) + '</span>' + score + result + '</td>' +
      '<td class="mle-v75-col-balls"><div class="mle-v75-balls">' + ballHtml(r.main, false) + extra + '</div></td>' +
    '</tr>';
  }
  function printOnePage(card, mode){
    mode = mode === 'result' ? 'result' : 'pending';
    var rowsRaw = mode === 'result' ? resultRows(card) : pendingRows(card);
    var rows = rowsRaw.map(function(row, idx){ return extractRow(row, idx, mode); });
    var title = mode === 'result' ? 'Result Sheet After Draw' : 'Prediction Sheet Before Draw';
    var name = cardName(card);
    var draw = nextDraw(card);
    var printed = (new Date()).toLocaleString ? (new Date()).toLocaleString() : String(new Date());
    var htmlRows = rows.length ? rows.map(rowHtml).join('') : '<tr><td colspan="3">No printable prediction rows were found for this lottery.</td></tr>';
    var LT = '\u003c', GT = '\u003e';
    var html = LT + '!DOCTYPE html' + GT + LT + 'html lang="en"' + GT + LT + 'head' + GT + LT + 'meta charset="UTF-8"' + GT + LT + 'title' + GT + esc(name + ' - ' + title) + LT + '/title' + GT +
      '<style>' +
      '@page{size:auto;margin:0.35in;}html,body{background:#fff;color:#111;margin:0;padding:0;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10px;line-height:1.18;}' +
      '.mle-v75-toolbar{position:sticky;top:0;background:#071a36;color:#fff;padding:8px 12px;z-index:9}.mle-v75-toolbar button{float:right;margin-left:7px;border:0;border-radius:6px;background:#1d4ed8;color:#fff;padding:6px 10px;font-weight:800;cursor:pointer}.mle-v75-toolbar .secondary{background:#475569}' +
      '.mle-v75-doc{max-width:1050px;margin:0 auto;padding:10px 12px}.mle-v75-head{display:grid;grid-template-columns:minmax(0,1fr) auto;gap:14px;align-items:start;border-bottom:2px solid #071a36;padding-bottom:7px;margin-bottom:7px}.mle-v75-kicker{font-size:9px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.12em;color:#1d4ed8;font-weight:950}.mle-v75-head h1{font-size:18px;line-height:1.1;margin:1px 0 3px;color:#071a36}.mle-v75-head p{margin:0;color:#334155;font-size:10px}.mle-v75-meta{display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(2,1fr);gap:5px;min-width:330px}.mle-v75-meta div{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:7px;padding:5px 7px;background:#f8fafc}.mle-v75-meta span{display:block;font-size:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;color:#64748b;font-weight:900}.mle-v75-meta strong{display:block;font-size:10px;color:#0f172a;white-space:nowrap}.mle-v75-note{border-left:3px solid #f59e0b;background:#fffbeb;padding:5px 8px;margin:0 0 7px;color:#334155;font-size:9px}' +
      '.mle-v75-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed}.mle-v75-table th{background:#071a36;color:#fff;text-align:left;padding:5px 6px;font-size:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em}.mle-v75-table td{border:1px solid #d7dee8;vertical-align:middle;padding:4px 6px}.mle-v75-col-run{width:38px;text-align:center}.mle-v75-col-settings{width:34%}.mle-v75-col-settings strong{display:block;font-size:10px;color:#0f172a;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis}.mle-v75-col-settings span{display:block;font-size:8.5px;color:#475569;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis}.mle-v75-score{display:inline-block!important;margin-top:2px;border:1px solid #bfdbfe;border-radius:999px;background:#eff6ff;color:#1d4ed8!important;padding:1px 5px;font-size:8px!important;font-weight:900}.mle-v75-result{font-size:8.5px;color:#166534;font-weight:800;margin-top:2px;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis}.mle-v75-balls{display:flex;align-items:center;gap:3px;flex-wrap:wrap}.mle-v75-ball{display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;width:19px;height:19px;border-radius:999px;border:1px solid #aeb9ca;background:#f8fafc;color:#0f172a;font-weight:900;font-size:9px}.mle-v75-ball--extra{background:#dc2626;border-color:#b91c1c;color:#fff}.mle-v75-extra-label{display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;border-radius:999px;background:#991b1b;color:#fff;font-size:7px;font-weight:950;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.05em;padding:3px 5px;margin-left:5px}.mle-v75-empty{font-size:9px;color:#64748b}.mle-v75-foot{margin-top:7px;color:#64748b;font-size:8.5px;text-align:center}' +
      '@media print{html,body{font-size:9px}.mle-v75-toolbar{display:none!important}.mle-v75-doc{padding:0}.mle-v75-table tr{break-inside:avoid;page-break-inside:avoid}.mle-v75-ball{width:18px;height:18px;font-size:8px}.mle-v75-head{margin-bottom:5px}.mle-v75-note{margin-bottom:5px}}' +
      LT + '/style' + GT + LT + '/head' + GT + LT + 'body' + GT +
      '<div class="mle-v75-toolbar"><strong>' + esc(title) + '</strong><button onclick="window.print()">Print</button><button class="secondary" onclick="window.close()">Close</button><div style="clear:both"></div></div>' +
      '<main class="mle-v75-doc"><header class="mle-v75-head"><div><div class="mle-v75-kicker">' + esc(title) + '</div><h1>' + esc(name) + '</h1><p>Compact one-page record of the prediction runs, settings, main balls, and extra balls.</p></div><div class="mle-v75-meta"><div><span>Target Draw</span><strong>' + esc(draw) + '</strong></div><div><span>Status</span><strong>' + esc(mode === 'result' ? 'Scored / Review' : 'Pending Before Draw') + '</strong></div><div><span>Printed</span><strong>' + esc(printed) + '</strong></div><div><span>Runs</span><strong>' + esc(String(rows.length)) + '</strong></div></div></header>' +
      '<div class="mle-v75-note">Lottery drawings are random. This sheet is a concise record of saved LottoExpert predictions for review and comparison; it is not a guarantee of winning.</div>' +
      '<table class="mle-v75-table"><thead><tr><th>Run</th><th>Settings</th><th>Predicted Numbers</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + htmlRows + '</tbody></table>' +
      '<div class="mle-v75-foot">LottoExpert prediction record - optional print or reprint as needed before and after the official draw.</div></main>' +
      
      LT + 'script' + GT + '(function(){function go(){try{window.focus();window.print();}catch(e){}} if(document.readyState==="complete"){setTimeout(go,250);}else{window.addEventListener("load",function(){setTimeout(go,250);});}}());' + LT + '/script' + GT + LT + '/body' + GT + LT + '/html' + GT;
    var w = null;
    try { w = window.open('', '_blank', 'width=1050,height=780,menubar=no,toolbar=yes,location=no,status=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes'); } catch(e) {}
    if(!w){ alert('The print window was blocked. Please allow popups for LottoExpert and try Print / Reprint (Optional) again.'); return; }
    try { w.document.open(); w.document.write(html); w.document.close(); w.focus(); } catch(e2) { try { w.close(); } catch(e3) {} }
  }

  window.mlePrintPendingBatchOnly = function(card){ printOnePage(card, 'pending'); };
  window.mleV70PrintPredictionSheet = function(card, mode){ printOnePage(card, mode === 'result' ? 'result' : 'pending'); };
  window.mleV75OnePagePredictionPrintSheet = printOnePage;

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if(window.__mleV76RestoreNarrowingEvidenceSections){return;}
  window.__mleV76RestoreNarrowingEvidenceSections=true;
  function qsa(s,r){return Array.prototype.slice.call((r||document).querySelectorAll(s));}
  function hasMeaningfulContent(el){
    if(!el){return false;}
    var text=String(el.textContent||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();
    if(text.length>12){return true;}
    return !!(el.querySelector && el.querySelector('button,a,input,select,textarea,table,img,svg,canvas,.mle-ball,.mle-precision-lock,.mle-precision-progress-v14,.mle-optimization-focus'));
  }
  function restoreCard(card){
    if(!card){return;}
    var body=card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body') || card;
    if(body){body.classList.add('mle-v77-restored-evidence');}

    qsa('.mle-v37-run-panel,.mle-v63-run-panel,.mle-v34-priority-stack,.mle-v70-guide,.mle-lottery-command-hero,.mle-precision-lock,.mle-precision-progress-v14,.mle-optimization-focus,.mle-next-settings-run,.mle-visual-proof,.mle-learning-track,.mle-current-locked-settings,.mle-evidence-intelligence,.mle-settings-repeat,.mle-skai-batch-test,.mle-pending-recommendations,.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown,.mle-visual-comparison', body).forEach(function(el){
      el.style.removeProperty('display');
      el.removeAttribute('hidden');
      el.setAttribute('data-mle-v77-restored','1');
    });

    qsa('details.mle-compact-group--action,.mle-compact-group--action', body).forEach(function(group){
      var content=group.querySelector('.mle-compact-group__body') || group;
      if(hasMeaningfulContent(content)){
        group.classList.remove('mle-v74-remove-empty-action-card');
        group.classList.remove('mle-v74-truly-empty');
        group.style.removeProperty('display');
      } else {
        group.classList.add('mle-v74-truly-empty');
      }
    });
  }
  function restore(){qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(restoreCard);}
  function scheduleRestore(delay){
    clearTimeout(window.__mleV76RestoreTimer);
    window.__mleV76RestoreTimer = setTimeout(restore, delay || 180);
  }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){scheduleRestore(900);});
  } else {
    scheduleRestore(900);
  }
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    if(e.target && e.target.closest && e.target.closest('.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-section-shortcut-btn,.mle-v73-btn,[data-mle-v73-action]')){
      scheduleRestore(220);
    }
  },true);
  window.mleV76RestoreNarrowingEvidenceSectionsRefresh=restore;
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV81DeepContrastRepair) { return; }
  window.__mleV81DeepContrastRepair = true;
  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function qs(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector(sel); }
  function txt(el){ return el ? String(el.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim() : ''; }
  function setProp(el, prop, value){ if (el && el.style) { el.style.setProperty(prop, value, 'important'); } }
  function removeBadInline(el){
    if (!el || !el.style) { return; }
    el.style.removeProperty('color');
    el.style.removeProperty('text-shadow');
    el.style.removeProperty('opacity');
    el.style.removeProperty('filter');
  }
  function setText(root, selector, color){ qsa(selector, root).forEach(function(n){ setProp(n, 'color', color); setProp(n, 'opacity', '1'); setProp(n, 'text-shadow', 'none'); }); }
  function makeDarkHeader(head, accent){
    if (!head) { return; }
    var bg = accent === 'amber'
      ? 'linear-gradient(135deg,#78350f 0%,#b45309 48%,#d97706 100%)'
      : accent === 'green'
        ? 'linear-gradient(135deg,#064e3b 0%,#047857 100%)'
        : 'linear-gradient(135deg,#071a36 0%,#123f7a 100%)';
    setProp(head, 'background', bg);
    setProp(head, 'color', '#ffffff');
    setProp(head, 'border-radius', '16px 16px 0 0');
    setProp(head, 'padding', '14px 16px');
    setProp(head, 'margin', '-1px -1px 12px');
    setText(head, 'h1,h2,h3,h4,h5,h6,strong,b,span,label,a,button,div', '#ffffff');
    setText(head, 'p,small,li', accent === 'amber' ? '#ffedd5' : '#dbeafe');
  }
  function makeLightBody(root){
    if (!root) { return; }
    qsa('.mle-v37-run-options,.mle-v37-run-option,.mle-v63-run-options,.mle-v63-run-option', root).forEach(function(el){
      removeBadInline(el);
      setProp(el, 'background', '#ffffff');
      setProp(el, 'color', '#0f172a');
      setText(el, 'h1,h2,h3,h4,h5,h6,strong,b,span,label,div', '#0f172a');
      setText(el, 'p,small,li,.mle-v37-run-note,.mle-muted,.mle-subtitle', '#334155');
      setText(el, 'a:not(.mle-v81-amber-cta)', '#1d4ed8');
    });
  }
  function pendingCount(card){
    var all = txt(card);
    var m = all.match(/(\d+)\s+(?:runs?|prediction runs?)\s+(?:are\s+)?(?:already\s+)?pending/i);
    return m ? (parseInt(m[1],10) || 0) : 0;
  }
  function hasResults(card){
    return /Results Ready|Results are ready|This draw has scored evidence|Print Result Sheet/i.test(txt(card).slice(0,3500));
  }
  function fixModebar(){
    qsa('.mle-v34-modebar').forEach(function(bar){
      makeDarkHeader(bar, 'blue');
      qsa('button', bar).forEach(function(btn){
        if (btn.getAttribute('aria-pressed') === 'true') {
          setProp(btn, 'background', '#ffffff');
          setProp(btn, 'color', '#0b2d61');
          setText(btn, '*', '#0b2d61');
        } else {
          setProp(btn, 'background', 'rgba(255,255,255,.13)');
          setProp(btn, 'color', '#ffffff');
          setText(btn, '*', '#ffffff');
        }
      });
    });
  }
  function markAmberCta(panel){
    if (!panel || !panel.classList.contains('mle-v78-action-ready')) { return; }
    var candidates = qsa('.mle-v37-run-actions a,.mle-v37-run-actions button,a,button', panel);
    for (var i=0;i<candidates.length;i++) {
      var label = txt(candidates[i]);
      if (/Create\s+Focus\s+9\-?Batch|Run\s+Recommended\s+9\-?Batch|Open\s+SKAI/i.test(label)) {
        candidates[i].classList.add('mle-v81-amber-cta');
        if (/Create\s+Focus\s+9\-?Batch/i.test(label)) { candidates[i].textContent = 'Open Current Step'; }
        setProp(candidates[i], 'background', 'linear-gradient(135deg,#b45309 0%,#f59e0b 100%)');
        setProp(candidates[i], 'color', '#111827');
        setProp(candidates[i], 'border', '1px solid rgba(217,119,6,.58)');
        setProp(candidates[i], 'border-radius', '999px');
        setProp(candidates[i], 'font-weight', '950');
        break;
      }
    }
  }
  function fixRunPanel(panel){
    if (!panel) { return; }
    var card = panel.closest ? panel.closest('.mle-advisory-card') : null;
    var head = qs('.mle-v37-run-panel__head,.mle-v63-run-panel__head', panel);
    var p = pendingCount(card || panel);
    if (panel.classList.contains('mle-v78-action-ready')) {
      makeDarkHeader(head, 'amber');
    } else if (p > 0) {
      makeDarkHeader(head, 'green');
    } else {
      makeDarkHeader(head, 'blue');
    }
    makeLightBody(panel);
    markAmberCta(panel);
    if (hasResults(card || panel) && !panel.classList.contains('mle-v78-action-ready') && p <= 0) {
      var eyebrow = qs('.mle-v37-run-panel__eyebrow,.mle-v63-run-panel__eyebrow', panel);
      if (eyebrow && /Choose your next run/i.test(txt(eyebrow))) { eyebrow.textContent = 'Additional SKAI run options'; }
    }
  }
  function fixDarkEvidenceHeaders(){
    qsa('.mle-v73-path__top,.mle-v70-head,.mle-skai-batch-test__head,.mle-skai-batch-test__header,.mle-precision-lock__head,.mle-precision-lock__headerer,.mle-current-locked-settings__head,.mle-current-locked-settings__header,.mle-strong-evidence__head,.mle-strong-evidence__header,.mle-learning-track__head,.mle-learning-track__header,.mle-evidence-intelligence__head,.mle-evidence-intelligence__header,.mle-visual-proof__head,.mle-visual-proof__header').forEach(function(head){
      makeDarkHeader(head, 'blue');
    });
  }
  function apply(){
    fixModebar();
    qsa('.mle-v37-run-panel,.mle-v63-run-panel').forEach(fixRunPanel);
    fixDarkEvidenceHeaders();
  }
  
  
  function scheduleApply(delay){
    window.clearTimeout(window.__mleV81ContrastTimer);
    window.__mleV81ContrastTimer = window.setTimeout(function(){
      if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) { window.requestIdleCallback(function(){ apply(); }, {timeout: 1200}); }
      else { apply(); }
    }, delay || 120);
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ scheduleApply(350); }); }
  else { scheduleApply(350); }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var t = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('.mle-v34-modebar button,.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-section-toggle,summary,.mle-v73-btn,.mle-v70-primary-action') : null;
    if (t) { scheduleApply(180); }
  }, true);
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV83Correct9BatchStateWiring) { return; }
  window.__mleV83Correct9BatchStateWiring = true;

  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function qs(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector(sel); }
  function txt(el){ return el ? String(el.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim() : ''; }
  function cls(el){ return el ? String(el.className || '') : ''; }

  function pendingCount(card){
    if (!card) { return 0; }
    var attr = parseInt(card.getAttribute('data-pending-count') || card.getAttribute('data-pending-runs') || '0', 10);
    if (!isNaN(attr) && attr > 0) { return attr; }
    var pendingStat = qs('.mle-adv-stat-chip--pending .mle-adv-stat-value', card);
    var statNum = pendingStat ? parseInt(txt(pendingStat), 10) : 0;
    if (!isNaN(statNum) && statNum > 0) { return statNum; }
    var guide = qs('.mle-v70-guide--pending', card);
    if (guide) {
      var gm = txt(guide).match(/(\d+)\s+(?:pending\s+)?(?:runs?|prediction runs?)/i);
      if (gm) { return parseInt(gm[1], 10) || 1; }
      return 1;
    }
    var all = txt(card);
    var m = all.match(/(\d+)\s+(?:runs?|prediction runs?)\s+(?:are\s+)?(?:already\s+)?pending/i);
    return m ? (parseInt(m[1], 10) || 0) : 0;
  }

  function topActionInfo(card){
    var jump = qs('.mle-status-action-jump', card);
    if (!jump) { return {state:'unknown', target:'', label:''}; }
    var target = String(jump.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '').toLowerCase();
    var label = txt(jump);
    var className = cls(jump);

    if (/mle-action-button-state--in-progress/.test(className) || /in progress|pending runs|wait for/i.test(label)) {
      return {state:'inprogress', target:target, label:label};
    }
    if (/mle-action-button-state--action/.test(className) || /action needed|create recommended|recommended next settings|run new runs|run predictions|precision batch/i.test(label)) {
      return {state:'needed', target:target, label:label};
    }
    if (/results|review|evidence|monitor|complete/i.test(target + ' ' + label)) {
      return {state:'complete', target:target, label:label};
    }
    return {state:'unknown', target:target, label:label};
  }

  function hasResultState(card){
    var top = txt(qs('.mle-v73-path,.mle-v70-guide,.mle-advisory-card__collapsed', card));
    return /Results Ready|Results are ready|scored evidence|Print Result Sheet|Review the completed draw/i.test(top);
  }

  function hasActionNeededText(card){
    var priority = txt(qs('.mle-v70-guide,.mle-v73-path,.mle-advisory-card__collapsed,.mle-v33-command,.mle-v34-modebar', card));
    return /Action\s+Next|Action Needed|Needs Action|Create Recommended Next Settings Run|Create Controlled SKAI Batch Test|Follow the recommended next test|Run new predictions|Run New Runs|Current Step is ready/i.test(priority);
  }

  function resolveBatchState(card){
    var pending = pendingCount(card);
    if (pending > 0) { return 'inprogress'; }

    var action = topActionInfo(card);
    if (action.state === 'needed') { return 'needed'; }
    if (hasActionNeededText(card)) { return 'needed'; }

    if (action.state === 'inprogress') { return 'inprogress'; }
    if (hasResultState(card) || action.state === 'complete') { return 'complete'; }

    return 'needed';
  }

  function isFocusBatchButton(el){
    if(!el){return false;}
    if(el.getAttribute && el.getAttribute('data-mle-v73-action')){return false;}
    if(el.classList && (el.classList.contains('mle-v73-btn') || el.classList.contains('mle-v70-primary-action'))){return false;}
    var label = txt(el);
    return /Create\s+Focus\s+9\-?Batch\s+and\s+Open\s+SKAI|Run\s+Recommended\s+9\-?Batch|Run\s+the\s+recommended\s+Focus\s+9\-?Batch|9\-?Batch\s+In\s+Progress|9\-?Batch\s+Completed/i.test(label);
  }

  function setButtonState(el, state){
    var currentState = el.getAttribute('data-mle-v83-batch-state') || '';
    var wantedLabel = state === 'needed'
      ? 'Create Focus 9-Batch and Open SKAI'
      : (state === 'inprogress' ? '9-Batch In Progress' : '9-Batch Completed');

    el.classList.add('mle-v83-batch-cta');
    el.classList.remove(
      'mle-v82-batch-cta--needed','mle-v82-batch-cta--inprogress','mle-v82-batch-cta--complete',
      'mle-v83-batch-cta--needed','mle-v83-batch-cta--inprogress','mle-v83-batch-cta--complete'
    );
    el.classList.add('mle-v83-batch-cta--' + state);

    if (currentState !== state || txt(el) !== wantedLabel) {
      el.textContent = wantedLabel;
      el.setAttribute('data-mle-v83-batch-state', state);
    }

    if (state === 'needed') {
      el.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Action needed: create the Focus 9-Batch and open SKAI');
      el.removeAttribute('aria-disabled');
      el.style.pointerEvents = '';
      el.style.opacity = '';
      el.style.filter = '';
    } else if (state === 'inprogress') {
      el.setAttribute('aria-label', '9-batch is already in progress for this lottery');
      el.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
      el.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
    } else {
      el.setAttribute('aria-label', '9-batch has already been completed or scored for this draw cycle');
      el.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
      el.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
    }
  }

  function applyToCard(card){
    if (!card) { return; }
    var state = resolveBatchState(card);
    qsa('a,button', card).forEach(function(el){
      if (isFocusBatchButton(el)) { setButtonState(el, state); }
    });
  }

  function apply(){ qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(applyToCard); }

  function scheduleInitialApply(){
    var run = function(){ try { apply(); } catch(e) {} };
    if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) { window.requestIdleCallback(run, {timeout: 1500}); }
    else { window.setTimeout(run, 450); }
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', scheduleInitialApply); } else { scheduleInitialApply(); }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var card = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('.mle-advisory-card') : null;
    if (card) { setTimeout(function(){ applyToCard(card); }, 120); }
  }, true);
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if(window.__mleV89ProductionCollapsePathGuard){return;}
  window.__mleV89ProductionCollapsePathGuard=true;
  if(typeof window.MLE_DEBUG_COLLAPSE_PATH==='undefined'){window.MLE_DEBUG_COLLAPSE_PATH=false;}
  function qsa(s,r){return Array.prototype.slice.call((r||document).querySelectorAll(s));}
  function qs(s,r){return (r||document).querySelector(s);}
  function clean(s){return String(s||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');}
  function txt(el){return clean(el?(el.textContent||el.innerText||''):'');}
  function closest(el,s){while(el&&el.nodeType===1){if(el.matches&&el.matches(s)){return el;}el=el.parentElement;}return null;}
  function isPrimary(card){
    return !!(card&&card.querySelector&&card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id')&&qs('.mle-advisory-card__collapsed',card)&&qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card)&&qs('.mle-lottery-toggle',card)&&!(card.classList&&(card.classList.contains('mle-optimizer-panel-card')||card.classList.contains('mle-optimizer-panel'))));
  }
  function parsePendingFromText(s){
    s=clean(s);
    var pats=[/(\d+)\s+pending\s+runs?/i,/(\d+)\s+pending\s+prediction\s+runs?/i,/in\s+progress\s*[:\-]?\s*(\d+)\s+pending/i,/pending\s+runs?\s*[:\-]?\s*(\d+)/i];
    for(var i=0;i<pats.length;i++){var m=s.match(pats[i]);if(m){var n=parseInt(m[1],10);if(!isNaN(n)&&n>0){return n;}}}
    return 0;
  }
  function resolvePending(card){
    if(!card){return 0;}
    var n=parseInt(card.getAttribute('data-pending-count')||card.getAttribute('data-pending-runs')||'0',10);
    if(!isNaN(n)&&n>0){return n;}
    var chip=qs('.mle-adv-stat-chip--pending .mle-adv-stat-value,.mle-stat--pending .mle-stat-value',card);
    n=chip?parseInt(txt(chip),10):0;
    if(!isNaN(n)&&n>0){return n;}
    var contexts=[card,closest(card,'.mle-lottery-outer'),closest(card,'.lottery-group')];
    for(var i=0;i<contexts.length;i++){n=parsePendingFromText(txt(contexts[i]));if(n>0){return n;}}
    return 0;
  }
  function setButtonText(btn,word){
    if(!btn){return;}
    var sp=btn.querySelector&&btn.querySelector('span');
    if(sp){sp.textContent=word;}else{btn.textContent=word;}
  }
  function syncCollapse(card){
    if(!isPrimary(card)){return;}
    var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card), btn=qs('.mle-lottery-toggle',card);
    if(!body||!btn){return;}
    var btnText=txt(btn).toLowerCase();
    var btnClosed=(btn.getAttribute('aria-expanded')==='false'||btnText.indexOf('expand')!==-1);
    var bodyClosed=(body.getAttribute('aria-hidden')==='true'||body.style.display==='none');
    if(btnClosed){
      body.style.display='none';
      body.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
      setButtonText(btn,'Expand');
    }else if(bodyClosed){
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
      setButtonText(btn,'Expand');
    }else{
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');
      setButtonText(btn,'Collapse');
    }
  }
  function makePendingPath(card,path,pending){
    if(!path||pending<=0){return;}
    path.className=String(path.className||'').replace(/mle-v73-path--\S+/g,'')+' mle-v73-path--pending';
    path.setAttribute('data-mle-path-state','pending');
    path.setAttribute('data-mle-path-pending-count',String(pending));
    var h4=qs('.mle-v73-path__top h4',path); if(h4){h4.textContent='Waiting for the next draw result';}
    var pill=qs('.mle-v73-pill',path); if(pill){pill.textContent='Review Pending Runs';}
    var h5=qs('.mle-v73-main h5',path); if(h5){h5.textContent='No action needed right now';}
    var p=qs('.mle-v73-main p',path); if(p){p.textContent='You already created the recommended batch for this lottery. '+pending+' prediction runs are waiting for the next official draw. After the result posts, score these runs so LottoExpert can update the evidence.';}
    var facts=qsa('.mle-v73-fact',path);
    if(facts[0]){var s=qs('strong',facts[0]);var fp=qs('p',facts[0]);if(s){s.textContent='In Progress';}if(fp){fp.textContent='The batch is already created.';}}
    if(facts[2]){var s2=qs('strong',facts[2]);var fp2=qs('p',facts[2]);if(s2){s2.textContent=String(pending);}if(fp2){fp2.textContent='Print/reprint remains available.';}}
    var warning=qs('[data-mle-v73-warning="1"]',path); if(warning){warning.hidden=true; warning.textContent='';}
    var actions=qs('.mle-v73-main__actions',path);
    if(actions){actions.innerHTML='<button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--green" data-mle-v73-action="review">Review Pending Runs</button><button type="button" class="mle-v73-btn mle-v73-btn--blue" data-mle-v73-action="print-before">Print / Reprint Sheet (Optional)</button>';}
  }
  function enforceCard(card){
    if(!card){return;}
    if(!isPrimary(card)){
      qsa('.mle-v73-path',card).forEach(function(path){if(path.parentNode){path.parentNode.removeChild(path);}});
      if(card.classList){card.classList.remove('mle-v73-active');}
      return;
    }
    syncCollapse(card);
    var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card), btn=qs('.mle-lottery-toggle',card);
    var isClosed=body&&(body.getAttribute('aria-hidden')==='true'||body.style.display==='none'||(btn&&btn.getAttribute('aria-expanded')==='false'));
    var pending=resolvePending(card);
    qsa('.mle-v73-path',card).forEach(function(path,idx){
      if(idx>0 && path.parentNode){path.parentNode.removeChild(path);return;}
      if(isClosed){path.style.display='none';path.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');return;}
      path.style.display='';path.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
      var pathText=txt(path);
      var state=path.getAttribute('data-mle-path-state')||'';
      if(pending>0 && (state==='unavailable'||/Action Not Ready|Batch controls are missing|No pending runs are active/i.test(pathText))){makePendingPath(card,path,pending);}
    });
  }
  function enforceAll(){qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(enforceCard);}
  window.mleV89ProductionCollapsePathGuard=enforceAll;
  window.mleAuditCollapseAndPaths=function(){
    var rows=[];
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(function(card,i){
      var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card), btn=qs('.mle-lottery-toggle',card), paths=qsa('.mle-v73-path',card);
      rows.push({index:i,title:txt(qs('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name,h3,h4',card)),primary:isPrimary(card),button:txt(btn),ariaExpanded:btn?btn.getAttribute('aria-expanded'):'',bodyDisplay:body?body.style.display:'',bodyHidden:body?body.getAttribute('aria-hidden'):'',pending:resolvePending(card),paths:paths.length,actionNotReady:/Action Not Ready|Batch controls are missing/i.test(txt(card))});
    });
    if(window.console&&console.table){console.table(rows);}else if(window.console){console.log(rows);}
    return rows;
  };
  
  
  function scheduleInitialEnforce(){
    var run = function(){ try { enforceAll(); } catch(e) {} };
    if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) { window.requestIdleCallback(run, {timeout: 1800}); }
    else { window.setTimeout(run, 700); }
  }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',scheduleInitialEnforce);}
  else{scheduleInitialEnforce();}
  document.addEventListener('click',function(evt){
    var card = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('.mle-advisory-card') : null;
    if(card){setTimeout(function(){try{enforceCard(card);}catch(e){}},80);setTimeout(function(){try{enforceCard(card);}catch(e){}},420);}
  },true);
})();
