(function(){
  'use strict';
  if(window.__mleV99RecommendationFirst){return;}
  window.__mleV99RecommendationFirst=true;

  function qs(s,r){return (r||document).querySelector(s);}
  function qsa(s,r){return Array.prototype.slice.call((r||document).querySelectorAll(s));}
  function clean(s){return String(s||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();}
  function esc(s){return String(s||'').replace(/[&<>"']/g,function(c){return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];});}
  function text(el){return clean(el?el.textContent:'');}
  function closest(el,s){return el&&el.closest?el.closest(s):null;}
  function cardTitle(card){return text(qs('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name,.mle-lottery-name,h3,h4',card))||'This lottery';}
  function isPrimaryCard(card){return !!(card&&qs('.mle-advisory-card__header',card)&&qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card));}
  function csv(v){var a=[];String(v||'').split(',').forEach(function(x){x=clean(x);if(x){a.push(x);}});return a;}
  function ballsFromCsv(values, cls, hitMap){
    var html='';
    for(var i=0;i<values.length;i++){
      var v=values[i];
      var hit=hitMap&&hitMap[String(v)]?' mle-official-draw-ball--hit':'';
      html+='<span class="mle-official-draw-ball '+(cls||'')+hit+'">'+esc(v)+'</span>';
    }
    return html;
  }
  function officialBox(card){
    var outer=closest(card,'.mle-lottery-outer');
    return outer?qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw[data-mle-last-draw-has-result="1"]',outer):null;
  }
  function officialData(card){
    var box=officialBox(card);
    if(!box){return null;}
    var main=csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main')||'');
    var extra=csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra')||'');
    if(!main.length&&!extra.length){return null;}
    return {
      date:clean(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-date')||text(qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__date',box))||''),
      main:main,
      extra:extra,
      hasExactPrediction: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1',
      predicted: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted')||'') : [],
      predictedExtra: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted-extra')||'') : [],
      matches: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-matches')||'') : [],
      extraMatches: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra-matches')||'') : [],
      rankingMatches:csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-ranking-matches')||''),
      mainHits:parseInt(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main-hits')||'0',10)||0,
      rankingHitCount:parseInt(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-ranking-hit-count')||'0',10)||0,
      top10:parseInt(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-top10')||'0',10)||0,
      top20:parseInt(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-top20')||'0',10)||0
    };
  }
  function recommendationSource(card){return qs('.mle-pending-recommendations',card);}
  function recCards(card){return qsa('.mle-pending-recommendation-card',recommendationSource(card)||card).slice(0,2);}
  function recInfoFromArticle(article,index){
    if(!article){return null;}
    var title=text(qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__title',article))||(index===0?'Top Recommendation':'Second Recommendation');
    var label=text(qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__top strong',article))||'Pending recommendation';
    var meta=text(qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__top small',article));
    var balls=qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__numbers',article);
    var reason=text(qs('p',article));
    var score=text(qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__score strong',article));
    return {title:title,label:label,meta:meta,ballsHtml:balls?balls.innerHTML:'',reason:reason,score:score};
  }
  function targetDraw(card){
    var rec=recommendationSource(card);
    var s=rec?text(qs('.mle-pending-recommendations__meta span:last-child',rec)):'';
    s=s.replace(/^Target draw:\s*/i,'');
    if(s){return s;}
    var chip=text(qs('.mle-next-draw-pill,.mle-draw-date,.mle-target-draw-date',card));
    return chip||'Next official draw';
  }
  function ensureHub(card){
    if(!isPrimaryCard(card)){return;}
    var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card);
    var recSrc=recommendationSource(card);
    var existing=qs('.mle-v99-rec-hub',body);
    var cards=recCards(card);
    var draw=targetDraw(card);
    var hasRecs=!!(recSrc&&cards.length);
    var hub=existing||document.createElement('section');
    hub.className='mle-v99-rec-hub';
    hub.setAttribute('aria-label','Your recommended numbers for '+cardTitle(card));
    var recHtml='';
    if(hasRecs){
      for(var i=0;i<cards.length;i++){
        var info=recInfoFromArticle(cards[i],i);
        if(!info){continue;}
        recHtml+='<article class="mle-v99-rec-card '+(i===0?'mle-v99-rec-card--primary':'')+'"><div class="mle-v99-rec-card__label"><span>'+esc(info.title)+'</span><strong>'+esc(info.score||'Review')+'</strong></div><strong>'+esc(info.label)+'</strong><small>'+esc(info.meta||('Target draw: '+draw))+'</small><div class="mle-v99-rec-card__balls">'+(info.ballsHtml||'<em>No visual numbers found yet.</em>')+'</div>'+(info.reason?'<div class="mle-v99-rec-card__reason">'+esc(info.reason)+'</div>':'')+'</article>';
      }
    } else {
      recHtml='<div class="mle-v99-no-rec"><strong>No active pending recommendation found yet.</strong><p>Create or review the next SKAI batch so LottoExpert can surface the recommended numbers for the upcoming draw.</p></div>';
    }
    hub.innerHTML='<div class="mle-v99-rec-hub__top"><div><span class="mle-v99-eyebrow">Your Recommended Numbers</span><h4>Recommended numbers for the next draw</h4><p>This is the main recommendation surface: the top pending SKAI runs, the draw they target, and the quickest actions to review them, with printing available as optional.</p></div><div class="mle-v99-rec-hub__status"><span class="mle-v99-chip mle-v99-chip--green">Target: '+esc(draw)+'</span><span class="mle-v99-chip">'+esc(hasRecs?String(cards.length)+' highlighted run'+(cards.length===1?'':'s'):'No highlighted run')+'</span></div></div><div class="mle-v99-rec-hub__recommendations">'+recHtml+'</div><div class="mle-v99-rec-hub__actions"><button type="button" class="mle-v99-action mle-v99-action--primary" data-mle-v99-action="review">Review full recommendation</button><button type="button" class="mle-v99-action mle-v99-action--blue" data-mle-v99-action="print">Print / Reprint sheet (Optional)</button><button type="button" class="mle-v99-action" data-mle-v99-action="why">See why these numbers</button></div>';
    if(!existing){body.insertBefore(hub,body.firstChild||null);} else if(body.firstChild!==hub){body.insertBefore(hub,body.firstChild||null);}
  }
  function ensureProof(card){
    if(!isPrimaryCard(card)){return;}
    var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card);
    var data=officialData(card);
    var hub=qs('.mle-v99-rec-hub',body);
    if(!hub){return;}
    var proof=qs('.mle-v99-proof-loop',body)||document.createElement('section');
    proof.className='mle-v99-proof-loop';
    proof.setAttribute('aria-label','After draw credibility check for '+cardTitle(card));
    if(!data){
      proof.innerHTML='<div class="mle-v99-proof-loop__grid"><div class="mle-v99-proof-cell"><span>After Draw Credibility Check</span><strong>No last official result found yet</strong><p>Once the official draw is available, LottoExpert should show the drawn numbers and compare them to the top recommendation.</p></div></div>';
    } else {
      var hitMap={}; data.matches.concat(data.rankingMatches).forEach(function(v){hitMap[String(v)]=true;});
      var actualHtml=ballsFromCsv(data.main,'',hitMap)+(data.extra.length?'<span class="mle-official-draw-plus">+</span>'+ballsFromCsv(data.extra,'mle-official-draw-ball--extra',{}):'');
      var predMap={}; data.matches.forEach(function(v){predMap[String(v)]=true;});
      var predictedHtml='';
      data.predicted.forEach(function(v){predictedHtml+='<span class="mle-official-pred-ball'+(predMap[String(v)]?' mle-official-pred-ball--hit':'')+'">'+esc(v)+'</span>';});
      proof.innerHTML='<div class="mle-v99-proof-loop__grid"><div class="mle-v99-proof-cell"><span>Last official draw</span><strong>'+esc(data.date||'Latest posted draw')+'</strong><div class="mle-v99-proof-loop__balls">'+actualHtml+'</div></div><div class="mle-v99-proof-cell"><span>Top predicted recommendation</span><strong>'+(predictedHtml?'Compared to actual draw':'No saved prediction for this draw')+'</strong><div class="mle-v99-proof-loop__predicted">'+(predictedHtml||'<em>No saved prediction was found for this exact draw. Run a prediction before the next draw to create a comparison.</em>')+'</div></div><div class="mle-v99-proof-cell mle-v99-proof-score"><span>Credibility check</span><strong>'+esc(String(data.mainHits))+' direct hit'+(data.mainHits===1?'':'s')+'</strong><p>'+esc(String(data.rankingHitCount))+' drawn number'+(data.rankingHitCount===1?'':'s')+' appeared anywhere in the ranked prediction. Top 20: '+esc(String(data.top20))+' | Top 10: '+esc(String(data.top10))+'</p></div></div>';
    }
    if(!proof.parentNode){body.insertBefore(proof,hub.nextSibling);} else if(hub.nextSibling!==proof){body.insertBefore(proof,hub.nextSibling);}
  }
  function ensureCollapsedPreview(card){
    if(!isPrimaryCard(card)){return;}
    var header=qs('.mle-advisory-card__header',card);
    if(!header){return;}
    var cards=recCards(card);
    var info=recInfoFromArticle(cards[0],0);
    var data=officialData(card);
    var existing=qs('.mle-v99-card-preview',header);
    if(!info&&!data){if(existing&&existing.parentNode){existing.parentNode.removeChild(existing);}return;}
    var preview=existing||document.createElement('div');
    preview.className='mle-v99-card-preview';
    var lastText=data?(data.date+' - '+data.main.join(' ') + (data.extra.length?' + '+data.extra.join(' '):'')):'Last draw not posted yet';
    preview.innerHTML='<div class="mle-v99-card-preview__row"><div><span>Recommendation preview</span><strong>'+esc(info?info.label:'No pending recommendation yet')+'</strong><div class="mle-v99-card-preview__meta">'+esc(targetDraw(card))+'</div></div><div><span>Top recommended numbers</span><div class="mle-v99-card-preview__balls">'+(info&&info.ballsHtml?info.ballsHtml:'<strong>Open card to create/review recommendations</strong>')+'</div></div><div><span>Last draw result</span><strong>'+esc(lastText)+'</strong></div></div>';
    var toggle=qs('.mle-lottery-toggle',header);
    if(!existing){header.insertBefore(preview,toggle||null);} else if(toggle&&preview.nextSibling!==toggle){header.insertBefore(preview,toggle);}
  }
  function enhanceCard(card){
    if(!isPrimaryCard(card)){return;}
    ensureHub(card);
    ensureProof(card);
    ensureCollapsedPreview(card);
  }
  function enhanceAll(){qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(enhanceCard);}
  function openTarget(card,target){
    if(!target){return;}
    var det=closest(target,'details');
    if(det){det.open=true;det.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');}
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card__body,.mle-lottery-body',card).forEach(function(b){b.style.display='';b.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');});
    setTimeout(function(){try{target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'});}catch(_){target.scrollIntoView(true);} if(target.focus){try{target.setAttribute('tabindex','-1');target.focus({preventScroll:true});}catch(_){}}},30);
  }
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    var btn=e.target&&e.target.closest?e.target.closest('[data-mle-v99-action]'):null;
    if(!btn){return;}
    var card=closest(btn,'.mle-advisory-card');
    if(!card){return;}
    var action=btn.getAttribute('data-mle-v99-action');
    if(action==='print'){
      var p=qs('.mle-print-pending-btn',card)||qs('.mle-v70-print-before',card);
      if(p){e.preventDefault();p.click();return;}
    }
    if(action==='review'){
      e.preventDefault();
      openTarget(card,qs('.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown, .mle-pending-recommendations, [id^="mle-pending-predictions-"]',card));
      return;
    }
    if(action==='why'){
      e.preventDefault();
      openTarget(card,qs('.mle-pending-recommendation-card__reason, .mle-pending-recommendation-card p, .mle-pending-recommendations',card));
      return;
    }
  });
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',enhanceAll);}else{enhanceAll();}
  window.addEventListener('load',function(){enhanceAll();setTimeout(enhanceAll,500);setTimeout(enhanceAll,1600);});
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){if(e.target&&e.target.closest&&e.target.closest('.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-section-shortcut-btn,.mle-v70-nav-btn')){setTimeout(enhanceAll,120);setTimeout(enhanceAll,600);}},true);
  window.mleV99RefreshRecommendationFirst=enhanceAll;
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV100TruthWiring) { return; }
  window.__mleV100TruthWiring = true;

  function qs(s,r){return (r||document).querySelector(s);}
  function qsa(s,r){return Array.prototype.slice.call((r||document).querySelectorAll(s));}
  function closest(el,s){return el&&el.closest?el.closest(s):null;}
  function clean(v){return String(v||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();}
  function esc(s){return String(s||'').replace(/[&<>"']/g,function(c){return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];});}
  function csv(v){var out=[]; String(v||'').split(',').forEach(function(x){x=clean(x); if(x){out.push(x);}}); return out;}
  function text(el){return clean(el?el.textContent:'');}
  function int(v){v=parseInt(v,10);return isNaN(v)?0:v;}
  function dateScore(d){var t=Date.parse(d||''); return isNaN(t)?0:t;}

  function ballHtml(values, hitSet, extra){
    var h='';
    values.forEach(function(v){
      var k=String(v);
      h+='<span class="mle-v100-ball '+(extra?'mle-v100-ball--extra ':'')+(hitSet&&hitSet[k]?'mle-v100-ball--hit':'')+'">'+esc(v)+'</span>';
    });
    return h;
  }

  function readOfficialData(outer){
    var box=qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw',outer);
    if(!box){return null;}
    var main=csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main')||'');
    var extra=csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra')||'');
    var has=(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-result')==='1') && (main.length||extra.length);
    if(!has){return null;}
    return {
      source:'outer-data',
      date:clean(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-date')||text(qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__date',box))||''),
      actualMain:main,
      actualExtra:extra,
      hasExactPrediction: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1',
      predicted: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted')||'') : [],
      predictedExtra: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted-extra')||'') : [],
      matches: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-matches')||'') : [],
      extraMatches: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra-matches')||'') : [],
      rankingMatches: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-ranking-matches')||'') : [],
      mainHits:int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main-hits')||'0'),
      totalHits:int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-ranking-hit-count')||'0') || int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main-hits')||'0'),
      extraHits:0,
      top10:int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-top10')||'0'),
      top20:int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-top20')||'0')
    };
  }

  function bestDrawData(outer){
    return readOfficialData(outer);
  }

  function updateNativeLastDrawBox(outer,data){
    var box=qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw',outer);
    if(!box || !data || !data.actualMain.length){return;}
    box.classList.remove('mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw--empty');
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-result','1');
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-date',data.date||'Latest draw');
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main',data.actualMain.join(','));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra',(data.actualExtra||[]).join(','));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted',(data.predicted||[]).join(','));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted-extra',(data.predictedExtra||[]).join(','));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-matches',(data.matches||[]).join(','));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra-matches',(data.extraMatches||[]).join(','));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main-hits',String(data.mainHits||0));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-ranking-hit-count',String(data.totalHits||0));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-top10',String(data.top10||0));
    box.setAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-top20',String(data.top20||0));
    data=normalizeComparison(data);
    var mainHit={}; (data.matches||[]).forEach(function(v){mainHit[String(v)]=true;});
    var extraHit={}; (data.extraMatches||[]).forEach(function(v){extraHit[String(v)]=true;});
    box.innerHTML='<span class="mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__label">Last Draw</span><strong class="mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__date">'+esc(data.date||'Latest draw')+'</strong><span class="mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__balls" aria-label="Winning numbers">'+ballHtml(data.actualMain,mainHit,false)+(data.actualExtra&&data.actualExtra.length?'<span class="mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__plus" aria-hidden="true">+</span>'+ballHtml(data.actualExtra,extraHit,true):'')+'</span><span class="mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__compare">'+esc(String(data.totalHits||data.mainHits||0))+' total hit'+((data.totalHits||data.mainHits||0)===1?'':'s')+'</span>';
  }

  function renderOuterProof(outer,data){
    var header=qs('.mle-lottery-outer-header',outer);
    if(!header){return;}
    var old=qs('.mle-v100-outer-proof',header);
    if(!data || !data.actualMain.length){
      if(old){old.parentNode.removeChild(old);}
      return;
    }
    var mainHit={}; (data.matches||[]).forEach(function(v){mainHit[String(v)]=true;});
    var extraHit={}; (data.extraMatches||[]).forEach(function(v){extraHit[String(v)]=true;});
    var proof=old||document.createElement('div');
    proof.className='mle-v100-outer-proof';
    proof.setAttribute('aria-label','Latest draw result and prediction comparison');
    var hasExactPrediction = data.hasExactPrediction === true || data.hasExactPrediction === 1 || data.hasExactPrediction === '1';
    var predictionHtml=hasExactPrediction&&data.predicted&&data.predicted.length?ballHtml(data.predicted,mainHit,false):'<strong>No saved prediction for this draw</strong>';
    if(hasExactPrediction&&data.predictedExtra&&data.predictedExtra.length){predictionHtml+='<span class="mle-v100-plus">+</span>'+ballHtml(data.predictedExtra,extraHit,true);}
    proof.innerHTML='<div class="mle-v100-outer-proof__cell"><span>Latest actual draw</span><strong>'+esc(data.date||'Latest draw')+'</strong><div class="mle-v100-balls">'+ballHtml(data.actualMain,mainHit,false)+(data.actualExtra&&data.actualExtra.length?'<span class="mle-v100-plus">+</span>'+ballHtml(data.actualExtra,extraHit,true):'')+'</div></div><div class="mle-v100-outer-proof__cell"><span>Compared with prediction</span><div class="mle-v100-balls">'+predictionHtml+'</div></div><div class="mle-v100-outer-proof__cell mle-v100-outer-proof__score"><span>Result check</span><strong>'+esc(String(data.mainHits||0))+' main match'+((data.mainHits||0)===1?'':'es')+'</strong><small>Total matches: '+esc(String(data.totalHits||data.mainHits||0))+(data.extraHits?' | Extra: '+esc(String(data.extraHits)):'')+'<br>Top 20: '+esc(String(data.top20||0))+' | Top 10: '+esc(String(data.top10||0))+'</small></div>';
    if(!old){header.appendChild(proof);}
  }

  function renderAfterDraw(card,data){
    var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card);
    if(!body){return;}
    var existing=qs('.mle-v100-afterdraw',body);
    var section=existing||document.createElement('section');
    section.className='mle-v100-afterdraw';
    section.setAttribute('aria-label','Latest draw result and prediction credibility check');
    if(!data || !data.actualMain.length){
      section.innerHTML='<div class="mle-v100-empty-note"><strong>Latest draw result not loaded yet.</strong><p>Once the official result is available, this section should show the drawn numbers and compare them with the saved prediction.</p></div>';
    } else {
      var mainHit={}; (data.matches||[]).forEach(function(v){mainHit[String(v)]=true;});
      var extraHit={}; (data.extraMatches||[]).forEach(function(v){extraHit[String(v)]=true;});
      var hasExactPrediction = data.hasExactPrediction === true || data.hasExactPrediction === 1 || data.hasExactPrediction === '1';
      var predictionHtml=hasExactPrediction&&data.predicted&&data.predicted.length?ballHtml(data.predicted,mainHit,false):'<em>No saved prediction was found for this exact draw. Run a prediction before the next draw to create a comparison.</em>';
      if(hasExactPrediction&&data.predictedExtra&&data.predictedExtra.length){predictionHtml+='<span class="mle-v100-plus">+</span>'+ballHtml(data.predictedExtra,extraHit,true);}
      section.innerHTML='<div class="mle-v100-afterdraw__head"><div><span class="mle-v100-afterdraw__eyebrow">After Draw Credibility Check</span><h4>Latest draw result and prediction comparison</h4><p>This is the proof loop: what actually came out, what LottoExpert predicted, and how many numbers matched.</p></div></div><div class="mle-v100-afterdraw__grid"><div class="mle-v100-afterdraw__cell"><span>Actual numbers drawn</span><strong>'+esc(data.date||'Latest draw')+'</strong><div class="mle-v100-balls">'+ballHtml(data.actualMain,mainHit,false)+(data.actualExtra&&data.actualExtra.length?'<span class="mle-v100-plus">+</span>'+ballHtml(data.actualExtra,extraHit,true):'')+'</div></div><div class="mle-v100-afterdraw__cell"><span>Top saved prediction</span><strong>'+(hasExactPrediction&&data.predicted&&data.predicted.length?'Prediction checked':'No saved prediction for this draw')+'</strong><div class="mle-v100-balls">'+predictionHtml+'</div></div><div class="mle-v100-afterdraw__cell mle-v100-afterdraw__score"><span>Credibility result</span><strong>'+esc(String(data.totalHits||data.mainHits||0))+'</strong><p>Total hits. Main hits: '+esc(String(data.mainHits||0))+(data.extraHits?' | Extra hits: '+esc(String(data.extraHits)):'')+'<br>Top 20: '+esc(String(data.top20||0))+' | Top 10: '+esc(String(data.top10||0))+'</p></div></div>';
    }
    var hub=qs('.mle-v99-rec-hub',body)||qs('.mle-pending-recommendations',body)||body.firstChild;
    if(!existing){
      if(hub && hub.nextSibling){body.insertBefore(section, hub.nextSibling);}else{body.insertBefore(section, body.firstChild||null);}
    } else if(hub && hub.nextSibling!==section) {
      body.insertBefore(section, hub.nextSibling);
    }
  }

  function moveRecommendationFirst(card){
    var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card);
    var rec=qs('.mle-pending-recommendations',card);
    var hub=qs('.mle-v99-rec-hub',body);
    if(body && rec && hub && rec.parentNode===body && hub.nextSibling!==rec){
      body.insertBefore(rec, hub.nextSibling);
    }
  }

  function enhanceOuter(outer){
    var data=bestDrawData(outer);
    if(data){ updateNativeLastDrawBox(outer,data); }
    renderOuterProof(outer,data);
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card',outer).forEach(function(card){
      if(qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card)){
        moveRecommendationFirst(card);
        renderAfterDraw(card,data);
      }
    });
    outer.setAttribute('data-mle-v100-lastdraw-source', data ? data.source : 'none');
  }
  function run(){qsa('.mle-lottery-outer').forEach(enhanceOuter);}

  function scheduleRun(delay){ clearTimeout(window.__mleV100RunTimer); window.__mleV100RunTimer=setTimeout(run, delay||180); }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){scheduleRun(900);});}else{scheduleRun(900);}
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    if(e.target && e.target.closest && e.target.closest('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-section-toggle,.mle-v99-action')){scheduleRun(180);}
  },true);
  window.mleV100RefreshTruthWiring=run;
  window.mleV100AuditLastDrawWiring=function(){
    var rows=qsa('.mle-lottery-outer').map(function(outer,i){
      var title=text(qs('.mle-lottery-outer-title',outer));
      var data=bestDrawData(outer);
      return {index:i,title:title,source:data?data.source:'none',date:data?data.date:'',actual:data?data.actualMain.join(' '):'',extra:data?data.actualExtra.join(' '):'',predicted:data?data.predicted.join(' '):'',hits:data?(data.totalHits||data.mainHits):0,visualRows:qsa('.mle-visual-row',outer).length,hasOuterBox:!!qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw',outer)};
    });
    if(window.console&&console.table){console.table(rows);}else if(window.console){console.log(rows);}
    return rows;
  };
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if(window.__mleV101VisibleLastDrawResultbar){return;}
  window.__mleV101VisibleLastDrawResultbar=true;
  function qs(s,r){return (r||document).querySelector(s);}
  function qsa(s,r){return Array.prototype.slice.call((r||document).querySelectorAll(s));}
  function clean(v){return String(v||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();}
  function esc(v){return String(v||'').replace(/[&<>"']/g,function(c){return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];});}
  function csv(v){var out=[];String(v||'').split(',').forEach(function(p){p=clean(p);if(p){out.push(p);}});return out;}
  function int(v){var n=parseInt(String(v||'0'),10);return isNaN(n)?0:n;}
  function text(el){return clean(el?el.textContent:'');}
  function dateScore(v){var t=Date.parse(v||'');return isNaN(t)?0:t;}
  function buildMatchPayload(actualMain,predictedMain,actualExtra,predictedExtra){
    function countMatches(actual,predicted){
      var counts={}, matches=[], i, key;
      actual=actual||[]; predicted=predicted||[];
      for(i=0;i<actual.length;i++){key=String(actual[i]);counts[key]=(counts[key]||0)+1;}
      for(i=0;i<predicted.length;i++){key=String(predicted[i]);if(counts[key]>0){matches.push(predicted[i]);counts[key]-=1;}}
      return matches;
    }
    var main=countMatches(actualMain||[],predictedMain||[]);
    var extra=countMatches(actualExtra||[],predictedExtra||[]);
    return {matches:main,extraMatches:extra,mainHits:main.length,extraHits:extra.length,totalHits:main.length+extra.length};
  }
  function normalizeComparison(data){
    var cmp;
    if(!data){return data;}
    if((data.hasExactPrediction === true || data.hasExactPrediction === 1 || data.hasExactPrediction === '1') && data.actualMain&&data.actualMain.length&&data.predicted&&data.predicted.length){
      cmp=buildMatchPayload(data.actualMain,data.predicted,data.actualExtra||[],data.predictedExtra||[]);
      data.matches=cmp.matches;
      data.extraMatches=cmp.extraMatches;
      data.mainHits=cmp.mainHits;
      data.extraHits=cmp.extraHits;
      data.totalHits=cmp.totalHits;
    }
    return data;
  }
  function ballHtml(values,hit,extra,pred){
    var h='';
    values=(values||[]);
    for(var i=0;i<values.length;i++){
      var val=values[i];
      var matched = !!(hit&&hit[String(val)]);
      var role = pred ? (extra ? (matched ? 'pred-extra-hit' : 'pred-extra') : (matched ? 'pred-main-hit' : 'pred-main')) : (extra ? 'actual-extra' : 'actual-main');
      h+='<span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball mle-ball-core mle-ball-role-'+role+' '+(extra?'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--extra ':'')+(pred?'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--predicted ':'')+(matched?'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--hit':'')+'" data-ball-role="'+esc(role)+'" data-ball-number="'+esc(val)+'"><span class="mle-ball-text">'+esc(val)+'</span></span>';
    }
    return h;
  }
  function readNative(outer){
    var box=qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw',outer);
    if(!box){return null;}
    var main=csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main')||'');
    var extra=csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra')||'');
    if(!main.length&&!extra.length){return null;}
    return {
      source:'native-header-data',
      date:clean(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-date')||text(qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__date',box))||'Latest draw'),
      actualMain:main,
      actualExtra:extra,
      hasExactPrediction: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1',
      predicted: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted')||'') : [],
      predictedExtra: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted-extra')||'') : [],
      matches: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-matches')||'') : [],
      extraMatches: box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1' ? csv(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra-matches')||'') : [],
      mainHits:int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main-hits')||'0'),
      totalHits:int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-ranking-hit-count')||box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main-hits')||'0'),
      top10:int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-top10')||'0'),
      top20:int(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-top20')||'0'),
      methodLabel:clean(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-method-label')||''),
      methodKey:clean(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-method-key')||''),
      trackLabel:clean(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-track-label')||''),
      scoreDate:dateScore(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-date')||'')
    };
  }
  function bestData(outer){return readNative(outer);}
  function renderBar(outer,data){
    var bar=qs('.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar',outer);
    var header=qs('.mle-lottery-outer-header',outer);
    if(!bar&&header){
      bar=document.createElement('div');
      bar.className='mle-lottery-outer-resultbar mle-lottery-outer-resultbar--empty';
      header.parentNode.insertBefore(bar, header.nextSibling);
    }
    if(!bar){return;}
    if(!data||!(data.actualMain&&data.actualMain.length||data.actualExtra&&data.actualExtra.length)){
      bar.className='mle-lottery-outer-resultbar mle-lottery-outer-resultbar--empty';
      bar.innerHTML='<div class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell--actual"><span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__label">Previous Draw Result</span><strong class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__date">Not loaded yet</strong><span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__empty">No official result was found in the rendered page for this lottery.</span></div><div class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell"><span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__label">Prediction For This Draw</span><strong class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__muted">No saved prediction for this draw</strong></div><div class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell"><span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__label">Result Check</span><strong>0 hits</strong><small>Waiting for scored evidence.</small></div>';
      return;
    }
    var mainHit={}; (data.matches||[]).forEach(function(v){mainHit[String(v)]=true;});
    var extraHit={}; (data.extraMatches||[]).forEach(function(v){extraHit[String(v)]=true;});
    bar.className='mle-lottery-outer-resultbar';
    bar.setAttribute('data-mle-resultbar-has-result','1');
    bar.setAttribute('data-mle-resultbar-date',data.date||'Latest draw');
    var hasExactPrediction = data.hasExactPrediction === true || data.hasExactPrediction === 1 || data.hasExactPrediction === '1';
    var predictedHtml = (hasExactPrediction && data.predicted&&data.predicted.length) ? ballHtml(data.predicted,mainHit,false,true) : '';
    if(hasExactPrediction && data.predictedExtra&&data.predictedExtra.length){predictedHtml += '<span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__plus" aria-hidden="true">+</span>' + ballHtml(data.predictedExtra,extraHit,true,true);}
    var methodBadge = (predictedHtml && data.methodLabel) ? '<span class="mle-exact-draw-method-badge">Method: '+esc(data.methodLabel)+(data.trackLabel?' <em>'+esc(data.trackLabel)+'</em>':'')+'</span>' : '';
    var provenanceLabel = bar.getAttribute('data-mle-resultbar-provenance-label') || data.provenanceLabel || 'Your Saved Prediction';
    var traceLine = bar.getAttribute('data-mle-resultbar-trace-line') || data.traceLine || '';
    var batchLine = bar.getAttribute('data-mle-resultbar-batch-line') || data.batchLine || '';
    var runDateLine = bar.getAttribute('data-mle-resultbar-run-date') || data.runDate || '';
    var targetDrawLine = bar.getAttribute('data-mle-resultbar-target-draw') || data.targetDraw || '';
    var sourceLine = '';
    if (runDateLine || targetDrawLine || batchLine) {
      sourceLine = 'Source run: ' + (runDateLine || 'not recorded') + (targetDrawLine ? ' for ' + targetDrawLine : '') + (batchLine ? ' | ' + batchLine : '');
    }
    bar.innerHTML='<div class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell--actual"><span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__label">Previous Draw Result</span><strong class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__date">'+esc(data.date||'Latest draw')+'</strong><span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__balls" aria-label="Actual numbers drawn">'+ballHtml(data.actualMain,mainHit,false,false)+(data.actualExtra&&data.actualExtra.length?'<span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__plus" aria-hidden="true">+</span>'+ballHtml(data.actualExtra,extraHit,true,false):'')+'</span></div><div class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell--comparison"><span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__label">Prediction For This Draw</span>'+methodBadge+(predictedHtml?'<small class="mle-exact-draw-comparison-note">Exact-draw check only. This is selected from your saved predictions for the draw shown here, not from historical winners.</small><small class="mle-exact-draw-provenance"><strong>'+esc(provenanceLabel)+'</strong>'+ (traceLine ? ' | '+esc(traceLine) : '') +'</small>'+ (batchLine ? '<small class="mle-exact-draw-batch-line">'+esc(batchLine)+'</small>' : '') +'<span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__balls" aria-label="Top saved prediction for this exact draw">'+predictedHtml+'</span>':'<strong class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__muted">No saved prediction for this draw</strong><small class="mle-exact-draw-comparison-note">The official result is shown, but LottoExpert has no saved prediction tied to this exact drawing. Run a prediction before the next draw to create a comparison.</small>')+'</div><div class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell--score"><span class="mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__label">Result Check</span><strong>'+esc(data.mainHits||0)+' main match'+((data.mainHits||0)===1?'':'es')+'</strong><small>'+esc(data.totalHits||0)+' total match'+((data.totalHits||0)===1?'':'es')+(data.extraHits?' | Extra: '+esc(data.extraHits):'')+' | Top 20: '+esc(data.top20||0)+' | Top 10: '+esc(data.top10||0)+'</small>'+(sourceLine?'<small class="mle-result-check-provenance">'+esc(sourceLine)+'</small>':'')+'</div>';
  }
  function run(){qsa('.mle-lottery-outer').forEach(function(outer){renderBar(outer,bestData(outer));});}
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',run);}else{run();}
  window.addEventListener('load',function(){run();setTimeout(run,500);setTimeout(run,1800);setTimeout(run,4000);});

  window.mleV101RefreshLastDrawResultbar=run;

    });
    if(window.console&&console.table){console.table(rows);}else if(window.console){console.log(rows);}
    return rows;
  };
