(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV104Previous9RunReportSurface) { return; }
  window.__mleV104Previous9RunReportSurface = true;

  function qs(s,r){return (r||document).querySelector(s);}
  function qsa(s,r){return Array.prototype.slice.call((r||document).querySelectorAll(s));}
  function clean(s){return String(s||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');}
  function txt(el){return clean(el && (el.textContent || el.innerText) ? (el.textContent || el.innerText) : '');}
  function esc(s){return String(s||'').replace(/[&<>"']/g,function(c){return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];});}
  function intFrom(s){var m=String(s||'').match(/-?\d+/);return m?parseInt(m[0],10):0;}
  function csvFromAttr(s){return clean(s).split(',').map(function(x){return clean(x);}).filter(Boolean);}
  function numbersFrom(node){
    var nums=[];
    if(!node){return nums;}
    qsa('.mle-ball,.mle-v102-ball,.mle-v104-ball,.prc-num',node).forEach(function(ball){
      var n=clean(ball.getAttribute('data-number')||txt(ball)).match(/\d+/);
      if(n){nums.push(n[0]);}
    });
    if(nums.length){return nums;}
    var raw=txt(node).match(/\b\d{1,3}\b/g);
    return raw?raw.slice(0,12):[];
  }
  function attrNums(row,name){
    return csvFromAttr(row && row.getAttribute ? row.getAttribute(name) : '');
  }
  function mapFrom(nums){
    var m={};
    (nums||[]).forEach(function(n){m[String(parseInt(n,10))]=1;});
    return m;
  }
  function ballListHtml(nums, hitMap, cls){
    if(!nums || !nums.length){return '';}
    return nums.map(function(n){
      var key=String(parseInt(n,10));
      var isHit=!!(hitMap && hitMap[key]);
      return '<span class="mle-v104-ball '+(cls||'')+(isHit?' mle-v104-ball--hit':'')+'" data-number="'+esc(n)+'">'+esc(n)+'</span>';
    }).join('');
  }
  function splitBallHtml(mainNums, extraNums, mainHitMap, extraHitMap, mainCls, extraCls){
    var mainHtml=ballListHtml(mainNums||[], mainHitMap||null, mainCls||'');
    var extraHtml='';
    if(extraNums && extraNums.length){
      extraHtml=ballListHtml(extraNums, extraHitMap||null, (extraCls||'mle-v104-ball--extra'));
    }
    if(!mainHtml && !extraHtml){return '<em>Not shown</em>';}
    return '<span class="mle-v107-ball-line">'+mainHtml+(extraHtml?'<span class="mle-v104-plus">+</span>'+extraHtml:'')+'</span>';
  }
  function ballHtml(nums, hitMap, cls){
    return splitBallHtml(nums||[], [], hitMap||null, null, cls||'', '');
  }
  function cardTitle(card){return txt(qs('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name',card)) || txt(qs('h2,h3',card)) || 'This lottery';}
  function isUpcomingRow(row){return !!qs('.mle-visual-upcoming',row) || /\b(upcoming|pending|waiting)\b/i.test(txt(row));}
  function completedRows(card){var originalRows=qsa('.mle-visual-row',card).filter(function(row){return !isUpcomingRow(row);});var rows=originalRows;if(window.mlePrintManifestFilterRows){try{var filtered=window.mlePrintManifestFilterRows(card,originalRows);if(filtered && filtered.length){rows=filtered;}else if(originalRows.length){rows=originalRows;card.setAttribute('data-mle-v139-history-filter-fallback','1');}}catch(e){rows=originalRows;}}return rows;}
  function pendingRows(card){return qsa('.mle-pending-prediction-row',card).concat(qsa('.mle-visual-row',card).filter(isUpcomingRow));}
  function getLastDrawBox(card){return qs('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip',card) || qs('.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw',card);}
  function getLastDrawData(card){
    var box=getLastDrawBox(card);
    var actual=[], extra=[], predicted=[];
    if(box){
      actual=csvFromAttr(card.getAttribute('data-mle-v102-last-draw-main')||box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-main')||'');
      extra=csvFromAttr(card.getAttribute('data-mle-v102-last-draw-extra')||box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-extra')||'');
      var hasExactPrediction = box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-has-exact-prediction') === '1';
      predicted=hasExactPrediction?csvFromAttr(box.getAttribute('data-mle-last-draw-predicted')||''):[];
      if(!actual.length){actual=numbersFrom(qs('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip__cell--actual',box));}
      if(hasExactPrediction && !predicted.length){predicted=numbersFrom(qs('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip__cell--prediction',box));}
    }
    return {date: clean((card.getAttribute('data-mle-v102-last-draw-date')||'') || (box ? txt(qs('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip__date,.mle-lottery-outer-lastdraw__date',box)) : '')), actual:actual, extra:extra, predicted:predicted};
  }
  function parseRow(row, rank){
    var meta=qs('.mle-visual-row__meta',row);
    var date=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-visual-draw-date')||'') || txt(qs('strong',meta)) || txt(qs('.mle-visual-row__meta strong',row)) || 'Completed draw';
    var method=txt(qs('span',meta)) || 'Saved prediction';
    var label=txt(qs('small',meta)) || '';
    var ballCells=qsa('.mle-visual-row__balls',row);
    var predictedMain=attrNums(row,'data-mle-visual-predicted-main');
    var predictedExtra=attrNums(row,'data-mle-visual-predicted-extra');
    var actualMain=attrNums(row,'data-mle-visual-actual-main');
    var actualExtra=attrNums(row,'data-mle-visual-actual-extra');
    if(!predictedMain.length){predictedMain=numbersFrom(ballCells[0]||row);}
    if(!actualMain.length){actualMain=numbersFrom(ballCells[1]||null);}
    var res=txt(qs('.mle-visual-row__result',row));
    var totalAttr=row.getAttribute('data-mle-visual-total-hits');
    var mainAttr=row.getAttribute('data-mle-visual-main-hits');
    var extraAttr=row.getAttribute('data-mle-visual-extra-hits');
    var top20Attr=row.getAttribute('data-mle-visual-top20');
    var top10Attr=row.getAttribute('data-mle-visual-top10');
    var total=totalAttr!==null && totalAttr!=='' ? parseInt(totalAttr,10) : intFrom(txt(qs('.mle-visual-row__result strong',row)) || res);
    var mainHitMatch=res.match(/Main hits:\s*(\d+)/i);
    var extraHitMatch=res.match(/Extra hits:\s*(\d+)/i);
    var top20Match=res.match(/Top\s*20:\s*(\d+)/i);
    var top10Match=res.match(/Top\s*10:\s*(\d+)/i);
    var mainHits=mainAttr!==null && mainAttr!=='' ? parseInt(mainAttr,10) : (mainHitMatch?parseInt(mainHitMatch[1],10):0);
    var extraHits=extraAttr!==null && extraAttr!=='' ? parseInt(extraAttr,10) : (extraHitMatch?parseInt(extraHitMatch[1],10):0);
    var top20=top20Attr!==null && top20Attr!=='' ? parseInt(top20Attr,10) : (top20Match?parseInt(top20Match[1],10):0);
    var top10=top10Attr!==null && top10Attr!=='' ? parseInt(top10Attr,10) : (top10Match?parseInt(top10Match[1],10):0);
    var actualMap=mapFrom(actualMain);
    var actualExtraMap=mapFrom(actualExtra);
    var direct=predictedMain.filter(function(n){return actualMap[String(parseInt(n,10))];}).length;
    var extraDirect=predictedExtra.filter(function(n){return actualExtraMap[String(parseInt(n,10))];}).length;
    if(!mainHits && direct){mainHits=direct;}
    if(!extraHits && extraDirect){extraHits=extraDirect;}
    if(!total && (mainHits||extraHits)){total=mainHits+extraHits;}
    var batchUuid=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-batch-uuid')||'');
    var targetId=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-prediction-target-id')||'');
    var targetKey=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-prediction-target-key')||'');
    var methodKey=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-analysis-method-key')||'');
    var sourceRecordId=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-source-record-id')||row.getAttribute('data-mle-saved-id')||'');
    var runUuid=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-run-uuid')||'');
    var snapshotRunUuid=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-snapshot-run-uuid')||'');
    var runIdentityKey=clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-run-identity-key')||'');
    var batchIndex=parseInt(row.getAttribute('data-mle-batch-index')||'0',10)||0;
    var batchTotal=parseInt(row.getAttribute('data-mle-batch-total')||'0',10)||0;
    var sourceBatchRunOrder=parseInt(row.getAttribute('data-mle-source-batch-run-order')||'0',10)||0;
    var explicitSavedRank=parseInt(
      row.getAttribute('data-mle-original-printed-group-number')
      || row.getAttribute('data-mle-saved-recommendation-rank')
      || row.getAttribute('data-mle-saved-rank')
      || row.getAttribute('data-mle-recommendation-rank')
      || row.getAttribute('data-mle-display-order')
      || row.getAttribute('data-mle-group-index')
      || '0'
    ,10)||0;
    var reportRowIndex=parseInt(row.getAttribute('data-mle-v104-row-index')||'-1',10);
    if(isNaN(reportRowIndex)){reportRowIndex=-1;}
    var printVerified=(row.getAttribute('data-mle-print-verified')==='1');
    return {rank:rank,date:date,method:method,label:label,
      predictedMain:predictedMain,predictedExtra:predictedExtra,actualMain:actualMain,actualExtra:actualExtra,
      predicted:predictedMain.concat(predictedExtra),actual:actualMain.concat(actualExtra),
      totalHits:total||0,mainHits:mainHits||0,extraHits:extraHits||0,top20:top20||0,top10:top10||0,
      postDrawHitCount:total||0,
      sourceRecordId:sourceRecordId,runUuid:runUuid,snapshotRunUuid:snapshotRunUuid,runIdentityKey:runIdentityKey,
      batchUuid:batchUuid,batchIndex:batchIndex,batchTotal:batchTotal,predictionTargetId:targetId,predictionTargetKey:targetKey,
      sourceBatchRunOrder:sourceBatchRunOrder,
      savedRecommendationRankRaw:explicitSavedRank,
      reportRowIndex:reportRowIndex,
      printedRowOrder:(typeof rank==='number' ? (rank+1) : 0),
      analysisMethodKey:methodKey,originSource:clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-origin-source')||''),source:clean(row.getAttribute('data-mle-source')||''),
      printVerified:printVerified,
      isBest:row.classList && row.classList.contains('mle-visual-row--best'),sourceRow:row};
  }
  function resolveSavedRecommendationRank(run){
    if(!run){return 0;}
    var rank=0;
    if((run.savedRecommendationRankRaw||0)>0){rank=run.savedRecommendationRankRaw;}
    else if((run.sourceBatchRunOrder||0)>0){rank=run.sourceBatchRunOrder;}
    else if((run.batchIndex||0)>0){rank=run.batchIndex;}
    else if((run.reportRowIndex||-1)>=0){rank=run.reportRowIndex+1;}
    else if((run.printedRowOrder||0)>0){rank=run.printedRowOrder;}
    return rank>0?rank:0;
  }
  function applySavedRecommendationRanks(runs){
    var used={};
    var fallback=1;
    (runs||[]).forEach(function(run){
      var proposed=resolveSavedRecommendationRank(run);
      if(proposed>0 && !used[proposed]){
        run.savedRecommendationRank=proposed;
        used[proposed]=1;
        return;
      }
      while(used[fallback]){fallback++;}
      run.savedRecommendationRank=fallback;
      used[fallback]=1;
      fallback++;
    });
  }
  function findRecommendationBySavedRank(runs, wantedRank){
    var i;
    for(i=0;i<(runs||[]).length;i++){
      if((runs[i].savedRecommendationRank||0)===wantedRank){return runs[i];}
    }
    return null;
  }

  
  
  
  function v104PredictionSignature(run){
    var main=(run && run.predictedMain) ? run.predictedMain : [];
    var extra=(run && run.predictedExtra) ? run.predictedExtra : [];
    return main.map(function(v){return String(parseInt(v,10));}).join(',')+'|'+extra.map(function(v){return String(parseInt(v,10));}).join(',');
  }
  function v104BatchPredictionIntegrity(rows){
    var map={}, unique=0, total=0, i, sig;
    if(!rows || !rows.length){return {warning:false,total:0,unique:0,duplicates:0};}
    for(i=0;i<rows.length;i++){
      sig=v104PredictionSignature(rows[i]);
      if(sig==='|'){continue;}
      total++;
      if(!map[sig]){map[sig]=1; unique++;} else {map[sig]++;}
    }
    return {
      warning: total>=3 && unique<=Math.max(1,Math.floor(total/3)),
      total: total,
      unique: unique,
      duplicates: Math.max(0,total-unique)
    };
  }
  function bestRun(runs){
    if(!runs.length){return null;}
    var best=runs[0];
    runs.forEach(function(r){
      if((r.totalHits||0)>(best.totalHits||0)){best=r;return;}
      if((r.totalHits||0)===(best.totalHits||0) && (r.top20||0)>(best.top20||0)){best=r;return;}
      if(r.isBest && !best.isBest){best=r;}
    });
    return best;
  }
  function mleForensicBatchKey(r){
    var method=clean(r.analysisMethodKey||r.method||'');
    var target=clean(r.predictionTargetId||r.predictionTargetKey||'');
    if(r.batchUuid){return 'batch|'+r.batchUuid+'|'+target+'|'+method;}
    if(target || method){return 'target|'+target+'|'+method+'|'+clean(r.date||'');}
    return 'legacy|'+clean(r.date||'');
  }
  function mleForensicPickBestGroup(rows){
    var groups={}, order=[], bestKey='', bestLen=-1, bestScore=-1;
    rows.forEach(function(r){
      var k=mleForensicBatchKey(r);
      if(!groups[k]){groups[k]=[];order.push(k);}
      groups[k].push(r);
    });
    order.forEach(function(k){
      var g=groups[k], score=0;
      g.forEach(function(r){score+=(r.totalHits||0)+(r.top20||0)*0.01+(r.top10||0)*0.02;});
      if(g.length>bestLen || (g.length===bestLen && score>bestScore)){bestKey=k;bestLen=g.length;bestScore=score;}
    });
    return groups[bestKey]||[];
  }
  function latestBatchRows(runs){
    if(!runs || !runs.length){return [];}
    var withDate=runs.filter(function(r){return r.date && !/completed draw/i.test(r.date);});
    if(!withDate.length){return mleForensicPickBestGroup(runs).slice(0,9);}
    withDate.sort(function(a,b){return String(b.date).localeCompare(String(a.date));});
    var latest=withDate[0].date;
    var latestRows=runs.filter(function(r){return r.date===latest;});
    var group=mleForensicPickBestGroup(latestRows.length?latestRows:withDate);
    group.sort(function(a,b){
      if((a.batchIndex||0)!==(b.batchIndex||0)){return (a.batchIndex||0)-(b.batchIndex||0);}
      return (a.rank||0)-(b.rank||0);
    });
    return group.slice(0,9);
  }
  function rowHtml(run, idx, hidden){
    var actualMap=mapFrom(run.actualMain);
    var extraMap=mapFrom(run.actualExtra);
    var groupNum=(run.savedRecommendationRank||0)?run.savedRecommendationRank:(idx+1);
    return '<article class="mle-v104-run-report__row'+(hidden?' mle-v104-hidden-item':'')+'" data-mle-v104-row-index="'+idx+'" data-mle-saved-recommendation-rank="'+esc(String(groupNum))+'">'
      + '<div><strong>Group #'+esc(String(groupNum))+'</strong><small>'+esc(run.date)+'<br>'+esc(run.method)+(run.label?' | '+esc(run.label):'')+'</small></div>'
      + '<div><span class="mle-v104-run-report__cell-label">Predicted numbers</span>'+splitBallHtml(run.predictedMain,run.predictedExtra,actualMap,extraMap,'mle-v104-ball--predicted','mle-v104-ball--extra')+'</div>'
      + '<div><span class="mle-v104-run-report__cell-label">Actual draw</span>'+splitBallHtml(run.actualMain,run.actualExtra,null,null,'mle-v104-ball--actual','mle-v104-ball--extra')+'</div>'
      + '<div class="mle-v104-hitbox"><strong>'+esc(String(run.totalHits||0))+'</strong><small>Total hits<br>Main: '+esc(String(run.mainHits||0))+' | Extra: '+esc(String(run.extraHits||0))+'<br>Top 20: '+esc(String(run.top20||0))+' | Top 10: '+esc(String(run.top10||0))+'</small></div>'
      + '</article>';
  }
  function openCard(card){
    if(!card){return;}
    var btn=qs('.mle-advisory-card__toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle],.mle-lottery-outer-toggle',card);
    if(btn && /expand/i.test(txt(btn))){btn.click();}
    qsa('details',card).forEach(function(d){d.open=true;});
  }
  function scrollToReport(card){
    openCard(card);
    var report=qs('.mle-v104-run-report',card);
    if(report){
      try{report.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'});}catch(e){report.scrollIntoView(true);}
      report.classList.add('mle-v104-flash');
      setTimeout(function(){report.classList.remove('mle-v104-flash');},1900);
    }
  }
  function buildReport(card){
    if(!card || card.getAttribute('data-mle-v104-built')==='1'){return;}
    var body=qs('.mle-advisory-card__body',card) || card;
    var old=qs('.mle-v104-run-report',card); if(old&&old.parentNode){old.parentNode.removeChild(old);}
    var completedDomRows=completedRows(card);
    var manifestStatus=(window.mlePrintManifestStatus?window.mlePrintManifestStatus(card,completedDomRows):null);
    var runs=completedDomRows.map(parseRow);
    applySavedRecommendationRanks(runs);
    var firstNine=latestBatchRows(runs);
    var integrity=v104BatchPredictionIntegrity(firstNine);
    var scoredRecommendationSet=firstNine.length?firstNine:runs;
    var hiddenPool=runs.filter(function(r){return firstNine.indexOf(r)<0;}).slice(0,9);
    var best=integrity.warning?null:bestRun(scoredRecommendationSet);
    var topPreDrawRecommendation=integrity.warning?null:findRecommendationBySavedRank(scoredRecommendationSet,1);
    var secondPreDrawRecommendation=integrity.warning?null:findRecommendationBySavedRank(scoredRecommendationSet,2);
    var bestPostDrawResult=best;
    var pending=pendingRows(card).length;
    var last=getLastDrawData(card);
    var report=document.createElement('section');
    report.className='mle-v104-run-report' + (integrity.warning ? ' mle-v104-run-report--integrity-warning' : '');
    report.setAttribute('aria-label','Previous 9-run batch report for '+cardTitle(card));
    report.setAttribute('data-mle-v104-run-count',String(firstNine.length));
    report.setAttribute('data-mle-v104-pending-count',String(pending));
    var listHtml='';
    firstNine.forEach(function(r,i){listHtml+=rowHtml(r,i,false);});
    if(!listHtml){
      listHtml='<div class="mle-v104-empty"><strong>No scored previous 9-run batch is visible yet.</strong><br>When the prior 9-run batch is scored after the official draw, this report will show the saved predictions, the actual draw, and what each prediction hit. Pending runs are still waiting for official results.</div>';
    }
    var hiddenHtml='';
    hiddenPool.forEach(function(r,i){hiddenHtml+=rowHtml(r,i+firstNine.length,true);});
    var topPreDrawText=integrity.warning
      ? 'Batch integrity warning: duplicate saved prediction payloads detected.'
      : (topPreDrawRecommendation
        ? ('Top pre-draw recommendation: Group #'+String(topPreDrawRecommendation.savedRecommendationRank||1)+', '+String(topPreDrawRecommendation.postDrawHitCount||0)+' hits.')
        : 'Top pre-draw recommendation: Not available for this saved recommendation set.');
    var secondPreDrawText=integrity.warning
      ? 'This batch is shown for audit only. Do not use it as clean SKAI evidence until it is rerun.'
      : (secondPreDrawRecommendation
        ? ('Second pre-draw recommendation: Group #'+String(secondPreDrawRecommendation.savedRecommendationRank||2)+', '+String(secondPreDrawRecommendation.postDrawHitCount||0)+' hits.')
        : 'Second pre-draw recommendation: Not available for this saved recommendation set.');
    var bestPostDrawText=integrity.warning
      ? 'Duplicate predictions found: '+String(integrity.unique)+' unique prediction set(s) across '+String(integrity.total)+' visible rows.'
      : (bestPostDrawResult
        ? ('Best post-draw result in this saved recommendation set: Group #'+String(bestPostDrawResult.savedRecommendationRank||0)+' caught '+String(bestPostDrawResult.postDrawHitCount||0)+' numbers.')
        : 'Best post-draw result in this saved recommendation set: Not available yet.');
    var bestPostDrawNotTopNote=(bestPostDrawResult && (bestPostDrawResult.savedRecommendationRank||0)!==1)
      ? 'This was not the #1 pre-draw recommendation. It was the strongest result after scoring.'
      : '';
    var integrityAlertHtml = integrity.warning
      ? '<div class="mle-v104-integrity-alert" role="alert"><strong>Batch integrity warning</strong><p>Multiple run labels saved the exact same prediction set. LottoExpert is showing these rows for audit, but this batch should not be treated as clean comparative evidence. Rerun the 9-run batch after installing the SKAI snapshot integrity hotfix.</p></div>'
      : '';
    
    
    report.innerHTML=''
      + '<div class="mle-v104-run-report__hero"><div><span class="mle-v104-run-report__eyebrow">'+esc(integrity.warning?'Batch integrity review':((manifestStatus&&manifestStatus.has_manifest)?'Print verified scored batch':'Exact-draw scored prediction evidence'))+'</span><h3>'+esc(integrity.warning?'Batch Integrity Review':((manifestStatus&&manifestStatus.has_manifest)?'Print Verified Scored Batch':'Exact-Draw Scored Prediction Evidence'))+'</h3><p>'+esc(integrity.warning?'Duplicate prediction payloads were detected across the visible batch rows. This view is preserved for audit only until the batch is rerun.':((manifestStatus&&manifestStatus.has_manifest)?('This report is locked to the exact pre-draw printed manifest. Manifest hash: '+(manifestStatus.hash||'')+'. Matched rows: '+String(manifestStatus.match_count||firstNine.length)+'.'):'No saved print manifest was matched for this view. Only saved predictions tied to this exact draw should be treated as comparable. Legacy visible evidence is shown only when it is tied to the same draw, and is not print verified.'))+'</p></div>'
      + '<div class="mle-v104-run-report__metrics"><div class="mle-v104-run-report__metric"><span>Batch predictions shown</span><strong>'+esc(String(firstNine.length))+'</strong></div><div class="mle-v104-run-report__metric"><span>Unique prediction sets</span><strong>'+esc(String(integrity.unique||firstNine.length))+'</strong></div><div class="mle-v104-run-report__metric"><span>Pending now</span><strong>'+esc(String(pending))+'</strong></div></div></div>'
      + integrityAlertHtml
      + '<div class="mle-v104-run-report__body"><div class="mle-v104-run-report__summary"><div class="mle-v104-run-report__summary-card"><span>Latest actual draw</span><strong>'+esc(last.date||'Not loaded yet')+'</strong><p>'+((last.actual.length||last.extra.length)?splitBallHtml(last.actual,last.extra,null,null,'mle-v104-ball--actual','mle-v104-ball--extra'):'The latest official numbers were not found in this card yet.')+'</p></div><div class="mle-v104-run-report__summary-card"><span>Top pre-draw recommendation</span><strong>'+esc(topPreDrawText)+'</strong><p>'+esc(secondPreDrawText)+'<br>'+esc(bestPostDrawText)+(bestPostDrawNotTopNote?('<br>'+esc(bestPostDrawNotTopNote)):'')+'</p></div></div>'
      + '<div class="mle-v104-run-report__actions"><button type="button" class="mle-v104-run-report__btn mle-v104-run-report__btn--primary" data-mle-v104-action="print-results">Print Previous Batch</button><button type="button" class="mle-v104-run-report__btn" data-mle-v104-action="toggle-more">Show More Scored Runs</button><button type="button" class="mle-v104-run-report__btn" data-mle-v104-action="jump-visual">Open optimizer evidence</button></div>'
      + '<div class="mle-v104-run-report__list">'+listHtml+'</div>'+(hiddenHtml?'<div class="mle-v104-hidden-rows">'+hiddenHtml+'</div>':'')+'</div>';
    var anchor=qs('.mle-v102-after-draw-proof,.mle-v99-recommendation-first,.mle-v34-priority-stack,.mle-v73-path',body);
    if(anchor && anchor.parentNode){anchor.parentNode.insertBefore(report,anchor.nextSibling);} else {body.insertBefore(report,body.firstChild);}
    card.setAttribute('data-mle-v104-built','1');
  }
  function buildPill(card){
    if(!card || qs('.mle-v104-history-pill',card)){return;}
    var head=qs('.mle-advisory-card__collapsed',card) || qs('.mle-advisory-card__header',card) || card;
    var completedDomRows=completedRows(card);
    var pillManifestStatus=(window.mlePrintManifestStatus?window.mlePrintManifestStatus(card,completedDomRows):null);
    var runs=completedDomRows.map(parseRow).slice(0,9);
    var best=bestRun(runs);
    var pill=document.createElement('div');
    pill.className='mle-v104-history-pill';
    pill.innerHTML='<span class="mle-v104-history-pill__kicker">'+(pillManifestStatus&&pillManifestStatus.has_manifest?'Print verified batch':'Scored history')+'</span><span class="mle-v104-history-pill__text">'+(runs.length?('View '+runs.length+' scored run'+(runs.length===1?'':'s')+'. '+(pillManifestStatus&&pillManifestStatus.has_manifest?'Matched to printed sheet. ':'Best scored visible row: ')+(best?(best.totalHits||0):0)+' total hit'+((best && (best.totalHits||0)===1)?'':'s')+'.'):'No exact scored 9-run batch is visible yet. Use Review Scored History to inspect saved, scored, and pending rows.')+'</span><button type="button" class="mle-v104-history-pill__btn">View Scored History</button>';
    var insertAfter=qs('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip',head) || qs('.mle-advisory-card__stats,.mle-adv-stat-row,.mle-scan-row',head);
    if(insertAfter && insertAfter.parentNode){insertAfter.parentNode.insertBefore(pill,insertAfter.nextSibling);}else{head.appendChild(pill);}
    qs('button',pill).addEventListener('click',function(ev){ev.preventDefault();ev.stopPropagation();buildReport(card);scrollToReport(card);});
  }
  function apply(){
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]').forEach(function(card){
      if(qs('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name',card)){
        buildReport(card);
        buildPill(card);
      }
    });
  }
  document.addEventListener('click',function(ev){
    var action=ev.target && ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('[data-mle-v104-action]') : null;
    if(!action){return;}
    var card=action.closest('.mle-advisory-card');
    var report=action.closest('.mle-v104-run-report');
    var mode=action.getAttribute('data-mle-v104-action');
    ev.preventDefault();
    if(mode==='toggle-more' && report){
      report.classList.toggle('is-expanded');
      action.textContent=report.classList.contains('is-expanded')?'Hide Extra Completed Runs':'Show More Scored Runs';
    } else if(mode==='jump-visual' && card){
      var target=qs('.mle-visual-comparison,.mle-visual-proof,.mle-learning-track',card) || qs('.mle-visual-row',card);
      if(target){qsa('details',card).forEach(function(d){d.open=true;});try{target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'});}catch(e){target.scrollIntoView(true);}}
    } else if(mode==='print-results' && card){
      var btn=qsa('button,a',card).filter(function(b){return /print\s*\/\s*reprint|print previous|result sheet|after draw/i.test(txt(b));})[0];
      if(btn){btn.click();}else if(window.print){window.print();}
    }
  });
  window.mleV104AuditPreviousRunReports=function(){
    var rows=qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]').map(function(card,i){
      return {index:i,title:cardTitle(card),lottery_id:card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id')||'',completed_rows:completedRows(card).length,pending_rows:pendingRows(card).length,report_present:!!qs('.mle-v104-run-report',card),pill_present:!!qs('.mle-v104-history-pill',card),last_draw_date:(getLastDrawData(card).date||''),last_actual:(getLastDrawData(card).actual||[]).join(',')};
    });
    if(window.console&&console.table){console.table(rows);}else if(window.console){console.log(rows);}return rows;
  };
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){setTimeout(apply,250);setTimeout(apply,1000);setTimeout(apply,2500);});
  } else {setTimeout(apply,150);setTimeout(apply,1000);setTimeout(apply,2500);}
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    if(e.target && e.target.closest && e.target.closest('.mle-advisory-card__toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle],.mle-lottery-outer-toggle')){setTimeout(apply,180);setTimeout(apply,650);}
  });
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV108UnifiedBallColorSystem) { return; }
  window.__mleV108UnifiedBallColorSystem = true;

  window.mleAuditBallColorSystem = function(){
    var rows = [];
    try {
      var selector =
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .mle-ball, .mle-elite-cockpit .mle-v100-ball, ' +
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .mle-v102-ball, .mle-elite-cockpit .mle-v104-ball, ' +
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .mle-official-draw-ball, ' +
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .mle-official-pred-ball, ' +
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball, ' +
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .prc-num, .mle-elite-cockpit .prc-num-hit, ' +
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .prc-num-extra, ' +
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .prc-num-extra-hit, ' +
        '.mle-elite-cockpit .prc-num-extra-miss';
      var balls = Array.prototype.slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
      balls.forEach(function(ball, idx){
        try {
          var cn = String(ball.className || '');
          var cs = window.getComputedStyle ? window.getComputedStyle(ball) : {};
          var hasExtra = /--extra|--bonus|prc-num-extra/.test(cn);
          var hasPredicted = /--predicted|official-pred-ball/.test(cn);
          var hasHit = /--hit|prc-num-hit|prc-num-extra-hit/.test(cn);
          var hasActual = /--actual|official-draw-ball/.test(cn) && !/official-pred/.test(cn);
          var isPrcExtraHit = /prc-num-extra-hit/.test(cn);
          var isPrcExtraMiss = /prc-num-extra-miss/.test(cn);
          var isPrcExtraGen = /prc-num-extra/.test(cn) && !isPrcExtraHit && !isPrcExtraMiss;
          var isPrcMainHit = /prc-num-hit/.test(cn) && !isPrcExtraHit;
          var isPrcMain = /\bprc-num\b/.test(cn) && !hasHit && !hasExtra && !isPrcExtraHit && !isPrcExtraMiss;
          var isActualMain = false, isActualExtra = false;
          var isPredictedMain = false, isPredictedExtra = false;
          var isMainHit = false, isExtraHit = false;
          var role = 'unknown';
          if (isPrcExtraHit || (hasExtra && hasHit && !hasActual)) {
            isExtraHit = true; role = 'predicted_extra_hit';
          } else if (isPrcExtraMiss || (isPrcExtraGen && !hasHit)) {
            isPredictedExtra = true; role = 'predicted_extra_miss';
          } else if (isPrcMainHit || (hasHit && !hasExtra && !hasActual)) {
            isMainHit = true; role = 'predicted_main_hit';
          } else if (isPrcMain || (hasPredicted && !hasExtra && !hasHit)) {
            isPredictedMain = true; role = 'predicted_main_miss';
          } else if (hasActual && hasExtra) {
            isActualExtra = true; role = 'actual_extra';
          } else if (hasActual && !hasExtra) {
            isActualMain = true; role = 'actual_main';
          } else if (hasExtra && !hasPredicted && !hasHit) {
            isActualExtra = true; role = 'actual_extra';
          } else {
            isActualMain = true; role = 'actual_main';
          }
          var numTxt = String(ball.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g,'').slice(0,6);
          var bg = String(cs.backgroundColor || '');
          var color = String(cs.color || '');
          var border = String(cs.borderTopColor || '');
          var warning = '';
          if ((role === 'actual_main' || role === 'predicted_main_hit') &&
              /rgba?\(255,\s*255,\s*255/.test(color)) {
            warning = 'White text OK for green ball.';
          }
          if (role === 'predicted_main_miss' &&
              /rgba?\(255,\s*255,\s*255/.test(color)) {
            warning = 'WARNING: white text on light predicted ball.';
          }
          if (role === 'predicted_extra_miss' &&
              /rgba?\(255,\s*255,\s*255/.test(color)) {
            warning = 'WARNING: white text on soft red predicted extra.';
          }
          if ((role === 'actual_main' || role === 'actual_extra') &&
              /rgba?\(248,\s*25[0-9]/.test(bg)) {
            warning = 'WARNING: actual ball appears near-white, not role color.';
          }
          rows.push({
            index: idx,
            text: numTxt,
            className: cn.slice(0, 72),
            roleInferred: role,
            color: color,
            backgroundColor: bg,
            borderColor: border,
            contrastWarning: warning,
            isActualMain: isActualMain,
            isActualExtra: isActualExtra,
            isPredictedMain: isPredictedMain,
            isPredictedExtra: isPredictedExtra,
            isMainHit: isMainHit,
            isExtraHit: isExtraHit
          });
        } catch (innerErr) {
          rows.push({
            index: idx, text: '', className: '',
            roleInferred: 'error',
            contrastWarning: String(innerErr)
          });
        }
      });
    } catch (outerErr) {
      if (window.console) {
        console.error('mleAuditBallColorSystem: ' + String(outerErr));
      }
    }
    if (window.console && console.table) { console.table(rows); }
    else if (window.console) { console.log(rows); }
    return rows;
  };
})();


(function () {
  'use strict';

  if (window.__mleV112Init) { return; }
  window.__mleV112Init = true;

  
  
  

  function hasC(el, c) {
    return el && typeof el.className === 'string' && (' ' + el.className + ' ').indexOf(' ' + c + ' ') !== -1;
  }

  function addC(el, c) {
    if (!hasC(el, c)) {
      el.className = (el.className ? el.className + ' ' + c : c);
    }
  }

  function remC(el, c) {
    if (!el || !el.className) { return; }
    el.className = el.className.replace(
      new RegExp('(?:^|\\s)' + c.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + '(?=\\s|$)', 'g'),
      ''
    ).replace(/\s\s+/g, ' ').trim();
  }

  function ancestorMatch(el, sel) {
    var p = el ? el.parentElement : null;
    while (p) {
      try {
        if (p.matches && p.matches(sel)) { return true; }
      } catch (ex) {}
      p = p.parentElement;
    }
    return false;
  }

  function closestCardFromEl(el) {
    var p = el;
    while (p) {
      if (p.getAttribute && (
          p.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') ||
          hasC(p, 'mle-advisory-card') ||
          hasC(p, 'mle-optimization-card') ||
          hasC(p, 'mle-ci-lottery-card')
        )) {
        return p;
      }
      p = p.parentElement;
    }
    return null;
  }

  function showMsg(near, txt, color) {
    if (!near) { return; }
    var msg = document.createElement('span');
    msg.style.cssText = 'display:inline-block;margin-left:8px;padding:3px 8px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;background:' + (color || '#fee2e2') + ';color:#7f1d1d;';
    msg.textContent = txt;
    if (near.parentElement) { near.parentElement.insertBefore(msg, near.nextSibling); }
    setTimeout(function () { if (msg.parentElement) { msg.parentElement.removeChild(msg); } }, 5000);
  }

  
  
  

  var ROLE_CLASSES = [
    'mle-ball-role-actual-main',
    'mle-ball-role-actual-extra',
    'mle-ball-role-pred-main',
    'mle-ball-role-pred-main-hit',
    'mle-ball-role-pred-extra',
    'mle-ball-role-pred-extra-hit',
    'mle-ball-role-neutral'
  ];

  function inferRole(el) {
    var cls = typeof el.className === 'string' ? el.className : '';
    var isExtra = cls.indexOf('--extra') !== -1 ||
                  hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra') ||
                  hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-hit') ||
                  hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-miss') ||
                  hasC(el, 'mle-ball--bonus');
    var isHit = cls.indexOf('--hit') !== -1 ||
                hasC(el, 'mle-ball--match') ||
                hasC(el, 'prc-num-hit') ||
                hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-hit');
    var isPred = cls.indexOf('--predicted') !== -1 ||
                 hasC(el, 'mle-official-pred-ball') ||
                 hasC(el, 'prc-num') ||
                 hasC(el, 'mle-v104-ball');

    
    if (hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-hit')) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
    if (hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-miss') || (hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra') && !isHit)) { return 'pred-extra'; }
    if (hasC(el, 'prc-num-hit')) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
    if (hasC(el, 'prc-num') && !isHit) { return 'pred-main'; }

    
    if (hasC(el, 'mle-official-draw-ball')) {
      return isExtra ? 'actual-extra' : 'actual-main';
    }

    
    if (hasC(el, 'mle-official-pred-ball')) {
      return isHit ? 'pred-main-hit' : 'pred-main';
    }

    
    if (hasC(el, 'mle-v100-ball')) {
      if (isExtra && isHit) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
      if (isExtra) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      if (isHit) { return 'actual-main'; }
      
      var inPredCol = ancestorMatch(el,
        '.mle-v100-afterdraw__cell ~ .mle-v100-afterdraw__cell,' +
        '.mle-v100-pred-row,.mle-v100-pred-col,.mle-v100-prediction');
      return inPredCol ? 'pred-main' : 'actual-main';
    }

    
    if (hasC(el, 'mle-v102-ball')) {
      if (isPred && isExtra && isHit) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
      if (isPred && isExtra) { return 'pred-extra'; }
      if (isExtra && isHit) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      if (isExtra) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      if (isPred && isHit) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
      if (isPred) { return 'pred-main'; }
      return 'actual-main';
    }

    
    if (hasC(el, 'mle-v104-ball')) {
      if (isExtra && isHit) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
      if (isExtra) { return 'pred-extra'; }
      if (isHit) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
      return 'pred-main';
    }

    
    if (hasC(el, 'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball')) {
      var isPredicted = cls.indexOf('--predicted') !== -1;
      if (isPredicted && isExtra && isHit) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
      if (isPredicted && isExtra) { return 'pred-extra'; }
      if (isPredicted && isHit) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
      if (isPredicted) { return 'pred-main'; }
      if (isExtra && isHit) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      if (isExtra) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      return 'actual-main';
    }

    
    if (hasC(el, 'mle-ball')) {
      if (cls.indexOf('mle-ball--bonus') !== -1 && isHit) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
      if (cls.indexOf('mle-ball--bonus') !== -1) { return 'pred-extra'; }
      if (cls.indexOf('mle-ball--extra') !== -1 && isHit) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      if (cls.indexOf('mle-ball--extra') !== -1) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      if (isHit || cls.indexOf('mle-ball--match') !== -1) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
      if (cls.indexOf('mle-ball--actual') !== -1) { return 'actual-main'; }
      
      if (ancestorMatch(el, '.mle-rs-group--keep,.mle-rs-run--keep,.mle-rs-item--keep')) {
        return 'actual-main';
      }
      return 'neutral';
    }

    return 'neutral';
  }

  function applyRoleToEl(el) {
    var role = inferRole(el);
    addC(el, 'mle-ball-core');
    for (var i = 0; i < ROLE_CLASSES.length; i++) { remC(el, ROLE_CLASSES[i]); }
    addC(el, 'mle-ball-role-' + role);
    try { el.setAttribute('data-ball-role', role); } catch (ex) {}
  }

  var BALL_SEL = [
    '.mle-ball',
    '.mle-v100-ball',
    '.mle-v102-ball',
    '.mle-v104-ball',
    '.mle-official-draw-ball',
    '.mle-official-pred-ball',
    '.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball',
    '.prc-num',
    '.prc-num-hit',
    '.prc-num-extra',
    '.prc-num-extra-hit',
    '.prc-num-extra-miss'
  ].join(',');

  window.mleAssignBallRoles = function (scope) {
    var root = scope || document;
    if (!root.querySelectorAll) { return; }
    var balls = root.querySelectorAll(BALL_SEL);
    for (var i = 0; i < balls.length; i++) {
      try { applyRoleToEl(balls[i]); } catch (ex) {}
    }
  };

  
  
  

  window.mleFindCardFromTrigger = function (trigger) {
    return closestCardFromEl(trigger);
  };

  window.mleOpenCard = function (card) {
    if (!card) { return; }
    var bodies = card.querySelectorAll ? card.querySelectorAll('[aria-hidden="true"]') : [];
    for (var i = 0; i < bodies.length; i++) {
      bodies[i].style.display = 'block';
      bodies[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
    }
    var toggles = card.querySelectorAll ? card.querySelectorAll('[aria-expanded="false"]') : [];
    for (var j = 0; j < toggles.length; j++) {
      toggles[j].setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
    }
  };

  window.mleOpenDetailsParents = function (el) {
    var p = el ? el.parentElement : null;
    while (p) {
      if (p.tagName === 'DETAILS') { p.open = true; }
      if (p.getAttribute && p.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'true') {
        p.style.display = 'block';
        p.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
      }
      p = p.parentElement;
    }
  };

  window.mleScrollToTarget = function (target) {
    if (!target) { return; }
    try {
      if (target.scrollIntoView) { target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' }); }
    } catch (ex) {
      try { target.scrollIntoView(true); } catch (ex2) {}
    }
  };

  
  window.mleOpenPendingRunsForCard = function (trigger) {
    if (typeof window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource === 'function') {
      return window.mleOpenPendingRunsSource(trigger);
    }
    return false;
  };

  window.mleOpenPreviousBatchReportForCard = function (trigger) {
    var card = window.mleFindCardFromTrigger(trigger);
    if (!card) { showMsg(trigger, 'Could not find lottery card.', '#fee2e2'); return false; }
    window.mleOpenCard(card);
    var lid = card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
    var batchEl = null;
    if (lid) {
      batchEl = document.getElementById('mle-batch-report-' + lid) ||
                document.getElementById('mle-v75-report-' + lid) ||
                document.getElementById('mle-9run-report-' + lid);
    }
    if (!batchEl) {
      var bs = card.querySelectorAll ? card.querySelectorAll('[id*="batch-report"],[id*="9run"],[id*="v75-report"]') : [];
      if (bs.length > 0) { batchEl = bs[0]; }
    }
    if (!batchEl) { showMsg(trigger, 'Batch report section not found.', '#fee2e2'); return false; }
    window.mleOpenDetailsParents(batchEl);
    batchEl.style.display = 'block';
    batchEl.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
    setTimeout(function () { window.mleAssignBallRoles(batchEl); }, 100);
    window.mleScrollToTarget(batchEl);
    return true;
  };

  window.mleOpenDetailedProofRowsForCard = function (trigger) {
    var card = window.mleFindCardFromTrigger(trigger);
    if (!card) { showMsg(trigger, 'Could not find lottery card.', '#fee2e2'); return false; }
    window.mleOpenCard(card);
    var lid = card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
    var proofEl = null;
    if (lid) {
      proofEl = document.getElementById('mle-proof-rows-' + lid) ||
                document.getElementById('mle-evidence-' + lid);
    }
    if (!proofEl) {
      var ps = card.querySelectorAll ? card.querySelectorAll('[id*="proof-rows"],[id*="evidence"]') : [];
      if (ps.length > 0) { proofEl = ps[0]; }
    }
    if (!proofEl) { showMsg(trigger, 'Proof rows section not found.', '#fee2e2'); return false; }
    window.mleOpenDetailsParents(proofEl);
    proofEl.style.display = 'block';
    proofEl.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
    setTimeout(function () { window.mleAssignBallRoles(proofEl); }, 100);
    window.mleScrollToTarget(proofEl);
    return true;
  };

  
  
  

  window.mleAuditBallColorSystem = function () {
    if (!document.querySelectorAll) {
      if (typeof console !== 'undefined' && console.log) { console.log('[V112] mleAuditBallColorSystem: document.querySelectorAll not available'); }
      return;
    }
    var balls = document.querySelectorAll(BALL_SEL);
    if (!balls || balls.length === 0) {
      if (typeof console !== 'undefined' && console.log) { console.log('[V112] mleAuditBallColorSystem: no ball elements found'); }
      return;
    }
    var rows = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < balls.length; i++) {
      var el = balls[i];
      var cs = window.getComputedStyle ? window.getComputedStyle(el) : null;
      var bg = cs ? cs.backgroundColor : '';
      var fg = cs ? cs.color : '';
      var bd = cs ? cs.borderColor : '';
      var role = el.getAttribute('data-ball-role') || '(none)';
      var cls = el.className || '';
      var txt = (el.textContent || el.innerText || '').replace(/\s+/g, '');
      var hasBallCore = cls.indexOf('mle-ball-core') !== -1;
      var warn = '';
      var isGreen = bg.indexOf('22, 163') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('22,163') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('74, 222') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('74,222') !== -1;
      var isRed = bg.indexOf('220, 38') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('220,38') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('239, 68') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('239,68') !== -1;
      var isSoftRed = bg.indexOf('254, 226') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('254,226') !== -1;
      var isWhite = bg.indexOf('255, 255') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('255,255') !== -1;
      var isLightBlue = bg.indexOf('219, 234') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('219,234') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('237, 242') !== -1 || bg.indexOf('237,242') !== -1;
      if (isLightBlue) { warn = 'LEGACY BLUE - role not applied'; }
      if (isWhite && (fg.indexOf('255, 255') !== -1 || fg.indexOf('255,255') !== -1)) { warn = 'WHITE TEXT ON LIGHT BALL'; }
      if (!hasBallCore) { warn = (warn ? warn + ' | ' : '') + 'mle-ball-core MISSING'; }
      rows.push({
        index: i,
        text: txt,
        className: cls.substring(0, 60),
        role: role,
        backgroundColor: bg,
        color: fg,
        borderColor: bd,
        warning: warn,
        hasBallCore: hasBallCore
      });
    }
    if (typeof console !== 'undefined') {
      if (console.group) { console.group('[V112] mleAuditBallColorSystem (' + rows.length + ' balls)'); }
      if (console.table) { console.table(rows); } else { console.log(rows); }
      if (console.groupEnd) { console.groupEnd(); }
    }
    return rows;
  };

  
  
  

  window.mleAuditBallCssConflicts = function () {
    var legacyKeywords = [
      '.mle-ball{', '.mle-ball--match{', '.mle-ball--extra{',
      '.mle-v100-ball{', '.mle-v102-ball{', '.mle-v104-ball{',
      '.mle-official-draw-ball{', '.mle-official-pred-ball{',
      '.prc-num{', '.prc-num-hit{'
    ];
    var report = [];
    if (!document.styleSheets) {
      if (typeof console !== 'undefined' && console.log) { console.log('[V112] mleAuditBallCssConflicts: document.styleSheets not available'); }
      return;
    }
    var sheets = document.styleSheets;
    for (var s = 0; s < sheets.length; s++) {
      var sheet = sheets[s];
      var rules = null;
      try { rules = sheet.cssRules || sheet.rules; } catch (ex) { continue; }
      if (!rules) { continue; }
      for (var r = 0; r < rules.length; r++) {
        var rule = rules[r];
        var sel = rule.selectorText || '';
        for (var k = 0; k < legacyKeywords.length; k++) {
          if (sel && sel.indexOf(legacyKeywords[k].replace('{', '')) !== -1) {
            var hasImportant = rule.cssText && rule.cssText.indexOf('!important') !== -1;
            report.push({
              sheet: sheet.href || '(inline)',
              selector: sel.substring(0, 80),
              hasImportant: hasImportant,
              warning: hasImportant ? 'IMPORTANT - may conflict' : 'no !important'
            });
          }
        }
      }
    }
    if (typeof console !== 'undefined') {
      if (console.group) { console.group('[V112] mleAuditBallCssConflicts (' + report.length + ' matches)'); }
      if (console.table) { console.table(report); } else { console.log(report); }
      if (console.groupEnd) { console.groupEnd(); }
    }
    return report;
  };

  
  
  

  function fullInit() {
    window.mleAssignBallRoles(document);
  }

  
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () { setTimeout(fullInit, 150); });
  } else {
    setTimeout(fullInit, 150);
  }
  setTimeout(function () { window.mleAssignBallRoles(document); }, 1600);
  setTimeout(function () { window.mleAssignBallRoles(document); }, 3200);
  setTimeout(function () { window.mleAssignBallRoles(document); }, 5600);

  
  document.addEventListener('click', function () {
    setTimeout(function () {
      window.mleAssignBallRoles(document);
    }, 350);
  });

})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  window.mleAuditSequentialBatchPhases = function(){
    var cards = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-advisory-card');
    var rows = [];
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(cards, function(card){
      var titleEl = card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name');
      var title = titleEl ? titleEl.textContent.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '') : '';
      var roadmap = card.querySelector('[data-mle-batch-roadmap="1"]');
      var forms = card.querySelectorAll('form input[name="mle_action"][value="create_skai_batch"]');
      var formPlans = [];
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(forms, function(inp){
        var form = inp.form;
        var plan = form && form.querySelector('input[name="mle_batch_plan"]') ? form.querySelector('input[name="mle_batch_plan"]').value : '';
        formPlans.push(plan || 'missing');
      });
      rows.push({
        card_title: title,
        roadmap_found: !!roadmap,
        create_batch_forms: forms.length,
        requested_plans: formPlans.join(','),
        has_horizon_form: formPlans.join(',').indexOf('horizon') !== -1,
        has_settings_form: formPlans.join(',').indexOf('settings') !== -1,
        warning: forms.length > 0 && formPlans.join(',').indexOf('missing') !== -1 ? 'A create batch form is missing mle_batch_plan.' : ''
      });
    });
    if (window.console && console.table) { console.table(rows); }
    return rows;
  };
}());


(function(){
  'use strict';

  function hasC(el, c) {
    return el && typeof el.className === 'string' && (' ' + el.className + ' ').indexOf(' ' + c + ' ') !== -1;
  }

  function addC(el, c) {
    if (el && !hasC(el, c)) {
      el.className = el.className ? el.className + ' ' + c : c;
    }
  }

  function remC(el, c) {
    if (!el || typeof el.className !== 'string') { return; }
    el.className = el.className.replace(new RegExp('(?:^|\\s)' + c.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + '(?=\\s|$)', 'g'), '').replace(/\s\s+/g, ' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
  }

  function ancestorHas(el, className) {
    var p = el ? el.parentElement : null;
    while (p) {
      if (hasC(p, className)) { return true; }
      p = p.parentElement;
    }
    return false;
  }

  function clearRoles(el) {
    var roles = [
      'mle-ball-role-actual-main',
      'mle-ball-role-actual-extra',
      'mle-ball-role-pred-main',
      'mle-ball-role-pred-main-hit',
      'mle-ball-role-pred-extra',
      'mle-ball-role-pred-extra-hit',
      'mle-ball-role-neutral'
    ];
    var i;
    for (i = 0; i < roles.length; i++) { remC(el, roles[i]); }
  }

  function inferRole(el) {
    var cls = typeof el.className === 'string' ? el.className : '';
    var isOuter = hasC(el, 'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball');
    var isV102 = hasC(el, 'mle-v102-ball');
    var isV104 = hasC(el, 'mle-v104-ball');
    var isOfficialDraw = hasC(el, 'mle-official-draw-ball');
    var isOfficialPred = hasC(el, 'mle-official-pred-ball');
    var isPred = cls.indexOf('--predicted') !== -1 || isOfficialPred || hasC(el, 'mle-ball--predicted');
    var isExtra = cls.indexOf('--extra') !== -1 || hasC(el, 'mle-ball--bonus') || hasC(el, 'mle-ball--extra') || hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra') || hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-hit') || hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-miss');
    var isHit = cls.indexOf('--hit') !== -1 || hasC(el, 'mle-ball--match') || hasC(el, 'prc-num-hit') || hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-hit');

    if (hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-hit')) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
    if (hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra-miss') || hasC(el, 'prc-num-extra')) { return 'pred-extra'; }
    if (hasC(el, 'prc-num-hit')) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
    if (hasC(el, 'prc-num')) { return 'pred-main'; }

    if (isOfficialDraw) { return isExtra ? 'actual-extra' : 'actual-main'; }
    if (isOfficialPred) { return isHit ? 'pred-main-hit' : 'pred-main'; }

    if (isOuter || isV102) {
      if (isPred && isExtra && isHit) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
      if (isPred && isExtra) { return 'pred-extra'; }
      if (isPred && isHit) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
      if (isPred) { return 'pred-main'; }
      if (isExtra) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      return 'actual-main';
    }

    if (isV104) {
      if (isExtra && isHit) { return 'pred-extra-hit'; }
      if (isExtra) { return 'pred-extra'; }
      if (isHit) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
      return 'pred-main';
    }

    if (hasC(el, 'mle-ball')) {
      if ((hasC(el, 'mle-ball--bonus') || hasC(el, 'mle-ball--extra')) && (isPred || ancestorHas(el, 'mle-pending') || ancestorHas(el, 'mle-v104-previous-batch'))) {
        return isHit ? 'pred-extra-hit' : 'pred-extra';
      }
      if (hasC(el, 'mle-ball--bonus') || hasC(el, 'mle-ball--extra')) { return 'actual-extra'; }
      if (isHit) { return 'pred-main-hit'; }
      if (hasC(el, 'mle-ball--actual')) { return 'actual-main'; }
      if (isPred || ancestorHas(el, 'mle-pending') || ancestorHas(el, 'mle-v104-previous-batch')) { return 'pred-main'; }
    }

    return 'neutral';
  }

  function apply(el) {
    var role;
    if (!el) { return; }
    role = inferRole(el);
    addC(el, 'mle-ball-core');
    clearRoles(el);
    addC(el, 'mle-ball-role-' + role);
    try { el.setAttribute('data-ball-role', role); } catch (ex) {}
    if (!el.getAttribute('data-ball-number')) {
      try { el.setAttribute('data-ball-number', (el.textContent || '').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '')); } catch (ex2) {}
    }
  }

  function run(scope) {
    var root = scope || document;
    var q = '.mle-ball,.mle-v100-ball,.mle-v102-ball,.mle-v103-ball,.mle-v104-ball,.mle-v105-ball,.mle-v106-ball,.mle-v107-ball,.mle-official-draw-ball,.mle-official-pred-ball,.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball,.prc-num,.prc-num-hit,.prc-num-extra,.prc-num-extra-hit,.prc-num-extra-miss';
    var nodes;
    var i;
    if (!root.querySelectorAll) { return; }
    nodes = root.querySelectorAll(q);
    for (i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
      try { apply(nodes[i]); } catch (ex) {}
    }
  }

  window.mleV118RestoreBallColors = run;

  window.mleAuditBallColorSystem = function(){
    var q = '.mle-ball-core,.mle-ball,.mle-v102-ball,.mle-v104-ball,.mle-official-draw-ball,.mle-official-pred-ball,.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball,.prc-num,.prc-num-hit,.prc-num-extra,.prc-num-extra-hit,.prc-num-extra-miss';
    var nodes = document.querySelectorAll(q);
    var rows = [];
    var i;
    var st;
    for (i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
      st = window.getComputedStyle ? window.getComputedStyle(nodes[i]) : null;
      rows.push({
        index: i,
        text: (nodes[i].textContent || '').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, ''),
        role: nodes[i].getAttribute('data-ball-role') || '',
        className: nodes[i].className,
        color: st ? st.color : '',
        backgroundColor: st ? st.backgroundColor : '',
        borderColor: st ? st.borderColor : ''
      });
    }
    if (window.console && console.table) { console.table(rows); }
    return rows;
  };

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ setTimeout(run, 0); setTimeout(run, 350); setTimeout(run, 1200); });
  } else {
    setTimeout(run, 0);
    setTimeout(run, 350);
    setTimeout(run, 1200);
  }
  if (window.addEventListener) {
    window.addEventListener('load', function(){ setTimeout(run, 100); setTimeout(run, 900); });
  }
}());


(function(){
  'use strict';
  function hasC(el,c){return !!(el && typeof el.className === 'string' && (' '+el.className+' ').indexOf(' '+c+' ') !== -1);}
  function addC(el,c){if(el && !hasC(el,c)){el.className = el.className ? el.className + ' ' + c : c;}}
  function remC(el,c){if(!el || typeof el.className !== 'string'){return;} el.className = el.className.replace(new RegExp('(?:^|\\s)' + c.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g,'\\$&') + '(?=\\s|$)','g'),'').replace(/\s\s+/g,' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');}
  function clearRoles(el){var r=['mle-ball-role-actual-main','mle-ball-role-actual-extra','mle-ball-role-pred-main','mle-ball-role-pred-main-hit','mle-ball-role-pred-extra','mle-ball-role-pred-extra-hit','mle-ball-role-neutral'];var i;for(i=0;i<r.length;i++){remC(el,r[i]);}}
  function inferRole(el){
    var cls = el && typeof el.className === 'string' ? el.className : '';
    var isPred = cls.indexOf('--predicted') !== -1 || hasC(el,'mle-ball--predicted') || hasC(el,'mle-official-pred-ball');
    var isActual = hasC(el,'mle-ball--actual') || hasC(el,'mle-official-draw-ball');
    var isExtra = cls.indexOf('--extra') !== -1 || hasC(el,'mle-ball--extra') || hasC(el,'mle-ball--bonus') || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra') || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra-hit') || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra-miss');
    var isHit = cls.indexOf('--hit') !== -1 || hasC(el,'mle-ball--match') || hasC(el,'prc-num-hit') || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra-hit');
    if(hasC(el,'prc-num-extra-hit')){return 'pred-extra-hit';}
    if(hasC(el,'prc-num-extra') || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra-miss')){return 'pred-extra';}
    if(hasC(el,'prc-num-hit')){return 'pred-main-hit';}
    if(hasC(el,'prc-num')){return 'pred-main';}
    if(isPred && isExtra && isHit){return 'pred-extra-hit';}
    if(isPred && isExtra){return 'pred-extra';}
    if(isPred && isHit){return 'pred-main-hit';}
    if(isPred){return 'pred-main';}
    if(isActual && isExtra){return 'actual-extra';}
    if(isActual){return 'actual-main';}
    if(isExtra && hasC(el,'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball')){return 'actual-extra';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball')){return 'actual-main';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-v102-ball') && isExtra){return 'actual-extra';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-v102-ball')){return 'actual-main';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-v104-ball') && isExtra && isHit){return 'pred-extra-hit';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-v104-ball') && isExtra){return 'pred-extra';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-v104-ball') && isHit){return 'pred-main-hit';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-v104-ball')){return 'pred-main';}
    if(isExtra && isHit){return 'pred-extra-hit';}
    if(isExtra){return 'pred-extra';}
    if(isHit){return 'pred-main-hit';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-ball')){return 'pred-main';}
    return 'neutral';
  }
  function apply(el){var role;if(!el){return;} role = inferRole(el); addC(el,'mle-ball-core'); clearRoles(el); addC(el,'mle-ball-role-' + role); try{el.setAttribute('data-ball-role', role);}catch(ex){} if(!el.getAttribute('data-ball-number')){try{el.setAttribute('data-ball-number',(el.textContent||'').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,''));}catch(ex2){}}}
  function run(scope){var root=scope||document;var q='.mle-ball,.mle-v100-ball,.mle-v102-ball,.mle-v103-ball,.mle-v104-ball,.mle-v105-ball,.mle-v106-ball,.mle-v107-ball,.mle-official-draw-ball,.mle-official-pred-ball,.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball,.prc-num,.prc-num-hit,.prc-num-extra,.prc-num-extra-hit,.prc-num-extra-miss';var nodes;var i;if(!root.querySelectorAll){return;} nodes=root.querySelectorAll(q);for(i=0;i<nodes.length;i++){try{apply(nodes[i]);}catch(ex){}}}
  window.mleV119RestoreBallColors = run;
  if(!window.mleAuditBallColorSystem){
    window.mleAuditBallColorSystem = function(){var nodes=document.querySelectorAll('.mle-ball-core,.mle-ball,.mle-v102-ball,.mle-v104-ball,.mle-official-draw-ball,.mle-official-pred-ball,.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball,.prc-num,.prc-num-hit,.prc-num-extra,.prc-num-extra-hit,.prc-num-extra-miss');var rows=[];var i;var st;for(i=0;i<nodes.length;i++){st=window.getComputedStyle?window.getComputedStyle(nodes[i]):null;rows.push({index:i,text:(nodes[i].textContent||'').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,''),role:nodes[i].getAttribute('data-ball-role')||'',className:nodes[i].className,color:st?st.color:'',backgroundColor:st?st.backgroundColor:'',borderColor:st?st.borderColor:''});} if(window.console&&console.table){console.table(rows);} return rows;};
  }
  if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){setTimeout(run,0);setTimeout(run,250);setTimeout(run,900);setTimeout(run,1800);});
  } else {
    setTimeout(run,0);setTimeout(run,250);setTimeout(run,900);setTimeout(run,1800);

(function(){
  'use strict';
  function hasC(el,c){return !!(el && typeof el.className === 'string' && (' '+el.className+' ').indexOf(' '+c+' ') !== -1);}
  function addC(el,c){if(el && !hasC(el,c)){el.className = el.className ? el.className + ' ' + c : c;}}
  function remC(el,c){if(!el || typeof el.className !== 'string'){return;} el.className = el.className.replace(new RegExp('(?:^|\\s)' + c.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g,'\\$&') + '(?=\\s|$)','g'),'').replace(/\s\s+/g,' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');}
  function cleanText(v){return String(v||'').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');}
  function inferRole(el){
    var cls = el && typeof el.className === 'string' ? el.className : '';
    var role = el ? (el.getAttribute('data-ball-role') || '') : '';
    var isPred = cls.indexOf('--predicted') !== -1 || hasC(el,'mle-ball--predicted') || hasC(el,'mle-official-pred-ball');
    var isActual = hasC(el,'mle-ball--actual') || hasC(el,'mle-official-draw-ball');
    var isExtra = cls.indexOf('--extra') !== -1 || cls.indexOf('--bonus') !== -1 || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra') || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra-hit') || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra-miss');
    var isHit = cls.indexOf('--hit') !== -1 || hasC(el,'mle-ball--match') || hasC(el,'prc-num-hit') || hasC(el,'prc-num-extra-hit');
    if(role){return role.replace(/_/g,'-');}
    if(isPred && isExtra && isHit){return 'pred-extra-hit';}
    if(isPred && isExtra){return 'pred-extra';}
    if(isPred && isHit){return 'pred-main-hit';}
    if(isPred){return 'pred-main';}
    if(isActual && isExtra){return 'actual-extra';}
    if(isActual){return 'actual-main';}
    if(hasC(el,'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball')){
      if(isExtra){return isPred ? (isHit ? 'pred-extra-hit' : 'pred-extra') : 'actual-extra';}
      return isPred ? (isHit ? 'pred-main-hit' : 'pred-main') : 'actual-main';
    }
    if(isExtra && isHit){return 'pred-extra-hit';}
    if(isExtra){return 'pred-extra';}
    if(isHit){return 'pred-main-hit';}
    return 'pred-main';
  }
  function setRole(el,role){
    var roles=['actual-main','actual-extra','pred-main','pred-main-hit','pred-extra','pred-extra-hit','neutral'];
    var i;
    for(i=0;i<roles.length;i++){remC(el,'mle-ball-role-'+roles[i]);}
    addC(el,'mle-ball-core');
    addC(el,'mle-ball-role-'+role);
    try{el.setAttribute('data-ball-role',role);}catch(ex){}
  }
  function ensureTextSpan(el){
    var span;
    if(!el || !el.querySelector){return;}
    span = el.querySelector('.mle-ball-text');
    if(span){return;}
    var text = cleanText(el.textContent || '');
    if(text === ''){return;}
    while(el.firstChild){el.removeChild(el.firstChild);}
    span = document.createElement('span');
    span.className = 'mle-ball-text';
    span.appendChild(document.createTextNode(text));
    el.appendChild(span);
    try{el.setAttribute('data-ball-number', text);}catch(ex2){}
  }
  function apply(el){
    var role;
    if(!el){return;}
    role = inferRole(el);
    setRole(el,role);
    ensureTextSpan(el);
  }
  function run(scope){
    var root = scope || document;
    var q = '.mle-ball,.mle-v100-ball,.mle-v102-ball,.mle-v103-ball,.mle-v104-ball,.mle-v105-ball,.mle-v106-ball,.mle-v107-ball,.mle-official-draw-ball,.mle-official-pred-ball,.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball,.prc-num,.prc-num-hit,.prc-num-extra,.prc-num-extra-hit,.prc-num-extra-miss';
    var nodes;
    var i;
    if(!root.querySelectorAll){return;}
    nodes = root.querySelectorAll(q);
    for(i=0;i<nodes.length;i++){try{apply(nodes[i]);}catch(ex){}}
  }
  window.mleV120RepairBallText = run;
  if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){setTimeout(run,0);setTimeout(run,250);setTimeout(run,1000);});
  } else {
    setTimeout(run,0);setTimeout(run,250);setTimeout(run,1000);
  }
  if(window.addEventListener){window.addEventListener('load',function(){setTimeout(run,100);setTimeout(run,1200);});}
}());

(function() {
  if (window.__mleV122RestoreNarrowingWindowTab) { return; }
  window.__mleV122RestoreNarrowingWindowTab = true;

  function qsa(sel, ctx) {
    return Array.prototype.slice.call((ctx || document).querySelectorAll(sel));
  }
  function qs(sel, ctx) {
    return (ctx || document).querySelector(sel);
  }
  function closest(el, sel) {
    while (el && el.nodeType === 1) {
      if (el.matches && el.matches(sel)) { return el; }
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function textOf(el) {
    return el ? String(el.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim() : '';
  }
  function movePrecisionLock(card) {
    var body = qs('.mle-advisory-card__body', card);
    if (!body) { return; }
    var stack = qs('.mle-v34-priority-stack', body);
    var lock = qs('.mle-precision-lock', body);
    if (!stack || !lock) { return; }

    if (lock.parentNode !== stack) {
      var process = qs('.mle-v109-process', stack);
      if (process && process.nextSibling) {
        stack.insertBefore(lock, process.nextSibling);
      } else {
        stack.appendChild(lock);
      }
    }
    lock.setAttribute('data-mle-v122-restored', '1');

    var moreButtons = qsa('.mle-v109-process__more', body);
    for (var i = 0; i < moreButtons.length; i++) {
      if (textOf(moreButtons[i]) === 'See Precision Progress in Full Evidence') {
        moreButtons[i].textContent = 'See Window and Settings Narrowing';
      }
    }
  }
  function restoreAll() {
    var cards = qsa('.mle-advisory-card');
    for (var i = 0; i < cards.length; i++) {
      movePrecisionLock(cards[i]);
    }
  }

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      setTimeout(restoreAll, 600);
      setTimeout(restoreAll, 2400);
      setTimeout(restoreAll, 5200);
    });
  } else {
    setTimeout(restoreAll, 600);
    setTimeout(restoreAll, 2400);
    setTimeout(restoreAll, 5200);
  }
  window.addEventListener('load', function() {
    setTimeout(restoreAll, 800);
    setTimeout(restoreAll, 3000);
    setTimeout(restoreAll, 6000);
  });

  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var trigger = e.target && closest(e.target, '.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-lottery-outer-toggle,.mle-advisory-card__toggle,[data-outer-lottery-toggle]');
    if (!trigger) { return; }
    setTimeout(restoreAll, 500);
    setTimeout(restoreAll, 1800);
  }, true);

  window.mleV122RestoreNarrowingWindowTab = restoreAll;
  window.mleAuditNarrowingWindowTab = function() {
    var rows = [];
    var cards = qsa('.mle-advisory-card');
    for (var i = 0; i < cards.length; i++) {
      var card = cards[i];
      var title = textOf(qs('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name', card)) || ('Card ' + (i + 1));
      var lock = qs('.mle-precision-lock', card);
      var computed = lock && window.getComputedStyle ? window.getComputedStyle(lock) : null;
      rows.push({
        title: title,
        narrowingTabFound: !!lock,
        restoredByV122: lock ? lock.getAttribute('data-mle-v122-restored') === '1' : false,
        display: computed ? computed.display : '',
        order: computed ? computed.order : '',
        titleText: textOf(qs('.mle-precision-lock__title', lock || card)),
        horizonSectionFound: !!qs('.mle-precision-lock__horizon-section', lock || card),
        progressTrackerFound: !!qs('.mle-precision-progress-v14', lock || card)
      });
    }
    if (window.console && console.table) { console.table(rows); }
    else if (window.console) { console.log(rows); }
    return rows;
  };
})();

(function(){

  window.mleAuditActionButtonsV130 = function(){
    var nodes = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-status-action-jump, .mle-open-skai-precision-batch, .mle-regular-skai-batch-action-btn, .mle-today-focus__action');

        batchPhase: el.getAttribute('data-batch-phase') || '',
        hasSkaiUrl: !!(el.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || el.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url')),
        isButton: ((el.tagName || '').toLowerCase() === 'button')
      });
    }
    if (window.console && console.table) { console.table(rows); }
