(function(){
  'use strict';

  function qsa(sel, root) {
    return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel));
  }

  function hasClass(el, cls) {
    return !!(el && el.className && (' ' + el.className + ' ').indexOf(' ' + cls + ' ') !== -1);
  }

  function closest(el, sel) {
    while (el && el.nodeType === 1) {
      if (el.matches && el.matches(sel)) { return el; }
      if (el.msMatchesSelector && el.msMatchesSelector(sel)) { return el; }
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }

  function text(el) {
    return el ? String(el.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '') : '';
  }

  function findCard(trigger) {
    var card = closest(trigger, '.mle-advisory-card');
    var id;
    if (card) { return card; }
    id = trigger && (trigger.getAttribute('data-target-card') || trigger.getAttribute('data-card-id'));
    if (id) {
      id = String(id).replace(/^#/, '');
      card = document.getElementById(id);
      if (card && hasClass(card, 'mle-advisory-card')) { return card; }
    }
    return null;
  }

  function openCard(card) {
    var body;
    var btn;
    if (!card) { return; }
    body = card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body');
    if (body) {
      body.style.display = 'block';
      body.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
    }
    btn = card.querySelector('.mle-lottery-toggle');
    if (btn) {
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
      if (btn.querySelector('span')) { btn.querySelector('span').innerHTML = 'Collapse'; }
      else { btn.innerHTML = 'Collapse'; }
    }
  }

  function openDetailsParents(target) {
    var node = target;
    var id;
    var toggle;
    while (node && node !== document) {
      if (String(node.tagName || '').toLowerCase() === 'details') {
        node.open = true;
      }
      if (hasClass(node, 'mle-section-body') || node.getAttribute('data-mle-primary-section-body') === '1') {
        node.style.display = 'block';
        node.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
        id = node.getAttribute('id');
        if (id) {
          toggle = document.querySelector('[aria-controls="' + id.replace(/"/g, '') + '"]');
          if (toggle) { toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); }
        }
      }
      node = node.parentNode;
    }
  }

  function focusTarget(target) {
    if (!target) { return; }
    if (!target.hasAttribute('tabindex')) { target.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); }
    try { target.focus({preventScroll: true}); } catch (e) { try { target.focus(); } catch (e2) {} }
  }

  function scrollToTarget(target) {
    if (!target) { return; }
    if (target.scrollIntoView) {
      try { target.scrollIntoView({behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start'}); }
      catch (e) { target.scrollIntoView(true); }
    }
    focusTarget(target);
  }

  function showCardMessage(card, msg) {
    var body = card ? card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body') : null;
    var old;
    var div;
    if (!body) { return; }
    old = body.querySelector('.mle-v132-section-message');
    if (old && old.parentNode) { old.parentNode.removeChild(old); }
    div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'mle-v132-section-message';
    div.setAttribute('role', 'status');
    div.innerHTML = msg;
    body.insertBefore(div, body.firstChild);
    scrollToTarget(div);
  }

  function firstExisting(card, selectors) {
    var i;
    var found;
    for (i = 0; i < selectors.length; i++) {
      found = card.querySelector(selectors[i]);
      if (found) { return found; }
    }
    return null;
  }

  function targetFor(card, type) {
    if (!card) { return null; }
    if (type === 'pending') {
      return firstExisting(card, [
        '.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown',
        '[id*="pending-predictions"]',
        '[id*="pending"]',
        '.mle-v34-pending-hub',
        '.mle-pending-runs-panel'
      ]);
    }
    if (type === 'scored') {
      return firstExisting(card, [
        '.mle-v104-run-report',
        '.mle-strong-evidence',
        '[id$="-strong-evidence"]',
        '.mle-batch-cleanup',
        '.mle-saved-runs-panel',
        '.mle-visual-comparison'
      ]);
    }
    if (type === 'runs') {
      return firstExisting(card, [
        '.mle-saved-runs-panel',
        '[id*="saved-runs"]',
        '[id*="runs-body"]',
        '.mle-visual-comparison',
        '.mle-v104-run-report'
      ]);
    }
    if (type === 'evidence') {
      return firstExisting(card, [
        '.mle-batch-cleanup',
        '[id*="evidence-panel"]',
        '.mle-strong-evidence',
        '[id$="-strong-evidence"]',
        '.mle-precision-lock',
        '.mle-precision-progress-v14'
      ]);
    }
    if (type === 'run_selection') {
      return firstExisting(card, [
        '.mle-batch-cleanup',
        '[id*="evidence-panel"]'
      ]);
    }
    if (type === 'progress') {
      return firstExisting(card, [
        '.mle-precision-progress-v14',
        '.mle-precision-lock',
        '[id*="precision-lock"]',
        '[id*="current-lock"]'
      ]);
    }
    if (type === 'batch_report') {
      return firstExisting(card, [
        '.mle-v104-run-report',
        '.mle-v104-history-pill',
        '.mle-batch-cleanup',
        '.mle-strong-evidence'
      ]);
    }
    if (type === 'batch') {
      return firstExisting(card, [
        '.mle-skai-batch-test',
        '[id$="-precision-lock-batches"]',
        '.mle-next-settings-run'
      ]);
    }
    return null;
  }

  function ensureVisibleMode(card, targetType) {
    var fullBtn;
    var strategyBtn;
    if (!card) { return; }
    if (targetType === 'scored' || targetType === 'runs' || targetType === 'evidence' || targetType === 'run_selection' || targetType === 'batch_report') {
      fullBtn = card.querySelector('.mle-v33-modebar__btn[data-mle-v33-mode="full"], .mle-v33-modebar__btn[data-view-mode="full"], [data-mle-view-mode="full"]');
      if (fullBtn && typeof fullBtn.click === 'function') { try { fullBtn.click(); } catch (e) {} }
    } else if (targetType === 'progress' || targetType === 'batch') {
      strategyBtn = card.querySelector('.mle-v33-modebar__btn[data-mle-v33-mode="strategy"], .mle-v33-modebar__btn[data-view-mode="strategy"], [data-mle-view-mode="strategy"]');
      if (strategyBtn && typeof strategyBtn.click === 'function') { try { strategyBtn.click(); } catch (e2) {} }
    }
  }

  window.mleOpenCardSection = function(trigger, targetType) {
    var card;
    var target;
    var type = targetType || (trigger && trigger.getAttribute && trigger.getAttribute('data-mle-section-target')) || '';
    card = findCard(trigger);
    if (!card) { return false; }
    openCard(card);
    ensureVisibleMode(card, type);
    target = targetFor(card, type);
    if (!target) {
      showCardMessage(card, 'That section is not available for this lottery yet. Nothing was changed.');
      return false;
    }
    openDetailsParents(target);
    setTimeout(function(){ scrollToTarget(target); }, 80);
    return true;
  };

  function decorateCard(card) {
    var proof = card.querySelector('.mle-adv-meta-item--proof');
    var scored = card.querySelector('.mle-adv-stat-chip--scored');
    var total = card.querySelector('.mle-adv-stat-chip--total');
    var pending = card.querySelector('.mle-adv-stat-chip--pending');
    var evidencePill = card.querySelector('.mle-scan-pill--evidence');
    var pendingPill = card.querySelector('.mle-scan-pill--pending, .mle-scan-pill--fresh-runs');
    var items = [
      [proof, 'evidence', 'Open evidence level details'],
      [evidencePill, 'evidence', 'Open evidence level details'],
      [scored, 'scored', 'Open scored runs and evidence'],
      [total, 'runs', 'Open saved runs'],
      [pending, 'pending', 'Open pending recommendations'],
      [pendingPill, 'pending', 'Open pending recommendations']
    ];
    var i;
    var el;
    for (i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
      el = items[i][0];
      if (!el) { continue; }
      el.setAttribute('data-mle-section-target', items[i][1]);
      el.setAttribute('role', 'button');
      el.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
      if (!el.getAttribute('aria-label')) { el.setAttribute('aria-label', items[i][2]); }
    }
  }

  function decorateAll() {
    var cards = qsa('.mle-advisory-card');
    var i;
    for (i = 0; i < cards.length; i++) { decorateCard(cards[i]); }
  }

  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt) {
    var btn;
    if (closest(evt.target, '.mle-help-tip')) { return; }
    btn = closest(evt.target, '[data-mle-section-target]');
    if (!btn) { return; }
    evt.preventDefault();
    window.mleOpenCardSection(btn, btn.getAttribute('data-mle-section-target') || '');
  }, true);

  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(evt) {
    var btn;
    var key = evt.key || evt.keyCode;
    if (key !== 'Enter' && key !== ' ' && key !== 13 && key !== 32) { return; }
    btn = closest(evt.target, '[data-mle-section-target]');
    if (!btn) { return; }
    evt.preventDefault();
    window.mleOpenCardSection(btn, btn.getAttribute('data-mle-section-target') || '');
  }, true);

  window.mleAuditRunSelectionLinks = function() {
    var nodes = qsa('[data-mle-section-target="run_selection"]');
    var rows = [];
    var i;
    var el;
    var card;
    var target;
    for (i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
      el = nodes[i];
      card = findCard(el);
      target = card ? targetFor(card, 'run_selection') : null;
      rows.push({
        index: i,
        label: text(el),
        cardTitle: card ? text(card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name')) : '',
        targetFound: !!target,
        targetId: target ? (target.getAttribute('id') || '') : '',
        targetClass: target ? String(target.className || '') : '',
        viewSwitchRequired: true
      });
    }
    if (window.console && console.table) { console.table(rows); }
    else if (window.console) { console.log(rows); }
    return rows;
  };

  window.mleAuditActionableStatusChips = function() {
    var nodes = qsa('[data-mle-section-target]');
    var rows = [];
    var i;
    var el;
    var card;
    var type;
    var target;
    for (i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
      el = nodes[i];
      card = findCard(el);
      type = el.getAttribute('data-mle-section-target') || '';
      target = card ? targetFor(card, type) : null;
      rows.push({
        index: i,
        label: text(el),
        targetType: type,
        cardTitle: card ? text(card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__lottery-name')) : '',
        targetFound: !!target,
        targetId: target ? (target.getAttribute('id') || '') : '',
        targetClass: target ? String(target.className || '') : ''
      });
    }
    if (window.console && console.table) { console.table(rows); }
    else if (window.console) { console.log(rows); }
    return rows;
  };

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', decorateAll);
  } else {
    decorateAll();
  }
  setTimeout(decorateAll, 500);
  setTimeout(decorateAll, 1500);
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV134RedundantGuidanceSourceCleanup) { return; }
  window.__mleV134RedundantGuidanceSourceCleanup = true;
  function qsa(sel, root) { return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function cleanupCard(card) {
    qsa('.mle-v70-guide,.mle-v69-guide', card).forEach(function(guide) {
      guide.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
    });
    qsa('.mle-v134-checklist-card,.mle-v73-facts', card).forEach(function(node) {
      if (node && node.parentNode) { node.parentNode.removeChild(node); }
    });
  }
  function apply() { qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(cleanupCard); }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

    });

(function(){
  if (window.__mleMethodDeepLinkFixV4) { return; }
  window.__mleMethodDeepLinkFixV4 = true;
  function closest(el, sel){ while(el && el.nodeType===1){ if(el.matches && el.matches(sel)){ return el; } el=el.parentNode; } return null; }
  function openPanel(panel){
    if(!panel){ return; }
    if(panel.tagName && panel.tagName.toLowerCase()==='details'){ panel.open = true; }
    panel.style.display = '';
    panel.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
    var btn = document.querySelector('[aria-controls="' + panel.id + '"]');
    if(btn){ btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true'); }
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    var btn = closest(e.target, '.mle-v133-run-selection-link, .mle-section-shortcut-btn');
    if(!btn){ return; }
    var card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card');
    var targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-open-details') || '';
    if(!targetId && btn.className.indexOf('mle-v133-run-selection-link') !== -1 && card){
      var cleanup = card.querySelector('.mle-batch-cleanup');
      if(cleanup && cleanup.id){ targetId = cleanup.id; }
    }
    if(!targetId){ return; }
    var target = document.getElementById(targetId);
    if(!target){ return; }
    e.preventDefault();
    openPanel(target);
    var parentDetails = closest(target, 'details');
    if(parentDetails){ parentDetails.open = true; }
    try { target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); }
    catch(_) { target.scrollIntoView(true); }
  }, true);
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if(window.__mleV139FinalVisibleMatchReconciler){return;}
  window.__mleV139FinalVisibleMatchReconciler=true;

  function qsa(sel,root){return Array.prototype.slice.call((root||document).querySelectorAll(sel));}
  function clean(v){return String(v||'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();}
  function text(el){return clean(el?el.textContent:'');}
  function hasClass(el,cls){return (' '+(el.className||'')+' ').indexOf(' '+cls+' ')>-1;}
  function addClass(el,cls){if(!hasClass(el,cls)){el.className=clean((el.className||'')+' '+cls);}}
  function removeClass(el,cls){el.className=clean((' '+(el.className||'')+' ').replace(' '+cls+' ',' '));}
  function selectBalls(root, selector){return qsa(selector,root).filter(function(el){return clean(el.textContent)!=='' && clean(el.textContent)!=='+';});}
  function ballValue(el){return clean(el.getAttribute('data-ball-number')||el.textContent);}
  function duplicateAwareMatchedIndexes(actualValues, predictedValues){
    var counts={}, indexes=[], i, key;
    actualValues=actualValues||[]; predictedValues=predictedValues||[];
    for(i=0;i<actualValues.length;i++){key=String(actualValues[i]);counts[key]=(counts[key]||0)+1;}
    for(i=0;i<predictedValues.length;i++){
      key=String(predictedValues[i]);
      if(counts[key]>0){indexes.push(i);counts[key]-=1;}
    }
    return indexes;
  }
  function valuesFromBalls(balls){return balls.map(function(ball){return ballValue(ball);});}
  function markPredictedHits(predBalls, matchedIndexes, hitClass, hitRole, missRole){
    var i, map={};
    hitClass=hitClass||'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--hit';
    for(i=0;i<matchedIndexes.length;i++){map[matchedIndexes[i]]=true;}
    for(i=0;i<predBalls.length;i++){
      removeClass(predBalls[i], hitClass);
      if(map[i]){
        addClass(predBalls[i], hitClass);
        if(hitRole){predBalls[i].setAttribute('data-ball-role', hitRole);}
      } else if(missRole) {
        predBalls[i].setAttribute('data-ball-role', missRole);
      }
    }
  }
  function reconcileOuterBar(bar){
    var actualCell, predCell, scoreCell, actualMainBalls, actualExtraBalls, predMainBalls, predExtraBalls;
    var mainIdx, extraIdx, mainHits, extraHits, totalHits, strong, small;
    if(!bar){return;}
    actualCell=bar.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell--actual');
    predCell=bar.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell--comparison');
    scoreCell=bar.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__cell--score');
    if(!actualCell||!predCell||!scoreCell){return;}
    actualMainBalls=selectBalls(actualCell,'.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball:not(.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--extra)');
    actualExtraBalls=selectBalls(actualCell,'.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--extra');
    predMainBalls=selectBalls(predCell,'.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--predicted:not(.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--extra)');
    predExtraBalls=selectBalls(predCell,'.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--predicted.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--extra');
    if(!actualMainBalls.length || !predMainBalls.length){return;}
    mainIdx=duplicateAwareMatchedIndexes(valuesFromBalls(actualMainBalls), valuesFromBalls(predMainBalls));
    extraIdx=duplicateAwareMatchedIndexes(valuesFromBalls(actualExtraBalls), valuesFromBalls(predExtraBalls));
    mainHits=mainIdx.length; extraHits=extraIdx.length; totalHits=mainHits+extraHits;
    markPredictedHits(predMainBalls, mainIdx, 'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--hit', 'pred-main-hit', 'pred-main');
    markPredictedHits(predExtraBalls, extraIdx, 'mle-lottery-outer-resultbar__ball--hit', 'pred-extra-hit', 'pred-extra');
    strong=scoreCell.querySelector('strong');
    small=scoreCell.querySelector('small');
    if(strong){strong.textContent=String(mainHits)+' main match'+(mainHits===1?'':'es');}
    if(small){small.textContent=String(totalHits)+' total match'+(totalHits===1?'':'es')+(extraHits?' | Extra: '+String(extraHits):'');}
    bar.setAttribute('data-mle-v139-reconciled','1');
    bar.setAttribute('data-mle-v139-main-matches',String(mainHits));
    bar.setAttribute('data-mle-v139-total-matches',String(totalHits));
  }
  function reconcileV102Strip(strip){
    var actualCell, predCell, scoreCell, actualMainBalls, actualExtraBalls, predMainBalls, predExtraBalls;
    var mainIdx, extraIdx, mainHits, extraHits, totalHits, strong, small;
    if(!strip){return;}
    actualCell=strip.querySelector('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip__cell--actual');
    predCell=strip.querySelector('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip__cell--prediction');
    scoreCell=strip.querySelector('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip__cell--score');
    if(!actualCell||!predCell||!scoreCell){return;}
    actualMainBalls=selectBalls(actualCell,'.mle-v102-ball:not(.mle-v102-ball--extra)');
    actualExtraBalls=selectBalls(actualCell,'.mle-v102-ball--extra');
    predMainBalls=selectBalls(predCell,'.mle-v102-ball--predicted:not(.mle-v102-ball--extra)');
    predExtraBalls=selectBalls(predCell,'.mle-v102-ball--predicted.mle-v102-ball--extra');
    if(!actualMainBalls.length || !predMainBalls.length){return;}
    mainIdx=duplicateAwareMatchedIndexes(valuesFromBalls(actualMainBalls), valuesFromBalls(predMainBalls));
    extraIdx=duplicateAwareMatchedIndexes(valuesFromBalls(actualExtraBalls), valuesFromBalls(predExtraBalls));
    mainHits=mainIdx.length; extraHits=extraIdx.length; totalHits=mainHits+extraHits;
    markPredictedHits(predMainBalls, mainIdx, 'mle-v102-ball--hit');
    markPredictedHits(predExtraBalls, extraIdx, 'mle-v102-ball--hit');
    strong=scoreCell.querySelector('strong');
    small=scoreCell.querySelector('small');
    if(strong){strong.textContent=String(mainHits)+' main match'+(mainHits===1?'':'es');}
    if(small){small.textContent=String(totalHits)+' total match'+(totalHits===1?'':'es')+(extraHits?' | Extra: '+String(extraHits):'');}
    strip.setAttribute('data-mle-v139-reconciled','1');
  }
  function run(){
    qsa('.mle-lottery-outer-resultbar').forEach(reconcileOuterBar);
    qsa('.mle-v102-last-draw-strip').forEach(reconcileV102Strip);
  }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',run);}else{run();}
  window.addEventListener('load',function(){run();setTimeout(run,250);setTimeout(run,900);setTimeout(run,2200);setTimeout(run,5200);setTimeout(run,8500);});
  document.addEventListener('click',function(){setTimeout(run,100);setTimeout(run,700);setTimeout(run,1600);},true);
  window.mleV139ReconcileVisibleMatches=run;
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__mleV37ConsolidatedUiCore) { return; }
  window.__mleV37ConsolidatedUiCore = true;

  function closest(el, sel) { while (el && el.nodeType === 1) { if (el.matches && el.matches(sel)) { return el; } el = el.parentNode; } return null; }
  function qsa(sel, root) { return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function qs(sel, root) { return (root || document).querySelector(sel); }
  function clean(v) { return String(v || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, ''); }
  function addClass(el, cls) { if (el && (' ' + (el.className || '') + ' ').indexOf(' ' + cls + ' ') < 0) { el.className = clean((el.className || '') + ' ' + cls); } }
  function removeClass(el, cls) { if (el) { el.className = clean((' ' + (el.className || '') + ' ').replace(' ' + cls + ' ', ' ')); } }
  function show(el) { if (!el) { return; } el.style.display = ''; el.removeAttribute('hidden'); el.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false'); if (el.tagName && String(el.tagName).toLowerCase() === 'details') { el.open = true; } }

  function ensureOverlay() {
    var overlay = document.getElementById('mleJumpLoadingOverlay');
    if (overlay) { return overlay; }
    overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.id = 'mleJumpLoadingOverlay';
    overlay.className = 'mle-jump-loading-overlay';
    overlay.setAttribute('role', 'status');
    overlay.setAttribute('aria-live', 'polite');
    overlay.innerHTML = '<div class="mle-jump-loading-card"><div class="mle-jump-loading-spinner" aria-hidden="true"></div><div><div class="mle-jump-loading-title">Opening lottery card...</div><div class="mle-jump-loading-subtitle">Please wait while this section expands and moves into view.</div></div></div>';
    if (document.body) { document.body.appendChild(overlay); }
    return overlay;
  }
  function showOverlay(message) {
    var overlay = ensureOverlay();
    var title;
    if (!overlay) { return; }
    title = overlay.querySelector ? overlay.querySelector('.mle-jump-loading-title') : null;
    if (title && message) { title.textContent = message; }
    overlay.classList.add('is-visible');
    window.clearTimeout(window.__mleJumpLoadingTimer);
    window.__mleJumpLoadingTimer = window.setTimeout(hideOverlay, 3500);
  }
  function hideOverlay() { var overlay = document.getElementById('mleJumpLoadingOverlay'); if (overlay) { overlay.classList.remove('is-visible'); } }
  window.mleShowJumpLoading = showOverlay;
  window.mleHideJumpLoading = hideOverlay;

  function setToggleText(toggle, open) {
    var span = toggle && toggle.querySelector ? toggle.querySelector('span') : null;
    var node = span || toggle;
    var txt = clean(node ? (node.textContent || node.innerText || '') : '');
    if (!node) { return; }
    if (txt === 'Expand' || txt === 'Collapse') { node.textContent = open ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand'; }
    else if (txt.indexOf('View ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'View ') + txt.substring(5); }
    else if (txt.indexOf('Show ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ') + txt.substring(5); }
    else if (txt.indexOf('Hide ') === 0) { node.textContent = (open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ') + txt.substring(5); }
  }
  function openCard(card) {
    var body, bodies, toggles, i, outer, group;
    if (!card) { return; }
    try {
      outer = closest(card, '.mle-lottery-outer');
      group = closest(card, '.lottery-group');
      if (outer && outer.classList && outer.classList.contains('body-collapsed') && typeof window.skaiLotterySetOneOuter === 'function') { window.skaiLotterySetOneOuter(outer, false); }
      if (group && group.classList && group.classList.contains('collapsed') && typeof window.skaiLotterySetOneGroup === 'function') { window.skaiLotterySetOneGroup(group, false); }
    } catch(_e0) {}
    body = qs('.mle-advisory-card__body, .mle-lottery-outer-body, .mle-lottery-body', card);
    show(body);
    bodies = qsa('.mle-advisory-card__body, .mle-lottery-outer-body, .mle-lottery-body', card);
    for (i = 0; i < bodies.length; i++) { show(bodies[i]); }
    toggles = qsa('.mle-lottery-toggle, .mle-lottery-outer-toggle', card);
    for (i = 0; i < toggles.length; i++) { toggles[i].setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); setToggleText(toggles[i], true); }
  }
  function setCardMode(card, mode) {
    var buttons, sections, i, active, secMode;
    if (!card || !mode) { return; }
    buttons = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-btn]', card);
    sections = qsa('[data-mle-card-mode-section]', card);
    for (i = 0; i < buttons.length; i++) {
      active = (buttons[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-btn') === mode);
      buttons[i].setAttribute('aria-selected', active ? 'true' : 'false');
      if (active) { addClass(buttons[i], 'is-active'); } else { removeClass(buttons[i], 'is-active'); }
    }
    for (i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
      secMode = sections[i].getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') || '';
      if (secMode === mode) { show(sections[i]); }
      else { sections[i].style.display = 'none'; sections[i].setAttribute('hidden', 'hidden'); sections[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true'); }
    }
  }
  function addManageNote(target, type) {
    var note, first;
    if (!target || qs('.mle-v37-manage-runs-note', target)) { return; }
    note = document.createElement('div');
    note.className = 'mle-v37-manage-runs-note';
    if (type === 'review') { note.innerHTML = '<strong>Review / Delete Runs:</strong> review saved runs, move selected runs to Use for Advice, Watch for Now, or Exclude, or permanently delete selected runs.'; }
    else { note.innerHTML = '<strong>Review / Delete Runs:</strong> review saved predictions for this lottery and delete a saved run when it should be removed.'; }
    first = target.firstChild;
    target.insertBefore(note, first);
  }
  function mleV140ReadCount(card, names) {
    var i, value, n;
    if (!card || !card.getAttribute) { return 0; }
    for (i = 0; i < names.length; i++) {
      value = card.getAttribute(names[i]);
      if (value !== null && value !== '') {
        n = parseInt(value, 10);
        if (!isNaN(n)) { return n; }
      }
    }
    return 0;
  }
  function mleV140IsInside(el, parent) {
    return !!(el && parent && (el === parent || (parent.contains && parent.contains(el))));
  }
  function mleV140FocusTarget(result, card) {
    var target = result && result.target ? result.target : null;
    var inner;
    if (!card) { return target; }
    if (result && result.type === 'pending') {
      inner = qs('.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown, .mle-pending-recommendations, [id*="pending"]', card);
      return inner || target;
    }
    if (result && result.type === 'review') {
      inner = qs('.mle-visual-comparison .mle-visual-row, .mle-visual-comparison, .mle-batch-cleanup .mle-batch-cleanup__body, .mle-batch-cleanup', card);
      return inner || target;
    }
    return target;
  }
  function mleV140OpenOnlyNeededDetails(card, target) {
    var details, i, d;
    if (!card) { return; }
    details = qsa('details', card);
    for (i = 0; i < details.length; i++) {
      d = details[i];
      try {
        if (mleV140IsInside(target, d) || mleV140IsInside(d, target)) { d.open = true; }
        else { d.open = false; }
      } catch(_e) {}
    }
  }
  function findManageTarget(card, btn) {
    var target, targetId, pending, scored, visibleCompleted, btnText;
    if (!card) { return {target:null, mode:'', type:''}; }

    pending = mleV140ReadCount(card, ['data-mle-history-pending-count', 'data-pending-count', 'data-pending-runs']);
    scored = mleV140ReadCount(card, ['data-mle-history-scored-count']);
    visibleCompleted = mleV140ReadCount(card, ['data-mle-history-completed-visible-count']);
    btnText = btn ? ((btn.textContent || btn.innerText || '') + ' ' + (btn.getAttribute ? (btn.getAttribute('aria-label') || '') : '')).toLowerCase() : '';

    if ((btnText.indexOf('pending') >= 0 || (pending > 0 && scored <= 0 && visibleCompleted <= 0))) {
      target = qs('.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown, .mle-pending-recommendations, [id*="pending"]', card);
      if (target) { return {target:target, mode:'numbers', type:'pending'}; }
    }

    target = qs('.mle-visual-comparison .mle-visual-row, .mle-visual-comparison', card);
    if ((scored > 0 || visibleCompleted > 0) && target) { return {target:target, mode:'review-runs', type:'review'}; }

    targetId = btn && btn.getAttribute ? (btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '') : '';
    if (targetId) {
      target = document.getElementById(targetId);
      if (target) {
        if (target.getAttribute && target.getAttribute('data-mle-card-mode-section') === 'review-runs') { return {target:mleV140FocusTarget({target:target,type:'review'}, card), mode:'review-runs', type:'review'}; }
        if ((' ' + (target.className || '') + ' ').indexOf(' mle-saved-runs-panel ') >= 0) { return {target:target, mode:'details', type:'saved'}; }
        return {target:target, mode:'review-runs', type:'review'};
      }
    }
    target = qs('.mle-batch-cleanup[data-mle-card-mode-section="review-runs"], .mle-batch-cleanup', card);
    if (target) { return {target:mleV140FocusTarget({target:target,type:'review'}, card), mode:'review-runs', type:'review'}; }
    target = qs('.mle-adv-pred-summary[data-mle-card-mode-section="review-runs"]', card);
    if (target) { return {target:target, mode:'review-runs', type:'review'}; }
    target = qs('.mle-saved-runs-panel', card);
    if (target) { return {target:target, mode:'details', type:'saved'}; }
    target = qs('.mle-pending-predictions-dropdown, .mle-pending-recommendations', card);
    if (target) { return {target:target, mode:'numbers', type:'pending'}; }
    return {target:null, mode:'', type:''};
  }
  function updateButtonLabels() {
    var i, btns;
    btns = qsa('.mle-advisory-manage-runs-btn');
    for (i = 0; i < btns.length; i++) {
      btns[i].textContent = 'View Results';
      btns[i].setAttribute('aria-label', 'View saved recommendations and scored results for this lottery');

    }
  }
  function openManageRuns(btn) {
    var card, result, target;
    card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card') || closest(btn, '.mle-lottery-outer');
    if (!card) { return false; }
    openCard(card);
    result = findManageTarget(card, btn);
    target = result.target;
    if (!target) { return false; }
    if (result.mode) { setCardMode(card, result.mode); }
    target = mleV140FocusTarget(result, card) || target;
    show(target);
    openAncestors(target);
    mleV140OpenOnlyNeededDetails(card, target);
    addManageNote(result.target || target, result.type);
    addClass(target, 'mle-manage-runs-target-flash-v37');
    if (!target.hasAttribute || !target.hasAttribute('tabindex')) { try { target.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); } catch(_e1) {} }
    window.setTimeout(function(){
      try { target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'center'}); } catch(e) { target.scrollIntoView(true); }
      try { target.focus({preventScroll:true}); } catch(_e2) { try { target.focus(); } catch(_e3) {} }
    }, 80);
    window.setTimeout(function(){ removeClass(target, 'mle-manage-runs-target-flash-v37'); }, 2400);
    return true;
  }
  window.mleManageOuterSavedRuns = function(btn) { return openManageRuns(btn) ? false : false; };

  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var btn = closest(e.target, '.mle-lottery-outer-manage-runs-btn, .mle-advisory-manage-runs-btn, .mle-manage-runs-shortcut-btn, .mle-scan-pill--manage-runs');
    if (!btn) { return; }
    if (e.preventDefault) { e.preventDefault(); }
    if (e.stopImmediatePropagation) { e.stopImmediatePropagation(); } else if (e.stopPropagation) { e.stopPropagation(); }

  }, true);

  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var btn = closest(e.target, '.mle-method-status-jump');
    var saved, pending, scored;
    if (!btn) { return; }
    saved = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-saved-count') || '0', 10) || 0;
    pending = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-pending-count') || '0', 10) || 0;
    scored = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-scored-count') || '0', 10) || 0;
    if (saved <= 0 && pending <= 0 && scored <= 0) { return; }
    if (e.preventDefault) { e.preventDefault(); }
    if (e.stopImmediatePropagation) { e.stopImmediatePropagation(); } else if (e.stopPropagation) { e.stopPropagation(); }

    
    if ((btn.getAttribute('data-method-key') || '').toLowerCase() === 'unknown') {
      var card, targetId, target, methodPanel, fallback, cur;
      card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card') || closest(btn, '.mle-lottery-outer');
      if (card) { openCard(card); setCardMode(card, 'details'); }
      targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
      target = targetId ? document.getElementById(targetId) : null;
      methodPanel = card ? qs('.mle-method-run-breakdown, [id$="-method-run-breakdown"]', card) : null;
      fallback = card ? qs('.mle-method-run-card--unknown, [id$="-unknown"]', card) : null;
      if (!target) { target = fallback || methodPanel || card; }
      if (methodPanel) { show(methodPanel); }
      if (target) {
        show(target);
        cur = target;
        while (cur && cur !== document) {
          if (cur.tagName && String(cur.tagName).toLowerCase() === 'details') {
            try { cur.open = true; } catch(_e1) {}
            show(cur);
          }
          cur = cur.parentNode;
        }
        try { target.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); } catch(_e2) {}
        addClass(target, 'mle-action-jump-target');
        window.setTimeout(function(){
          try { target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); } catch(_e3) { try { target.scrollIntoView(true); } catch(_e4) {} }
          try { target.focus({preventScroll:true}); } catch(_e5) { try { target.focus(); } catch(_e6) {} }
          window.setTimeout(function(){ removeClass(target, 'mle-action-jump-target'); }, 2200);
        }, 80);
      }
      return false;
    }

    if (typeof window.mleActionJump === 'function') { window.mleActionJump(btn); }
  }, true);

  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt) {
    var jump = closest(evt.target, '.mle-action-jump');

    else { showOverlay('Opening section...'); }
  }, true);
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(evt) { if (evt && evt.key === 'Escape') { hideOverlay(); } }, true);

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', updateButtonLabels); }
  else { updateButtonLabels(); }
  window.addEventListener('load', function(){ updateButtonLabels(); setTimeout(updateButtonLabels, 500); setTimeout(updateButtonLabels, 1500); });

  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt) {
    var b = closest(evt.target, '[data-mle-v71-open-saved-runs]');
    var id, panel, card, wrap, toggle;
    if (!b) { return; }
    if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); }
    id = b.getAttribute('data-mle-v71-open-saved-runs') || '';
    panel = id ? document.getElementById(id) : null;
    card = closest(b, '.mle-advisory-card') || closest(b, '.mle-lottery-outer');
    if (card) { openCard(card); setCardMode(card, 'details'); }
    if (panel) {
      wrap = panel.parentNode;
      if (wrap) { show(wrap); }
      show(panel);
      toggle = card ? qs('[aria-controls="' + id + '"]', card) : null;
      if (toggle) { toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); setToggleText(toggle, true); }
      addManageNote(panel, 'saved');
      addClass(panel, 'mle-manage-runs-target-flash-v37');
      try { panel.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); } catch(e) { panel.scrollIntoView(true); }
      window.setTimeout(function(){ removeClass(panel, 'mle-manage-runs-target-flash-v37'); }, 2200);
    }
  }, true);
})();

(function(){
  if (window.__mleV67UnknownTraceWiringFix) { return; }
  window.__mleV67UnknownTraceWiringFix = true;

  function byId(id) {
    id = String(id || '').replace(/^#/, '');
    return id ? document.getElementById(id) : null;
  }
  function closest(el, selector) {
    while (el && el !== document) {
      if (el.matches && el.matches(selector)) { return el; }
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function showNode(node) {
    if (!node || !node.style) { return; }
    node.style.display = '';
    try { node.removeAttribute('hidden'); } catch(e) {}
    try { node.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false'); } catch(e2) {}
  }
  function openDetailsAncestors(node) {
    var cur = node;
    while (cur && cur !== document) {
      if (cur.tagName && String(cur.tagName).toLowerCase() === 'details') {
        try { cur.open = true; } catch(e) {}
        showNode(cur);
      }
      cur = cur.parentNode;
    }
  }
  function openLotteryCard(card) {
    var outer, group, body, toggle, sp;
    if (!card) { return; }
    outer = closest(card, '.mle-lottery-outer');
    group = closest(card, '.lottery-group');
    try {
      if (outer && outer.classList && outer.classList.contains('body-collapsed') && typeof window.skaiLotterySetOneOuter === 'function') { window.skaiLotterySetOneOuter(outer, false); }
      if (group && group.classList && group.classList.contains('collapsed') && typeof window.skaiLotterySetOneGroup === 'function') { window.skaiLotterySetOneGroup(group, false); }
    } catch(e) {}
    body = card.querySelector ? card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body') : null;
    toggle = card.querySelector ? card.querySelector('.mle-lottery-toggle') : null;
    showNode(card);
    if (body) { showNode(body); }
    if (toggle) {
      try { toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); } catch(e2) {}
      sp = toggle.querySelector ? toggle.querySelector('span') : null;
      if (sp) { sp.textContent = 'Collapse'; }
    }
    if (card.classList) { card.classList.add('is-expanded'); }
  }
  function revealMethodBreakdown(card, lotteryId) {
    var section = byId('mle-section-' + lotteryId + '-method-run-breakdown');
    if (!section && card && card.querySelector) { section = card.querySelector('[id$="-method-run-breakdown"]'); }
    if (section) {
      showNode(section);
      openDetailsAncestors(section);
    }
    return section;
  }
  function scrollToTarget(target) {
    if (!target) { return; }
    showNode(target);
    openDetailsAncestors(target);
    if (target.classList) { target.classList.add('mle-action-jump-target'); }
    if (!target.hasAttribute || !target.hasAttribute('tabindex')) {
      try { target.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); } catch(e) {}
    }
    window.setTimeout(function(){
      try { target.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'}); } catch(e1) { try { target.scrollIntoView(true); } catch(e2) {} }
      try { target.focus({preventScroll:true}); } catch(e3) { try { target.focus(); } catch(e4) {} }
      window.setTimeout(function(){ try { if (target.classList) { target.classList.remove('mle-action-jump-target'); } } catch(e5) {} }, 2200);
    }, 60);
  }
  function handleUnknownTrace(btn, evt) {
    var card, lotteryId, target, fallback, section;
    if (!btn || !btn.getAttribute) { return false; }
    if ((btn.getAttribute('data-method-key') || '').toLowerCase() !== 'unknown') { return false; }
    if (evt && evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); }
    if (evt && evt.stopImmediatePropagation) { evt.stopImmediatePropagation(); }
    else if (evt && evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); }

    card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card');
    if (!card) { card = closest(btn, '.mle-lottery-outer'); }
    openLotteryCard(card);

    lotteryId = '';
    if (card && card.id) { lotteryId = String(card.id).replace(/^mle-adv-card-/, '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, ''); }
    if (!lotteryId) {
      var targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
      var m = String(targetId).match(/mle-unknown-run-trace-([0-9]+)/);
      if (m && m[1]) { lotteryId = m[1]; }
    }

    section = revealMethodBreakdown(card, lotteryId);
    target = byId(btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '');
    fallback = lotteryId ? byId('mle-method-run-card-' + lotteryId + '-unknown') : null;
    if (!fallback && card && card.querySelector) { fallback = card.querySelector('.mle-method-run-card--unknown'); }
    if (!target) { target = fallback || section || card; }

    scrollToTarget(target);
    return true;
  }

  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var btn = closest(evt.target, '.mle-method-status-jump[data-method-key="unknown"]');
    if (!btn) { return; }
    handleUnknownTrace(btn, evt);
    return false;
  }, true);
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_DISPLAY_CONTROL_CENTER_V112__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_DISPLAY_CONTROL_CENTER_V112__ = true;

  var STORE_KEY = 'mle_display_control_v112';
  var CARD_KEY_PREFIX = 'mle_display_card_open_v112_';
  var GUIDE_KEY = 'mle_display_guide_open_v112';
  var CONTROL_OPEN_KEY = 'mle_display_control_open_v112';

  function byId(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function safeParse(raw, fallback){ try { return JSON.parse(raw); } catch(e) { return fallback; } }
  function lsGet(key){ try { return localStorage.getItem(key); } catch(e) { return null; } }
  function lsSet(key, value){ try { localStorage.setItem(key, value); } catch(e) {} }
  function lsRemove(key){ try { localStorage.removeItem(key); } catch(e) {} }
  function has(el){ return !!(el && el.nodeType === 1); }

  function defaultState(){
    return {
      guide: true,
      dashboard: true,
      summary: true,
      nav: true,
      lotteryCards: true,
      adminHive: true,
      rememberCards: true
    };
  }
  function loadState(){
    var base = defaultState();
    var saved = safeParse(lsGet(STORE_KEY) || '{}', {});
    var k;
    for (k in saved) { if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(saved, k) && Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(base, k)) { base[k] = !!saved[k]; } }
    return base;
  }
  function saveState(state){ lsSet(STORE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state)); }

  function showHide(el, visible){
    if (!has(el)) { return; }
    if (visible) {
      el.classList.remove('mle-display-control-hidden-by-user');
      el.removeAttribute('data-mle-display-hidden-by-user');
    } else {
      el.classList.add('mle-display-control-hidden-by-user');
      el.setAttribute('data-mle-display-hidden-by-user', '1');
    }
  }

  function getSections(){
    return {
      guide: [byId('mle-user-manual')],
      dashboard: [byId('mle-decision-workspace')],
      summary: qsa('.mle-workspace-hero-shell,.mle-workspace-hero,.mle-start-panel,.mle-section-explainer,.mle-decision-summary').filter(function(el){ return el.id !== 'mle-admin-hive-research-dashboard' && el.id !== 'mle-decision-workspace'; }),
      nav: qsa('.mle-strategic-nav,.mle-lottery-control-strip'),
      lotteryCards: qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]'),
      adminHive: [byId('mle-admin-hive-research-dashboard')]
    };
  }

  function setCardOpen(card, open){
    var body;
    var buttons;
    var i;
    if (!has(card)) { return; }
    body = card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body');
    if (body) {
      body.style.display = open ? 'block' : 'none';
      body.setAttribute('aria-hidden', open ? 'false' : 'true');
    }
    if (open) { card.classList.remove('mle-v107-card-collapsed'); card.classList.add('is-expanded'); }
    else { card.classList.add('mle-v107-card-collapsed'); card.classList.remove('is-expanded'); }
    buttons = qsa('.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-v107-bottom-toggle,[data-mle-bottom-collapse="1"]', card);
    for (i = 0; i < buttons.length; i++) {
      buttons[i].setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');
      if (buttons[i].querySelector('span')) { buttons[i].querySelector('span').textContent = open ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand'; }
      else { buttons[i].textContent = open ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand'; }
    }
  }
  function cardKey(card){ return CARD_KEY_PREFIX + String(card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || card.id || 'unknown'); }
  function restoreCardStates(state){
    if (!state.rememberCards) { return; }
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]').forEach(function(card){
      var saved = lsGet(cardKey(card));
      if (saved === '1') { setCardOpen(card, true); }
      if (saved === '0') { setCardOpen(card, false); }
    });
  }
  function saveOneCardState(card){
    var body;
    var open;
    if (!has(card)) { return; }
    body = card.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card__body');
    open = !!(body && !(body.style.display === 'none' || body.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'true'));
    lsSet(cardKey(card), open ? '1' : '0');
  }
  function saveAllCardStates(){ qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]').forEach(saveOneCardState); }

  function restoreGuideState(){
    var guide = byId('mle-user-manual');
    var details = guide ? guide.querySelector('details') : null;
    var saved = lsGet(GUIDE_KEY);
    if (!details) { return; }
    if (saved === '1') { details.setAttribute('open', 'open'); }
    if (saved === '0') { details.removeAttribute('open'); }
  }

  function applyState(state){
    var sections = getSections();
    var key;
    var i;
    for (key in sections) {
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(sections, key)) { continue; }
      for (i = 0; i < sections[key].length; i++) { showHide(sections[key][i], state[key] !== false); }
    }
    saveState(state);
  }

  function buildOption(name, label, help, checked){
    var id = 'mle-dc-' + name;
    return '' +
      '<label class="mle-display-control__option" for="' + id + '">' +
        '<input id="' + id + '" type="checkbox" data-mle-display-option="' + name + '"' + (checked ? ' checked' : '') + '>' +
        '<span><strong>' + label + '</strong><span>' + help + '</span></span>' +
      '</label>';
  }

  function insertControl(state){
    var existing = byId('mle-display-control-center');
    var anchor;
    var html;
    var panel;
    if (existing) { return existing; }
    html = '' +
      '<details id="mle-display-control-center" class="mle-display-control">' +
        '<summary class="mle-display-control__summary">' +
          '<span class="mle-display-control__copy">' +
            '<span class="mle-display-control__eyebrow">Display Control</span>' +
            '<span class="mle-display-control__title">Choose what you want to see</span>' +
            '<span class="mle-display-control__text">Your choices are remembered on this browser. You can reset anytime.</span>' +
          '</span>' +
          '<span class="mle-display-control__summary-action" aria-hidden="true"></span>' +
        '</summary>' +
        '<div class="mle-display-control__body">' +
          '<div class="mle-display-control__grid">' +
            buildOption('guide', 'Guide', 'Show or hide the how-to guide.', state.guide) +
            buildOption('dashboard', 'Focus Summary', 'Show or hide the main decision summary.', state.dashboard) +
            buildOption('summary', 'Intro Panels', 'Show or hide top explainer and briefing panels.', state.summary) +
            buildOption('nav', 'Jump Controls', 'Show or hide jump and collapse controls.', state.nav) +
            buildOption('lotteryCards', 'Lottery Cards', 'Show or hide the lottery workspaces.', state.lotteryCards) +
            buildOption('adminHive', 'Admin Hive Panel', 'Admin-only hive activity panel when available.', state.adminHive) +
            buildOption('rememberCards', 'Remember Card Open/Closed', 'Keep each lottery card the way you left it.', state.rememberCards) +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="mle-display-control__actions">' +
            '<button type="button" data-mle-display-show-all="1">Show Everything</button>' +
            '<button type="button" data-mle-display-expand-cards="1">Expand Lottery Cards</button>' +
            '<button type="button" data-mle-display-collapse-cards="1">Collapse Lottery Cards</button>' +
            '<button type="button" data-mle-display-reset="1">Reset Display</button>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="mle-display-control__status" aria-live="polite">Display choices are saved on this device only.</div>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</details>';
    panel = document.createElement('div');
    panel.innerHTML = html;
    panel = panel.firstChild;
    anchor = byId('mle-user-manual') || byId('mle-decision-workspace') || document.querySelector('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]') || document.body.firstChild;
    if (anchor && anchor.parentNode) { anchor.parentNode.insertBefore(panel, anchor); }
    else { document.body.insertBefore(panel, document.body.firstChild); }
    if (lsGet(CONTROL_OPEN_KEY) === '1') { panel.setAttribute('open', 'open'); }
    return panel;
  }

  function wireControl(panel, state){
    if (!panel || panel.getAttribute('data-mle-display-wired') === '1') { return; }
    panel.setAttribute('data-mle-display-wired', '1');
    panel.addEventListener('toggle', function(){ lsSet(CONTROL_OPEN_KEY, panel.open ? '1' : '0'); });
    panel.addEventListener('change', function(e){
      var t = e.target || e.srcElement;
      var key;
      if (!t || !t.getAttribute) { return; }
      key = t.getAttribute('data-mle-display-option');
      if (!key) { return; }
      state[key] = !!t.checked;
      applyState(state);
      if (key === 'rememberCards' && state.rememberCards) { saveAllCardStates(); }
    });
    panel.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      var t = e.target || e.srcElement;
      var base;
      if (!t || !t.getAttribute) { return; }
      if (t.getAttribute('data-mle-display-show-all') === '1') {
        e.preventDefault();
        base = defaultState();
        state.guide = base.guide; state.dashboard = base.dashboard; state.summary = base.summary; state.nav = base.nav; state.lotteryCards = base.lotteryCards; state.adminHive = base.adminHive; state.rememberCards = base.rememberCards;
        qsa('[data-mle-display-option]', panel).forEach(function(cb){ cb.checked = state[cb.getAttribute('data-mle-display-option')] !== false; });
        applyState(state);
      }
      if (t.getAttribute('data-mle-display-expand-cards') === '1') {
        e.preventDefault();
        qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]').forEach(function(card){ setCardOpen(card, true); saveOneCardState(card); });
      }
      if (t.getAttribute('data-mle-display-collapse-cards') === '1') {
        e.preventDefault();
        qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]').forEach(function(card){ setCardOpen(card, false); saveOneCardState(card); });
      }
      if (t.getAttribute('data-mle-display-reset') === '1') {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (window.confirm && !window.confirm('Reset your display choices on this browser?')) { return; }
        lsRemove(STORE_KEY); lsRemove(GUIDE_KEY); lsRemove(CONTROL_OPEN_KEY);
        qsa('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]').forEach(function(card){ lsRemove(cardKey(card)); });
        window.location.reload();
      }
    });
  }

  function wireCardMemory(){
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      var t = e.target;
      var btn = t && t.closest ? t.closest('.mle-lottery-toggle,.mle-v107-bottom-toggle,[data-mle-bottom-collapse="1"]') : null;
      var card;
      var state = loadState();
      if (!btn || !state.rememberCards) { return; }
      card = btn.closest ? btn.closest('.mle-advisory-card[data-lottery-id]') : null;
      if (!card) { return; }
      setTimeout(function(){ saveOneCardState(card); }, 180);
    }, true);
  }

  function wireGuideMemory(){
    var guide = byId('mle-user-manual');
    var details = guide ? guide.querySelector('details') : null;
    if (!details || details.getAttribute('data-mle-display-guide-wired') === '1') { return; }
    details.setAttribute('data-mle-display-guide-wired', '1');
    details.addEventListener('toggle', function(){ lsSet(GUIDE_KEY, details.open ? '1' : '0'); });
  }

  function init(){
    var state = loadState();
    var panel = insertControl(state);
    wireControl(panel, state);
    applyState(state);
    restoreGuideState();
    restoreCardStates(state);
    wireCardMemory();
    wireGuideMemory();
  }

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init); }
  else { init(); }
}());




(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_PHASE2F_LAYOUT_STABILITY__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_PHASE2F_LAYOUT_STABILITY__ = true;

  var userIntent = false;
  var stabilizing = true;
  var startedAt = Date.now ? Date.now() : (new Date()).getTime();
  var MAX_STABILIZE_MS = 9000;
  var html = document.documentElement;

  function now(){ return Date.now ? Date.now() : (new Date()).getTime(); }
  function markUserIntent(){
    userIntent = true;
    stabilizing = false;
    try { html.classList.remove('mle-load-stabilizing'); } catch(e) {}
  }
  function isStabilizing(){
    if (!stabilizing) { return false; }
    if ((now() - startedAt) > MAX_STABILIZE_MS) {
      stabilizing = false;
      try { html.classList.remove('mle-load-stabilizing'); } catch(e) {}
      return false;
    }
    return true;
  }

  try { html.classList.add('mle-load-stabilizing'); } catch(e) {}

  ['pointerdown','mousedown','touchstart','keydown','wheel'].forEach(function(evt){
    try { document.addEventListener(evt, markUserIntent, {capture:true, passive:true, once:true}); }
    catch(e) { try { document.addEventListener(evt, markUserIntent, true); } catch(ignore) {} }
  });

  
  try {
    if (window.Element && Element.prototype && !Element.prototype.__mlePhase2fScrollPatched) {
      var nativeScrollIntoView = Element.prototype.scrollIntoView;
      Element.prototype.__mlePhase2fScrollPatched = true;
      Element.prototype.scrollIntoView = function(arg){
        if (!userIntent && isStabilizing()) { return; }
        return nativeScrollIntoView.call(this, arg);
      };
    }
  } catch(e) {}

  try {
    if (window.HTMLElement && HTMLElement.prototype && !HTMLElement.prototype.__mlePhase2fFocusPatched) {
      var nativeFocus = HTMLElement.prototype.focus;
      HTMLElement.prototype.__mlePhase2fFocusPatched = true;
      HTMLElement.prototype.focus = function(arg){
        if (!userIntent && isStabilizing()) {
          try { return nativeFocus.call(this, {preventScroll:true}); }
          catch(e) { return; }
        }
        return nativeFocus.call(this, arg);
      };
    }
  } catch(e2) {}

  function releaseStabilizer(){
    stabilizing = false;
    try { html.classList.remove('mle-load-stabilizing'); } catch(e) {}
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
    window.setTimeout(releaseStabilizer, 1800);
  } else {
    try { window.addEventListener('load', function(){ window.setTimeout(releaseStabilizer, 1800); }, {once:true}); }
    catch(e) { window.addEventListener('load', function(){ window.setTimeout(releaseStabilizer, 1800); }); }
  }
  window.setTimeout(releaseStabilizer, MAX_STABILIZE_MS + 250);
})();


(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_PHASE2L_COLLAPSE_STATE__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_PHASE2L_COLLAPSE_STATE__ = true;

  function qs(sel, root){ try { return (root || document).querySelector(sel); } catch(e) { return null; } }
  function qsa(sel, root){ try { return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); } catch(e) { return []; } }
  function closest(el, sel){ while(el && el.nodeType === 1){ if(el.matches && el.matches(sel)){ return el; } el = el.parentElement; } return null; }
  function byId(id){ try { return id ? document.getElementById(id) : null; } catch(e) { return null; } }
  function storageOk(){ try { var k='mle2l_t'; localStorage.setItem(k,'1'); localStorage.removeItem(k); return true; } catch(e) { return false; } }
  var canStore = storageOk();

  function selectedMode(){
    try {
      var u = new URL(window.location.href);
      if (u.searchParams.get('mle_full_workspace') === '1') { return false; }
      if (u.searchParams.get('mle_lottery_id')) { return true; }
      if (window.MLE_PHASE2L_SELECTED_LOTTERY_ID) { return true; }
    } catch(e) {
      if (window.MLE_PHASE2L_SELECTED_LOTTERY_ID) { return true; }
    }
    return false;
  }

  function lotteryIdFor(card){
    if (!card) { return '0'; }
    return card.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || card.getAttribute('data-mle-lottery-id') || String(window.MLE_PHASE2L_SELECTED_LOTTERY_ID || '0');
  }
  function panelKey(card, panel){
    var lid = lotteryIdFor(card);
    var pid = panel && panel.id ? panel.id : '';
    return 'mle.phase2l.section.' + lid + '.' + pid;
  }
  function readState(card, panel){
    if (!canStore) { return ''; }
    try { return localStorage.getItem(panelKey(card, panel)) || ''; } catch(e) { return ''; }
  }
  function writeState(card, panel, open){
    if (!canStore || !panel) { return; }
    try { localStorage.setItem(panelKey(card, panel), open ? 'open' : 'closed'); } catch(e) {}
  }
  function setButton(btn, open){
    if (!btn) { return; }
    try { btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false'); } catch(e) {}
    var node = qs('span', btn) || btn;
    var txt = String(node.textContent || '');
    if (/^\s*(Hide|Show)\s+/i.test(txt)) {
      node.textContent = txt.replace(/^\s*(Hide|Show)\s+/i, open ? 'Hide ' : 'Show ');
    } else if (/^\s*(Collapse|Expand)\s*$/i.test(txt)) {
      node.textContent = open ? 'Collapse' : 'Expand';
    } else if (/^\s*View\s+/i.test(txt) && open) {
      node.textContent = txt.replace(/^\s*View\s+/i, 'Hide ');
    } else if (/^\s*Hide\s+/i.test(txt) && !open) {
      node.textContent = txt.replace(/^\s*Hide\s+/i, 'View ');
    }
  }
  function setPanel(card, panel, open, persist){
    if (!panel) { return; }
    try {
      panel.style.display = open ? 'block' : 'none';
      panel.hidden = false;
      if (open) { panel.removeAttribute('hidden'); }
      panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', open ? 'false' : 'true');
    } catch(e) {}
    if (panel.id) {
      qsa('[aria-controls="' + panel.id.replace(/(["\\])/g, '\\$1') + '"]').forEach(function(btn){ setButton(btn, open); });
    }
    if (persist) { writeState(card, panel, open); }
  }
  function managedPanels(card){
    return qsa('[data-mle-primary-section-body="1"]', card);
  }
  function restoreCard(card){
    var panels = managedPanels(card);
    panels.forEach(function(panel){
      var saved = readState(card, panel);
      var open = saved === 'open';
      
      setPanel(card, panel, open, false);
    });
  }
  function restoreAll(){
    if (!selectedMode()) { return; }
    qsa('.mle-advisory-card').forEach(restoreCard);
    try { document.documentElement.classList.add('mle-phase2l-state-applied'); } catch(e) {}
  }

  function rememberFromButton(btn){
    if (!selectedMode() || !btn || !btn.getAttribute) { return; }
    var id = btn.getAttribute('aria-controls') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-panel') || btn.getAttribute('data-target-section') || '';
    var panel = byId(id);
    if (!panel || !panel.getAttribute || panel.getAttribute('data-mle-primary-section-body') !== '1') { return; }
    var card = closest(btn, '.mle-advisory-card') || closest(panel, '.mle-advisory-card');
    window.setTimeout(function(){
      var open = panel.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'false' && panel.style.display !== 'none';
      writeState(card, panel, open);
    }, 80);
  }

  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    var t = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('[aria-controls], [data-target-panel], [data-target-section], .mle-section-shortcut-btn') : null;
    if (!t) { return; }
    rememberFromButton(t);
  }, true);

  
  document.addEventListener('click', function(evt){
    if (!selectedMode()) { return; }
    var card = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('.mle-advisory-card') : null;
    if (!card) { return; }
    window.setTimeout(function(){
      managedPanels(card).forEach(function(panel){
        var open = panel.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'false' && panel.style.display !== 'none';
        writeState(card, panel, open);
      });
    }, 350);
  }, false);

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', restoreAll, {once:true});
  } else {
    restoreAll();
  }
  
  window.setTimeout(restoreAll, 700);
})();


(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_AJAX_LAZY_SAVED_RUNS_V1__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_AJAX_LAZY_SAVED_RUNS_V1__ = true;
  function byId(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function setText(el, value){ if (el) { el.textContent = String(value || ''); } }
  function addClass(el, cls){ if (!el) { return; } if (el.classList) { el.classList.add(cls); } else if (String(el.className || '').indexOf(cls) === -1) { el.className = String(el.className || '') + ' ' + cls; } }
  function removeNode(el){ if (el && el.parentNode) { el.parentNode.removeChild(el); } }
  function loadSavedRunsMore(btn){
    var href = btn ? (btn.getAttribute('data-mle-load-href') || '') : '';
    var targetId = btn ? (btn.getAttribute('data-mle-saved-more-target') || '') : '';
    var target = targetId ? byId(targetId) : null;
    var shell = btn && btn.closest ? btn.closest('[data-mle-saved-runs-more-shell]') : null;
    var fallback = shell && shell.querySelector ? shell.querySelector('.mle-sp-show-more__fallback') : null;
    if (!href || !target) { return true; }
    if (!window.DOMParser) { window.location.href = href; return false; }
    if (target.getAttribute('data-mle-loading') === '1' || target.getAttribute('data-mle-saved-runs-more-loaded') === '1') { return false; }
    target.setAttribute('data-mle-loading', '1');
    if (btn.disabled !== undefined) { btn.disabled = true; }
    setText(btn, 'Loading older saved predictions...');
    var xhrSavedRuns = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhrSavedRuns.open('GET', href, true);
    xhrSavedRuns.withCredentials = true;
    xhrSavedRuns.onreadystatechange = function() {
      if (xhrSavedRuns.readyState !== 4) { return; }
      if (xhrSavedRuns.status < 200 || xhrSavedRuns.status >= 300) {
        target.removeAttribute('data-mle-loading');
        if (btn.disabled !== undefined) { btn.disabled = false; }
        setText(btn, 'Could not load older predictions. Try again.');
        return;
      }
      var parser = new DOMParser();
      var doc = parser.parseFromString(String(xhrSavedRuns.responseText || ''), 'text/html');
      var loaded = targetId ? doc.getElementById(targetId) : null;
      if (!loaded || loaded.getAttribute('data-mle-saved-runs-more-loaded') !== '1') {
        target.removeAttribute('data-mle-loading');
        if (btn.disabled !== undefined) { btn.disabled = false; }
        setText(btn, 'Could not load older predictions. Try again.');
        return;
      }
      target.parentNode.replaceChild(document.importNode(loaded, true), target);
      if (btn) { removeNode(btn); }
      if (fallback) { removeNode(fallback); }
      if (shell) { addClass(shell, 'is-loaded'); }
    };
    xhrSavedRuns.onerror = function() {
      target.removeAttribute('data-mle-loading');
      if (btn.disabled !== undefined) { btn.disabled = false; }
      setText(btn, 'Could not load older predictions. Try again.');
    };
    xhrSavedRuns.send(null);
    return false;
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var t = ev.target && ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('[data-mle-load-saved-more]') : null;
    if (!t) { return; }
    ev.preventDefault();
    loadSavedRunsMore(t);
  }, false);
}());

  function replaceVisualSection(targetId, html){
    var parser;
    var doc;
    var loaded;
    var current;
    if (!targetId || !window.DOMParser) { return false; }
    parser = new DOMParser();
    doc = parser.parseFromString(String(html || ''), 'text/html');
    loaded = doc.getElementById(targetId);
    current = byId(targetId);
    if (!loaded || !current) { return false; }
    if (loaded.getAttribute('data-mle-visual-lazy') === '1') { return false; }
    current.parentNode.replaceChild(document.importNode(loaded, true), current);
    try {
      loaded = byId(targetId);
      if (loaded) {
        loaded.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth', block:'start'});
        if (!loaded.hasAttribute('tabindex')) { loaded.setAttribute('tabindex','-1'); }
        try { loaded.focus({preventScroll:true}); } catch(focusErr) { try { loaded.focus(); } catch(ignoreFocus) {} }
      }
    } catch(ignoreScroll) {}
    return true;
  }
  function loadVisual(btn){
    var targetId;
    var href;
    var shell;
    if (!btn || !btn.getAttribute) { return true; }
    targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-mle-load-target') || '';
    href = btn.getAttribute('data-mle-load-href') || btn.getAttribute('href') || '';
    shell = targetId ? byId(targetId) : null;
    if (!targetId || !href || !shell) { return true; }
    if (!window.DOMParser) { window.location.href = href; return false; }
    if (shell.getAttribute('data-mle-loading') === '1') { return false; }
    shell.setAttribute('data-mle-loading', '1');
    if (btn.disabled !== undefined) { btn.disabled = true; }
    setText(btn, 'Loading visual evidence...');
    var xhrVisual = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhrVisual.open('GET', href, true);
    xhrVisual.withCredentials = true;
    xhrVisual.onreadystatechange = function() {
      if (xhrVisual.readyState !== 4) { return; }
      if (xhrVisual.status < 200 || xhrVisual.status >= 300) {
        shell.removeAttribute('data-mle-loading');
        if (btn.disabled !== undefined) { btn.disabled = false; }
        setText(btn, 'Could not load visual evidence. Try again.');
        return;
      }
      if (!replaceVisualSection(targetId, xhrVisual.responseText)) {
        shell.removeAttribute('data-mle-loading');
        if (btn.disabled !== undefined) { btn.disabled = false; }
        setText(btn, 'Could not load visual evidence. Try again.');
      }
    };
    xhrVisual.onerror = function() {
      shell.removeAttribute('data-mle-loading');
      if (btn.disabled !== undefined) { btn.disabled = false; }
      setText(btn, 'Could not load visual evidence. Try again.');
    };
    xhrVisual.send(null);
    return false;
  }

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_AJAX_LAZY_ADMIN_AUDIT_V1__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_AJAX_LAZY_ADMIN_AUDIT_V1__ = true;

  function closest(el, selector) {
    while (el && el !== document) {
      if (el.matches && el.matches(selector)) { return el; }
      el = el.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }

  function getSectionFromHtml(html) {
    var wrap = document.createElement('div');
    wrap.innerHTML = String(html || '');
    return wrap.querySelector ? wrap.querySelector('#mle-duplicate-batch-integrity-center') : null;
  }

  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var btn = closest(ev.target || ev.srcElement, '[data-mle-dbi-lazy-load="1"]');
    var shell;
    var url;
    if (!btn) { return; }
    shell = closest(btn, '[data-mle-dbi-lazy-admin="1"]');
    url = btn.getAttribute('data-mle-dbi-url') || btn.getAttribute('href') || '';
    if (!shell || !url) { return; }
    ev.preventDefault();
    if (shell.getAttribute('data-mle-dbi-loading') === '1') { return; }
    shell.setAttribute('data-mle-dbi-loading', '1');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
    btn.disabled = true;
    if (!btn.getAttribute('data-original-text')) { btn.setAttribute('data-original-text', btn.textContent || ''); }
    btn.textContent = 'Loading admin audit...';
    var xhrAdminAudit = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhrAdminAudit.open('GET', url, true);
    xhrAdminAudit.withCredentials = true;
    xhrAdminAudit.onreadystatechange = function() {
      if (xhrAdminAudit.readyState !== 4) { return; }
      if (xhrAdminAudit.status < 200 || xhrAdminAudit.status >= 300) {
        shell.removeAttribute('data-mle-dbi-loading');
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.removeAttribute('aria-disabled');
        btn.textContent = btn.getAttribute('data-original-text') || 'Load Duplicate Batch Integrity Center';
        return;
      }
      var loaded = getSectionFromHtml(xhrAdminAudit.responseText);
      if (!loaded) {
        shell.removeAttribute('data-mle-dbi-loading');
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.removeAttribute('aria-disabled');
        btn.textContent = btn.getAttribute('data-original-text') || 'Load Duplicate Batch Integrity Center';
        return;
      }
      shell.parentNode.replaceChild(loaded, shell);
      try { loaded.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' }); } catch (e) { try { loaded.scrollIntoView(true); } catch (ignore) {} }
    };
    xhrAdminAudit.onerror = function() {
      shell.removeAttribute('data-mle-dbi-loading');
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.removeAttribute('aria-disabled');
      btn.textContent = btn.getAttribute('data-original-text') || 'Load Duplicate Batch Integrity Center';
    };
    xhrAdminAudit.send(null);
  }, false);
}());


(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_PHASE5E_PRECISION_TOGGLE__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_PHASE5E_PRECISION_TOGGLE__ = true;
  function closest(node, selector){
    while (node && node !== document) {
      if (node.matches && node.matches(selector)) { return node; }
      node = node.parentNode;
    }
    return null;
  }
  function q(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector ? (root || document).querySelector(sel) : null; }
  function setOpen(panel, open){
    var btn, body, label;
    if (!panel) { return; }
    btn = q('[data-mle-precision-summary-toggle="1"]', panel);
    body = q('[data-mle-precision-summary-body="1"]', panel);
    label = q('.mle-precision-focus-summary__toggle-text', panel);
    if (open) {
      if (panel.className.indexOf('is-open') === -1) { panel.className += ' is-open'; }
      panel.setAttribute('data-mle-precision-open', '1');
      if (body) { body.style.display = ''; body.removeAttribute('hidden'); body.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false'); }
      if (btn) { btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); }
      if (label) { label.textContent = 'Hide precision lock'; }
    } else {
      panel.className = String(panel.className || '').replace(/\bis-open\b/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
      panel.setAttribute('data-mle-precision-open', '0');
      if (body) { body.style.display = 'none'; body.setAttribute('hidden', 'hidden'); body.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true'); }
      if (btn) { btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false'); }
      if (label) { label.textContent = 'Show precision lock'; }
    }
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var btn = closest(ev.target || ev.srcElement, '[data-mle-precision-summary-toggle="1"]');
    var panel;
    if (!btn) { return; }
    panel = closest(btn, '[data-mle-precision-summary="1"]');
    if (!panel) { return; }
    ev.preventDefault();
    ev.stopPropagation();
    setOpen(panel, panel.className.indexOf('is-open') === -1);
  }, true);
  function init(){
    var panels = document.querySelectorAll ? document.querySelectorAll('[data-mle-precision-summary="1"]') : [];
    var i;
    for (i = 0; i < panels.length; i++) { setOpen(panels[i], panels[i].className.indexOf('is-open') !== -1); }
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init); }
  else { init(); }
}());

(function(){
  'use strict';
  if (window.__MLE_SKAI_REGULAR_BATCH_URL_FIX_V1__) { return; }
  window.__MLE_SKAI_REGULAR_BATCH_URL_FIX_V1__ = true;
  function closest(el, sel){ return el && el.closest ? el.closest(sel) : null; }
  function hasBatchText(el){
    var txt = String((el && (el.textContent || el.innerText)) || '');
    var cls = String((el && el.className) || '');
    var target = el && el.getAttribute ? String(el.getAttribute('data-action-target') || '') : '';
    return /9\s*-?\s*(batch|run)|global-learning|regular_skai_batch|prediction_9_batch/i.test(txt + ' ' + cls + ' ' + target);
  }
  function addParam(url, key, value){
    var hash = '';
    var parts;
    if (!url) { return url; }
    parts = String(url).split('#');
    url = parts[0];
    hash = parts.length > 1 ? '#' + parts.slice(1).join('#') : '';
    if (url.indexOf(key + '=') !== -1) { return url + hash; }
    url += (url.indexOf('?') === -1 ? '?' : '&') + encodeURIComponent(key) + '=' + encodeURIComponent(value);
    return url + hash;
  }
  function ensureRegularBatchUrl(url){
    if (!url || String(url).indexOf('skai-lottery-prediction') === -1) { return url || ''; }
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_skai_batch', '1');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_skai_bridge', '1');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_global_batch', '1');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_batch_scope', 'exact_lottery');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_guided_mode', 'global_learning');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_required_action', 'regular_9_batch');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_command_source', 'mylottoexpert');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_batch_type', 'regular_global_learning');
    url = addParam(url, 'open', 'regular_9_batch');
    url = addParam(url, 'source', 'mylottoexpert');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_single_mode', 'best_global_settings');
    url = addParam(url, 'mle_single_source', 'global_learning');
    return url;
  }
  function applyOne(el){
    var url;
    if (!el || !el.getAttribute || !hasBatchText(el)) { return; }
    url = el.getAttribute('data-skai-regular-url') || el.getAttribute('data-skai-url') || el.getAttribute('href') || '';
    url = ensureRegularBatchUrl(url);
    if (!url) { return; }
    if (el.tagName && el.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'a') { el.setAttribute('href', url); el.setAttribute('target', '_blank'); el.setAttribute('rel', 'noopener noreferrer'); }
    el.setAttribute('data-skai-regular-url', url);
    el.setAttribute('data-skai-url', url);
    el.setAttribute('data-mle-no-loading', '1');
  }
  function applyAll(){
    var nodes = document.querySelectorAll('a[data-skai-regular-url],a[href*="skai-lottery-prediction"],button[data-skai-regular-url],button[data-skai-url],.mle-regular-skai-batch-action-btn');
    var i;
    for (i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) { applyOne(nodes[i]); }
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev){
    var el = closest(ev.target, 'a[data-skai-regular-url],a[href*="skai-lottery-prediction"],button[data-skai-regular-url],button[data-skai-url],.mle-regular-skai-batch-action-btn');
    if (el) { applyOne(el); }
  }, true);
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ applyAll(); window.setTimeout(applyAll, 600); }); }
  else { applyAll(); window.setTimeout(applyAll, 600); }
  window.mleEnsureRegularSkaiBatchUrls = applyAll;
}());
